Bismi Allahi alrrahmani alrraheemi
Alhamdu lillahi rabbi alaalameena
Alrrahmani alrraheemi
Maliki yawmi alddeeni
Iyyaka naabudu waiyyaka nastaaeenu
Ihdina alssirata almustaqeema
Sirata allatheena anaamta aalayhim ghayri almaghdoobi aalayhim wala alddalleena
Aliflammeem
Thalika alkitabu la rayba feehi hudan lilmuttaqeena
Allatheena yuminoona bialghaybi wayuqeemoona alssalata wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona
Waallatheena yuminoona bima onzila ilayka wama onzila min qablika wabialakhirati hum yooqinoona
Olaika aala hudan min rabbihim waolaika humu almuflihoona
Inna allatheena kafaroo sawaon aalayhim aanthartahum am lam tunthirhum la yuminoona
Khatama Allahu aala quloobihim waaala samaihim waaala absarihim ghishawatun walahum aathabun aatheemun
Wamina alnnasi man yaqoolu amanna biAllahi wabialyawmi alakhiri wama hum bimumineena
Yukhadiaoona Allaha waallatheena amanoo wama yakhdaaoona illa anfusahum wama yashauroona
Fee quloobihim maradun fazadahumu Allahu maradan walahum aathabun aleemun bima kanoo yakthiboona
Waitha qeela lahum la tufsidoo fee alardi qaloo innama nahnu muslihoona
Ala innahum humu almufsidoona walakin la yashauroona
Waitha qeela lahum aminoo kama amana alnnasu qaloo anuminu kama amana alssufahao ala innahum humu alssufahao walakin la yaalamoona
Waitha laqoo allatheena amanoo qaloo amanna waitha khalaw ila shayateenihim qaloo inna maaakum innama nahnu mustahzioona
Allahu yastahzio bihim wayamudduhum fee tughyanihim yaamahoona
Olaika allatheena ishtarawoo alddalalata bialhuda fama rabihat tijaratuhum wama kanoo muhtadeena
Mathaluhum kamathali allathee istawqada naran falamma adaat ma hawlahu thahaba Allahu binoorihim watarakahum fee thulumatin la ubsiroona
Summun bukmun aumyun fahum la yarjiaoona
Aw kasayyibin mina alssamai feehi thulumatun waraadun wabarqun yajaaloona asabiaahum fee athanihim mina alssawaaiqi hathara almawti aAllahu muheetun bialkafireena
Yakadu albarqu yakhtafu absarahum kullama adaa lahum mashaw feehi waitha athlama aalayhim qamoo walaw shaa Allahu lathahaba bisamaihim aabsarihim inna Allaha aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Ya ayyuha alnnasu oabudoo rabbakumu allathee khalaqakum waallatheena min qablikum laaallakum tattaqoona
Allathee jaaala lakumu alarda firashan waalssamaa binaan waanzala mina alssamai maan faakhraja bihi mina alththamarati rizqan lakum ala tajaaloo lillahi andadan waantum taalamoona
Wain kuntum fee raybin mimma nazzalna aala aabdina fatoo bisooratin min mithlihi waodaoo shuhadaakum min dooni Allahi in kuntum adiqeena
Fain lam tafaaloo walan tafaaloo faittaqoo alnnara allatee waqooduha alnnasu waalhijaratu oaiddat lilkafireena
Wabashshiri allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati anna lahum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu kullama ruziqoo minha min thamaratin rizqan qaloo hatha allathee ruziqna min qablu waotoo bihi mutashabihan walahum feeha azwajun mutahharatun wahum feeha halidoona
Inna Allaha la yastahyee an yadriba mathalan ma baaoodatan fama fawqaha faamma allatheena amanoo fayaalamoona annahu alhaqqu min rabbihim waamma allatheena kafaroo fayaqooloona matha arada Allahu bihatha mathalan yudillu bihi katheeran wayahdee bihi katheeran wama udillu bihi illa alfasiqeena
Allatheena yanqudoona aahda Allahi min baadi meethaqihi wayaqtaaoona ma amara Allahu bihi an yoosala wayufsidoona fee alardi olaika umu alkhasiroona
Kayfa takfuroona biAllahi wakuntum amwatan faahyakum thumma yumeetukum thumma yuhyeekum thumma ilayhi turjaaoona
Huwa allathee khalaqa lakum ma fee alardi jameeaan thumma istawa ila alssamai fasawwahunna sabaa samawatin wahuwa bikulli shayin aleemun
Waith qala rabbuka lilmalaikati innee jaailun fee alardi khaleefatan qaloo atajaalu feeha man yufsidu feeha wayasfiku alddimaa wanahnu usabbihu bihamdika wanuqaddisu laka qala innee aalamu ma la taalamoona
Waaallama adama alasmaa kullaha thumma aaradahum aala almalaikati faqala anbioonee biasmai haolai in kuntum sadiqeena
Qaloo subhanaka la ailma lana illa ma aallamtana innaka anta alaaleemu alhakeemu
Qala ya adamu anbihum biasmaihim falamma anbaahum biasmaihim qala alam aqul lakum innee aalamu ghayba alssamawati waalardi waaalamu ma ubdoona wama kuntum taktumoona
Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa aba waistakbara wakana mina alkafireena
Waqulna ya adamu oskun anta wazawjuka aljannata wakula minha raghadan haythu shituma wala taqraba hathihi alshshajarata fatakoona mina lththalimeena
Faazallahuma alshshaytanu aanha faakhrajahuma mimma kana feehi waqulna ihbitoo baadukum libaadin aaduwwun walakum fee alardi ustaqarrun wamataaun ila heenin
Fatalaqqa adamu min rabbihi kalimatin fataba aalayhi innahu huwa alttawwabu alrraheemu
Qulna ihbitoo minha jameeaan faimma yatiyannakum minnee hudan faman tabiaa hudaya fala khawfun aalayhim wala hum yahzanoona
Waallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu alnnari hum feeha khalidoona
Ya banee israeela othkuroo niamatiya allatee anaamtu aalaykum waawfoo biaahdee oofi biaahdikum waiyyaya fairhabooni
Waaminoo bima anzaltu musaddiqan lima maaakum wala takoonoo awwala kafirin bihi wala tashtaroo biayatee thamanan qaleelan waiyyaya aittaqooni
Wala talbisoo alhaqqa bialbatili wataktumoo alhaqqa waantum taalamoona
Waaqeemoo alssalata waatoo alzzakata wairkaaoo maaa alrrakiaeena
Atamuroona alnnasa bialbirri watansawna anfusakum waantum tatloona alkitaba afala taaqiloona
Waistaaeenoo bialssabri waalssalati wainnaha lakabeeratun illa aala alkhashiaeena
Allatheena yathunnoona annahum mulaqoo rabbihim waannahum ilayhi rajiaoona
Ya banee israeela othkuroo niamatiya allatee anaamtu aalaykum waannee faddaltukum aala alaalameena
Waittaqoo yawman la tajzee nafsun aan nafsin shayan wala yuqbalu minha shafaaatun wala yukhathu minha aadlun wala hum yunsaroona
Waith najjaynakum min ali firaawna yasoomoonakum sooa alaathabi yuthabbihoona abnaakum wayastahyoona nisaakum wafee thalikum balaon min abbikum aatheemun
Waith faraqna bikumu albahra faanjaynakum waaghraqna ala firaawna waantum tanthuroona
Waith waaadna moosa arbaaeena laylatan thumma ittakhathtumu alaijla min baadihi waantum thalimoona
Thumma aafawna aankum min baadi thalika laaallakum tashkuroona
Waith atayna moosa alkitaba waalfurqana laaallakum tahtadoona
Waith qala moosa liqawmihi ya qawmi innakum thalamtum anfusakum biittikhathikumu alaijla fatooboo ila bariikum faoqtuloo anfusakum halikum khayrun lakum ainda bariikum fataba aalaykum innahu huwa alttawwabu alrraheemu
Waith qultum ya moosa lan numina laka hatta nara Allaha jahratan faakhathatkumu alssaaiqatu waantum tanthuroona
Thumma baaathnakum min baadi mawtikum laaallakum tashkuroona
Wathallalna aalaykumu alghamama waanzalna aalaykumu almanna waalssalwa kuloo min tayyibati ma razaqnakum wama thalamoona walakin kanoo nfusahum yathlimoona
Waith qulna odkhuloo hathihi alqaryata fakuloo minha haythu shitum raghadan waodkhuloo albaba sujjadan waqooloo hittatun naghfir lakum hatayakum wasanazeedu almuhsineena
Fabaddala allatheena thalamoo qawlan ghayra allathee qeela lahum faanzalna aala allatheena thalamoo rijzan mina alssamai bima kanoo afsuqoona
Waithi istasqa moosa liqawmihi faqulna idrib biaasaka alhajara fainfajarat minhu ithnata aashrata aaynan qad aalima kullu onasin ashrabahum kuloo waishraboo min rizqi Allahi wala taathaw fee alardi mufsideena
Waith qultum ya moosa lan nasbira aala taaamin wahidin faodau lana rabbaka yukhrij lana mimma tunbitu alardu min baqliha waqiththaiha wafoomiha waaadasiha wabasaliha qala atastabdiloona allathee huwa adna biallathee huwa khayrun ihbitoo misran fainna lakum ma saaltum waduribat aalayhimu alththillatu waalmaskanatu wabaoo bighadabin mina Allahi thalika biannahum kanoo yakfuroona biayati Allahi ayaqtuloona alnnabiyyeena bighayri alhaqqi thalika bima aasaw wakanoo yaatadoona
Inna allatheena amanoo waallatheena hadoo waalnnasara waalssabieena man amana biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri waaamila salihan falahum jruhum ainda rabbihim wala khawfun aalayhim wala hum yahzanoona
Waith akhathna meethaqakum warafaana fawqakumu alttoora khuthoo ma ataynakum biquwwatin waothkuroo ma feehi laaallakum tattaqoona
Thumma tawallaytum min baadi thalika falawla fadlu Allahi aalaykum warahmatuhu lakuntum mina alkhasireena
Walaqad aalimtumu allatheena iatadaw minkum fee alssabti faqulna lahum koonoo qiradatan khasieena
Fajaaalnaha nakalan lima bayna yadayha wama khalfaha wamawaithatan lilmuttaqeena
Waith qala moosa liqawmihi inna Allaha yamurukum an tathbahoo baqaratan qaloo atattakhithuna huzuwan qala aaoothu biAllahi an akoona ina aljahileena
Qaloo odau lana rabbaka yubayyin lana ma hiya qala innahu yaqoolu innaha baqaratun la faridun wala bikrun aawanun bayna thalika aifaaloo ma tumaroona
Qaloo odau lana rabbaka yubayyin lana ma lawnuha qala innahu yaqoolu innaha baqaratun safrao faqiaun lawnuha tasurru alnnathireena
Qaloo odau lana rabbaka yubayyin lana ma hiya inna albaqara tashabaha aalayna wainna in shaa Allahu lamuhtadoona
Qala innahu yaqoolu innaha baqaratun la thaloolun tutheeru alarda wala tasqee alhartha musallamatun la shiyata feeha qaloo alana jita ialhaqqi fathabahooha wama kadoo yafaaloona
Waith qataltum nafsan faiddaratum feeha waAllahu mukhrijun ma kuntum taktumoona
Faqulna idriboohu bibaadiha kathalika yuhyee Allahu almawta wayureekum ayatihi laaallakum taaqiloona
Thumma qasat quloobukum min baadi thalika fahiya kaalhijarati aw ashaddu qaswatan wainna mina alhijarati lama yatafajjaru minhu alanharu wainna minha lama yashshaqqaqu fayakhruju minhu almao wainna minha lama yahbitu min khashyati Allahi wama Allahu bighafilin amma taamaloona
Afatatmaaoona an yuminoo lakum waqad kana fareequn minhum yasmaaoona kalama Allahi thumma yuharrifoonahu min baadi ma aaqaloohu wahum aalamoona
Waitha laqoo allatheena amanoo qaloo amanna waitha khala baaduhum ila baadin qaloo atuhaddithoonahum bima fataha Allahu aalaykum iyuhajjookum bihi ainda rabbikum afala taaqiloona
Awala yaalamoona anna Allaha yaalamu ma yusirroona wama yualinoona
Waminhum ommiyyoona la yaalamoona alkitaba illa amaniyya wain hum illa yathunnoona
Fawaylun lillatheena yaktuboona alkitaba biaydeehim thumma yaqooloona hatha min aindi Allahi liyashtaroo bihi thamanan qaleelan awaylun lahum mimma katabat aydeehim wawaylun lahum mimma yaksiboona
Waqaloo lan tamassana alnnaru illa ayyaman maadoodatan qul attakhathtum ainda Allahi aahdan falan yukhlifa Allahu aahdahu am taqooloona ala Allahi ma la taalamoona
Bala man kasaba sayyiatan waahatat bihi khateeatuhu faolaika ashabu alnnari hum feeha khalidoona
Waallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoona
Waith akhathna meethaqa banee israeela la taabudoona illa Allaha wabialwalidayni ihsanan wathee alqurba waalyatama waalmasakeeni aqooloo lilnnasi husnan waaqeemoo alssalata waatoo alzzakata thumma tawallaytum illa qaleelan minkum waantum muaridoona
Waith akhathna meethaqakum la tasfikoona dimaakum wala tukhrijoona anfusakum min diyarikum thumma aqrartum waantum tashhadoona
Thumma antum haolai taqtuloona anfusakum watukhrijoona fareeqan minkum min diyarihim tathaharoona aalayhim bialithmi waalaudwani wain yatookum osara tufadoohum wahuwa muharramun aalaykum ikhrajuhum afatuminoona bibaadi alkitabi watakfuroona bibaadin fama jazao man yafaalu thalika minkum illa khizyun fee alhayati alddunya wayawma alqiyamati yuraddoona ila ashaddi alaathabi wama Allahu bighafilin amma taamaloona
Olaika allatheena ishtarawoo alhayata alddunya bialakhirati fala yukhaffafu aanhumu alaathabu wala hum yunsaroona
Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba waqaffayna min baadihi bialrrusuli waatayna aeesa ibna maryama albayyinati waayyadnahu biroohi alqudusi fakullama jaakum rasoolun bima la tahwa anfusukumu istakbartum fafareeqan kaththabtum wafareeqan taqtuloona
Waqaloo quloobuna ghulfun bal laaanahumu Allahu bikufrihim faqaleelan ma yuminoona
Walamma jaahum kitabun min aindi Allahi musaddiqun lima maaahum wakanoo min qablu yastaftihoona aala allatheena kafaroo falamma jaahum a aarafoo kafaroo bihi falaanatu Allahi aala alkafireena
Bisama ishtaraw bihi anfusahum an yakfuroo bima anzala Allahu baghyan an yunazzila Allahu min fadlihi aala man yashao min aibadihi abaoo bighadabin aala ghadabin walilkafireena aathabun muheenun
Waitha qeela lahum aminoo bima anzala Allahu qaloo numinu bima onzila aalayna wayakfuroona bima waraahu wahuwa alhaqqu musaddiqan lima aaahum qul falima taqtuloona anbiyaa Allahi min qablu in kuntum mumineena
Walaqad jaakum moosa bialbayyinati thumma ittakhathtumu alaijla min baadihi waantum thalimoona
Waith akhathna meethaqakum warafaana fawqakumu alttoora khuthoo ma ataynakum biquwwatin waismaaoo qaloo samiana waaasayna waoshriboo ee quloobihimu alaijla bikufrihim qul bisama yamurukum bihi eemanukum in kuntum mumineena
Qul in kanat lakumu alddaru alakhiratu ainda Allahi khalisatan min dooni alnnasi fatamannawoo almawta in kuntum sadiqeena
Walan yatamannawhu abadan bima qaddamat aydeehim waAllahu aaleemun bialththalimeena
Walatajidannahum ahrasa alnnasi aala hayatin wamina allatheena ashrakoo yawaddu ahaduhum law yuaammaru alfa sanatin wama huwa imuzahzihihi mina alaathabi an yuaammara waAllahu baseerun bima yaamaloona
Qul man kana aaduwwan lijibreela fainnahu nazzalahu aala qalbika biithni Allahi musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi wahudan wabushra ilmumineena
Man kana aaduwwan lillahi wamalaikatihi warusulihi wajibreela wameekala fainna Allaha aaduwwun lilkafireena
Walaqad anzalna ilayka ayatin bayyinatin wama yakfuru biha illa alfasiqoona
Awakullama aahadoo aahdan nabathahu fareequn minhum bal aktharuhum la yuminoona
Walamma jaahum rasoolun min aindi Allahi musaddiqun lima maaahum nabatha fareequn mina allatheena ootoo alkitaba kitaba Allahi waraa huhoorihim kaannahum la yaalamoona
Waittabaaoo ma tatloo alshshayateenu aala mulki sulaymana wama kafara sulaymanu walakinna alshshayateena kafaroo yuaallimoona alnnasa alssihra wama onzila aala almalakayni bibabila haroota wamaroota wama yuaallimani min ahadin hatta yaqoola innama nahnu fitnatun fala takfur fayataaallamoona minhuma ma yufarriqoona bihi bayna almari wazawjihi wama hum bidarreena bihi min ahadin illa biithni Allahi wayataaallamoona ma yadurruhum wala yanfaauhum walaqad aalimoo lamani ishtarahu ma lahu fee alakhirati min khalaqin walabisa ma sharaw ihi anfusahum law kanoo yaalamoona
Walaw annahum amanoo waittaqaw lamathoobatun min aindi Allahi khayrun law kanoo yaalamoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la taqooloo raaina waqooloo onthurna waismaaoo walilkafireena aathabun aleemun
Ma yawaddu allatheena kafaroo min ahli alkitabi wala almushrikeena an yunazzala aalaykum min khayrin min rabbikum waAllahu yakhtassu irahmatihi man yashao waAllahu thoo alfadli alaatheemi
Ma nansakh min ayatin aw nunsiha nati bikhayrin minha aw mithliha alam taalam anna Allaha aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Alam taalam anna Allaha lahu mulku alssamawati waalardi wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseerin
Am tureedoona an tasaloo rasoolakum kama suila moosa min qablu waman yatabaddali alkufra bialeemani faqad dalla sawaa alssabeeli
Wadda katheerun min ahli alkitabi law yaruddoonakum min baadi eemanikum kuffaran hasadan min aindi anfusihim min baadi ma tabayyana ahumu alhaqqu faoafoo waisfahoo hatta yatiya Allahu biamrihi inna Allaha aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Waaqeemoo alssalata waatoo alzzakata wama tuqaddimoo lianfusikum min khayrin tajidoohu ainda Allahi inna Allaha bima taamaloona baseerun
Waqaloo lan yadkhula aljannata illa man kana hoodan aw nasara tilka amaniyyuhum qul hatoo burhanakum in kuntum sadiqeena
Bala man aslama wajhahu lillahi wahuwa muhsinun falahu ajruhu ainda rabbihi wala khawfun aalayhim wala hum yahzanoona
Waqalati alyahoodu laysati alnnasara aala shayin waqalati alnnasara laysati alyahoodu aala shayin wahum yatloona alkitaba kathalika ala allatheena la yaalamoona mithla qawlihim faAllahu yahkumu baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoona
Waman athlamu mimman manaaa masajida Allahi an yuthkara feeha ismuhu wasaaa fee kharabiha olaika ma kana lahum an yadkhulooha illa haifeena lahum fee alddunya khizyun walahum fee alakhirati aathabun aatheemun
Walillahi almashriqu waalmaghribu faaynama tuwalloo fathamma wajhu Allahi inna Allaha wasiaun aaleemun
Waqaloo itakhatha Allahu waladan subhanahu bal lahu ma fee alssamawati waalardi kullun lahu qanitoona
Badeeau alssamawati waalardi waitha qada amran fainnama yaqoolu lahu kun fayakoonu
Waqala allatheena la yaalamoona lawla yukallimuna Allahu aw tateena ayatun kathalika qala allatheena min qablihim mithla qawlihim ashabahat quloobuhum qad bayyanna alayati liqawmin yooqinoona
Inna arsalnaka bialhaqqi basheeran wanatheeran wala tusalu Aaan ashabi aljaheemi
Walan tarda aanka alyahoodu wala alnnasara hatta tattabiaa millatahum qul inna huda Allahi huwa alhuda walaini ittabaata ahwaahum baada llathee jaaka mina alailmi ma laka mina Allahi min waliyyin wala naseerin
Allatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yatloonahu haqqa tilawatihi olaika yuminoona bihi waman yakfur bihi faolaika humu alkhasiroona
Ya banee israeela othkuroo niamatiya allatee anaamtu aalaykum waannee faddaltukum aala alaalameena
Waittaqoo yawman la tajzee nafsun aan nafsin shayan wala yuqbalu minha aadlun wala tanfaauha shafaaatun wala hum yunsaroona
Waithi ibtala ibraheema rabbuhu bikalimatin faatammahunna qala innee jaailuka lilnnasi imaman qala wamin thurriyyatee qala la yanalu ahdee alththalimeena
Waith jaaalna albayta mathabatan lilnnasi waamnan waittakhithoo min maqami ibraheema musallan waaahidna ila ibraheema waismaaeela an ahhira baytiya lilttaifeena waalaakifeena waalrrukkaai alssujoodi
Waith qala ibraheemu rabbi ijaal hatha baladan aminan waorzuq ahlahu mina alththamarati man amana minhum biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri ala waman kafara faomattiauhu qaleelan thumma adtarruhu ila aathabi alnnari wabisa almaseeru
Waith yarfaau ibraheemu alqawaaida mina albayti waismaaeelu rabbana taqabbal minna innaka anta alssameeau alaaleemu
Rabbana waijaalna muslimayni laka wamin thurriyyatina ommatan muslimatan laka waarina manasikana watub aalayna innaka anta alttawwabu lrraheemu
Rabbana waibaath feehim rasoolan minhum yatloo aalayhim ayatika wayuaallimuhumu alkitaba waalhikmata wayuzakkeehim innaka anta laazeezu alhakeemu
Waman yarghabu aan millati ibraheema illa man safiha nafsahu walaqadi istafaynahu fee alddunya wainnahu fee alakhirati lamina lssaliheena
Ith qala lahu rabbuhu aslim qala aslamtu lirabbi alaalameena
Wawassa biha ibraheemu baneehi wayaaqoobu ya baniyya inna Allaha istafa lakumu alddeena fala tamootunna illa waantum muslimoona
Am kuntum shuhadaa ith hadara yaaqooba almawtu ith qala libaneehi ma taabudoona min baadee qaloo naabudu ilahaka wailaha abaika braheema waismaaeela waishaqa ilahan wahidan wanahnu lahu muslimoona
Tilka ommatun qad khalat laha ma kasabat walakum ma kasabtum wala tusaloona aamma kano yaamaloona
Waqaloo koonoo hoodan aw nasara tahtadoo qul bal millata ibraheema haneefan wama kana mina almushrikeena
Qooloo amanna biAllahi wama onzila ilayna wama onzila ila ibraheema waismaaeela waishaqa wayaaqooba waalasbati wama ootiya moosa aaeesa wama ootiya alnnabiyyoona min rabbihim la nufarriqu bayna ahadin minhum wanahnu lahu muslimoona
Fain amanoo bimithli ma amantum bihi faqadi ihtadaw wain tawallaw fainnama hum fee shiqaqin fasayakfeekahumu Allahu wahuwa alssameeau laaleemu
Sibghata Allahi waman ahsanu mina Allahi sibghatan wanahnu lahu aabidoona
Qul atuhajjoonana fee Allahi wahuwa rabbuna warabbukum walana aamaluna walakum aamalukum wanahnu lahu mukhlisoona
Am taqooloona inna ibraheema waismaaeela waishaqa wayaaqooba waalasbata kanoo hoodan aw nasara qul aantum aalamu ami Allahu waman thlamu mimman katama shahadatan aindahu mina Allahi wama Allahu bighafilin aamma taamaloona
Tilka ommatun qad khalat laha ma kasabat walakum ma kasabtum wala tusaloona aamma kanoo yaamaloona
Sayaqoolu alssufahao mina alnnasi ma wallahum aan qiblatihimu allatee kanoo aalayha qul lillahi almashriqu waalmaghribu yahdee man ashao ila siratin mustaqeemin
Wakathalika jaaalnakum ommatan wasatan litakoonoo shuhadaa aala alnnasi wayakoona alrrasoolu aalaykum shaheedan wama jaaalna alqiblata allatee kunta aalayha illa linaalama man yattabiau alrrasoola mimman yanqalibu aala aaqibayhi wain kanat lakabeeratan illa aala llatheena hada Allahu wama kana Allahu liyudeeaa eemanakum inna Allaha bialnnasi laraoofun raheemun
Qad nara taqalluba wajhika fee alssamai falanuwalliyannaka qiblatan tardaha fawalli wajhaka shatra almasjidi alharami wahaythu ma kuntum fawalloo wujoohakum shatrahu wainna allatheena ootoo alkitaba layaalamoona annahu alhaqqu min rabbihim wama Allahu bighafilin amma yaamaloona
Walain atayta allatheena ootoo alkitaba bikulli ayatin ma tabiaoo qiblataka wama anta bitabiain qiblatahum wama baaduhum bitabiain iblata baadin walaini ittabaata ahwaahum min baadi ma jaaka mina alailmi innaka ithan lamina alththalimeena
Allatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yaarifoonahu kama yaarifoona abnaahum wainna fareeqan minhum layaktumoona alhaqqa wahum yaalamoona
Alhaqqu min rabbika fala takoonanna mina almumtareena
Walikullin wijhatun huwa muwalleeha faistabiqoo alkhayrati ayna ma takoonoo yati bikumu Allahu jameeaan inna Allaha aala kulli shayin adeerun
Wamin haythu kharajta fawalli wajhaka shatra almasjidi alharami wainnahu lalhaqqu min rabbika wama Allahu bighafilin aamma taamaloona
Wamin haythu kharajta fawalli wajhaka shatra almasjidi alharami wahaythu ma kuntum fawalloo wujoohakum shatrahu lialla yakoona lilnnasi alaykum hujjatun illa allatheena thalamoo minhum fala takhshawhum waikhshawnee waliotimma niamatee aalaykum walaaallakum tahtadoona
Kama arsalna feekum rasoolan minkum yatloo aalaykum ayatina wayuzakkeekum wayuaallimukumu alkitaba waalhikmata wayuaallimukum ma lam akoonoo taalamoona
Faothkuroonee athkurkum waoshkuroo lee wala takfurooni
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo istaaeenoo bialssabri waalssalati inna Allaha maaa alssabireena
Wala taqooloo liman yuqtalu fee sabeeli Allahi amwatun bal ahyaon walakin la tashauroona
Walanabluwannakum bishayin mina alkhawfi waaljooai wanaqsin mina alamwali waalanfusi waalththamarati wabashshiri alssabireena
Allatheena itha asabathum museebatun qaloo inna lillahi wainna ilayhi rajiaoona
Olaika aalayhim salawatun min rabbihim warahmatun waolaika humu almuhtadoona
Inna alssafa waalmarwata min shaaairi Allahi faman hajja albayta awi iatamara fala junaha aalayhi an yattawwafa bihima waman tatawwaaa hayran fainna Allaha shakirun aaleemun
Inna allatheena yaktumoona ma anzalna mina albayyinati waalhuda min baadi ma bayyannahu lilnnasi fee alkitabi olaika yalaanuhumu Allahu ayalaanuhumu allaainoona
Illa allatheena taboo waaslahoo wabayyanoo faolaika atoobu aalayhim waana alttawwabu alrraheemu
Inna allatheena kafaroo wamatoo wahum kuffarun olaika aalayhim laanatu Allahi waalmalaikati waalnnasi ajmaaeena
Khalideena feeha la yukhaffafu aanhumu alaathabu wala hum yuntharoona
Wailahukum ilahun wahidun la ilaha illa huwa alrrahmanu alrraheemu
Inna fee khalqi alssamawati waalardi waikhtilafi allayli waalnnahari waalfulki allatee tajree fee albahri bima yanfaau alnnasa wama anzala Allahu mina alssamai min main faahya bihi alarda baada mawtiha wabaththa feeha min kulli dabbatin watasreefi alrriyahi aalssahabi almusakhkhari bayna alssamai waalardi laayatin liqawmin yaaqiloona
Wamina alnnasi man yattakhithu min dooni Allahi andadan yuhibboonahum kahubbi Allahi waallatheena amanoo ashaddu hubban lillahi walaw ara allatheena thalamoo ith yarawna alaathaba anna alquwwata lillahi jameeaan waanna Allaha shadeedu alaathabi
Ith tabarraa allatheena ittubiaoo mina allatheena ittabaaoo waraawoo alaathaba wataqattaaat bihimu alasbabu
Waqala allatheena ittabaaoo law anna lana karratan fanatabarraa minhum kama tabarraoo minna kathalika yureehimu Allahu aamalahum asaratin aalayhim wama hum bikharijeena mina alnnari
Ya ayyuha alnnasu kuloo mimma fee alardi halalan tayyiban wala tattabiaoo khutuwati alshshaytani innahu lakum aaduwwun mubeenun
Innama yamurukum bialssooi waalfahshai waan taqooloo aala Allahi ma la taalamoona
Waitha qeela lahumu ittabiaoo ma anzala Allahu qaloo bal nattabiau ma alfayna aalayhi abaana awalaw kana abaohum la yaaqiloona shayan ala yahtadoona
Wamathalu allatheena kafaroo kamathali allathee yanaiqu bima la yasmaau illa duaaan wanidaan summun bukmun aumyun fahum la yaaqiloona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo kuloo min tayyibati ma razaqnakum waoshkuroo lillahi in kuntum iyyahu taabudoona
Innama harrama aalaykumu almaytata waalddama walahma alkhinzeeri wama ohilla bihi lighayri Allahi famani idturra ghayra baghin wala adin fala ithma aalayhi inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Inna allatheena yaktumoona ma anzala Allahu mina alkitabi wayashtaroona bihi thamanan qaleelan olaika ma yakuloona fee butoonihim illa lnnara wala yukallimuhumu Allahu yawma alqiyamati wala yuzakkeehim walahum aathabun aleemun
Olaika allatheena ishtarawoo alddalalata bialhuda waalaathaba bialmaghfirati fama asbarahum aala alnnari
Thalika bianna Allaha nazzala alkitaba bialhaqqi wainna allatheena ikhtalafoo fee alkitabi lafee shiqaqin baaeedin
Laysa albirra an tuwalloo wujoohakum qibala almashriqi waalmaghribi walakinna albirra man amana biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri waalmalaikati waalkitabi waalnnabiyyeena waata almala aala hubbihi thawee alqurba waalyatama waalmasakeena waibna alssabeeli waalssaileena wafee alrriqabi waaqama alssalata waata alzzakata waalmoofoona biaahdihim itha aahadoo waalssabireena fee albasai aalddarrai waheena albasi olaika allatheena sadaqoo waolaika humu almuttaqoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo kutiba aalaykumu alqisasu fee alqatla alhurru bialhurri waalaabdu bialaabdi waalontha bialontha faman aufiya lahu min akheehi shayon faittibaaun bialmaaroofi waadaon ilayhi biihsanin thalika takhfeefun min rabbikum warahmatun famani atada baada thalika falahu aathabun aleemun
Walakum fee alqisasi hayatun ya olee alalbabi laaallakum tattaqoona
Kutiba aalaykum itha hadara ahadakumu almawtu in taraka khayran alwasiyyatu lilwalidayni waalaqrabeena bialmaaroofi haqqan aala lmuttaqeena
Faman baddalahu baadama samiaahu fainnama ithmuhu aala allatheena yubaddiloonahu inna Allaha sameeaun aaleemun
Faman khafa min moosin janafan aw ithman faaslaha baynahum fala ithma aalayhi inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo kutiba aalaykumu alssiyamu kama kutiba aala allatheena min qablikum laaallakum tattaqoona
Ayyaman maadoodatin faman kana minkum mareedan aw aala safarin faaiddatun min ayyamin okhara waaala allatheena yuteeqoonahu fidyatun aaamu miskeenin faman tatawwaaa khayran fahuwa khayrun lahu waan tasoomoo khayrun lakum in kuntum taalamoona
Shahru ramadana allathee onzila feehi alquranu hudan lilnnasi wabayyinatin mina alhuda waalfurqani faman shahida minkumu alshshahra falyasumhu waman kana mareedan aw aala safarin faaiddatun min ayyamin okhara yureedu Allahu bikumu alyusra wala yureedu bikumu alausra alitukmiloo alaiddata walitukabbiroo Allaha aala ma hadakum walaaallakum tashkuroona
Waitha saalaka aibadee aannee fainnee qareebun ojeebu daawata alddaai itha daaani falyastajeeboo lee walyuminoo bee laaallahum arshudoona
Ohilla lakum laylata alssiyami alrrafathu ila nisaikum hunna libasun lakum waantum libasun lahunna aalima Allahu annakum kuntum takhtanoona anfusakum fataba aalaykum waaafa aankum faalana bashiroohunna waibtaghoo ma kataba Allahu lakum wakuloo waishraboo hatta yatabayyana lakumu alkhaytu alabyadu mina alkhayti alaswadi mina alfajri thumma atimmoo alssiyama ila allayli wala tubashiroohunna aantum aakifoona fee almasajidi tilka hudoodu Allahi fala taqrabooha kathalika yubayyinu Allahu ayatihi lilnnasi laaallahum yattaqoona
Wala takuloo amwalakum baynakum bialbatili watudloo biha ila alhukkami litakuloo fareeqan min amwali alnnasi bialithmi waantum aalamoona
Yasaloonaka aani alahillati qul hiya mawaqeetu lilnnasi waalhajji walaysa albirru bian tatoo albuyoota min thuhooriha walakinna albirra ani ittaqa watoo albuyoota min abwabiha waittaqoo Allaha laaallakum tuflihoona
Waqatiloo fee sabeeli Allahi allatheena yuqatiloonakum wala taatadoo inna Allaha la yuhibbu almuatadeena
Waoqtuloohum haythu thaqiftumoohum waakhrijoohum min haythu akhrajookum waalfitnatu ashaddu mina alqatli wala tuqatiloohum ainda lmasjidi alharami hatta yuqatilookum feehi fain qatalookum faoqtuloohum kathalika jazao alkafireena
Faini intahaw fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Waqatiloohum hatta la takoona fitnatun wayakoona alddeenu lillahi faini intahaw fala audwana illa aala alththalimeena
Alshshahru alharamu bialshshahri alharami waalhurumatu qisasun famani iatada aalaykum faiatadoo aalayhi bimithli ma iatada aalaykum aittaqoo Allaha waialamoo anna Allaha maaa almuttaqeena
Waanfiqoo fee sabeeli Allahi wala tulqoo biaydeekum ila alttahlukati waahsinoo inna Allaha yuhibbu almuhsineena
Waatimmoo alhajja waalaumrata lillahi fain ohsirtum fama istaysara mina alhadyi wala tahliqoo ruoosakum hatta yablugha alhadyu mahillahu faman kana minkum mareedan aw bihi athan min rasihi fafidyatun min siyamin aw sadaqatin aw nusukin faitha amintum faman tamattaaa bialaumrati ila alhajji fama istaysara mina alhadyi faman lam yajid fasiyamu thalathati ayyamin fee alhajji wasabaatin itha rajaatum tilka aasharatun kamilatun thalika liman lam yakun ahluhu hadiree almasjidi alharami waittaqoo Allaha waialamoo anna Allaha hadeedu alaiqabi
Alhajju ashhurun maaloomatun faman farada feehinna alhajja fala rafatha wala fusooqa wala jidala fee alhajji wama tafaaloo min khayrin aalamhu Allahu watazawwadoo fainna khayra alzzadi alttaqwa waittaqooni ya olee alalbabi
Laysa aalaykum junahun an tabtaghoo fadlan min rabbikum faitha afadtum min aarafatin faothkuroo Allaha ainda almashaari alharami aothkuroohu kama hadakum wain kuntum min qablihi lamina alddalleena
Thumma afeedoo min haythu afada alnnasu waistaghfiroo Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Faitha qadaytum manasikakum faothkuroo Allaha kathikrikum abaakum aw ashadda thikran famina alnnasi man yaqoolu rabbana atina fee lddunya wama lahu fee alakhirati min khalaqin
Waminhum man yaqoolu rabbana atina fee alddunya hasanatan wafee alakhirati hasanatan waqina aathaba alnnari
Olaika lahum naseebun mimma kasaboo waAllahu sareeau alhisabi
Waothkuroo Allaha fee ayyamin maadoodatin faman taaajjala fee yawmayni fala ithma aalayhi waman taakhkhara fala ithma aalayhi limani ttaqa waittaqoo Allaha waialamoo annakum ilayhi tuhsharoona
Wamina alnnasi man yuajibuka qawluhu fee alhayati alddunya wayushhidu Allaha aala ma fee qalbihi wahuwa aladdu alkhisami
Waitha tawalla saaa fee alardi liyufsida feeha wayuhlika alhartha waalnnasla waAllahu la yuhibbu alfasada
Waitha qeela lahu ittaqi Allaha akhathathu alaizzatu bialithmi fahasbuhu jahannamu walabisa almihadu
Wamina alnnasi man yashree nafsahu ibtighaa mardati Allahi waAllahu raoofun bialaibadi
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo odkhuloo fee alssilmi kaffatan wala tattabiaoo khutuwati alshshaytani innahu lakum aaduwwun mubeenun
Fain zalaltum min baadi ma jaatkumu albayyinatu faialamoo anna Allaha aazeezun hakeemun
Hal yanthuroona illa an yatiyahumu Allahu fee thulalin mina alghamami waalmalaikatu waqudiya alamru waila Allahi turjaau alomooru
Sal banee israeela kam ataynahum min ayatin bayyinatin waman yubaddil niamata Allahi min baadi ma jaathu fainna Allaha shadeedu alaiqabi
Zuyyina lillatheena kafaroo alhayatu alddunya wayaskharoona mina allatheena amanoo waallatheena ittaqaw fawqahum yawma alqiyamati aAllahu yarzuqu man yashao bighayri hisabin
Kana alnnasu ommatan wahidatan fabaaatha Allahu alnnabiyyeena mubashshireena wamunthireena waanzala maaahumu alkitaba bialhaqqi liyahkuma bayna alnnasi feema ikhtalafoo feehi wama ikhtalafa feehi illa allatheena ootoohu min baadi ma jaathumu albayyinatu baghyan aynahum fahada Allahu allatheena amanoo lima ikhtalafoo feehi mina alhaqqi biithnihi waAllahu yahdee man yashao ila siratin mustaqeemin
Am hasibtum an tadkhuloo aljannata walamma yatikum mathalu allatheena khalaw min qablikum massathumu albasao waalddarrao wazulziloo atta yaqoola alrrasoolu waallatheena amanoo maaahu mata nasru Allahi ala inna nasra Allahi qareebun
Yasaloonaka matha yunfiqoona qul ma anfaqtum min khayrin falilwalidayni waalaqrabeena waalyatama waalmasakeeni waibni alssabeeli wama afaaloo min khayrin fainna Allaha bihi aaleemun
Kutiba aalaykumu alqitalu wahuwa kurhun lakum waaasa an takrahoo shayan wahuwa khayrun lakum waaasa an tuhibboo shayan wahuwa sharrun akum waAllahu yaalamu waantum la taalamoona
Yasaloonaka aani alshshahri alharami qitalin feehi qul qitalun feehi kabeerun wasaddun aan sabeeli Allahi wakufrun bihi waalmasjidi alharami waikhraju ahlihi minhu akbaru ainda Allahi waalfitnatu akbaru mina alqatli wala yazaloona yuqatiloonakum hatta yaruddookum aan deenikum ini istataaoo waman yartadid minkum aan deenihi fayamut wahuwa kafirun faolaika habitat aamaluhum fee alddunya waalakhirati aolaika ashabu alnnari hum feeha khalidoona
Inna allatheena amanoo waallatheena hajaroo wajahadoo fee sabeeli Allahi olaika yarjoona rahmata Allahi waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Yasaloonaka aani alkhamri waalmaysiri qul feehima ithmun kabeerun wamanafiau lilnnasi waithmuhuma akbaru min nafaihima wayasaloonaka atha yunfiqoona quli alaafwa kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati laaallakum tatafakkaroona
Fee alddunya waalakhirati wayasaloonaka aani alyatama qul islahun lahum khayrun wain tukhalitoohum faikhwanukum waAllahu yaalamu lmufsida mina almuslihi walaw shaa Allahu laaanatakum inna Allaha aazeezun hakeemun
Wala tankihoo almushrikati hatta yuminna walaamatun muminatun khayrun min mushrikatin walaw aajabatkum wala tunkihoo almushrikeena hatta yuminoo walaaabdun muminun khayrun min mushrikin walaw aajabakum olaika yadaoona ila alnnari waAllahu yadaoo ila aljannati aalmaghfirati biithnihi wayubayyinu ayatihi lilnnasi laaallahum yatathakkaroona
Wayasaloonaka aani almaheedi qul huwa athan faiataziloo alnnisaa fee almaheedi wala taqraboohunna hatta yathurna faitha tatahharna atoohunna min haythu amarakumu Allahu inna Allaha yuhibbu alttawwabeena wayuhibbu almutatahhireena
Nisaokum harthun lakum fatoo harthakum anna shitum waqaddimoo lianfusikum waittaqoo Allaha waialamoo annakum mulaqoohu wabashshiri lmumineena
Wala tajaaloo Allaha aurdatan liaymanikum an tabarroo watattaqoo watuslihoo bayna alnnasi waAllahu sameeaun aaleemun
La yuakhithukumu Allahu biallaghwi fee aymanikum walakin yuakhithukum bima kasabat quloobukum waAllahu ghafoorun haleemun
Lillatheena yuloona min nisaihim tarabbusu arbaaati ashhurin fain faoo fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Wain aazamoo alttalaqa fainna Allaha sameeaun aaleemun
Waalmutallaqatu yatarabbasna bianfusihinna thalathata qurooin wala yahillu lahunna an yaktumna ma khalaqa Allahu fee arhamihinna in kunna yuminna biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri wabuaoolatuhunna ahaqqu biraddihinna fee thalika in aradoo islahan walahunna mithlu allathee alayhinna bialmaaroofi walilrrijali aalayhinna darajatun waAllahu aazeezun hakeemun
Alttalaqu marratani faimsakun bimaaroofin aw tasreehun biihsanin wala yahillu lakum an takhuthoo mimma ataytumoohunna shayan illa an yakhafa alla yuqeema hudooda Allahi fain khiftum alla yuqeema hudooda Allahi fala junaha aalayhima feema iftadat bihi tilka hudoodu llahi fala taatadooha waman yataaadda hudooda Allahi faolaika humu alththalimoona
Fain tallaqaha fala tahillu lahu min baadu hatta tankiha zawjan ghayrahu fain tallaqaha fala junaha aalayhima an yatarajaaa in thanna n yuqeema hudooda Allahi watilka hudoodu Allahi yubayyinuha liqawmin yaalamoona
Waitha tallaqtumu alnnisaa fabalaghna ajalahunna faamsikoohunna bimaaroofin aw sarrihoohunna bimaaroofin wala tumsikoohunna diraran litaatadoo waman yafaal thalika faqad thalama nafsahu wala tattakhithoo ayati Allahi huzuwan waothkuroo niamata Allahi aalaykum wama nzala aalaykum mina alkitabi waalhikmati yaaithukum bihi waittaqoo Allaha waialamoo anna Allaha bikulli shayin aaleemun
Waitha tallaqtumu alnnisaa fabalaghna ajalahunna fala taaduloohunna an yankihna azwajahunna itha taradaw baynahum bialmaaroofi thalika ooaathu bihi man kana minkum yuminu biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri thalikum azka lakum waatharu waAllahu yaalamu waantum la taalamoona
Waalwalidatu yurdiana awladahunna hawlayni kamilayni liman arada an yutimma alrradaaata waaala almawloodi lahu rizquhunna wakiswatuhunna bialmaaroofi la tukallafu nafsun illa wusaaha la tudarra walidatun biwaladiha wala mawloodun lahu biwaladihi waaala alwarithi mithlu thalika fain arada fisalan aan taradin minhuma watashawurin fala junaha aalayhima wain aradtum an tastardiaoo awladakum ala junaha aalaykum itha sallamtum ma ataytum bialmaaroofi waittaqoo Allaha waialamoo anna Allaha bima taamaloona baseerun
Waallatheena yutawaffawna minkum wayatharoona azwajan yatarabbasna bianfusihinna arbaaata ashhurin waaashran faitha balaghna ajalahunna ala junaha aalaykum feema faaalna fee anfusihinna bialmaaroofi waAllahu bima taamaloona khabeerun
Wala junaha aalaykum feema aarradtum bihi min khitbati alnnisai aw aknantum fee anfusikum aalima Allahu annakum satathkuroonahunna walakin la tuwaaidoohunna sirran illa an taqooloo qawlan maaroofan wala taazimoo auqdata alnnikahi hatta yablugha alkitabu ajalahu aialamoo anna Allaha yaalamu ma fee anfusikum faihtharoohu waialamoo anna Allaha ghafoorun haleemun
La junaha aalaykum in tallaqtumu alnnisaa ma lam tamassoohunna aw tafridoo lahunna fareedatan wamattiaoohunna aala almoosiai qadaruhu aaala almuqtiri qadaruhu mataaan bialmaaroofi haqqan aala almuhsineena
Wain tallaqtumoohunna min qabli an tamassoohunna waqad faradtum lahunna fareedatan fanisfu ma faradtum illa an yaafoona aw yaafuwa llathee biyadihi auqdatu alnnikahi waan taafoo aqrabu lilttaqwa wala tansawoo alfadla baynakum inna Allaha bima taamaloona baseerun
Hafithoo aala alssalawati waalssalati alwusta waqoomoo lillahi qaniteena
Fain khiftum farijalan aw rukbanan faitha amintum faothkuroo Allaha kama aallamakum ma lam takoonoo taalamoona
Waallatheena yutawaffawna minkum wayatharoona azwajan wasiyyatan liazwajihim mataaan ila alhawli ghayra ikhrajin fain kharajna fala unaha aalaykum fee ma faaalna fee anfusihinna min maaroofin waAllahu aazeezun hakeemun
Walilmutallaqati mataaun bialmaaroofi haqqan aala almuttaqeena
Kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakum ayatihi laaallakum taaqiloona
Alam tara ila allatheena kharajoo min diyarihim wahum oloofun hathara almawti faqala lahumu Allahu mootoo thumma ahyahum inna Allaha athoo fadlin aala alnnasi walakinna akthara alnnasi la yashkuroona
Waqatiloo fee sabeeli Allahi waialamoo anna Allaha sameeaun aaleemun
Man tha allathee yuqridu Allaha qardan hasanan fayudaaifahu lahu adaafan katheeratan waAllahu yaqbidu wayabsutu wailayhi turjaaoona
Alam tara ila almalai min banee israeela min baadi moosa ith qaloo linabiyyin lahumu ibaath lana malikan nuqatil fee sabeeli Allahi qala hal aasaytum in kutiba aalaykumu alqitalu alla tuqatiloo qaloo wama lana alla nuqatila fee sabeeli Allahi waqad okhrijna min iyarina waabnaina falamma kutiba aalayhimu alqitalu tawallaw illa qaleelan minhum waAllahu aaleemun bialththalimeena
Waqala lahum nabiyyuhum inna Allaha qad baaatha lakum taloota malikan qaloo anna yakoonu lahu almulku aalayna wanahnu ahaqqu bialmulki minhu walam yuta saaatan mina almali qala inna Allaha istafahu aalaykum wazadahu bastatan fee alailmi waaljismi waAllahu yutee mulkahu an yashao waAllahu wasiaun aaleemun
Waqala lahum nabiyyuhum inna ayata mulkihi an yatiyakumu alttabootu feehi sakeenatun min rabbikum wabaqiyyatun mimma taraka alu moosa aalu haroona tahmiluhu almalaikatu inna fee thalika laayatan lakum in kuntum mumineena
Falamma fasala talootu bialjunoodi qala inna Allaha mubtaleekum binaharin faman shariba minhu falaysa minnee waman lam yataamhu fainnahu minnee illa mani ightarafa ghurfatan biyadihi fashariboo minhu illa qaleelan minhum falamma jawazahu huwa waallatheena amanoo maaahu qaloo la taqata lana alyawma bijaloota wajunoodihi qala allatheena yathunnoona annahum mulaqoo Allahi kam min fiatin qaleelatin halabat fiatan katheeratan biithni Allahi waAllahu maaa alssabireena
Walamma barazoo lijaloota wajunoodihi qaloo rabbana afrigh aalayna sabran wathabbit aqdamana waonsurna aala alqawmi alkafireena
Fahazamoohum biithni Allahi waqatala dawoodu jaloota waatahu Allahu almulka waalhikmata waaallamahu mimma yashao walawla dafau Allahi lnnasa baadahum bibaadin lafasadati alardu walakinna Allaha thoo fadlin aala alaalameena
Tilka ayatu Allahi natlooha aalayka bialhaqqi wainnaka lamina almursaleena
Tilka alrrusulu faddalna baadahum aala baadin minhum man kallama Allahu warafaaa baadahum darajatin waatayna aeesa ibna maryama albayyinati waayyadnahu biroohi alqudusi walaw shaa Allahu ma iqtatala allatheena min baadihim min baadi ma jaathumu albayyinatu alakini ikhtalafoo faminhum man amana waminhum man kafara walaw shaa Allahu ma iqtataloo walakinna Allaha yafaalu ma yureedu
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo anfiqoo mimma razaqnakum min qabli an yatiya yawmun la bayaun feehi wala khullatun wala shafaaatun aalkafiroona humu alththalimoona
Allahu la ilaha illa huwa alhayyu alqayyoomu la takhuthuhu sinatun wala nawmun lahu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi man tha allathee yashfaau aindahu illa biithnihi yaalamu ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum wala yuheetoona bishayin min ailmihi illa bima shaa wasiaa ursiyyuhu alssamawati waalarda wala yaooduhu hifthuhuma wahuwa alaaliyyu alaatheemu
La ikraha fee alddeeni qad tabayyana alrrushdu mina alghayyi faman yakfur bialttaghooti wayumin biAllahi faqadi istamsaka bialaurwati lwuthqa la infisama laha waAllahu sameeaun aaleemun
Allahu waliyyu allatheena amanoo yukhrijuhum mina alththulumati ila alnnoori waallatheena kafaroo awliyaohumu alttaghootu ukhrijoonahum mina alnnoori ila alththulumati olaika ashabu alnnari hum feeha khalidoona
Alam tara ila allathee hajja ibraheema fee rabbihi an atahu Allahu almulka ith qala ibraheemu rabbiya allathee yuhyee wayumeetu qala ana ohyee waomeetu qala ibraheemu fainna Allaha yatee bialshshamsi mina almashriqi fati biha mina almaghribi fabuhita allathee kafara aAllahu la yahdee alqawma alththalimeena
Aw kaallathee marra aala qaryatin wahiya khawiyatun aala aurooshiha qala anna yuhyee hathihi Allahu baada mawtiha faamatahu Allahu miata aamin thumma baaathahu qala kam labithta qala labithtu yawman aw baada yawmin qala bal labithta miata aamin faonthur ila taaamika washarabika lam yatasannah waonthur ila himarika walinajaalaka ayatan lilnnasi waonthur ila alaithami kayfa nunshizuha thumma naksooha ahman falamma tabayyana lahu qala aalamu anna Allaha aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Waith qala ibraheemu rabbi arinee kayfa tuhyee almawta qala awalam tumin qala bala walakin liyatmainna qalbee qala fakhuth arbaaatan mina alttayri fasurhunna ilayka thumma ijaal aala kulli jabalin minhunna juzan thumma odauhunna yateenaka saayan waialam anna Allaha azeezun hakeemun
Mathalu allatheena yunfiqoona amwalahum fee sabeeli Allahi kamathali habbatin anbatat sabaa sanabila fee kulli sunbulatin miatu abbatin waAllahu yudaaifu liman yashao waAllahu wasiaun aaleemun
Allatheena yunfiqoona amwalahum fee sabeeli Allahi thumma la yutbiaoona ma anfaqoo mannan wala athan lahum ajruhum ainda rabbihim wala hawfun aalayhim wala hum yahzanoona
Qawlun maaroofun wamaghfiratun khayrun min sadaqatin yatbaauha athan waAllahu ghaniyyun haleemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tubtiloo sadaqatikum bialmanni waalatha kaallathee yunfiqu malahu riaa alnnasi wala yuminu biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri famathaluhu kamathali safwanin aalayhi turabun faasabahu wabilun fatarakahu saldan la yaqdiroona aala shayin mimma asaboo waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alkafireena
Wamathalu allatheena yunfiqoona amwalahumu ibtighaa mardati Allahi watathbeetan min anfusihim kamathali jannatin birabwatin asabaha abilun faatat okulaha diafayni fain lam yusibha wabilun fatallun waAllahu bima taamaloona baseerun
Ayawaddu ahadukum an takoona lahu jannatun min nakheelin waaanabin tajree min tahtiha alanharu lahu feeha min kulli alththamarati waasabahu alkibaru walahu thurriyyatun duaafao faasabaha iasarun feehi narun faihtaraqat kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati aaallakum tatafakkaroona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo anfiqoo min tayyibati ma kasabtum wamimma akhrajna lakum mina alardi wala tayammamoo alkhabeetha minhu unfiqoona walastum biakhitheehi illa an tughmidoo feehi waialamoo anna Allaha ghaniyyun hameedun
Alshshaytanu yaaidukumu alfaqra wayamurukum bialfahshai waAllahu yaaidukum maghfiratan minhu wafadlan waAllahu wasiaun aaleemun
Yutee alhikmata man yashao waman yuta alhikmata faqad ootiya khayran katheeran wama yaththakkaru illa oloo alalbabi
Wama anfaqtum min nafaqatin aw nathartum min nathrin fainna Allaha yaalamuhu wama lilththalimeena min ansarin
In tubdoo alssadaqati faniaimma hiya wain tukhfooha watutooha alfuqaraa fahuwa khayrun lakum wayukaffiru aankum min sayyiatikum aAllahu bima taamaloona khabeerun
Laysa aalayka hudahum walakinna Allaha yahdee man yashao wama tunfiqoo min khayrin falianfusikum wama tunfiqoona illa ibtighaa wajhi llahi wama tunfiqoo min khayrin yuwaffa ilaykum waantum la tuthlamoona
Lilfuqarai allatheena ohsiroo fee sabeeli Allahi la yastateeaoona darban fee alardi yahsabuhumu aljahilu aghniyaa mina alttaaaffufi aarifuhum biseemahum la yasaloona alnnasa ilhafan wama tunfiqoo min khayrin fainna Allaha bihi aaleemun
Allatheena yunfiqoona amwalahum biallayli waalnnahari sirran waaalaniyatan falahum ajruhum ainda rabbihim wala khawfun aalayhim wala um yahzanoona
Allatheena yakuloona alrriba la yaqoomoona illa kama yaqoomu allathee yatakhabbatuhu alshshaytanu mina almassi thalika biannahum qaloo innama albayau mithlu alrriba waahalla Allahu albayaa waharrama alrriba faman jaahu mawaithatun min rabbihi faintaha falahu ma salafa aamruhu ila Allahi waman aada faolaika ashabu alnnari hum feeha khalidoona
Yamhaqu Allahu alrriba wayurbee alssadaqati waAllahu la yuhibbu kulla kaffarin atheemin
Inna allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati waaqamoo alssalata waatawoo alzzakata lahum ajruhum ainda rabbihim wala khawfun aalayhim ala hum yahzanoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha watharoo ma baqiya mina alrriba in kuntum mumineena
Fain lam tafaaloo fathanoo biharbin mina Allahi warasoolihi wain tubtum falakum ruoosu amwalikum la tathlimoona wala tuthlamoona
Wain kana thoo ausratin fanathiratun ila maysaratin waan tasaddaqoo khayrun lakum in kuntum taalamoona
Waittaqoo yawman turjaaoona feehi ila Allahi thumma tuwaffa kullu nafsin ma kasabat wahum la yuthlamoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha tadayantum bidaynin ila ajalin musamman faoktuboohu walyaktub baynakum katibun bialaadli wala yaba katibun an yaktuba kama aallamahu Allahu falyaktub walyumlili allathee aalayhi alhaqqu walyattaqi Allaha rabbahu wala yabkhas minhu shayan fain kana allathee aalayhi alhaqqu safeehan aw daaeefan aw la yastateeau an yumilla huwa falyumlil waliyyuhu bialaadli waistashhidoo shaheedayni min rijalikum fain lam yakoona rajulayni farajulun waimraatani mimman tardawna mina alshshuhadai an tadilla ihdahuma fatuthakkira ihdahuma alokhra wala yaba alshshuhadao itha ma duaoo wala tasamoo an taktuboohu sagheeran aw kabeeran ila ajalihi thalikum aqsatu ainda Allahi waaqwamu lilshshahadati waadna alla tartaboo illa an takoona tijaratan hadiratan tudeeroonaha baynakum falaysa aalaykum junahun alla taktubooha waashhidoo itha tabayaatum wala yudarra katibun wala shaheedun wain tafaaloo fainnahu fusooqun ikum waittaqoo Allaha wayuaallimukumu Allahu waAllahu bikulli shayin aaleemun
Wain kuntum aala safarin walam tajidoo katiban farihanun maqboodatun fain amina baadukum baadan falyuaddi allathee itumina amanatahu alyattaqi Allaha rabbahu wala taktumoo alshshahadata waman yaktumha fainnahu athimun qalbuhu waAllahu bima taamaloona aaleemun
Lillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wain tubdoo ma fee anfusikum aw tukhfoohu yuhasibkum bihi Allahu fayaghfiru liman yashao ayuaaththibu man yashao waAllahu aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Amana alrrasoolu bima onzila ilayhi min rabbihi waalmuminoona kullun amana biAllahi wamalaikatihi wakutubihi warusulihi la nufarriqu ayna ahadin min rusulihi waqaloo samiana waataana ghufranaka rabbana wailayka almaseeru
La yukallifu Allahu nafsan illa wusaaha laha ma kasabat waaalayha ma iktasabat rabbana la tuakhithna in naseena aw akhtana rabbana wala tahmil aalayna isran kama hamaltahu aala allatheena min qablina rabbana wala tuhammilna ma la taqata lana bihi waoafu aanna waighfir ana wairhamna anta mawlana faonsurna aala alqawmi alkafireena
Aliflammeem
Allahu la ilaha illa huwa alhayyu alqayyoomu
Nazzala aalayka alkitaba bialhaqqi musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi waanzala alttawrata waalinjeela
Min qablu hudan lilnnasi waanzala alfurqana inna allatheena kafaroo biayati Allahi lahum aathabun shadeedun waAllahu aazeezun thoo ntiqamin
Inna Allaha la yakhfa aalayhi shayon fee alardi wala fee alssamai
Huwa allathee yusawwirukum fee alarhami kayfa yashao la ilaha illa huwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Huwa allathee anzala aalayka alkitaba minhu ayatun muhkamatun hunna ommu alkitabi waokharu mutashabihatun faamma allatheena fee quloobihim zayghun fayattabiaoona ma tashabaha minhu ibtighaa alfitnati waibtighaa taweelihi wama yaalamu taweelahu illa Allahu aalrrasikhoona fee alailmi yaqooloona amanna bihi kullun min aindi rabbina wama yaththakkaru illa oloo alalbabi
Rabbana la tuzigh quloobana baada ith hadaytana wahab lana min ladunka rahmatan innaka anta alwahhabu
Rabbana innaka jamiau alnnasi liyawmin la rayba feehi inna Allaha la yukhlifu almeeaada
Inna allatheena kafaroo lan tughniya aanhum amwaluhum wala awladuhum mina Allahi shayan waolaika hum waqoodu alnnari
Kadabi ali firaawna waallatheena min qablihim kaththaboo biayatina faakhathahumu Allahu bithunoobihim waAllahu shadeedu alaiqabi
Qul lillatheena kafaroo satughlaboona watuhsharoona ila jahannama wabisa almihadu
Qad kana lakum ayatun fee fiatayni iltaqata fiatun tuqatilu fee sabeeli Allahi waokhra kafiratun yarawnahum mithlayhim raya alaayni aAllahu yuayyidu binasrihi man yashao inna fee thalika laaibratan liolee alabsari
Zuyyina lilnnasi hubbu alshshahawati mina alnnisai waalbaneena waalqanateeri almuqantarati mina alththahabi waalfiddati waalkhayli lmusawwamati waalanaami waalharthi thalika mataau alhayati alddunya waAllahu aindahu husnu almaabi
Qul aonabbiokum bikhayrin min thalikum lillatheena ittaqaw ainda rabbihim jannatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha aazwajun mutahharatun waridwanun mina Allahi waAllahu baseerun bialaibadi
Allatheena yaqooloona rabbana innana amanna faighfir lana thunoobana waqina aathaba alnnari
Alssabireena waalssadiqeena waalqaniteena waalmunfiqeena waalmustaghfireena bialashari
Shahida Allahu annahu la ilaha illa huwa waalmalaikatu waoloo alailmi qaiman bialqisti la ilaha illa huwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Inna alddeena ainda Allahi alislamu wama ikhtalafa allatheena ootoo alkitaba illa min baadi ma jaahumu alailmu baghyan baynahum waman akfur biayati Allahi fainna Allaha sareeau alhisabi
Fain hajjooka faqul aslamtu wajhiya lillahi wamani ittabaaani waqul lillatheena ootoo alkitaba waalommiyyeena aaslamtum fain aslamoo aqadi ihtadaw wain tawallaw fainnama aalayka albalaghu waAllahu baseerun bialaibadi
Inna allatheena yakfuroona biayati Allahi wayaqtuloona alnnabiyyeena bighayri haqqin wayaqtuloona allatheena yamuroona bialqisti mina lnnasi fabashshirhum biaathabin aleemin
Olaika allatheena habitat aamaluhum fee alddunya waalakhirati wama lahum min nasireena
Alam tara ila allatheena ootoo naseeban mina alkitabi yudaawna ila kitabi Allahi liyahkuma baynahum thumma yatawalla fareequn minhum ahum muaridoona
Thalika biannahum qaloo lan tamassana alnnaru illa ayyaman maadoodatin wagharrahum fee deenihim ma kanoo yaftaroona
Fakayfa itha jamaanahum liyawmin la rayba feehi wawuffiyat kullu nafsin ma kasabat wahum la yuthlamoona
Quli allahumma malika almulki tutee almulka man tashao watanziau almulka mimman tashao watuaizzu man tashao watuthillu man tashao iyadika alkhayru innaka aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Tooliju allayla fee alnnahari watooliju alnnahara fee allayli watukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti watukhriju almayyita mina alhayyi atarzuqu man tashao bighayri hisabin
La yattakhithi almuminoona alkafireena awliyaa min dooni almumineena waman yafaal thalika falaysa mina Allahi fee shayin illa an attaqoo minhum tuqatan wayuhaththirukumu Allahu nafsahu waila Allahi almaseeru
Qul in tukhfoo ma fee sudoorikum aw tubdoohu yaalamhu Allahu wayaalamu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi waAllahu aala kulli shayin adeerun
Yawma tajidu kullu nafsin ma aamilat min khayrin muhdaran wama aamilat min sooin tawaddu law anna baynaha wabaynahu amadan baaeedan ayuhaththirukumu Allahu nafsahu waAllahu raoofun bialaibadi
Qul in kuntum tuhibboona Allaha faittabiaoonee yuhbibkumu Allahu wayaghfir lakum thunoobakum waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Qul ateeaoo Allaha waalrrasoola fain tawallaw fainna Allaha la yuhibbu alkafireena
Inna Allaha istafa adama wanoohan waala ibraheema waala aimrana aala alaalameena
Thurriyyatan baaduha min baadin waAllahu sameeaun aaleemun
Ith qalati imraatu aimrana rabbi innee nathartu laka ma fee batnee muharraran fataqabbal minnee innaka anta alssameeau alaaleemu
Falamma wadaaatha qalat rabbi innee wadaatuha ontha waAllahu aalamu bima wadaaat walaysa alththakaru kaalontha wainnee sammaytuha aryama wainnee oaeethuha bika wathurriyyataha mina alshshaytani alrrajeemi
Fataqabbalaha rabbuha biqaboolin hasanin waanbataha nabatan hasanan wakaffalaha zakariyya kullama dakhala aalayha zakariyya almihraba ajada aindaha rizqan qala ya maryamu anna laki hatha qalat huwa min aindi Allahi inna Allaha yarzuqu man yashao bighayri hisabin
Hunalika daaa zakariyya rabbahu qala rabbi hab lee min ladunka thurriyyatan tayyibatan innaka sameeau aldduaai
Fanadathu almalaikatu wahuwa qaimun yusallee fee almihrabi anna Allaha yubashshiruka biyahya musaddiqan bikalimatin mina Allahi asayyidan wahasooran wanabiyyan mina alssaliheena
Qala rabbi anna yakoonu lee ghulamun waqad balaghaniya alkibaru waimraatee aaqirun qala kathalika Allahu yafaalu ma yashao
Qala rabbi ijaal lee ayatan qala ayatuka alla tukallima alnnasa thalathata ayyamin illa ramzan waothkur rabbaka katheeran wasabbih ialaashiyyi waalibkari
Waith qalati almalaikatu ya maryamu inna Allaha istafaki watahharaki waistafaki aala nisai alaalameena
Ya maryamu oqnutee lirabbiki waosjudee wairkaaee maaa alrrakiaeena
Thalika min anbai alghaybi nooheehi ilayka wama kunta ladayhim ith yulqoona aqlamahum ayyuhum yakfulu maryama wama kunta ladayhim ith akhtasimoona
Ith qalati almalaikatu ya maryamu inna Allaha yubashshiruki bikalimatin minhu ismuhu almaseehu aeesa ibnu maryama wajeehan fee alddunya aalakhirati wamina almuqarrabeena
Wayukallimu alnnasa fee almahdi wakahlan wamina alssaliheena
Qalat rabbi anna yakoonu lee waladun walam yamsasnee basharun qala kathaliki Allahu yakhluqu ma yashao itha qada amran fainnama yaqoolu ahu kun fayakoonu
Wayuaallimuhu alkitaba waalhikmata waalttawrata waalinjeela
Warasoolan ila banee israeela annee qad jitukum biayatin min rabbikum annee akhluqu lakum mina altteeni kahayati alttayri faanfukhu feehi fayakoonu tayran biithni Allahi waobrio alakmaha waalabrasa waohyee almawta biithni Allahi waonabbiokum bima takuloona wama addakhiroona fee buyootikum inna fee thalika laayatan lakum in kuntum mumineena
Wamusaddiqan lima bayna yadayya mina alttawrati waliohilla lakum baada allathee hurrima aalaykum wajitukum biayatin min rabbikum aittaqoo Allaha waateeaooni
Inna Allaha rabbee warabbukum faoabudoohu hatha siratun mustaqeemun
Falamma ahassa aeesa minhumu alkufra qala man ansaree ila Allahi qala alhawariyyoona nahnu ansaru Allahi amanna biAllahi waishhad ianna muslimoona
Rabbana amanna bima anzalta waittabaana alrrasoola faoktubna maaa alshshahideena
Wamakaroo wamakara Allahu waAllahu khayru almakireena
Ith qala Allahu ya aeesa innee mutawaffeeka warafiauka ilayya wamutahhiruka mina allatheena kafaroo wajaailu allatheena ittabaaooka awqa allatheena kafaroo ila yawmi alqiyamati thumma ilayya marjiaukum faahkumu baynakum feema kuntum feehi takhtalifoona
Faamma allatheena kafaroo faoaaththibuhum aathaban shadeedan fee alddunya waalakhirati wama lahum min nasireena
Waamma allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati fayuwaffeehim ojoorahum waAllahu la yuhibbu alththalimeena
Thalika natloohu aalayka mina alayati waalththikri alhakeemi
Inna mathala aeesa ainda Allahi kamathali adama khalaqahu min turabin thumma qala lahu kun fayakoonu
Alhaqqu min rabbika fala takun mina almumtareena
Faman hajjaka feehi min baadi ma jaaka mina alailmi faqul taaalaw nadau abnaana waabnaakum wanisaana wanisaakum waanfusana waanfusakum humma nabtahil fanajaal laanata Allahi aala alkathibeena
Inna hatha lahuwa alqasasu alhaqqu wama min ilahin illa Allahu wainna Allaha lahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Fain tawallaw fainna Allaha aaleemun bialmufsideena
Qul ya ahla alkitabi taaalaw ila kalimatin sawain baynana wabaynakum alla naabuda illa Allaha wala nushrika bihi shayan wala attakhitha baaduna baadan arbaban min dooni Allahi fain tawallaw faqooloo ishhadoo bianna muslimoona
Ya ahla alkitabi lima tuhajjoona fee ibraheema wama onzilati alttawratu waalinjeelu illa min baadihi afala taaqiloona
Haantum haolai hajajtum feema lakum bihi ailmun falima tuhajjoona feema laysa lakum bihi ailmun waAllahu yaalamu waantum la taalamoona
Ma kana ibraheemu yahoodiyyan wala nasraniyyan walakin kana haneefan musliman wama kana mina almushrikeena
Inna awla alnnasi biibraheema lallatheena ittabaaoohu wahatha alnnabiyyu waallatheena amanoo waAllahu waliyyu almumineena
Waddat taifatun min ahli alkitabi law yudilloonakum wama yudilloona illa anfusahum wama yashauroona
Ya ahla alkitabi lima takfuroona biayati Allahi waantum tashhadoona
Ya ahla alkitabi lima talbisoona alhaqqa bialbatili wataktumoona alhaqqa waantum taalamoona
Waqalat taifatun min ahli alkitabi aminoo biallathee onzila aala allatheena amanoo wajha alnnahari waokfuroo akhirahu laaallahum arjiaoona
Wala tuminoo illa liman tabiaa deenakum qul inna alhuda huda Allahi an yuta ahadun mithla ma ooteetum aw yuhajjookum ainda rabbikum qul nna alfadla biyadi Allahi yuteehi man yashao waAllahu wasiaun aaleemun
Yakhtassu birahmatihi man yashao waAllahu thoo alfadli alaatheemi
Wamin ahli alkitabi man in tamanhu biqintarin yuaddihi ilayka waminhum man in tamanhu bideenarin la yuaddihi ilayka illa ma dumta alayhi qaiman thalika biannahum qaloo laysa aalayna fee alommiyyeena sabeelun wayaqooloona aala Allahi alkathiba wahum yaalamoona
Bala man awfa biaahdihi waittaqa fainna Allaha yuhibbu almuttaqeena
Inna allatheena yashtaroona biaahdi Allahi waaymanihim thamanan qaleelan olaika la khalaqa lahum fee alakhirati wala yukallimuhumu llahu wala yanthuru ilayhim yawma alqiyamati wala yuzakkeehim walahum aathabun aleemun
Wainna minhum lafareeqan yalwoona alsinatahum bialkitabi litahsaboohu mina alkitabi wama huwa mina alkitabi wayaqooloona huwa min aindi llahi wama huwa min aindi Allahi wayaqooloona aala Allahi alkathiba wahum yaalamoona
Ma kana libasharin an yutiyahu Allahu alkitaba waalhukma waalnnubuwwata thumma yaqoola lilnnasi koonoo aibadan lee min dooni Allahi alakin koonoo rabbaniyyeena bima kuntum tuaallimoona alkitaba wabima kuntum tadrusoona
Wala yamurakum an tattakhithoo almalaikata waalnnabiyyeena arbaban ayamurukum bialkufri baada ith antum muslimoona
Waith akhatha Allahu meethaqa alnnabiyyeena lama ataytukum min kitabin wahikmatin thumma jaakum rasoolun musaddiqun lima maaakum latuminunna bihi walatansurunnahu qala aaqrartum waakhathtum aala thalikum isree qaloo aqrarna qala faishhadoo waana maaakum mina lshshahideena
Faman tawalla baada thalika faolaika humu alfasiqoona
Afaghayra deeni Allahi yabghoona walahu aslama man fee alssamawati waalardi tawaan wakarhan wailayhi yurjaaoona
Qul amanna biAllahi wama onzila aalayna wama onzila aala ibraheema waismaaeela waishaqa wayaaqooba waalasbati wama ootiya moosa waaeesa aalnnabiyyoona min rabbihim la nufarriqu bayna ahadin minhum wanahnu lahu muslimoona
Waman yabtaghi ghayra alislami deenan falan yuqbala minhu wahuwa fee alakhirati mina alkhasireena
Kayfa yahdee Allahu qawman kafaroo baada eemanihim washahidoo anna alrrasoola haqqun wajaahumu albayyinatu waAllahu la yahdee alqawma lththalimeena
Olaika jazaohum anna aalayhim laanata Allahi waalmalaikati waalnnasi ajmaaeena
Khalideena feeha la yukhaffafu aanhumu alaathabu wala hum yuntharoona
Illa allatheena taboo min baadi thalika waaslahoo fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Inna allatheena kafaroo baada eemanihim thumma izdadoo kufran lan tuqbala tawbatuhum waolaika humu alddalloona
Inna allatheena kafaroo wamatoo wahum kuffarun falan yuqbala min ahadihim milo alardi thahaban walawi iftada bihi olaika lahum aathabun leemun wama lahum min nasireena
Lan tanaloo albirra hatta tunfiqoo mimma tuhibboona wama tunfiqoo min shayin fainna Allaha bihi aaleemun
Kullu alttaaami kana hillan libanee israeela illa ma harrama israeelu aala nafsihi min qabli an tunazzala alttawratu qul fatoo ialttawrati faotlooha in kuntum sadiqeena
Famani iftara aala Allahi alkathiba min baadi thalika faolaika humu althalimoona
Qul sadaqa Allahu faittabiaoo millata ibraheema haneefan wama kana mina almushrikeena
Inna awwala baytin wudiaa lilnnasi lallathee bibakkata mubarakan wahudan lilaalameena
Feehi ayatun bayyinatun maqamu ibraheema waman dakhalahu kana aminan walillahi aala alnnasi hijju albayti mani istataaa ilayhi sabeelan aman kafara fainna Allaha ghaniyyun aani alaalameena
Qul ya ahla alkitabi lima takfuroona biayati Allahi waAllahu shaheedun aala ma taamaloona
Qul ya ahla alkitabi lima tasuddoona aan sabeeli Allahi man amana tabghoonaha aiwajan waantum shuhadao wama Allahu bighafilin aamma aamaloona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in tuteeaoo fareeqan mina allatheena ootoo alkitaba yaruddookum baada eemanikum kafireena
Wakayfa takfuroona waantum tutla aalaykum ayatu Allahi wafeekum rasooluhu waman yaatasim biAllahi faqad hudiya ila siratin mustaqeemin
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha haqqa tuqatihi wala tamootunna illa waantum muslimoona
Waiatasimoo bihabli Allahi jameeaan wala tafarraqoo waothkuroo niamata Allahi aalaykum ith kuntum aadaan faallafa bayna quloobikum faasbahtum biniamatihi ikhwanan wakuntum aala shafa hufratin mina alnnari faanqathakum minha kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakum ayatihi aaallakum tahtadoona
Waltakun minkum ommatun yadaoona ila alkhayri wayamuroona bialmaaroofi wayanhawna aani almunkari waolaika humu almuflihoona
Wala takoonoo kaallatheena tafarraqoo waikhtalafoo min baadi ma jaahumu albayyinatu waolaika lahum aathabun aatheemun
Yawma tabyaddu wujoohun wataswaddu wujoohun faamma allatheena iswaddat wujoohuhum akafartum baada eemanikum fathooqoo alaathaba bima untum takfuroona
Waamma allatheena ibyaddat wujoohuhum fafee rahmati Allahi hum feeha khalidoona
Tilka ayatu Allahi natlooha aalayka bialhaqqi wama Allahu yureedu thulman lilaalameena
Walillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi waila Allahi turjaau alomooru
Kuntum khayra ommatin okhrijat lilnnasi tamuroona bialmaaroofi watanhawna aani almunkari watuminoona biAllahi walaw amana ahlu alkitabi akana khayran lahum minhumu almuminoona waaktharuhumu alfasiqoona
Lan yadurrookum illa athan wain yuqatilookum yuwallookumu aladbara thumma la yunsaroona
Duribat aalayhimu alththillatu ayna ma thuqifoo illa bihablin mina Allahi wahablin mina alnnasi wabaoo bighadabin mina Allahi waduribat aalayhimu almaskanatu thalika biannahum kanoo yakfuroona biayati Allahi wayaqtuloona alanbiyaa bighayri haqqin thalika bima aasaw akanoo yaatadoona
Laysoo sawaan min ahli alkitabi ommatun qaimatun yatloona ayati Allahi anaa allayli wahum yasjudoona
Yuminoona biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri wayamuroona bialmaaroofi wayanhawna aani almunkari wayusariaoona fee alkhayrati waolaika mina lssaliheena
Wama yafaaloo min khayrin falan yukfaroohu waAllahu aaleemun bialmuttaqeena
Inna allatheena kafaroo lan tughniya aanhum amwaluhum wala awladuhum mina Allahi shayan waolaika ashabu alnnari hum feeha khalidoona
Mathalu ma yunfiqoona fee hathihi alhayati alddunya kamathali reehin feeha sirrun asabat hartha qawmin thalamoo anfusahum faahlakathu ama thalamahumu Allahu walakin anfusahum yathlimoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo bitanatan min doonikum la yaloonakum khabalan waddoo ma aanittum qad badati albaghdao min fwahihim wama tukhfee sudooruhum akbaru qad bayyanna lakumu alayati in kuntum taaqiloona
Haantum olai tuhibboonahum wala yuhibboonakum watuminoona bialkitabi kullihi waitha laqookum qaloo amanna waitha khalaw aaddoo alaykumu alanamila mina alghaythi qul mootoo bighaythikum inna Allaha aaleemun bithati alssudoori
In tamsaskum hasanatun tasuhum wain tusibkum sayyiatun yafrahoo biha wain tasbiroo watattaqoo la yadurrukum kayduhum shayan inna Allaha ima yaamaloona muheetun
Waith ghadawta min ahlika tubawwio almumineena maqaaida lilqitali waAllahu sameeaun aaleemun
Ith hammat taifatani minkum an tafshala waAllahu waliyyuhuma waaala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoona
Walaqad nasarakumu Allahu bibadrin waantum athillatun faittaqoo Allaha laaallakum tashkuroona
Ith taqoolu lilmumineena alan yakfiyakum an yumiddakum rabbukum bithalathati alafin mina almalaikati munzaleena
Bala in tasbiroo watattaqoo wayatookum min fawrihim hatha yumdidkum rabbukum bikhamsati alafin mina almalaikati musawwimeena
Wama jaaalahu Allahu illa bushra lakum walitatmainna quloobukum bihi wama alnnasru illa min aindi Allahi alaazeezi alhakeemi
Liyaqtaaa tarafan mina allatheena kafaroo aw yakbitahum fayanqaliboo khaibeena
Laysa laka mina alamri shayon aw yatooba aalayhim aw yuaaththibahum fainnahum thalimoona
Walillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi yaghfiru liman yashao wayuaaththibu man yashao waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la takuloo alrriba adaafan mudaaafatan waittaqoo Allaha laaallakum tuflihoona
Waittaqoo alnnara allatee oaiddat lilkafireena
Waateeaoo Allaha waalrrasoola laaallakum turhamoona
Wasariaoo ila maghfiratin min rabbikum wajannatin aarduha alssamawatu waalardu oaiddat lilmuttaqeena
Allatheena yunfiqoona fee alssarrai waalddarrai waalkathimeena alghaytha waalaafeena aani alnnasi waAllahu yuhibbu almuhsineena
Waallatheena itha faaaloo fahishatan aw thalamoo anfusahum thakaroo Allaha faistaghfaroo lithunoobihim waman yaghfiru alththunooba illa llahu walam yusirroo aala ma faaaloo wahum yaalamoona
Olaika jazaohum maghfiratun min rabbihim wajannatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha waniama ajru alaamileena
Qad khalat min qablikum sunanun faseeroo fee alardi faonthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu almukaththibeena
Hatha bayanun lilnnasi wahudan wamawaithatun lilmuttaqeena
Wala tahinoo wala tahzanoo waantumu alaalawna in kuntum mumineena
In yamsaskum qarhun faqad massa alqawma qarhun mithluhu watilka alayyamu nudawiluha bayna alnnasi waliyaalama Allahu allatheena amanoo ayattakhitha minkum shuhadaa waAllahu la yuhibbu alththalimeena
Waliyumahhisa Allahu allatheena amanoo wayamhaqa alkafireena
Am hasibtum an tadkhuloo aljannata walamma yaalami Allahu allatheena jahadoo minkum wayaalama alssabireena
Walaqad kuntum tamannawna almawta min qabli an talqawhu faqad raaytumoohu waantum tanthuroona
Wama muhammadun illa rasoolun qad khalat min qablihi alrrusulu afain mata aw qutila inqalabtum aala aaqabikum waman yanqalib aala aqibayhi falan yadurra Allaha shayan wasayajzee Allahu alshshakireena
Wama kana linafsin an tamoota illa biithni Allahi kitaban muajjalan waman yurid thawaba alddunya nutihi minha waman yurid thawaba lakhirati nutihi minha wasanajzee alshshakireena
Wakaayyin min nabiyyin qatala maaahu ribbiyyoona katheerun fama wahanoo lima asabahum fee sabeeli Allahi wama daaufoo wama istakanoo aAllahu yuhibbu alssabireena
Wama kana qawlahum illa an qaloo rabbana ighfir lana thunoobana waisrafana fee amrina wathabbit aqdamana waonsurna aala alqawmi lkafireena
Faatahumu Allahu thawaba alddunya wahusna thawabi alakhirati waAllahu yuhibbu almuhsineena
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in tuteeaoo allatheena kafaroo yaruddookum aala aaqabikum fatanqaliboo khasireena
Bali Allahu mawlakum wahuwa khayru alnnasireena
Sanulqee fee quloobi allatheena kafaroo alrruaba bima ashrakoo biAllahi ma lam yunazzil bihi sultanan wamawahumu alnnaru wabisa mathwa lththalimeena
Walaqad sadaqakumu Allahu waadahu ith tahussoonahum biithnihi hatta itha fashiltum watanazaatum fee alamri waaasaytum min baadi ma arakum ma tuhibboona minkum man yureedu alddunya waminkum man yureedu alakhirata thumma sarafakum aanhum liyabtaliyakum walaqad aafa ankum waAllahu thoo fadlin aala almumineena
Ith tusaidoona wala talwoona aala ahadin waalrrasoolu yadaookum fee okhrakum faathabakum ghamman bighammin likayla tahzanoo aala ma atakum wala ma asabakum waAllahu khabeerun bima taamaloona
Thumma anzala aalaykum min baadi alghammi amanatan nuaasan yaghsha taifatan minkum wataifatun qad ahammathum anfusuhum yathunnoona biAllahi ghayra alhaqqi thanna aljahiliyyati yaqooloona hal lana mina alamri min shayin qul inna alamra kullahu lillahi yukhfoona fee anfusihim ma la yubdoona laka yaqooloona law kana lana mina alamri shayon ma qutilna hahuna qul law kuntum fee buyootikum labaraza allatheena kutiba aalayhimu alqatlu ila madajiaihim waliyabtaliya Allahu ma fee sudoorikum waliyumahhisa ma fee quloobikum waAllahu aleemun bithati alssudoori
Inna allatheena tawallaw minkum yawma iltaqa aljamaani innama istazallahumu alshshaytanu bibaadi ma kasaboo walaqad aafa Allahu aanhum nna Allaha ghafoorun haleemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la takoonoo kaallatheena kafaroo waqaloo liikhwanihim itha daraboo fee alardi aw kanoo ghuzzan law kanoo aindana ma matoo wama qutiloo liyajaala Allahu thalika hasratan fee quloobihim waAllahu yuhyee wayumeetu waAllahu bima taamaloona aseerun
Walain qutiltum fee sabeeli Allahi aw muttum lamaghfiratun mina Allahi warahmatun khayrun mimma yajmaaoona
Walain muttum aw qutiltum laila Allahi tuhsharoona
Fabima rahmatin mina Allahi linta lahum walaw kunta faththan ghaleetha alqalbi lainfaddoo min hawlika faoafu aanhum waistaghfir lahum ashawirhum fee alamri faitha aazamta fatawakkal aala Allahi inna Allaha yuhibbu almutawakkileena
In yansurkumu Allahu fala ghaliba lakum wain yakhthulkum faman tha allathee yansurukum min baadihi waaala Allahi falyatawakkali lmuminoona
Wama kana linabiyyin an yaghulla waman yaghlul yati bima ghalla yawma alqiyamati thumma tuwaffa kullu nafsin ma kasabat wahum la uthlamoona
Afamani ittabaaa ridwana Allahi kaman baa bisakhatin mina Allahi wamawahu jahannamu wabisa almaseeru
Hum darajatun ainda Allahi waAllahu baseerun bima yaamaloona
Laqad manna Allahu aala almumineena ith baaatha feehim rasoolan min anfusihim yatloo aalayhim ayatihi wayuzakkeehim wayuaallimuhumu lkitaba waalhikmata wain kanoo min qablu lafee dalalin mubeenin
Awalamma asabatkum museebatun qad asabtum mithlayha qultum anna hatha qul huwa min aindi anfusikum inna Allaha aala kulli shayin adeerun
Wama asabakum yawma iltaqa aljamaani fabiithni Allahi waliyaalama almumineena
Waliyaalama allatheena nafaqoo waqeela lahum taaalaw qatiloo fee sabeeli Allahi awi idfaaoo qaloo law naalamu qitalan laittabaanakum um lilkufri yawmaithin aqrabu minhum lileemani yaqooloona biafwahihim ma laysa fee quloobihim waAllahu aalamu bima yaktumoona
Allatheena qaloo liikhwanihim waqaaadoo law ataaoona ma qutiloo qul faidraoo aan anfusikumu almawta in kuntum sadiqeena
Wala tahsabanna allatheena qutiloo fee sabeeli Allahi amwatan bal ahyaon ainda rabbihim yurzaqoona
Fariheena bima atahumu Allahu min fadlihi wayastabshiroona biallatheena lam yalhaqoo bihim min khalfihim alla khawfun aalayhim wala hum ahzanoona
Yastabshiroona biniamatin mina Allahi wafadlin waanna Allaha la yudeeau ajra almumineena
Allatheena istajaboo lillahi waalrrasooli min baadi ma asabahumu alqarhu lillatheena ahsanoo minhum waittaqaw ajrun aatheemun
Allatheena qala lahumu alnnasu inna alnnasa qad jamaaoo lakum faikhshawhum fazadahum eemanan waqaloo hasbuna Allahu waniama alwakeelu
Fainqalaboo biniamatin mina Allahi wafadlin lam yamsashum sooon waittabaaoo ridwana Allahi waAllahu thoo fadlin aatheemin
Innama thalikumu alshshaytanu yukhawwifu awliyaahu fala takhafoohum wakhafooni in kuntum mumineena
Wala yahzunka allatheena yusariaoona fee alkufri innahum lan yadurroo Allaha shayan yureedu Allahu alla yajaala lahum haththan fee lakhirati walahum aathabun aatheemun
Inna allatheena ishtarawoo alkufra bialeemani lan yadurroo Allaha shayan walahum aathabun aleemun
Wala yahsabanna allatheena kafaroo annama numlee lahum khayrun lianfusihim innama numlee lahum liyazdadoo ithman walahum aathabun uheenun
Ma kana Allahu liyathara almumineena aala ma antum aalayhi hatta yameeza alkhabeetha mina alttayyibi wama kana Allahu liyutliaakum aala lghaybi walakinna Allaha yajtabee min rusulihi man yashao faaminoo biAllahi warusulihi wain tuminoo watattaqoo falakum ajrun aatheemun
Wala yahsabanna allatheena yabkhaloona bima atahummu Allahu min fadlihi huwa khayran lahum bal huwa sharrun lahum sayutawwaqoona ma akhiloo bihi yawma alqiyamati walillahi meerathu alssamawati waalardi waAllahu bima taamaloona khabeerun
Laqad samiaa Allahu qawla allatheena qaloo inna Allaha faqeerun wanahnu aghniyaon sanaktubu ma qaloo waqatlahumu alanbiyaa bighayri aqqin wanaqoolu thooqoo aathaba alhareeqi
Thalika bima qaddamat aydeekum waanna Allaha laysa bithallamin lilaabeedi
Allatheena qaloo inna Allaha aahida ilayna alla numina lirasoolin hatta yatiyana biqurbanin takuluhu alnnaru qul qad jaakum rusulun min ablee bialbayyinati wabiallathee qultum falima qataltumoohum in kutum sadiqeena
Fain kaththabooka faqad kuththiba rusulun min qablika jaoo bialbayyinati waalzzuburi waalkitabi almuneeri
Kullu nafsin thaiqatu almawti wainnama tuwaffawna ojoorakum yawma alqiyamati faman zuhziha aani alnnari waodkhila aljannata faqad faza ama alhayatu alddunya illa mataau alghuroori
Latublawunna fee amwalikum waanfusikum walatasmaaunna mina allatheena ootoo alkitaba min qablikum wamina allatheena ashrakoo athan atheeran wain tasbiroo watattaqoo fainna thalika min aazmi alomoori
Waith akhatha Allahu meethaqa allatheena ootoo alkitaba latubayyinunnahu lilnnasi wala taktumoonahu fanabathoohu waraa thuhoorihim aishtaraw bihi thamanan qaleelan fabisa ma yashtaroona
La tahsabanna allatheena yafrahoona bima ataw wayuhibboona an yuhmadoo bima lam yafaaloo fala tahsabannahum bimafazatin mina alaathabi alahum aathabun aleemun
Walillahi mulku alssamawati waalardi waAllahu aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Inna fee khalqi alssamawati waalardi waikhtilafi allayli waalnnahari laayatin liolee alalbabi
Allatheena yathkuroona Allaha qiyaman waquaoodan waaala junoobihim wayatafakkaroona fee khalqi alssamawati waalardi rabbana ma khalaqta atha batilan subhanaka faqina aathaba alnnari
Rabbana innaka man tudkhili alnnara faqad akhzaytahu wama lilththalimeena min ansarin
Rabbana innana samiana munadiyan yunadee lileemani an aminoo birabbikum faamanna rabbana faighfir lana thunoobana wakaffir aanna ayyiatina watawaffana maaa alabrari
Rabbana waatina ma waaadtana aala rusulika wala tukhzina yawma alqiyamati innaka la tukhlifu almeeaada
Faistajaba lahum rabbuhum annee la odeeau aamala aamilin minkum min thakarin aw ontha baadukum min baadin faallatheena hajaroo waokhrijoo min diyarihim waoothoo fee sabeelee waqataloo waqutiloo laokaffiranna aanhum sayyiatihim walaodkhilannahum jannatin tajree in tahtiha alanharu thawaban min aindi Allahi waAllahu aindahu husnu alththawabi
La yaghurrannaka taqallubu allatheena kafaroo fee albiladi
Mataaun qaleelun thumma mawahum jahannamu wabisa almihadu
Lakini allatheena ittaqaw rabbahum lahum jannatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha nuzulan min aindi Allahi wama ainda llahi khayrun lilabrari
Wainna min ahli alkitabi laman yuminu biAllahi wama onzila ilaykum wama onzila ilayhim khashiaeena lillahi la yashtaroona biayati llahi thamanan qaleelan olaika lahum ajruhum ainda rabbihim inna Allaha sareeau alhisabi
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo isbiroo wasabiroo warabitoo waittaqoo Allaha laaallakum tuflihoona
Ya ayyuha alnnasu ittaqoo rabbakumu allathee khalaqakum min nafsin wahidatin wakhalaqa minha zawjaha wabaththa minhuma rijalan atheeran wanisaan waittaqoo Allaha allathee tasaaloona bihi waalarhama inna Allaha kana aalaykum raqeeban
Waatoo alyatama amwalahum wala tatabaddaloo alkhabeetha bialttayyibi wala takuloo amwalahum ila amwalikum innahu kana hooban kabeeran
Wain khiftum alla tuqsitoo fee alyatama fainkihoo ma taba lakum mina alnnisai mathna wathulatha warubaaa fain khiftum alla taadiloo awahidatan aw ma malakat aymanukum thalika adna alla taaooloo
Waatoo alnnisaa saduqatihinna nihlatan fain tibna lakum aan shayin minhu nafsan fakuloohu haneean mareean
Wala tutoo alssufahaa amwalakumu allatee jaaala Allahu lakum qiyaman waorzuqoohum feeha waoksoohum waqooloo lahum qawlan maaroofan
Waibtaloo alyatama hatta itha balaghoo alnnikaha fain anastum minhum rushdan faidfaaoo ilayhim amwalahum wala takulooha israfan wabidaran an yakbaroo waman kana ghaniyyan falyastaafif waman kana faqeeran falyakul bialmaaroofi faitha dafaatum ilayhim amwalahum aashhidoo aalayhim wakafa biAllahi haseeban
Lilrrijali naseebun mimma taraka alwalidani waalaqraboona walilnnisai naseebun mimma taraka alwalidani waalaqraboona mimma qalla minhu w kathura naseeban mafroodan
Waitha hadara alqismata oloo alqurba waalyatama waalmasakeenu faorzuqoohum minhu waqooloo lahum qawlan maaroofan
Walyakhsha allatheena law tarakoo min khalfihim thurriyyatan diaafan khafoo aalayhim falyattaqoo Allaha walyaqooloo qawlan sadeedan
Inna allatheena yakuloona amwala alyatama thulman innama yakuloona fee butoonihim naran wasayaslawna saaeeran
Yooseekumu Allahu fee awladikum lilththakari mithlu haththi alonthayayni fain kunna nisaan fawqa ithnatayni falahunna thulutha ma taraka wain kanat wahidatan falaha alnnisfu waliabawayhi likulli wahidin minhuma alssudusu mimma taraka in kana lahu waladun fain lam yakun lahu waladun wawarithahu abawahu faliommihi alththuluthu fain kana lahu ikhwatun faliommihi alssudusu min baadi wasiyyatin yoosee iha aw daynin abaokum waabnaokum la tadroona ayyuhum aqrabu lakum nafaan fareedatan mina Allahi inna Allaha kana aaleeman hakeeman
Walakum nisfu ma taraka azwajukum in lam yakun lahunna waladun fain kana lahunna waladun falakumu alrrubuau mimma tarakna min baadi wasiyyatin yooseena biha aw daynin walahunna alrrubuau mimma taraktum in lam yakun lakum waladun fain kana lakum waladun falahunna alththumunu mimma taraktum min baadi wasiyyatin toosoona biha aw daynin wain kana rajulun yoorathu kalalatan awi imraatun walahu akhun aw okhtun falikulli wahidin minhuma alssudusu fain kanoo akthara min thalika fahum shurakao fee alththuluthi min baadi wasiyyatin yoosa iha aw daynin ghayra mudarrin wasiyyatan mina Allahi waAllahu aaleemun haleemun
Tilka hudoodu Allahi waman yutiai Allaha warasoolahu yudkhilhu jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wathalika alfawzu laatheemu
Waman yaasi Allaha warasoolahu wayataaadda hudoodahu yudkhilhu naran khalidan feeha walahu aathabun muheenun

Waallathani yatiyaniha minkum faathoohuma fain taba waaslaha faaaridoo aanhuma inna Allaha kana tawwaban raheeman
Innama alttawbatu aala Allahi lillatheena yaamaloona alssooa bijahalatin thumma yatooboona min qareebin faolaika yatoobu Allahu alayhim wakana Allahu aaleeman hakeeman
Walaysati alttawbatu lillatheena yaamaloona alssayyiati hatta itha hadara ahadahumu almawtu qala innee tubtu alana wala allatheena amootoona wahum kuffarun olaika aatadna lahum aathaban aleeman
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la yahillu lakum an tarithoo alnnisaa karhan wala taaduloohunna litathhaboo bibaadi ma ataytumoohunna illa an yateena bifahishatin mubayyinatin waaashiroohunna bialmaaroofi fain karihtumoohunna faaasa an takrahoo shayan wayajaala Allahu feehi hayran katheeran

Wala tankihoo ma nakaha abaokum mina alnnisai illa ma qad salafa innahu kana fahishatan wamaqtan wasaa sabeelan
