Waalmuhsanatu mina alnnisai illa ma malakat aymanukum kitaba Allahi aalaykum waohilla lakum ma waraa thalikum an tabtaghoo biamwalikum muhsineena ghayra musafiheena fama istamtaatum bihi minhunna faatoohunna ojoorahunna fareedatan wala junaha aalaykum feema taradaytum ihi min baadi alfareedati inna Allaha kana aaleeman hakeeman
Waman lam yastatia minkum tawlan an yankiha almuhsanati almuminati famin ma malakat aymanukum min fatayatikumu almuminati waAllahu aalamu bieemanikum baadukum min baadin fainkihoohunna biithni ahlihinna waatoohunna ojoorahunna bialmaaroofi muhsanatin ghayra masafihatin wala muttakhithati akhdanin faitha ohsinna fain atayna bifahishatin faaalayhinna nisfu ma aala almuhsanati mina alaathabi halika liman khashiya alaanata minkum waan tasbiroo khayrun lakum waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun

Fakayfa itha jina min kulli ommatin bishaheedin wajina bika aala haolai shaheedan
Yawmaithin yawaddu allatheena kafaroo waaasawoo alrrasoola law tusawwa bihimu alardu wala yaktumoona Allaha hadeethan

Alam tara ila allatheena ootoo naseeban mina alkitabi yashtaroona alddalalata wayureedoona an tadilloo alssabeela

Mina allatheena hadoo yuharrifoona alkalima aan mawadiaihi wayaqooloona samiana waaasayna waismaa ghayra musmaain waraaina layyan bialsinatihim wataanan fee alddeeni walaw annahum qaloo samiana waataana waismaa waonthurna lakana khayran lahum waaqwama walakin aaanahumu Allahu bikufrihim fala yuminoona illa qaleelan
Ya ayyuha allatheena ootoo alkitaba aminoo bima nazzalna musaddiqan lima maaakum min qabli an natmisa wujoohan fanaruddaha aala dbariha aw nalaanahum kama laaanna ashaba alssabti wakana amru Allahi mafaoolan

Wama lakum la tuqatiloona fee sabeeli Allahi waalmustadaafeena mina alrrijali waalnnisai waalwildani allatheena yaqooloona rabbana khrijna min hathihi alqaryati alththalimi ahluha waijaal lana min ladunka waliyyan waijaal lana min ladunka naseeran

Alam tara ila allatheena qeela lahum kuffoo aydiyakum waaqeemoo alssalata waatoo alzzakata falamma kutiba aalayhimu alqitalu itha fareequn minhum yakhshawna alnnasa kakhashyati Allahi aw ashadda khashyatan waqaloo rabbana lima katabta aalayna alqitala lawla khkhartana ila ajalin qareebin qul mataau alddunya qaleelun waalakhiratu khayrun limani ittaqa wala tuthlamoona fateelan

Waman ahsanu deenan mimman aslama wajhahu lillahi wahuwa muhsinun waittabaaa millata ibraheema haneefan waittakhatha Allahu ibraheema haleelan
Walillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wakana Allahu bikulli shayin muheetan
Wayastaftoonaka fee alnnisai quli Allahu yufteekum feehinna wama yutla aalaykum fee alkitabi fee yatama alnnisai allatee la tutoonahunna ma kutiba lahunna watarghaboona an tankihoohunna waalmustadaafeena mina alwildani waan taqoomoo lilyatama bialqisti wama afaaloo min khayrin fainna Allaha kana bihi aaleeman
Waini imraatun khafat min baaliha nushoozan aw iaradan fala junaha aalayhima an yusliha baynahuma sulhan waalssulhu khayrun waohdirati lanfusu alshshuhha wain tuhsinoo watattaqoo fainna Allaha kana bima taamaloona khabeeran
Walan tastateeaoo an taadiloo bayna alnnisai walaw harastum fala tameeloo kulla almayli fatatharooha kaalmuaallaqati wain tuslihoo atattaqoo fainna Allaha kana ghafooran raheeman
Wain yatafarraqa yughni Allahu kullan min saaatihi wakana Allahu wasiaan hakeeman
Walillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi walaqad wassayna allatheena ootoo alkitaba min qablikum waiyyakum ani ittaqoo Allaha wain akfuroo fainna lillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wakana Allahu ghaniyyan hameedan
Walillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wakafa biAllahi wakeelan
In yasha yuthhibkum ayyuha alnnasu wayati biakhareena wakana Allahu aala thalika qadeeran
Man kana yureedu thawaba alddunya faainda Allahi thawabu alddunya waalakhirati wakana Allahu sameeaan baseeran
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo koonoo qawwameena bialqisti shuhadaa lillahi walaw aala anfusikum awi alwalidayni waalaqrabeena in yakun ghaniyyan aw faqeeran faAllahu awla bihima fala tattabiaoo alhawa an taadiloo wain talwoo aw tuaridoo fainna Allaha kana bima taamaloona habeeran
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo aminoo biAllahi warasoolihi waalkitabi allathee nazzala aala rasoolihi waalkitabi allathee anzala min qablu aman yakfur biAllahi wamalaikatihi wakutubihi warusulihi waalyawmi alakhiri faqad dalla dalalan baaeedan
Inna allatheena amanoo thumma kafaroo thumma amanoo thumma kafaroo thumma izdadoo kufran lam yakuni Allahu liyaghfira lahum wala iyahdiyahum sabeelan
Bashshiri almunafiqeena bianna lahum aathaban aleeman
Allatheena yattakhithoona alkafireena awliyaa min dooni almumineena ayabtaghoona aindahumu alaizzata fainna alaizzata lillahi jameeaan
Waqad nazzala aalaykum fee alkitabi an itha samiatum ayati Allahi yukfaru biha wayustahzao biha fala taqaudoo maaahum hatta yakhoodoo ee hadeethin ghayrihi innakum ithan mithluhum inna Allaha jamiau almunafiqeena waalkafireena fee jahannama jameeaan
Allatheena yatarabbasoona bikum fain kana lakum fathun mina Allahi qaloo alam nakun maaakum wain kana lilkafireena naseebun qaloo alam nastahwith aalaykum wanamnaakum mina almumineena faAllahu yahkumu baynakum yawma alqiyamati walan yajaala Allahu lilkafireena aala lmumineena sabeelan
Inna almunafiqeena yukhadiaoona Allaha wahuwa khadiauhum waitha qamoo ila alssalati qamoo kusala yuraoona alnnasa wala yathkuroona llaha illa qaleelan
Muthabthabeena bayna thalika la ila haolai wala ila haolai waman yudlili Allahu falan tajida lahu sabeelan
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo alkafireena awliyaa min dooni almumineena atureedoona an tajaaloo lillahi aalaykum sultanan ubeenan
Inna almunafiqeena fee alddarki alasfali mina alnnari walan tajida lahum naseeran
Illa allatheena taboo waaslahoo waiatasamoo biAllahi waakhlasoo deenahum lillahi faolaika maaa almumineena wasawfa yuti Allahu lmumineena ajran aatheeman
Ma yafaalu Allahu biaathabikum in shakartum waamantum wakana Allahu shakiran aaleeman
La yuhibbu Allahu aljahra bialssooi mina alqawli illa man thulima wakana Allahu sameeaan aaleeman
In tubdoo khayran aw tukhfoohu aw taafoo aan sooin fainna Allaha kana aafuwwan qadeeran
Inna allatheena yakfuroona biAllahi warusulihi wayureedoona an yufarriqoo bayna Allahi warusulihi wayaqooloona numinu bibaadin anakfuru bibaadin wayureedoona an yattakhithoo bayna thalika sabeelan
Olaika humu alkafiroona haqqan waaatadna lilkafireena aathaban muheenan
Waallatheena amanoo biAllahi warusulihi walam yufarriqoo bayna ahadin minhum olaika sawfa yuteehim ojoorahum wakana Allahu ghafooran aheeman
Yasaluka ahlu alkitabi an tunazzila aalayhim kitaban mina alssamai faqad saaloo moosa akbara min thalika faqaloo arina Allaha jahratan faakhathathumu alssaaiqatu bithulmihim thumma ittakhathoo alaijla min baadi ma jaathumu albayyinatu faaafawna aan thalika waatayna moosa ultanan mubeenan
Warafaana fawqahumu alttoora bimeethaqihim waqulna lahumu odkhuloo albaba sujjadan waqulna lahum la taadoo fee alssabti waakhathna inhum meethaqan ghaleethan
Fabima naqdihim meethaqahum wakufrihim biayati Allahi waqatlihimu alanbiyaa bighayri haqqin waqawlihim quloobuna ghulfun bal tabaaa llahu aalayha bikufrihim fala yuminoona illa qaleelan
Wabikufrihim waqawlihim aala maryama buhtanan aatheeman
Waqawlihim inna qatalna almaseeha aeesa ibna maryama rasoola Allahi wama qataloohu wama salaboohu walakin shubbiha lahum wainna llatheena ikhtalafoo feehi lafee shakkin minhu ma lahum bihi min ailmin illa ittibaaa alththanni wama qataloohu yaqeenan
Bal rafaaahu Allahu ilayhi wakana Allahu aazeezan hakeeman
Wain min ahli alkitabi illa layuminanna bihi qabla mawtihi wayawma alqiyamati yakoonu aalayhim shaheedan
Fabithulmin mina allatheena hadoo harramna aalayhim tayyibatin ohillat lahum wabisaddihim aan sabeeli Allahi katheeran
Waakhthihimu alrriba waqad nuhoo aanhu waaklihim amwala alnnasi bialbatili waaatadna lilkafireena minhum aathaban aleeman
Lakini alrrasikhoona fee alailmi minhum waalmuminoona yuminoona bima onzila ilayka wama onzila min qablika waalmuqeemeena alssalata aalmutoona alzzakata waalmuminoona biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri olaika sanuteehim ajran aatheeman
Inna awhayna ilayka kama awhayna ila noohin waalnnabiyyeena min baadihi waawhayna ila ibraheema waismaaeela waishaqa wayaaqooba aalasbati waaeesa waayyooba wayoonusa waharoona wasulaymana waatayna dawooda zabooran
Warusulan qad qasasnahum aalayka min qablu warusulan lam naqsushum aalayka wakallama Allahu moosa takleeman
Rusulan mubashshireena wamunthireena lialla yakoona lilnnasi aala Allahi hujjatun baada alrrusuli wakana Allahu aazeezan hakeeman
Lakini Allahu yashhadu bima anzala ilayka anzalahu biailmihi waalmalaikatu yashhadoona wakafa biAllahi shaheedan
Inna allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo aan sabeeli Allahi qad dalloo dalalan baaeedan
Inna allatheena kafaroo wathalamoo lam yakuni Allahu liyaghfira lahum wala liyahdiyahum tareeqan
Illa tareeqa jahannama khalideena feeha abadan wakana thalika aala Allahi yaseeran
Ya ayyuha alnnasu qad jaakumu alrrasoolu bialhaqqi min rabbikum faaminoo khayran lakum wain takfuroo fainna lillahi ma fee alssamawati aalardi wakana Allahu aaleeman hakeeman
Ya ahla alkitabi la taghloo fee deenikum wala taqooloo aala Allahi illa alhaqqa innama almaseehu aeesa ibnu maryama rasoolu Allahi wakalimatuhu alqaha ila maryama waroohun minhu faaminoo biAllahi warusulihi wala taqooloo thalathatun intahoo khayran lakum innama llahu ilahun wahidun subhanahu an yakoona lahu waladun lahu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wakafa biAllahi wakeelan
Lan yastankifa almaseehu an yakoona aabdan lillahi wala almalaikatu almuqarraboona waman yastankif aan aibadatihi wayastakbir asayahshuruhum ilayhi jameeaan
Faamma allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati fayuwaffeehim ojoorahum wayazeeduhum min fadlihi waamma allatheena istankafoo aistakbaroo fayuaaththibuhum aathaban aleeman wala yajidoona lahum min dooni Allahi waliyyan wala naseeran
Ya ayyuha alnnasu qad jaakum burhanun min rabbikum waanzalna ilaykum nooran mubeenan
Faamma allatheena amanoo biAllahi waiatasamoo bihi fasayudkhiluhum fee rahmatin minhu wafadlin wayahdeehim ilayhi siratan mustaqeeman
Yastaftoonaka quli Allahu yufteekum fee alkalalati ini imruon halaka laysa lahu waladun walahu okhtun falaha nisfu ma taraka wahuwa yarithuha in lam yakun laha waladun fain kanata ithnatayni falahuma alththuluthani mimma taraka wain kanoo ikhwatan rijalan wanisaan alilththakari mithlu haththi alonthayayni yubayyinu Allahu lakum an tadilloo waAllahu bikulli shayin aaleemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo awfoo bialauqoodi ohillat lakum baheematu alanaami illa ma yutla aalaykum ghayra muhillee alssaydi waantum urumun inna Allaha yahkumu ma yureedu
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tuhilloo shaaaira Allahi wala alshshahra alharama wala alhadya wala alqalaida wala ammeena albayta alharama yabtaghoona fadlan min rabbihim waridwanan waitha halaltum faistadoo wala yajrimannakum shanaanu qawmin an saddookum aani almasjidi alharami an taatadoo wataaawanoo aala albirri waalttaqwa wala taaawanoo aala alithmi waalaudwani waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha hadeedu alaiqabi
Hurrimat aalaykumu almaytatu waalddamu walahmu alkhinzeeri wama ohilla lighayri Allahi bihi waalmunkhaniqatu waalmawqoothatu waalmutaraddiyatu waalnnateehatu wama akala alssabuau illa ma thakkaytum wama thubiha aala alnnusubi waan tastaqsimoo bialazlami thalikum fisqun alyawma yaisa allatheena kafaroo min deenikum fala takhshawhum waikhshawni alyawma akmaltu lakum deenakum waatmamtu aalaykum niamatee waradeetu lakumu alislama deenan famani idturra fee makhmasatin ghayra mutajanifin liithmin fainna Allaha ghafoorun aheemun
Yasaloonaka matha ohilla lahum qul ohilla lakumu alttayyibatu wama aallamtum mina aljawarihi mukallibeena tuaallimoonahunna mimma allamakumu Allahu fakuloo mimma amsakna aalaykum waothkuroo isma Allahi aalayhi waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha sareeau alhisabi
Alyawma ohilla lakumu alttayyibatu wataaamu allatheena ootoo alkitaba hillun lakum wataaamukum hillun lahum waalmuhsanatu mina almuminati waalmuhsanatu mina allatheena ootoo alkitaba min qablikum itha ataytumoohunna ojoorahunna muhsineena ghayra musafiheena wala uttakhithee akhdanin waman yakfur bialeemani faqad habita aamaluhu wahuwa fee alakhirati mina alkhasireena
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha qumtum ila alssalati faighsiloo wujoohakum waaydiyakum ila almarafiqi waimsahoo biruoosikum waarjulakum ila alkaabayni wain kuntum junuban faittahharoo wain kuntum marda aw aala safarin aw jaa ahadun minkum mina alghaiti aw lamastumu alnnisaa falam tajidoo maan fatayammamoo saaeedan tayyiban faimsahoo biwujoohikum waaydeekum minhu ma yureedu Allahu liyajaala alaykum min harajin walakin yureedu liyutahhirakum waliyutimma niamatahu aalaykum laaallakum tashkuroona
Waothkuroo niamata Allahi aalaykum wameethaqahu allathee wathaqakum bihi ith qultum samiana waataana waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha aleemun bithati alssudoori
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo koonoo qawwameena lillahi shuhadaa bialqisti wala yajrimannakum shanaanu qawmin aala alla taadiloo iadiloo uwa aqrabu lilttaqwa waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha khabeerun bima taamaloona
Waaada Allahu allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati lahum maghfiratun waajrun aatheemun
Waallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu aljaheemi
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo othkuroo niamata Allahi aalaykum ith hamma qawmun an yabsutoo ilaykum aydiyahum fakaffa aydiyahum aankum aittaqoo Allaha waaala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoona
Walaqad akhatha Allahu meethaqa banee israeela wabaaathna minhumu ithnay aashara naqeeban waqala Allahu innee maaakum lain aqamtumu alssalata waataytumu alzzakata waamantum birusulee waaazzartumoohum waaqradtumu Allaha qardan hasanan laokaffiranna aankum sayyiatikum alaodkhilannakum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu faman kafara baada thalika minkum faqad dalla sawaa alssabeeli
Fabima naqdihim meethaqahum laaannahum wajaaalna quloobahum qasiyatan yuharrifoona alkalima aan mawadiaihi wanasoo haththan mimma hukkiroo bihi wala tazalu tattaliau aala khainatin minhum illa qaleelan minhum faoafu aanhum waisfah inna Allaha yuhibbu almuhsineena
Wamina allatheena qaloo inna nasara akhathna meethaqahum fanasoo haththan mimma thukkiroo bihi faaghrayna baynahumu alaadawata aalbaghdaa ila yawmi alqiyamati wasawfa yunabbiohumu Allahu bima kanoo yasnaaoona
Ya ahla alkitabi qad jaakum rasooluna yubayyinu lakum katheeran mimma kuntum tukhfoona mina alkitabi wayaafoo aan katheerin qad jaakum ina Allahi noorun wakitabun mubeenun
Yahdee bihi Allahu mani ittabaaa ridwanahu subula alssalami wayukhrijuhum mina alththulumati ila alnnoori biithnihi wayahdeehim ila iratin mustaqeemin
Laqad kafara allatheena qaloo inna Allaha huwa almaseehu ibnu maryama qul faman yamliku mina Allahi shayan in arada an yuhlika almaseeha ibna maryama waommahu waman fee alardi jameeaan walillahi mulku alssamawati waalardi wama baynahuma yakhluqu ma yashao aAllahu aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Waqalati alyahoodu waalnnasara nahnu abnao Allahi waahibbaohu qul falima yuaaththibukum bithunoobikum bal antum basharun mimman khalaqa aghfiru liman yashao wayuaaththibu man yashao walillahi mulku alssamawati waalardi wama baynahuma wailayhi almaseeru
Ya ahla alkitabi qad jaakum rasooluna yubayyinu lakum aala fatratin mina alrrusuli an taqooloo ma jaana min basheerin wala natheerin aqad jaakum basheerun wanatheerun waAllahu aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Waith qala moosa liqawmihi ya qawmi othkuroo niamata Allahi aalaykum ith jaaala feekum anbiyaa wajaaalakum mulookan waatakum ma lam uti ahadan mina alaalameena
Ya qawmi odkhuloo alarda almuqaddasata allatee kataba Allahu lakum wala tartaddoo aala adbarikum fatanqaliboo khasireena
Qaloo ya moosa inna feeha qawman jabbareena wainna lan nadkhulaha hatta yakhrujoo minha fain yakhrujoo minha fainna dakhiloona
Qala rajulani mina allatheena yakhafoona anaama Allahu aalayhima odkhuloo aalayhimu albaba faitha dakhaltumoohu fainnakum ghaliboona aaala Allahi fatawakkaloo in kuntum mumineena
Qaloo ya moosa inna lan nadkhulaha abadan ma damoo feeha faithhab anta warabbuka faqatila inna hahuna qaaidoona
Qala rabbi innee la amliku illa nafsee waakhee faofruq baynana wabayna alqawmi alfasiqeena
Qala fainnaha muharramatun aalayhim arbaaeena sanatan yateehoona fee alardi fala tasa aala alqawmi alfasiqeena
Waotlu aalayhim nabaa ibnay adama bialhaqqi ith qarraba qurbanan fatuqubbila min ahadihima walam yutaqabbal mina alakhari qala aaqtulannaka qala innama yataqabbalu Allahu mina almuttaqeena
Lain basatta ilayya yadaka litaqtulanee ma ana bibasitin yadiya ilayka liaqtulaka innee akhafu Allaha rabba alaalameena
Innee oreedu an tabooa biithmee waithmika fatakoona min ashabi alnnari wathalika jazao alththalimeena
Fatawwaaat lahu nafsuhu qatla akheehi faqatalahu faasbaha mina alkhasireena
Fabaaatha Allahu ghuraban yabhathu fee alardi liyuriyahu kayfa yuwaree sawata akheehi qala ya waylata aaajaztu an akoona mithla hatha lghurabi faowariya sawata akhee faasbaha mina alnnadimeena
Min ajli thalika katabna aala banee israeela annahu man qatala nafsan bighayri nafsin aw fasadin fee alardi fakaannama qatala alnnasa jameeaan waman ahyaha fakaannama ahya alnnasa jameeaan walaqad jaa thum rusuluna bialbayyinati thumma inna katheeran minhum baada halika fee alardi lamusrifoona
Innama jazao allatheena yuhariboona Allaha warasoolahu wayasaawna fee alardi fasadan an yuqattaloo aw yusallaboo aw tuqattaaa aydeehim aarjuluhum min khilafin aw yunfaw mina alardi thalika lahum khizyun fee alddunya walahum fee alakhirati aathabun aatheemun
Illa allatheena taboo min qabli an taqdiroo aalayhim faialamoo anna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha waibtaghoo ilayhi alwaseelata wajahidoo fee sabeelihi laaallakum tuflihoona
Inna allatheena kafaroo law anna lahum ma fee alardi jameeaan wamithlahu maaahu liyaftadoo bihi min aathabi yawmi alqiyamati ma uqubbila minhum walahum aathabun aleemun
Yureedoona an yakhrujoo mina alnnari wama hum bikharijeena minha walahum aathabun muqeemun
Waalssariqu waalssariqatu faiqtaaoo aydiyahuma jazaan bima kasaba nakalan mina Allahi waAllahu aazeezun hakeemun
Faman taba min baadi thulmihi waaslaha fainna Allaha yatoobu aalayhi inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Alam taalam anna Allaha lahu mulku alssamawati waalardi yuaaththibu man yashao wayaghfiru liman yashao waAllahu aala kulli shayin adeerun
Ya ayyuha alrrasoolu la yahzunka allatheena yusariaoona fee alkufri mina allatheena qaloo amanna biafwahihim walam tumin quloobuhum wamina allatheena hadoo sammaaoona lilkathibi sammaaoona liqawmin akhareena lam yatooka yuharrifoona alkalima min baadi mawadiaihi yaqooloona in ooteetum hatha fakhuthoohu wain lam tutawhu faihtharoo waman yuridi Allahu fitnatahu falan tamlika lahu mina Allahi shayan laika allatheena lam yuridi Allahu an yutahhira quloobahum lahum fee alddunya khizyun walahum fee alakhirati aathabun aatheemun
Sammaaoona lilkathibi akkaloona lilssuhti fain jaooka faohkum baynahum aw aarid aanhum wain tuarid aanhum falan yadurrooka shayan wain akamta faohkum baynahum bialqisti inna Allaha yuhibbu almuqsiteena
Wakayfa yuhakkimoonaka waaindahumu alttawratu feeha hukmu Allahi thumma yatawallawna min baadi thalika wama olaika bialmumineena
Inna anzalna alttawrata feeha hudan wanoorun yahkumu biha alnnabiyyoona allatheena aslamoo lillatheena hadoo waalrrabbaniyyoona waalahbaru bima istuhfithoo min kitabi Allahi wakanoo aalayhi shuhadaa fala takhshawoo alnnasa waikhshawni wala tashtaroo biayatee hamanan qaleelan waman lam yahkum bima anzala Allahu faolaika humu alkafiroona
Wakatabna aalayhim feeha anna alnnafsa bialnnafsi waalaayna bialaayni waalanfa bialanfi waalothuna bialothuni waalssinna bialssinni aaljurooha qisasun faman tasaddaqa bihi fahuwa kaffaratun lahu waman lam yahkum bima anzala Allahu faolaika humu alththalimoona
Waqaffayna aala atharihim biaeesa ibni maryama musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi mina alttawrati waataynahu alinjeela feehi hudan wanoorun amusaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi mina alttawrati wahudan wamawaithatan lilmuttaqeena
Walyahkum ahlu alinjeeli bima anzala Allahu feehi waman lam yahkum bima anzala Allahu faolaika humu alfasiqoona
Waanzalna ilayka alkitaba bialhaqqi musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi mina alkitabi wamuhayminan aalayhi faohkum baynahum bima anzala Allahu wala tattabia ahwaahum aamma jaaka mina alhaqqi likullin jaaalna minkum shiraatan waminhajan walaw shaa Allahu lajaaalakum ommatan wahidatan walakin liyabluwakum fee ma atakum faistabiqoo alkhayrati ila Allahi marjiaukum jameeaan fayunabbiokum bima kuntum eehi takhtalifoona
Waani ohkum baynahum bima anzala Allahu wala tattabia ahwaahum waihtharhum an yaftinooka aan baadi ma anzala Allahu ilayka fain awallaw faialam annama yureedu Allahu an yuseebahum bibaadi thunoobihim wainna katheeran mina alnnasi lafasiqoona
Afahukma aljahiliyyati yabghoona waman ahsanu mina Allahu hukman liqawmin yooqinoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo alyahooda waalnnasara awliyaa baaduhum awliyao baadin waman yatawallahum minkum fainnahu inhum inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alththalimeena
Fatara allatheena fee quloobihim maradun yusariaoona feehim yaqooloona nakhsha an tuseebana dairatun faaasa Allahu an yatiya bialfathi w amrin min aindihi fayusbihoo aala ma asarroo fee anfusihim nadimeena
Wayaqoolu allatheena amanoo ahaolai allatheena aqsamoo biAllahi jahda aymanihim innahum lamaaakum habitat aamaluhum faasbahoo khasireena
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo man yartadda minkum aan deenihi fasawfa yatee Allahu biqawmin yuhibbuhum wayuhibboonahu athillatin aala almumineena aaizzatin aala alkafireena yujahidoona fee sabeeli Allahi wala yakhafoona lawmata laimin thalika fadlu Allahi yuteehi man ashao waAllahu wasiaun aaleemun
Innama waliyyukumu Allahu warasooluhu waallatheena amanoo allatheena yuqeemoona alssalata wayutoona alzzakata wahum rakiaoona
Waman yatawalla Allaha warasoolahu waallatheena amanoo fainna hizba Allahi humu alghaliboona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo allatheena ittakhathoo deenakum huzuwan walaaiban mina allatheena ootoo alkitaba min ablikum waalkuffara awliyaa waittaqoo Allaha in kuntum mumineena
Waitha nadaytum ila alssalati ittakhathooha huzuwan walaaiban thalika biannahum qawmun la yaaqiloona
Qul ya ahla alkitabi hal tanqimoona minna illa an amanna biAllahi wama onzila ilayna wama onzila min qablu waanna aktharakum fasiqoona
Qul hal onabbiokum bisharrin min thalika mathoobatan ainda Allahi man laaanahu Allahu waghadiba aalayhi wajaaala minhumu alqiradata aalkhanazeera waaabada alttaghooti olaika sharrun makanan waadallu aan sawai alssabeeli
Waitha jaookum qaloo amanna waqad dakhaloo bialkufri wahum qad kharajoo bihi waAllahu aalamu bima kanoo yaktumoona
Watara katheeran minhum yusariaoona fee alithmi waalaudwani waaklihimu alssuhta labisa ma kanoo yaamaloona
Lawla yanhahumu alrrabbaniyyoona waalahbaru aan qawlihimu alithma waaklihimu alssuhta labisa ma kanoo yasnaaoona
Waqalati alyahoodu yadu Allahi maghloolatun ghullat aydeehim waluainoo bima qaloo bal yadahu mabsootatani yunfiqu kayfa yashao walayazeedanna katheeran minhum ma onzila ilayka min rabbika tughyanan wakufran waalqayna baynahumu alaadawata waalbaghdaa ila yawmi lqiyamati kullama awqadoo naran lilharbi atfaaha Allahu wayasaawna fee alardi fasadan waAllahu la yuhibbu almufsideena
Walaw anna ahla alkitabi amanoo waittaqaw lakaffarna aanhum sayyiatihim walaadkhalnahum jannati alnnaaeemi
Walaw annahum aqamoo alttawrata waalinjeela wama onzila ilayhim min rabbihim laakaloo min fawqihim wamin tahti arjulihim minhum ommatun uqtasidatun wakatheerun minhum saa ma yaamaloona
Ya ayyuha alrrasoolu balligh ma onzila ilayka min rabbika wain lam tafaal fama ballaghta risalatahu waAllahu yaasimuka mina alnnasi nna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alkafireena
Qul ya ahla alkitabi lastum aala shayin hatta tuqeemoo alttawrata waalinjeela wama onzila ilaykum min rabbikum walayazeedanna katheeran inhum ma onzila ilayka min rabbika tughyanan wakufran fala tasa aala alqawmi alkafireena
Inna allatheena amanoo waallatheena hadoo waalssabioona waalnnasara man amana biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri waaamila salihan fala khawfun alayhim wala hum yahzanoona
Laqad akhathna meethaqa banee israeela waarsalna ilayhim rusulan kullama jaahum rasoolun bima la tahwa anfusuhum fareeqan kaththaboo afareeqan yaqtuloona
Wahasiboo alla takoona fitnatun faaamoo wasammoo thumma taba Allahu aalayhim thumma aamoo wasammoo katheerun minhum waAllahu baseerun ima yaamaloona
Laqad kafara allatheena qaloo inna Allaha huwa almaseehu ibnu maryama waqala almaseehu ya banee israeela oabudoo Allaha rabbee arabbakum innahu man yushrik biAllahi faqad harrama Allahu aalayhi aljannata wamawahu alnnaru wama lilththalimeena min ansarin
Laqad kafara allatheena qaloo inna Allaha thalithu thalathatin wama min ilahin illa ilahun wahidun wain lam yantahoo aamma yaqooloona ayamassanna allatheena kafaroo minhum aathabun aleemun
Afala yatooboona ila Allahi wayastaghfiroonahu waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Ma almaseehu ibnu maryama illa rasoolun qad khalat min qablihi alrrusulu waommuhu siddeeqatun kana yakulani alttaaama onthur kayfa ubayyinu lahumu alayati thumma onthur anna yufakoona
Qul ataabudoona min dooni Allahi ma la yamliku lakum darran wala nafaan waAllahu huwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Qul ya ahla alkitabi la taghloo fee deenikum ghayra alhaqqi wala tattabiaoo ahwaa qawmin qad dalloo min qablu waadalloo katheeran adalloo aan sawai alssabeeli
Luaina allatheena kafaroo min banee israeela aala lisani dawooda waaeesa ibni maryama thalika bima aasaw wakanoo yaatadoona
Kanoo la yatanahawna aan munkarin faaaloohu labisa ma kanoo yafaaloona
Tara katheeran minhum yatawallawna allatheena kafaroo labisa ma qaddamat lahum anfusuhum an sakhita Allahu aalayhim wafee alaathabi hum halidoona
Walaw kanoo yuminoona biAllahi waalnnabiyyi wama onzila ilayhi ma ittakhathoohum awliyaa walakinna katheeran minhum fasiqoona
Latajidanna ashadda alnnasi aadawatan lillatheena amanoo alyahooda waallatheena ashrakoo walatajidanna aqrabahum mawaddatan lillatheena manoo allatheena qaloo inna nasara thalika bianna minhum qisseeseena waruhbanan waannahum la yastakbiroona
Waitha samiaoo ma onzila ila alrrasooli tara aayunahum tafeedu mina alddamai mimma aarafoo mina alhaqqi yaqooloona rabbana amanna aoktubna maaa alshshahideena
Wama lana la numinu biAllahi wama jaana mina alhaqqi wanatmaau an yudkhilana rabbuna maaa alqawmi alssaliheena
Faathabahumu Allahu bima qaloo jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wathalika jazao almuhsineena
Waallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu aljaheemi
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tuharrimoo tayyibati ma ahalla Allahu lakum wala taatadoo inna Allaha la yuhibbu almuatadeena
Wakuloo mimma razaqakumu Allahu halalan tayyiban waittaqoo Allaha allathee antum bihi muminoona
La yuakhithukumu Allahu biallaghwi fee aymanikum walakin yuakhithukum bima aaqqadtumu alaymana fakaffaratuhu itaamu aasharati masakeena min awsati ma tutaimoona ahleekum aw kiswatuhum aw tahreeru raqabatin faman lam yajid fasiyamu thalathati ayyamin thalika kaffaratu ymanikum itha halaftum waihfathoo aymanakum kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakum ayatihi laaallakum tashkuroona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo innama alkhamru waalmaysiru waalansabu waalazlamu rijsun min aamali alshshaytani faijtaniboohu laaallakum uflihoona
Innama yureedu alshshaytanu an yooqiaa baynakumu alaadawata waalbaghdaa fee alkhamri waalmaysiri wayasuddakum aan thikri Allahi waaani lssalati fahal antum muntahoona
Waateeaoo Allaha waateeaoo alrrasoola waihtharoo fain tawallaytum faialamoo annama aala rasoolina albalaghu almubeenu
Laysa aala allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati junahun feema taaimoo itha ma ittaqaw waamanoo waaamiloo alssalihati thumma ittaqaw aamanoo thumma ittaqaw waahsanoo waAllahu yuhibbu almuhsineena
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo layabluwannakumu Allahu bishayin mina alssaydi tanaluhu aydeekum warimahukum liyaalama Allahu man yakhafuhu ialghaybi famani iatada baada thalika falahu aathabun aleemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la taqtuloo alssayda waantum hurumun waman qatalahu minkum mutaaammidan fajazaon mithlu ma qatala mina alnnaaami yahkumu bihi thawa aadlin minkum hadyan baligha alkaabati aw kaffaratun taaamu masakeena aw aadlu thalika siyaman liyathooqa abala amrihi aafa Allahu aamma salafa waman aada fayantaqimu Allahu minhu waAllahu aazeezun thoo intiqamin
Ohilla lakum saydu albahri wataaamuhu mataaan lakum walilssayyarati wahurrima aalaykum saydu albarri ma dumtum huruman waittaqoo Allaha llathee ilayhi tuhsharoona
Jaaala Allahu alkaabata albayta alharama qiyaman lilnnasi waalshshahra alharama waalhadya waalqalaida thalika litaalamoo anna Allaha aalamu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi waanna Allaha bikulli shayin aaleemun
Ialamoo anna Allaha shadeedu alaiqabi waanna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Ma aala alrrasooli illa albalaghu waAllahu yaalamu ma tubdoona wama taktumoona
Qul la yastawee alkhabeethu waalttayyibu walaw aajabaka kathratu alkhabeethi faittaqoo Allaha ya olee alalbabi laaallakum tuflihoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tasaloo aan ashyaa in tubda lakum tasukum wain tasaloo aanha heena yunazzalu alquranu tubda lakum aafa llahu aanha waAllahu ghafoorun haleemun
Qad saalaha qawmun min qablikum thumma asbahoo biha kafireena
Ma jaaala Allahu min baheeratin wala saibatin wala waseelatin wala hamin walakinna allatheena kafaroo yaftaroona aala Allahi alkathiba aaktharuhum la yaaqiloona
Waitha qeela lahum taaalaw ila ma anzala Allahu waila alrrasooli qaloo hasbuna ma wajadna aalayhi abaana awalaw kana abaohum la aalamoona shayan wala yahtadoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo aalaykum anfusakum la yadurrukum man dalla itha ihtadaytum ila Allahi marjiaukum jameeaan fayunabbiokum ima kuntum taamaloona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo shahadatu baynikum itha hadara ahadakumu almawtu heena alwasiyyati ithnani thawa aadlin minkum aw akharani min ghayrikum in antum darabtum fee alardi faasabatkum museebatu almawti tahbisoonahuma min baadi alssalati fayuqsimani biAllahi ini rtabtum la nashtaree bihi thamanan walaw kana tha qurba wala naktumu shahadata Allahi inna ithan lamina alathimeena
Fain authira aala annahuma istahaqqa ithman faakharani yaqoomani maqamahuma mina allatheena istahaqqa aalayhimu alawlayani fayuqsimani iAllahi lashahadatuna ahaqqu min shahadatihima wama iatadayna inna ithan lamina alththalimeena
Thalika adna an yatoo bialshshahadati aala wajhiha aw yakhafoo an turadda aymanun baada aymanihim waittaqoo Allaha waismaaoo waAllahu a yahdee alqawma alfasiqeena
Yawma yajmaau Allahu alrrusula fayaqoolu matha ojibtum qaloo la ailma lana innaka anta aallamu alghuyoobi
Ith qala Allahu ya aeesa ibna maryama othkur niamatee aalayka waaala walidatika ith ayyadtuka biroohi alqudusi tukallimu alnnasa fee almahdi wakahlan waith aallamtuka alkitaba waalhikmata waalttawrata waalinjeela waith takhluqu mina altteeni kahayati alttayri biithnee fatanfukhu feeha fatakoonu tayran biithnee watubrio alakmaha waalabrasa biithnee waith tukhriju almawta biithnee waith kafaftu banee sraeela aanka ith jitahum bialbayyinati faqala allatheena kafaroo minhum in hatha illa sihrun mubeenun
Waith awhaytu ila alhawariyyeena an aminoo bee wabirasoolee qaloo amanna waishhad biannana muslimoona
Ith qala alhawariyyoona ya aeesa ibna maryama hal yastateeau rabbuka an yunazzila aalayna maidatan mina alssamai qala ittaqoo Allaha in untum mumineena
Qaloo nureedu an nakula minha watatmainna quloobuna wanaalama an qad sadaqtana wanakoona aalayha mina alshshahideena
Qala aeesa ibnu maryama allahumma rabbana anzil aalayna maidatan mina alssamai takoonu lana aeedan liawwalina waakhirina waayatan minka aorzuqna waanta khayru alrraziqeena
Qala Allahu innee munazziluha aalaykum faman yakfur baadu minkum fainnee oaaththibuhu aathaban la oaaththibuhu ahadan mina alaalameena
Waith qala Allahu ya aeesa ibna maryama aanta qulta lilnnasi ittakhithoonee waommiya ilahayni min dooni Allahi qala subhanaka ma yakoonu lee an aqoola ma laysa lee bihaqqin in kuntu qultuhu faqad aalimtahu taalamu ma fee nafsee wala aalamu ma fee nafsika innaka nta aallamu alghuyoobi
Ma qultu lahum illa ma amartanee bihi ani oabudoo Allaha rabbee warabbakum wakuntu aalayhim shaheedan ma dumtu feehim falamma awaffaytanee kunta anta alrraqeeba aalayhim waanta aala kulli shayin shaheedun
In tuaaththibhum fainnahum aibaduka wain taghfir lahum fainnaka anta alaazeezu alhakeemu
Qala Allahu hatha yawmu yanfaau alssadiqeena sidquhum lahum jannatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan radiya Allahu anhum waradoo aanhu thalika alfawzu alaatheemu
Lillahi mulku alssamawati waalardi wama feehinna wahuwa aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Alhamdu lillahi allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda wajaaala alththulumati waalnnoora thumma allatheena kafaroo birabbihim yaadiloona
Huwa allathee khalaqakum min teenin thumma qada ajalan waajalun musamman aindahu thumma antum tamtaroona
Wahuwa Allahu fee alssamawati wafee alardi yaalamu sirrakum wajahrakum wayaalamu ma taksiboona
Wama tateehim min ayatin min ayati rabbihim illa kanoo aanha muarideena
Faqad kaththaboo bialhaqqi lamma jaahum fasawfa yateehim anbao ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Alam yaraw kam ahlakna min qablihim min qarnin makkannahum fee alardi ma lam numakkin lakum waarsalna alssamaa aalayhim midraran ajaaalna alanhara tajree min tahtihim faahlaknahum bithunoobihim waanshana min baadihim qarnan akhareena
Walaw nazzalna aalayka kitaban fee qirtasin falamasoohu biaydeehim laqala allatheena kafaroo in hatha illa sihrun mubeenun
Waqaloo lawla onzila aalayhi malakun walaw anzalna malakan laqudiya alamru thumma la yuntharoona
Walaw jaaalnahu malakan lajaaalnahu rajulan walalabasna aalayhim ma yalbisoona
Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika fahaqa biallatheena sakhiroo minhum ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Qul seeroo fee alardi thumma onthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu almukaththibeena
Qul liman ma fee alssamawati waalardi qul lillahi kataba aala nafsihi alrrahmata layajmaaannakum ila yawmi alqiyamati la rayba feehi llatheena khasiroo anfusahum fahum la yuminoona
Walahu ma sakana fee allayli waalnnahari wahuwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Qul aghayra Allahi attakhithu waliyyan fatiri alssamawati waalardi wahuwa yutaimu wala yutaamu qul innee omirtu an akoona awwala man slama wala takoonanna mina almushrikeena
Qul innee akhafu in aasaytu rabbee aathaba yawmin aatheemin
Man yusraf aanhu yawmaithin faqad rahimahu wathalika alfawzu almubeenu
Wain yamsaska Allahu bidurrin fala kashifa lahu illa huwa wain yamsaska bikhayrin fahuwa aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Wahuwa alqahiru fawqa aibadihi wahuwa alhakeemu alkhabeeru
Qul ayyu shayin akbaru shahadatan quli Allahu shaheedun baynee wabaynakum waoohiya ilayya hatha alquranu lionthirakum bihi waman balagha ainnakum latashhadoona anna maaa Allahi alihatan okhra qul la ashhadu qul innama huwa ilahun wahidun wainnanee bareeon mimma ushrikoona
Allatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yaarifoonahu kama yaarifoona abnaahum allatheena khasiroo anfusahum fahum la yuminoona
Waman athlamu mimmani iftara aala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba biayatihi innahu la yuflihu alththalimoona
Wayawma nahshuruhum jameeaan thumma naqoolu lillatheena ashrakoo ayna shurakaokumu allatheena kuntum tazaumoona
Thumma lam takun fitnatuhum illa an qaloo waAllahi rabbina ma kunna mushrikeena
Onthur kayfa kathaboo aala anfusihim wadalla aanhum ma kanoo yaftaroona
Waminhum man yastamiau ilayka wajaaalna aala quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee athanihim waqran wain yaraw kulla ayatin la uminoo biha hatta itha jaooka yujadiloonaka yaqoolu allatheena kafaroo in hatha illa asateeru alawwaleena
Wahum yanhawna aanhu wayanawna aanhu wain yuhlikoona illa anfusahum wama yashauroona
Walaw tara ith wuqifoo aala alnnari faqaloo ya laytana nuraddu wala nukaththiba biayati rabbina wanakoona mina almumineena
Bal bada lahum ma kanoo yukhfoona min qablu walaw ruddoo laaadoo lima nuhoo aanhu wainnahum lakathiboona
Waqaloo in hiya illa hayatuna alddunya wama nahnu bimabaootheena
Walaw tara ith wuqifoo aala rabbihim qala alaysa hatha bialhaqqi qaloo bala warabbina qala fathooqoo alaathaba bima kuntum takfuroona
Qad khasira allatheena kaththaboo biliqai Allahi hatta itha jaathumu alssaaatu baghtatan qaloo ya hasratana aala ma farratna feeha ahum yahmiloona awzarahum aala thuhoorihim ala saa ma yaziroona
Wama alhayatu alddunya illa laaibun walahwun walalddaru alakhirati khayrun lillatheena yattaqoona afala taaqiloona
Qad naalamu innahu layahzunuka allathee yaqooloona fainnahum la yukaththiboonaka walakinna alththalimeena biayati Allahi yajhadoona
Walaqad kuththibat rusulun min qablika fasabaroo aala ma kuththiboo waoothoo hatta atahum nasruna wala mubaddila likalimati Allahi alaqad jaaka min nabai almursaleena
Wain kana kabura aalayka iaraduhum faini istataata an tabtaghiya nafaqan fee alardi aw sullaman fee alssamai fatatiyahum biayatin walaw haa Allahu lajamaaahum aala alhuda fala takoonanna mina aljahileena
Innama yastajeebu allatheena yasmaaoona waalmawta yabaathuhumu Allahu thumma ilayhi yurjaaoona
Waqaloo lawla nuzzila aalayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul inna Allaha qadirun aala an yunazzila ayatan walakinna aktharahum la yaalamoona
Wama min dabbatin fee alardi wala tairin yateeru bijanahayhi illa omamun amthalukum ma farratna fee alkitabi min shayin thumma ila abbihim yuhsharoona
Waallatheena kaththaboo biayatina summun wabukmun fee alththulumati man yashai Allahu yudlilhu waman yasha yajaalhu aala siratin ustaqeemin
Qul araaytakum in atakum aathabu Allahi aw atatkumu alssaaatu aghayra Allahi tadaoona in kuntum sadiqeena
Bal iyyahu tadaoona fayakshifu ma tadaoona ilayhi in shaa watansawna ma tushrikoona
Walaqad arsalna ila omamin min qablika faakhathnahum bialbasai waalddarrai laaallahum yatadarraaoona
Falawla ith jaahum basuna tadarraaoo walakin qasat quloobuhum wazayyana lahumu alshshaytanu ma kanoo yaamaloona
Falamma nasoo ma thukkiroo bihi fatahna aalayhim abwaba kulli shayin hatta itha farihoo bima ootoo akhathnahum baghtatan faitha hum ublisoona
Faqutiaa dabiru alqawmi allatheena thalamoo waalhamdu lillahi rabbi alaalameena
Qul araaytum in akhatha Allahu samaakum waabsarakum wakhatama aala quloobikum man ilahun ghayru Allahi yateekum bihi onthur kayfa usarrifu alayati thumma hum yasdifoona
Qul araaytakum in atakum aathabu Allahi baghtatan aw jahratan hal yuhlaku illa alqawmu alththalimoona
Wama nursilu almursaleena illa mubashshireena wamunthireena faman amana waaslaha fala khawfun aalayhim wala hum yahzanoona
Waallatheena kaththaboo biayatina yamassuhumu alaathabu bima kanoo yafsuqoona
Qul la aqoolu lakum aindee khazainu Allahi wala aalamu alghayba wala aqoolu lakum innee malakun in attabiau illa ma yooha ilayya qul al yastawee alaama waalbaseeru afala tatafakkaroona
Waanthir bihi allatheena yakhafoona an yuhsharoo ila rabbihim laysa lahum min doonihi waliyyun wala shafeeaun laaallahum yattaqoona
Wala tatrudi allatheena yadaoona rabbahum bialghadati waalaashiyyi yureedoona wajhahu ma aalayka min hisabihim min shayin wama min isabika aalayhim min shayin fatatrudahum fatakoona mina alththalimeena
Wakathalika fatanna baadahum bibaadin liyaqooloo ahaolai manna Allahu aalayhim min baynina alaysa Allahu biaalama bialshshakireena
Waitha jaaka allatheena yuminoona biayatina faqul salamun aalaykum kataba rabbukum aala nafsihi alrrahmata annahu man aamila minkum ooan bijahalatin thumma taba min baadihi waaslaha faannahu ghafoorun raheemun
Wakathalika nufassilu alayati walitastabeena sabeelu almujrimeena
Qul innee nuheetu an aabuda allatheena tadaoona min dooni Allahi qul la attabiau ahwaakum qad dalaltu ithan wama ana mina almuhtadeena
Qul innee aala bayyinatin min rabbee wakaththabtum bihi ma aindee ma tastaajiloona bihi ini alhukmu illa lillahi yaqussu alhaqqa wahuwa hayru alfasileena
Qul law anna aindee ma tastaajiloona bihi laqudiya alamru baynee wabaynakum waAllahu aalamu bialththalimeena
Waaindahu mafatihu alghaybi la yaalamuha illa huwa wayaalamu ma fee albarri waalbahri wama tasqutu min waraqatin illa yaalamuha wala abbatin fee thulumati alardi wala ratbin wala yabisin illa fee kitabin mubeenin
Wahuwa allathee yatawaffakum biallayli wayaalamu ma jarahtum bialnnahari thumma yabaathukum feehi liyuqda ajalun musamman thumma ilayhi arjiaukum thumma yunabbiokum bima kuntum taamaloona
Wahuwa alqahiru fawqa aibadihi wayursilu aalaykum hafathatan hatta itha jaa ahadakumu almawtu tawaffathu rusuluna wahum la yufarritoona
Thumma ruddoo ila Allahi mawlahumu alhaqqi ala lahu alhukmu wahuwa asraau alhasibeena
Qul man yunajjeekum min thulumati albarri waalbahri tadaoonahu tadarruaan wakhufyatan lain anjana min hathihi lanakoonanna mina lshshakireena
Quli Allahu yunajjeekum minha wamin kulli karbin thumma antum tushrikoona
Qul huwa alqadiru aala an yabaatha aalaykum aathaban min fawqikum aw min tahti arjulikum aw yalbisakum shiyaaan wayutheeqa baadakum asa baadin onthur kayfa nusarrifu alayati laaallahum yafqahoona
Wakaththaba bihi qawmuka wahuwa alhaqqu qul lastu aalaykum biwakeelin
Likulli nabain mustaqarrun wasawfa taalamoona
Waitha raayta allatheena yakhoodoona fee ayatina faaarid aanhum hatta yakhoodoo fee hadeethin ghayrihi waimma yunsiyannaka alshshaytanu ala taqaud baada alththikra maaa alqawmi alththalimeena
Wama aala allatheena yattaqoona min hisabihim min shayin walakin thikra laaallahum yattaqoona
Wathari allatheena ittakhathoo deenahum laaiban walahwan wagharrathumu alhayatu alddunya wathakkir bihi an tubsala nafsun bima kasabat laysa laha min dooni Allahi waliyyun wala shafeeaun wain taadil kulla aadlin la yukhath minha olaika allatheena obsiloo bima kasaboo ahum sharabun min hameemin waaathabun aleemun bima kanoo yakfuroona
Qul anadaoo min dooni Allahi ma la yanfaauna wala yadurruna wanuraddu aala aaqabina baada ith hadana Allahu kaallathee istahwathu alshshayateenu fee alardi hayrana lahu ashabun yadaoonahu ila alhuda itina qul inna huda Allahi huwa alhuda waomirna linuslima lirabbi laalameena
Waan aqeemoo alssalata waittaqoohu wahuwa allathee ilayhi tuhsharoona
Wahuwa allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda bialhaqqi wayawma yaqoolu kun fayakoonu qawluhu alhaqqu walahu almulku yawma yunfakhu fee lssoori aalimu alghaybi waalshshahadati wahuwa alhakeemu alkhabeeru
Waith qala ibraheemu liabeehi azara atattakhithu asnaman alihatan innee araka waqawmaka fee dalalin mubeenin
Wakathalika nuree ibraheema malakoota alssamawati waalardi waliyakoona mina almooqineena
Falamma janna aalayhi allaylu raa kawkaban qala hatha rabbee falamma afala qala la ohibbu alafileena
Falamma raa alqamara bazighan qala hatha rabbee falamma afala qala lain lam yahdinee rabbee laakoonanna mina alqawmi alddalleena
Falamma raa alshshamsa bazighatan qala hatha rabbee hatha akbaru falamma afalat qala ya qawmi innee bareeon mimma tushrikoona
Innee wajjahtu wajhiya lillathee fatara alssamawati waalarda haneefan wama ana mina almushrikeena
Wahajjahu qawmuhu qala atuhajjoonnee fee Allahi waqad hadani wala akhafu ma tushrikoona bihi illa an yashaa rabbee shayan wasiaa rabbee ulla shayin ailman afala tatathakkaroona
Wakayfa akhafu ma ashraktum wala takhafoona annakum ashraktum biAllahi ma lam yunazzil bihi aalaykum sultanan faayyu alfareeqayni haqqu bialamni in kuntum taalamoona
Allatheena amanoo walam yalbisoo eemanahum bithulmin olaika lahumu alamnu wahum muhtadoona
Watilka hujjatuna ataynaha ibraheema aala qawmihi narfaau darajatin man nashao inna rabbaka hakeemun aaleemun
Wawahabna lahu ishaqa wayaaqooba kullan hadayna wanoohan hadayna min qablu wamin thurriyyatihi dawooda wasulaymana waayyooba wayoosufa amoosa waharoona wakathalika najzee almuhsineena
Wazakariyya wayahya waaeesa wailyasa kullun mina alssaliheena
Waismaaeela wailyasaaa wayoonusa walootan wakullan faddalna aala alaalameena
Wamin abaihim wathurriyyatihim waikhwanihim waijtabaynahum wahadaynahum ila siratin mustaqeemin
Thalika huda Allahi yahdee bihi man yashao min aibadihi walaw ashrakoo lahabita aanhum ma kanoo yaamaloona
Olaika allatheena ataynahumu alkitaba waalhukma waalnnubuwwata fain yakfur biha haolai faqad wakkalna biha qawman laysoo biha ikafireena
Olaika allatheena hada Allahu fabihudahumu iqtadih qul la asalukum aalayhi ajran in huwa illa thikra lilaalameena
Wama qadaroo Allaha haqqa qadrihi ith qaloo ma anzala Allahu aala basharin min shayin qul man anzala alkitaba allathee jaa bihi moosa nooran wahudan lilnnasi tajaaloonahu qarateesa tubdoonaha watukhfoona katheeran waaullimtum ma lam taalamoo antum wala abaokum quli llahu thumma tharhum fee khawdihim yalaaboona
Wahatha kitabun anzalnahu mubarakun musaddiqu allathee bayna yadayhi walitunthira omma alqura waman hawlaha waallatheena yuminoona ialakhirati yuminoona bihi wahum aala salatihim yuhafithoona
Waman athlamu mimmani iftara aala Allahi kathiban aw qala oohiya ilayya walam yooha ilayhi shayon waman qala saonzilu mithla ma anzala Allahu walaw tara ithi alththalimoona fee ghamarati almawti waalmalaikatu basitoo aydeehim akhrijoo anfusakumu alyawma tujzawna aathaba lhooni bima kuntum taqooloona aala Allahi ghayra alhaqqi wakuntum aan ayatihi tastakbiroona
Walaqad jitumoona furada kama khalaqnakum awwala marratin wataraktum ma khawwalnakum waraa thuhoorikum wama nara maaakum shufaaaakumu llatheena zaaamtum annahum feekum shurakao laqad taqattaaa baynakum wadalla aankum ma kuntum tazaumoona
Inna Allaha faliqu alhabbi waalnnawa yukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti wamukhriju almayyiti mina alhayyi thalikumu Allahu faanna tufakoona
Faliqu alisbahi wajaaala allayla sakanan waalshshamsa waalqamara husbanan thalika taqdeeru alaazeezi alaaleemi
Wahuwa allathee jaaala lakumu alnnujooma litahtadoo biha fee thulumati albarri waalbahri qad fassalna alayati liqawmin yaalamoona
Wahuwa allathee anshaakum min nafsin wahidatin famustaqarrun wamustawdaaun qad fassalna alayati liqawmin yafqahoona
Wahuwa allathee anzala mina alssamai maan faakhrajna bihi nabata kulli shayin faakhrajna minhu khadiran nukhriju minhu habban mutarakiban wamina alnnakhli min talaiha qinwanun daniyatun wajannatin min aanabin waalzzaytoona waalrrummana mushtabihan waghayra utashabihin onthuroo ila thamarihi itha athmara wayanaihi inna fee thalikum laayatin liqawmin yuminoona
Wajaaaloo lillahi shurakaa aljinna wakhalaqahum wakharaqoo lahu baneena wabanatin bighayri ailmin subhanahu wataaala aamma yasifoona
Badeeau alssamawati waalardi anna yakoonu lahu waladun walam takun lahu sahibatun wakhalaqa kulla shayin wahuwa bikulli shayin aaleemun
Thalikumu Allahu rabbukum la ilaha illa huwa khaliqu kulli shayin faoabudoohu wahuwa aala kulli shayin wakeelun
La tudrikuhu alabsaru wahuwa yudriku alabsara wahuwa allateefu alkhabeeru
Qad jaakum basairu min rabbikum faman absara falinafsihi waman aamiya faaalayha wama ana aalaykum bihafeethin
Wakathalika nusarrifu alayati waliyaqooloo darasta walinubayyinahu liqawmin yaalamoona
Ittabia ma oohiya ilayka min rabbika la ilaha illa huwa waaarid aani almushrikeena
Walaw shaa Allahu ma ashrakoo wama jaaalnaka aalayhim hafeethan wama anta aalayhim biwakeelin
Wala tasubboo allatheena yadaoona min dooni Allahi fayasubboo Allaha aadwan bighayri ailmin kathalika zayyanna likulli ommatin amalahum thumma ila rabbihim marjiauhum fayunabbiohum bima kanoo yaamaloona
Waaqsamoo biAllahi jahda aymanihim lain jaathum ayatun layuminunna biha qul innama alayatu ainda Allahi wama yushairukum annaha itha aat la yuminoona
Wanuqallibu afidatahum waabsarahum kama lam yuminoo bihi awwala marratin wanatharuhum fee tughyanihim yaamahoona
Walaw annana nazzalna ilayhimu almalaikata wakallamahumu almawta wahasharna aalayhim kulla shayin qubulan ma kanoo liyuminoo illa an ashaa Allahu walakinna aktharahum yajhaloona
Wakathalika jaaalna likulli nabiyyin aaduwwan shayateena alinsi waaljinni yoohee baaduhum ila baadin zukhrufa alqawli ghurooran walaw haa rabbuka ma faaaloohu fatharhum wama yaftaroona
Walitasgha ilayhi afidatu allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati waliyardawhu waliyaqtarifoo ma hum muqtarifoona
Afaghayra Allahi abtaghee hakaman wahuwa allathee anzala ilaykumu alkitaba mufassalan waallatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yaalamoona nnahu munazzalun min rabbika bialhaqqi fala takoonanna mina almumtareena
Watammat kalimatu rabbika sidqan waaadlan la mubaddila likalimatihi wahuwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Wain tutia akthara man fee alardi yudillooka aan sabeeli Allahi in yattabiaoona illa alththanna wain hum illa yakhrusoona
Inna rabbaka huwa aalamu man yadillu aan sabeelihi wahuwa aalamu bialmuhtadeena
Fakuloo mimma thukira ismu Allahi aalayhi in kuntum biayatihi mumineena
Wama lakum alla takuloo mimma thukira ismu Allahi aalayhi waqad fassala lakum ma harrama aalaykum illa ma idturirtum ilayhi wainna atheeran layudilloona biahwaihim bighayri ailmin inna rabbaka huwa aalamu bialmuatadeena
Watharoo thahira alithmi wabatinahu inna allatheena yaksiboona alithma sayujzawna bima kanoo yaqtarifoona
Wala takuloo mimma lam yuthkari ismu Allahi aalayhi wainnahu lafisqun wainna alshshayateena layoohoona ila awliyaihim liyujadilookum ain ataatumoohum innakum lamushrikoona
Awa man kana maytan faahyaynahu wajaaalna lahu nooran yamshee bihi fee alnnasi kaman mathaluhu fee alththulumati laysa bikharijin minha athalika zuyyina lilkafireena ma kanoo yaamaloona
Wakathalika jaaalna fee kulli qaryatin akabira mujrimeeha liyamkuroo feeha wama yamkuroona illa bianfusihim wama yashauroona
Waitha jaathum ayatun qaloo lan numina hatta nuta mithla ma ootiya rusulu Allahi Allahu aalamu haythu yajaalu risalatahu sayuseebu llatheena ajramoo sagharun ainda Allahi waaathabun shadeedun bima kanoo yamkuroona
Faman yuridi Allahu an yahdiyahu yashrah sadrahu lilislami waman yurid an yudillahu yajaal sadrahu dayyiqan harajan kaannama yassaaadu ee alssamai kathalika yajaalu Allahu alrrijsa aala allatheena la yuminoona
Wahatha siratu rabbika mustaqeeman qad fassalna alayati liqawmin yaththakkaroona
Lahum daru alssalami ainda rabbihim wahuwa waliyyuhum bima kanoo yaamaloona
Wayawma yahshuruhum jameeaan ya maashara aljinni qadi istakthartum mina alinsi waqala awliyaohum mina alinsi rabbana istamtaaa baaduna bibaadin wabalaghna ajalana allathee ajjalta lana qala alnnaru mathwakum khalideena feeha illa ma shaa Allahu inna rabbaka hakeemun aleemun
Wakathalika nuwallee baada alththalimeena baadan bima kanoo yaksiboona
Ya maashara aljinni waalinsi alam yatikum rusulun minkum yaqussoona aalaykum ayatee wayunthiroonakum liqaa yawmikum hatha qaloo hahidna aala anfusina wagharrathumu alhayatu alddunya washahidoo aala anfusihim annahum kanoo kafireena
Thalika an lam yakun rabbuka muhlika alqura bithulmin waahluha ghafiloona
Walikullin darajatun mimma aamiloo wama rabbuka bighafilin aamma yaamaloona
Warabbuka alghaniyyu thoo alrrahmati in yasha yuthhibkum wayastakhlif min baadikum ma yashao kama anshaakum min thurriyyati qawmin khareena
Inna ma tooaadoona laatin wama antum bimuajizeena
Qul ya qawmi iamaloo aala makanatikum innee aamilun fasawfa taalamoona man takoonu lahu aaqibatu alddari innahu la yuflihu lththalimoona
Wajaaaloo lillahi mimma tharaa mina alharthi waalanaami naseeban faqaloo hatha lillahi bizaamihim wahatha lishurakaina fama kana ishurakaihim fala yasilu ila Allahi wama kana lillahi fahuwa yasilu ila shurakaihim saa ma yahkumoona
Wakathalika zayyana likatheerin mina almushrikeena qatla awladihim shurakaohum liyurdoohum waliyalbisoo aalayhim deenahum walaw shaa llahu ma faaaloohu fatharhum wama yaftaroona
Waqaloo hathihi anaamun waharthun hijrun la yataamuha illa man nashao bizaamihim waanaamun hurrimat thuhooruha waanaamun la yathkuroona sma Allahi aalayha iftiraan aalayhi sayajzeehim bima kanoo yaftaroona
Waqaloo ma fee butooni hathihi alanaami khalisatun lithukoorina wamuharramun aala azwajina wain yakun maytatan fahum feehi shurakao ayajzeehim wasfahum innahu hakeemun aaleemun
Qad khasira allatheena qataloo awladahum safahan bighayri ailmin waharramoo ma razaqahumu Allahu iftiraan aala Allahi qad dalloo wama anoo muhtadeena
Wahuwa allathee anshaa jannatin maarooshatin waghayra maarooshatin waalnnakhla waalzzaraa mukhtalifan okuluhu waalzzaytoona waalrrummana mutashabihan waghayra mutashabihin kuloo min thamarihi itha athmara waatoo haqqahu yawma hasadihi wala tusrifoo innahu la uhibbu almusrifeena
Wamina alanaami hamoolatan wafarshan kuloo mimma razaqakumu Allahu wala tattabiaoo khutuwati alshshaytani innahu lakum aaduwwun mubeenun
Thamaniyata azwajin mina alddani ithnayni wamina almaazi ithnayni qul alththakarayni harrama ami alonthayayni amma ishtamalat aalayhi rhamu alonthayayni nabbioonee biailmin in kuntum sadiqeena
Wamina alibili ithnayni wamina albaqari ithnayni qul alththakarayni harrama ami alonthayayni amma ishtamalat aalayhi arhamu alonthayayni am kuntum shuhadaa ith wassakumu Allahu bihatha faman athlamu mimmani iftara aala Allahi kathiban liyudilla alnnasa ighayri ailmin inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alththalimeena
Qul la ajidu fee ma oohiya ilayya muharraman aala taaimin yataamuhu illa an yakoona maytatan aw daman masfoohan aw lahma khinzeerin ainnahu rijsun aw fisqan ohilla lighayri Allahi bihi famani idturra ghayra baghin wala aadin fainna rabbaka ghafoorun raheemun
Waaala allatheena hadoo harramna kulla thee thufurin wamina albaqari waalghanami harramna aalayhim shuhoomahuma illa ma hamalat huhooruhuma awi alhawaya aw ma ikhtalata biaathmin thalika jazaynahum bibaghyihim wainna lasadiqoona
Fain kaththabooka faqul rabbukum thoo rahmatin wasiaatin wala yuraddu basuhu aani alqawmi almujrimeena
Sayaqoolu allatheena ashrakoo law shaa Allahu ma ashrakna wala abaona wala harramna min shayin kathalika kaththaba allatheena min ablihim hatta thaqoo basana qul hal aindakum min ailmin fatukhrijoohu lana in tattabiaoona illa alththanna wain antum illa takhrusoona
Qul falillahi alhujjatu albalighatu falaw shaa lahadakum ajmaaeena
Qul halumma shuhadaakumu allatheena yashhadoona anna Allaha harrama hatha fain shahidoo fala tashhad maaahum wala tattabia ahwaa llatheena kaththaboo biayatina waallatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati wahum birabbihim yaadiloona
Qul taaalaw atlu ma harrama rabbukum aalaykum alla tushrikoo bihi shayan wabialwalidayni ihsanan wala taqtuloo awladakum min imlaqin nahnu narzuqukum waiyyahum wala taqraboo alfawahisha ma thahara minha wama batana wala taqtuloo alnnafsa allatee harrama Allahu illa ialhaqqi thalikum wassakum bihi laaallakum taaqiloona
Wala taqraboo mala alyateemi illa biallatee hiya ahsanu hatta yablugha ashuddahu waawfoo alkayla waalmeezana bialqisti la nukallifu afsan illa wusaaha waitha qultum faiadiloo walaw kana tha qurba wabiaahdi Allahi awfoo thalikum wassakum bihi laaallakum tathakkaroona
Waanna hatha siratee mustaqeeman faittabiaoohu wala tattabiaoo alssubula fatafarraqa bikum aan sabeelihi thalikum wassakum bihi aaallakum tattaqoona
Thumma atayna moosa alkitaba tamaman aala allathee ahsana watafseelan likulli shayin wahudan warahmatan laaallahum biliqai rabbihim uminoona
Wahatha kitabun anzalnahu mubarakun faittabiaoohu waittaqoo laaallakum turhamoona
An taqooloo innama onzila alkitabu aala taifatayni min qablina wain kunna aan dirasatihim laghafileena
Aw taqooloo law anna onzila aalayna alkitabu lakunna ahda minhum faqad jaakum bayyinatun min rabbikum wahudan warahmatun faman athlamu imman kaththaba biayati Allahi wasadafa aanha sanajzee allatheena yasdifoona aan ayatina sooa alaathabi bima kanoo yasdifoona
Hal yanthuroona illa an tatiyahumu almalaikatu aw yatiya rabbuka aw yatiya baadu ayati rabbika yawma yatee baadu ayati rabbika la anfaau nafsan eemanuha lam takun amanat min qablu aw kasabat fee eemaniha khayran quli intathiroo inna muntathiroona
Inna allatheena farraqoo deenahum wakanoo shiyaaan lasta minhum fee shayin innama amruhum ila Allahi thumma yunabbiohum bima kanoo afaaloona
Man jaa bialhasanati falahu aashru amthaliha waman jaa bialssayyiati fala yujza illa mithlaha wahum la yuthlamoona
Qul innanee hadanee rabbee ila siratin mustaqeemin deenan qiyaman millata ibraheema haneefan wama kana mina almushrikeena
Qul inna salatee wanusukee wamahyaya wamamatee lillahi rabbi alaalameena
La shareeka lahu wabithalika omirtu waana awwalu almuslimeena
Qul aghayra Allahi abghee rabban wahuwa rabbu kulli shayin wala taksibu kullu nafsin illa aalayha wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra humma ila rabbikum marjiaukum fayunabbiokum bima kuntum feehi takhtalifoona
Wahuwa allathee jaaalakum khalaifa alardi warafaaa baadakum fawqa baadin darajatin liyabluwakum fee ma atakum inna rabbaka sareeau laiqabi wainnahu laghafoorun raheemun
Aliflammeemsad
Kitabun onzila ilayka fala yakun fee sadrika harajun minhu litunthira bihi wathikra lilmumineena
Ittabiaoo ma onzila ilaykum min rabbikum wala tattabiaoo min doonihi awliyaa qaleelan ma tathakkaroona
Wakam min qaryatin ahlaknaha fajaaha basuna bayatan aw hum qailoona
Fama kana daawahum ith jaahum basuna illa an qaloo inna kunna thalimeena
Falanasalanna allatheena orsila ilayhim walanasalanna almursaleena
Falanaqussanna aalayhim biailmin wama kunna ghaibeena
Waalwaznu yawmaithini alhaqqu faman thaqulat mawazeenuhu faolaika humu almuflihoona
Waman khaffat mawazeenuhu faolaika allatheena khasiroo anfusahum bima kanoo biayatina yathlimoona
Walaqad makkannakum fee alardi wajaaalna lakum feeha maaayisha qaleelan ma tashkuroona
Walaqad khalaqnakum thumma sawwarnakum thumma qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa lam yakun mina alssajideena
Qala ma manaaaka alla tasjuda ith amartuka qala ana khayrun minhu khalaqtanee min narin wakhalaqtahu min teenin
Qala faihbit minha fama yakoonu laka an tatakabbara feeha faokhruj innaka mina alssaghireena
Qala anthirnee ila yawmi yubaathoona
Qala innaka mina almunthareena
Qala fabima aghwaytanee laaqaudanna lahum sirataka almustaqeema
Thumma laatiyannahum min bayni aydeehim wamin khalfihim waaan aymanihim waaan shamailihim wala tajidu aktharahum shakireena
Qala okhruj minha mathooman madhooran laman tabiaaka minhum laamlaanna jahannama minkum ajmaaeena
Waya adamu oskun anta wazawjuka aljannata fakula min haythu shituma wala taqraba hathihi alshshajarata fatakoona mina alththalimeena
Fawaswasa lahuma alshshaytanu liyubdiya lahuma ma wooriya aanhuma min sawatihima waqala ma nahakuma rabbukuma aan hathihi alshshajarati lla an takoona malakayni aw takoona mina alkhalideena
Waqasamahuma innee lakuma lamina alnnasiheena
Fadallahuma bighuroorin falamma thaqa alshshajarata badat lahuma sawatuhuma watafiqa yakhsifani aalayhima min waraqi aljannati anadahuma rabbuhuma alam anhakuma aan tilkuma alshshajarati waaqul lakuma inna alshshaytana lakuma aaduwwun mubeenun
Qala rabbana thalamna anfusana wain lam taghfir lana watarhamna lanakoonanna mina alkhasireena
Qala ihbitoo baadukum libaadin aaduwwun walakum fee alardi mustaqarrun wamataaun ila heenin
Qala feeha tahyawna wafeeha tamootoona waminha tukhrajoona
Ya banee adama qad anzalna aalaykum libasan yuwaree sawatikum wareeshan walibasu alttaqwa thalika khayrun thalika min ayati Allahi aaallahum yaththakkaroona
Ya banee adama la yaftinannakumu alshshaytanu kama akhraja abawaykum mina aljannati yanziau aanhuma libasahuma liyuriyahuma sawatihima nnahu yarakum huwa waqabeeluhu min haythu la tarawnahum inna jaaalna alshshayateena awliyaa lillatheena la yuminoona
Waitha faaaloo fahishatan qaloo wajadna aalayha abaana waAllahu amarana biha qul inna Allaha la yamuru bialfahshai ataqooloona aala llahi ma la taalamoona
Qul amara rabbee bialqisti waaqeemoo wujoohakum ainda kulli masjidin waodaoohu mukhliseena lahu alddeena kama badaakum taaoodoona
Fareeqan hada wafareeqan haqqa aalayhimu alddalalatu innahumu ittakhathoo alshshayateena awliyaa min dooni Allahi wayahsaboona annahum uhtadoona
Ya banee adama khuthoo zeenatakum ainda kulli masjidin wakuloo waishraboo wala tusrifoo innahu la yuhibbu almusrifeena
Qul man harrama zeenata Allahi allatee akhraja liaibadihi waalttayyibati mina alrrizqi qul hiya lillatheena amanoo fee alhayati lddunya khalisatan yawma alqiyamati kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin yaalamoona
Qul innama harrama rabbiya alfawahisha ma thahara minha wama batana waalithma waalbaghya bighayri alhaqqi waan tushrikoo biAllahi ma am yunazzil bihi sultanan waan taqooloo aala Allahi ma la taalamoona
Walikulli ommatin ajalun faitha jaa ajaluhum la yastakhiroona saaatan wala yastaqdimoona
Ya banee adama imma yatiyannakum rusulun minkum yaqussoona aalaykum ayatee famani ittaqa waaslaha fala khawfun aalayhim wala hum ahzanoona
Waallatheena kaththaboo biayatina waistakbaroo aanha olaika ashabu alnnari hum feeha khalidoona
Faman athlamu mimmani iftara aala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba biayatihi olaika yanaluhum naseebuhum mina alkitabi hatta itha jaathum rusuluna yatawaffawnahum qaloo ayna ma kuntum tadaoona min dooni Allahi qaloo dalloo aanna washahidoo aala anfusihim annahum kanoo afireena
Qala odkhuloo fee omamin qad khalat min qablikum mina aljinni waalinsi fee alnnari kullama dakhalat ommatun laaanat okhtaha hatta itha iddarakoo feeha jameeaan qalat okhrahum lioolahum rabbana haolai adalloona faatihim aathaban diafan mina alnnari qala likullin diafun alakin la taalamoona
Waqalat oolahum liokhrahum fama kana lakum aalayna min fadlin fathooqoo alaathaba bima kuntum taksiboona
Inna allatheena kaththaboo biayatina waistakbaroo aanha la tufattahu lahum abwabu alssamai wala yadkhuloona aljannata hatta yalija ljamalu fee sammi alkhiyati wakathalika najzee almujrimeena
Lahum min jahannama mihadun wamin fawqihim ghawashin wakathalika najzee alththalimeena
Waallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati la nukallifu nafsan illa wusaaha olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoona
Wanazaana ma fee sudoorihim min ghillin tajree min tahtihimu alanharu waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee hadana lihatha wama kunna inahtadiya lawla an hadana Allahu laqad jaat rusulu rabbina bialhaqqi wanoodoo an tilkumu aljannatu oorithtumooha bima kuntum taamaloona
Wanada ashabu aljannati ashaba alnnari an qad wajadna ma waaadana rabbuna haqqan fahal wajadtum ma waaada rabbukum haqqan qaloo naaam aaththana muaththinun baynahum an laanatu Allahi aala alththalimeena
Allatheena yasuddoona aan sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha aiwajan wahum bialakhirati kafiroona
Wabaynahuma hijabun waaala alaarafi rijalun yaarifoona kullan biseemahum wanadaw ashaba aljannati an salamun aalaykum lam yadkhulooha ahum yatmaaoona
Waitha surifat absaruhum tilqaa ashabi alnnari qaloo rabbana la tajaalna maaa alqawmi alththalimeena
Wanada ashabu alaarafi rijalan yaarifoonahum biseemahum qaloo ma aghna aankum jamaukum wama kuntum tastakbiroona
Ahaolai allatheena aqsamtum la yanaluhumu Allahu birahmatin odkhuloo aljannata la khawfun aalaykum wala antum tahzanoona
Wanada ashabu alnari ashaba aljannati an afeedoo aalayna mina almai aw mimma razaqakumu Allahu qaloo inna Allaha harramahuma aala lkafireena
Allatheena ittakhathoo deenahum lahwan walaaiban wagharrathumu alhayatu alddunya faalyawma nansahum kama nasoo liqaa yawmihim hatha ama kanoo biayatina yajhadoona
Walaqad jinahum bikitabin fassalnahu aala ailmin hudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoona
Hal yanthuroona illa taweelahu yawma yatee taweeluhu yaqoolu allatheena nasoohu min qablu qad jaat rusulu rabbina bialhaqqi fahal lana min shufaaaa fayashfaaoo lana aw nuraddu fanaamala ghayra allathee kunna naamalu qad khasiroo anfusahum wadalla aanhum ma kanoo aftaroona
Inna rabbakumu Allahu allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa aala alaarshi yughshee allayla alnnahara yatlubuhu hatheethan waalshshamsa waalqamara waalnnujooma musakhkharatin biamrihi ala lahu alkhalqu waalamru tabaraka Allahu rabbu laalameena
Odaoo rabbakum tadarruaan wakhufyatan innahu la yuhibbu almuatadeena
Wala tufsidoo fee alardi baada islahiha waodaoohu khawfan watamaaan inna rahmata Allahi qareebun mina almuhsineena
Wahuwa allathee yursilu alrriyaha bushran bayna yaday rahmatihi hatta itha aqallat sahaban thiqalan suqnahu libaladin mayyitin aanzalna bihi almaa faakhrajna bihi min kulli alththamarati kathalika nukhriju almawta laaallakum tathakkaroona
Waalbaladu alttayyibu yakhruju nabatuhu biithni rabbihi waallathee khabutha la yakhruju illa nakidan kathalika nusarrifu alayati iqawmin yashkuroona
Laqad arsalna noohan ila qawmihi faqala ya qawmi oabudoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu innee akhafu aalaykum aathaba yawmin atheemin
Qala almalao min qawmihi inna lanaraka fee dalalin mubeenin
Qala ya qawmi laysa bee dalalatun walakinnee rasoolun min rabbi alaalameena
Oballighukum risalati rabbee waansahu lakum waaalamu mina Allahi ma la taalamoona
Awaaajibtum an jaakum thikrun min rabbikum aala rajulin minkum liyunthirakum walitattaqoo walaaallakum turhamoona
Fakaththaboohu faanjaynahu waallatheena maaahu fee alfulki waaghraqna allatheena kaththaboo biayatina innahum kanoo qawman aameena
Waila aadin akhahum hoodan qala ya qawmi oabudoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaqoona
Qala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi inna lanaraka fee safahatin wainna lanathunnuka mina alkathibeena
Qala ya qawmi laysa bee safahatun walakinnee rasoolun min rabbi alaalameena
Oballighukum risalati rabbee waana lakum nasihun ameenun
Awaaajibtum an jaakum thikrun min rabbikum aala rajulin minkum liyunthirakum waothkuroo ith jaaalakum khulafaa min baadi qawmi noohin azadakum fee alkhalqi bastatan faothkuroo alaa Allahi laaallakum tuflihoona
Qaloo ajitana linaabuda Allaha wahdahu wanathara ma kana yaabudu abaona fatina bima taaiduna in kunta mina alssadiqeena
Qala qad waqaaa aalaykum min rabbikum rijsun waghadabun atujadiloonanee fee asmain sammaytumooha antum waabaokum ma nazzala Allahu biha in sultanin faintathiroo innee maaakum mina almuntathireena
Faanjaynahu waallatheena maaahu birahmatin minna waqataana dabira allatheena kaththaboo biayatina wama kanoo mumineena
Waila thamooda akhahum salihan qala ya qawmi oabudoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu qad jaatkum bayyinatun min rabbikum hathihi aqatu Allahi lakum ayatan fatharooha takul fee ardi Allahi wala tamassooha bisooin fayakhuthakum aathabun aleemun
Waothkuroo ith jaaalakum khulafaa min baadi aadin wabawwaakum fee alardi tattakhithoona min suhooliha qusooran watanhitoona aljibala uyootan faothkuroo alaa Allahi wala taathaw fee alardi mufsideena
Qala almalao allatheena istakbaroo min qawmihi lillatheena istudaifoo liman amana minhum ataalamoona anna salihan mursalun min rabbihi aloo inna bima orsila bihi muminoona
Qala allatheena istakbaroo inna biallathee amantum bihi kafiroona
Faaaqaroo alnnaqata waaataw aan amri rabbihim waqaloo ya salihu itina bima taaiduna in kunta mina almursaleena
Faakhathathumu alrrajfatu faasbahoo fee darihim jathimeena
Fatawalla aanhum waqala ya qawmi laqad ablaghtukum risalata rabbee wanasahtu lakum walakin la tuhibboona alnnasiheena
Walootan ith qala liqawmihi atatoona alfahishata ma sabaqakum biha min ahadin mina alaalameena
Innakum latatoona alrrijala shahwatan min dooni alnnisai bal antum qawmun musrifoona
Wama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo akhrijoohum min qaryatikum innahum onasun yatatahharoona
Faanjaynahu waahlahu illa imraatahu kanat mina alghabireena
Waamtarna aalayhim mataran faonthur kayfa kana aaqibatu almujrimeena
Waila madyana akhahum shuaayban qala ya qawmi oabudoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu qad jaatkum bayyinatun min rabbikum faawfoo lkayla waalmeezana wala tabkhasoo alnnasa ashyaahum wala tufsidoo fee alardi baada islahiha thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum mumineena
Wala taqaudoo bikulli siratin tooaidoona watasuddoona aan sabeeli Allahi man amana bihi watabghoonaha aiwajan waothkuroo ith kuntum aleelan fakaththarakum waonthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu almufsideena
Wain kana taifatun minkum amanoo biallathee orsiltu bihi wataifatun lam yuminoo faisbiroo hatta yahkuma Allahu baynana wahuwa khayru lhakimeena
Qala almalao allatheena istakbaroo min qawmihi lanukhrijannaka ya shuaaybu waallatheena amanoo maaaka min qaryatina aw lataaoodunna fee illatina qala awalaw kunna kariheena
Qadi iftarayna aala Allahi kathiban in audna fee millatikum baada ith najjana Allahu minha wama yakoonu lana an naaooda feeha illa an yashaa Allahu rabbuna wasiaa rabbuna kulla shayin ailman aala Allahi tawakkalna rabbana iftah baynana wabayna qawmina bialhaqqi waanta hayru alfatiheena
Waqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi laini ittabaatum shuaayban innakum ithan lakhasiroona
Faakhathathumu alrrajfatu faasbahoo fee darihim jathimeena
Allatheena kaththaboo shuaayban kaan lam yaghnaw feeha allatheena kaththaboo shuaayban kanoo humu alkhasireena
Fatawalla aanhum waqala ya qawmi laqad ablaghtukum risalati rabbee wanasahtu lakum fakayfa asa aala qawmin kafireena
Wama arsalna fee qaryatin min nabiyyin illa akhathna ahlaha bialbasai waalddarrai laaallahum yaddarraaoona
Thumma baddalna makana alssayyiati alhasanata hatta aafaw waqaloo qad massa abaana alddarrao waalssarrao faakhathnahum baghtatan wahum a yashauroona
Walaw anna ahla alqura amanoo waittaqaw lafatahna aalayhim barakatin mina alssamai waalardi walakin kaththaboo faakhathnahum bima kanoo aksiboona
Afaamina ahlu alqura an yatiyahum basuna bayatan wahum naimoona
Awa amina ahlu alqura an yatiyahum basuna duhan wahum yalaaboona
Afaaminoo makra Allahi fala yamanu makra Allahi illa alqawmu alkhasiroona
Awalam yahdi lillatheena yarithoona alarda min baadi ahliha an law nashao asabnahum bithunoobihim wanatbaau aala quloobihim fahum la asmaaoona
Tilka alqura naqussu aalayka min anbaiha walaqad jaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati fama kanoo liyuminoo bima kaththaboo min qablu athalika yatbaau Allahu aala quloobi alkafireena
Wama wajadna liaktharihim min aahdin wain wajadna aktharahum lafasiqeena
Thumma baaathna min baadihim moosa biayatina ila firaawna wamalaihi fathalamoo biha faonuthur kayfa kana aaqibatu almufsideena
Waqala moosa ya firaawnu innee rasoolun min rabbi alaalameena
Haqeequn aala an la aqoola aala Allahi illa alhaqqa qad jitukum bibayyinatin min rabbikum faarsil maaiya banee israeela
Qala in kunta jita biayatin fati biha in kunta mina alssadiqeena
Faalqa aasahu faitha hiya thuabanun mubeenun
Wanazaaa yadahu faitha hiya baydao lilnnathireena
Qala almalao min qawmi firaawna inna hatha lasahirun aaleemun
Yureedu an yukhrijakum min ardikum famatha tamuroona
Qaloo arjih waakhahu waarsil fee almadaini hashireena
Yatooka bikulli sahirin aaleemin
Wajaa alssaharatu firaawna qaloo inna lana laajran in kunna nahnu alghalibeena
Qala naaam wainnakum lamina almuqarrabeena
Qaloo ya moosa imma an tulqiya waimma an nakoona nahnu almulqeena
Qala alqoo falamma alqaw saharoo aayuna alnnasi waistarhaboohum wajaoo bisihrin aatheemin
Waawhayna ila moosa an alqi aasaka faitha hiya talqafu ma yafikoona
Fawaqaaa alhaqqu wabatala ma kanoo yaamaloona
Faghuliboo hunalika wainqalaboo saghireena
Waolqiya alssaharatu sajideena
Qaloo amanna birabbi alaalameena
Rabbi moosa waharoona
Qala firaawnu amantum bihi qabla an athana lakum inna hatha lamakrun makartumoohu fee almadeenati litukhrijoo minha ahlaha fasawfa aalamoona
Laoqatiaanna aydiyakum waarjulakum min khilafin thumma laosallibannakum ajmaaeena
Qaloo inna ila rabbina munqaliboona
Wama tanqimu minna illa an amanna biayati rabbina lamma jaatna rabbana afrigh aalayna sabran watawaffana muslimeena
Waqala almalao min qawmi firaawna atatharu moosa waqawmahu liyufsidoo fee alardi wayatharaka waalihataka qala sanuqattilu abnaahum anastahyee nisaahum wainna fawqahum qahiroona
Qala moosa liqawmihi istaaeenoo biAllahi waisbiroo inna alarda lillahi yoorithuha man yashao min aibadihi waalaaqibatu lilmuttaqeena
Qaloo ootheena min qabli an tatiyana wamin baadi ma jitana qala aasa rabbukum an yuhlika aaduwwakum wayastakhlifakum fee alardi ayanthura kayfa taamaloona
Walaqad akhathna ala firaawna bialssineena wanaqsin mina alththamarati laaallahum yaththakkaroona
Faitha jaathumu alhasanatu qaloo lana hathihi wain tusibhum sayyiatun yattayyaroo bimoosa waman maaahu ala innama tairuhum ainda Allahi alakinna aktharahum la yaalamoona
Waqaloo mahma tatina bihi min ayatin litasharana biha fama nahnu laka bimumineena
Faarsalna aalayhimu alttoofana waaljarada waalqummala waalddafadiaa waalddama ayatin mufassalatin faistakbaroo wakanoo qawman mujrimeena
Walamma waqaaa aalayhimu alrrijzu qaloo ya moosa odau lana rabbaka bima aahida aindaka lain kashafta aanna alrrijza lanuminanna laka alanursilanna maaaka banee israeela
Falamma kashafna aanhumu alrrijza ila ajalin hum balighoohu itha hum yankuthoona
Faintaqamna minhum faaghraqnahum fee alyammi biannahum kaththaboo biayatina wakanoo aanha ghafileena
Waawrathna alqawma allatheena kanoo yustadaafoona mashariqa alardi wamagharibaha allatee barakna feeha watammat kalimatu rabbika lhusna aala banee israeela bima sabaroo wadammarna ma kana yasnaau firaawnu waqawmuhu wama kanoo yaarishoona
Wajawazna bibanee israeela albahra faataw aala qawmin yaakufoona aala asnamin lahum qaloo ya moosa ijaal lana ilahan kama lahum lihatun qala innakum qawmun tajhaloona
Inna haolai mutabbarun ma hum feehi wabatilun ma kanoo yaamaloona
Qala aghayra Allahi abgheekum ilahan wahuwa faddalakum aala alaalameena
Waith anjaynakum min ali firaawna yasoomoonakum sooa alaathabi yuqattiloona abnaakum wayastahyoona nisaakum wafee thalikum balaon min abbikum aatheemun
Wawaaadna moosa thalatheena laylatan waatmamnaha biaashrin fatamma meeqatu rabbihi arbaaeena laylatan waqala moosa liakheehi haroona khlufnee fee qawmee waaslih wala tattabia sabeela almufsideena
Walamma jaa moosa limeeqatina wakallamahu rabbuhu qala rabbi arinee anthur ilayka qala lan taranee walakini onthur ila aljabali faini istaqarra makanahu fasawfa taranee falamma tajalla rabbuhu liljabali jaaalahu dakkan wakharra moosa saaiqan falamma afaqa qala subhanaka ubtu ilayka waana awwalu almumineena
Qala ya moosa innee istafaytuka aala alnnasi birisalatee wabikalamee fakhuth ma ataytuka wakun mina alshshakireena
Wakatabna lahu fee alalwahi min kulli shayin mawaithatan watafseelan likulli shayin fakhuthha biquwwatin wamur qawmaka yakhuthoo iahsaniha saoreekum dara alfasiqeena
Saasrifu aan ayatiya allatheena yatakabbaroona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wain yaraw kulla ayatin la yuminoo biha wain yaraw sabeela alrrushdi la yattakhithoohu sabeelan wain yaraw sabeela alghayyi yattakhithoohu sabeelan thalika biannahum kaththaboo biayatina wakanoo anha ghafileena
Waallatheena kaththaboo biayatina waliqai alakhirati habitat aamaluhum hal yujzawna illa ma kanoo yaamaloona
Waittakhatha qawmu moosa min baadihi min huliyyihim aijlan jasadan lahu khuwarun alam yaraw annahu la yukallimuhum wala yahdeehim abeelan ittakhathoohu wakanoo thalimeena
Walamma suqita fee aydeehim waraaw annahum qad dalloo qaloo lain lam yarhamna rabbuna wayaghfir lana lanakoonanna mina alkhasireena
Walamma rajaaa moosa ila qawmihi ghadbana asifan qala bisama khalaftumoonee min baadee aaajiltum amra rabbikum waalqa alalwaha waakhatha birasi akheehi yajurruhu ilayhi qala ibna omma inna alqawma istadaafoonee wakadoo yaqtuloonanee fala tushmit biya alaadaa wala ajaalnee maaa alqawmi alththalimeena
Qala rabbi ighfir lee waliakhee waadkhilna fee rahmatika waanta arhamu alrrahimeena
Inna allatheena ittakhathoo alaijla sayanaluhum ghadabun min rabbihim wathillatun fee alhayati alddunya wakathalika najzee almuftareena
Waallatheena aamiloo alssayyiati thumma taboo min baadiha waamanoo inna rabbaka min baadiha laghafoorun raheemun
Walamma sakata aan moosa alghadabu akhatha alalwaha wafee nuskhatiha hudan warahmatun lillatheena hum lirabbihim yarhaboona
Waikhtara moosa qawmahu sabaeena rajulan limeeqatina falamma akhathathumu alrrajfatu qala rabbi law shita ahlaktahum min qablu waiyyaya atuhlikuna bima faaala alssufahao minna in hiya illa fitnatuka tudillu biha man tashao watahdee man tashao anta waliyyuna faighfir lana airhamna waanta khayru alghafireena
Waoktub lana fee hathihi alddunya hasanatan wafee alakhirati inna hudna ilayka qala aathabee oseebu bihi man ashao warahmatee wasiaat ulla shayin fasaaktubuha lillatheena yattaqoona wayutoona alzzakata waallatheena hum biayatina yuminoona
Allatheena yattabiaoona alrrasoola alnnabiyya alommiyya allathee yajidoonahu maktooban aindahum fee alttawrati waalinjeeli yamuruhum bialmaaroofi wayanhahum aani almunkari wayuhillu lahumu alttayyibati wayuharrimu aalayhimu alkhabaitha wayadaau aanhum israhum waalaghlala allatee kanat aalayhim faallatheena amanoo bihi waaazzaroohu wanasaroohu waittabaaoo alnnoora allathee onzila maaahu olaika umu almuflihoona
Qul ya ayyuha alnnasu innee rasoolu Allahi ilaykum jameeaan allathee lahu mulku alssamawati waalardi la ilaha illa huwa yuhyee ayumeetu faaminoo biAllahi warasoolihi alnnabiyyi alommiyyi allathee yuminu biAllahi wakalimatihi waittabiaoohu laaallakum tahtadoona
Wamin qawmi moosa ommatun yahdoona bialhaqqi wabihi yaadiloona
Waqattaanahumu ithnatay aashrata asbatan omaman waawhayna ila moosa ithi istasqahu qawmuhu ani idrib biaasaka alhajara fainbajasat minhu ithnata aashrata aaynan qad aalima kullu onasin mashrabahum wathallalna aalayhimu alghamama waanzalna aalayhimu almanna waalssalwa uloo min tayyibati ma razaqnakum wama thalamoona walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona
Waith qeela lahumu oskunoo hathihi alqaryata wakuloo minha haythu shitum waqooloo hittatun waodkhuloo albaba sujjadan naghfir lakum hateeatikum sanazeedu almuhsineena
Fabaddala allatheena thalamoo minhum qawlan ghayra allathee qeela lahum faarsalna aalayhim rijzan mina alssamai bima kanoo yathlimoona
Waisalhum aani alqaryati allatee kanat hadirata albahri ith yaadoona fee alssabti ith tateehim heetanuhum yawma sabtihim shurraaan ayawma la yasbitoona la tateehim kathalika nabloohum bima kanoo yafsuqoona
Waith qalat ommatun minhum lima taaithoona qawman Allahu muhlikuhum aw muaaththibuhum aathaban shadeedan qaloo maathiratan ila rabbikum alaaallahum yattaqoona
Falamma nasoo ma thukkiroo bihi anjayna allatheena yanhawna aani alssooi waakhathna allatheena thalamoo biaathabin baeesin bima kanoo afsuqoona
Falamma aataw aan ma nuhoo aanhu qulna lahum koonoo qiradatan khasieena
Waith taaththana rabbuka layabaathanna aalayhim ila yawmi alqiyamati man yasoomuhum sooa alaathabi inna rabbaka lasareeau alaiqabi ainnahu laghafoorun raheemun
Waqattaanahum fee alardi omaman minhumu alssalihoona waminhum doona thalika wabalawnahum bialhasanati waalssayyiati laaallahum arjiaoona
Fakhalafa min baadihim khalfun warithoo alkitaba yakhuthoona aarada hatha aladna wayaqooloona sayughfaru lana wain yatihim aaradun mithluhu yakhuthoohu alam yukhath aalayhim meethaqu alkitabi an la yaqooloo aala Allahi illa alhaqqa wadarasoo ma feehi waalddaru lakhiratu khayrun lillatheena yattaqoona afala taaqiloona
Waallatheena yumassikoona bialkitabi waaqamoo alssalata inna la nudeeau ajra almusliheena
Waith nataqna aljabala fawqahum kaannahu thullatun wathannoo annahu waqiaun bihim khuthoo ma ataynakum biquwwatin waothkuroo ma feehi aaallakum tattaqoona
Waith akhatha rabbuka min banee adama min thuhoorihim thurriyyatahum waashhadahum aala anfusihim alastu birabbikum qaloo bala shahidna n taqooloo yawma alqiyamati inna kunna aan hatha ghafileena
Aw taqooloo innama ashraka abaona min qablu wakunna thurriyyatan min baadihim afatuhlikuna bima faaala almubtiloona
Wakathalika nufassilu alayati walaaallahum yarjiaoona
Waotlu aalayhim nabaa allathee ataynahu ayatina fainsalakha minha faatbaaahu alshshaytanu fakana mina alghaweena

Saa mathalan alqawmu allatheena kaththaboo biayatina waanfusahum kanoo yathlimoona
Man yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadee waman yudlil faolaika humu alkhasiroona
Walaqad tharana lijahannama katheeran mina aljinni waalinsi lahum quloobun la yafqahoona biha walahum aayunun la yubsiroona biha alahum athanun la yasmaaoona biha olaika kaalanaami bal hum adallu olaika humu alghafiloona

Waallatheena kaththaboo biayatina sanastadrijuhum min haythu la yaalamoona
Waomlee lahum inna kaydee mateenun
Awalam yatafakkaroo ma bisahibihim min jinnatin in huwa illa natheerun mubeenun
Awalam yanthuroo fee malakooti alssamawati waalardi wama khalaqa Allahu min shayin waan aasa an yakoona qadi iqtaraba ajaluhum fabiayyi adeethin baadahu yuminoona
Man yudlili Allahu fala hadiya lahu wayatharuhum fee tughyanihim yaamahoona
