Yasaloonaka aani alssaaati ayyana mursaha qul innama ailmuha ainda rabbee la yujalleeha liwaqtiha illa huwa thaqulat fee alssamawati waalardi la tateekum illa baghtatan yasaloonaka kaannaka hafiyyun aanha qul innama ailmuha ainda Allahi walakinna akthara alnnasi la aalamoona
Qul la amliku linafsee nafaan wala darran illa ma shaa Allahu walaw kuntu aalamu alghayba laistakthartu mina alkhayri wama massaniya lssooo in ana illa natheerun wabasheerun liqawmin yuminoona
Huwa allathee khalaqakum min nafsin wahidatin wajaaala minha zawjaha liyaskuna ilayha falamma taghashshaha hamalat hamlan khafeefan amarrat bihi falamma athqalat daaawa Allaha rabbahuma lain ataytana salihan lanakoonanna mina alshshakireena
Falamma atahuma salihan jaaala lahu shurakaa feema atahuma fataaala Allahu aamma yushrikoona
Ayushrikoona ma la yakhluqu shayan wahum yukhlaqoona
Wala yastateeaoona lahum nasran wala anfusahum yansuroona
Wain tadaoohum ila alhuda la yattabiaookum sawaon aalaykum adaaawtumoohum am antum samitoona
Inna allatheena tadaoona min dooni Allahi aibadun amthalukum faodaoohum falyastajeeboo lakum in kuntum sadiqeena
Alahum arjulun yamshoona biha am lahum aydin yabtishoona biha am lahum aayunun yubsiroona biha am lahum athanun yasmaaoona biha quli daoo shurakaakum thumma keedooni fala tunthirooni
Inna waliyyiya Allahu allathee nazzala alkitaba wahuwa yatawalla alssaliheena
Waallatheena tadaoona min doonihi la yastateeaoona nasrakum wala anfusahum yansuroona
Wain tadaoohum ila alhuda la yasmaaoo watarahum yanthuroona ilayka wahum la yubsiroona
Khuthi alaafwa wamur bialaurfi waaarid aani aljahileena
Waimma yanzaghannaka mina alshshaytani nazghun faistaaith biAllahi innahu sameeaun aaleemun
Inna allatheena ittaqaw itha massahum taifun mina alshshaytani tathakkaroo faitha hum mubsiroona
Waikhwanuhum yamuddoonahum fee alghayyi thumma la yuqsiroona
Waitha lam tatihim biayatin qaloo lawla ijtabaytaha qul innama attabiau ma yooha ilayya min rabbee hatha basairu min rabbikum wahudan arahmatun liqawmin yuminoona
Waitha quria alquranu faistamiaoo lahu waansitoo laaallakum turhamoona
Waothkur rabbaka fee nafsika tadarruaan wakheefatan wadoona aljahri mina alqawli bialghuduwwi waalasali wala takun mina alghafileena
Inna allatheena ainda rabbika la yastakbiroona aan aibadatihi wayusabbihoonahu walahu yasjudoona
Yasaloonaka aani alanfali quli alanfalu lillahi waalrrasooli faittaqoo Allaha waaslihoo thata baynikum waateeaoo Allaha warasoolahu in untum mumineena
Innama almuminoona allatheena itha thukira Allahu wajilat quloobuhum waitha tuliyat aalayhim ayatuhu zadathum eemanan waaala rabbihim atawakkaloona
Allatheena yuqeemoona alssalata wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona
Olaika humu almuminoona haqqan lahum darajatun ainda rabbihim wamaghfiratun warizqun kareemun
Kama akhrajaka rabbuka min baytika bialhaqqi wainna fareeqan mina almumineena lakarihoona
Yujadiloonaka fee alhaqqi baadama tabayyana kaannama yusaqoona ila almawti wahum yanthuroona
Waith yaaidukumu Allahu ihda alttaifatayni annaha lakum watawaddoona anna ghayra thati alshshawkati takoonu lakum wayureedu Allahu an uhiqqa alhaqqa bikalimatihi wayaqtaaa dabira alkafireena
Liyuhiqqa alhaqqa wayubtila albatila walaw kariha almujrimoona
Ith tastagheethoona rabbakum faistajaba lakum annee mumiddukum bialfin mina almalaikati murdifeena
Wama jaaalahu Allahu illa bushra walitatmainna bihi quloobukum wama alnnasru illa min aindi Allahi inna Allaha aazeezun hakeemun
Ith yughashsheekumu alnnuaasa amanatan minhu wayunazzilu aalaykum mina alssamai maan liyutahhirakum bihi wayuthhiba aankum rijza lshshaytani waliyarbita aala quloobikum wayuthabbita bihi alaqdama
Ith yoohee rabbuka ila almalaikati annee maaakum fathabbitoo allatheena amanoo saolqee fee quloobi allatheena kafaroo alrruaba aidriboo fawqa alaanaqi waidriboo minhum kulla bananin
Thalika biannahum shaqqoo Allaha warasoolahu waman yushaqiqi Allaha warasoolahu fainna Allaha shadeedu alaiqabi
Thalikum fathooqoohu waanna lilkafireena aathaba alnnari
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha laqeetumu allatheena kafaroo zahfan fala tuwalloohumu aladbara
Waman yuwallihim yawmaithin duburahu illa mutaharrifan liqitalin aw mutahayyizan ila fiatin faqad baa bighadabin mina Allahi wamawahu ahannamu wabisa almaseeru
Falam taqtuloohum walakinna Allaha qatalahum wama ramayta ith ramayta walakinna Allaha rama waliyubliya almumineena minhu balaan asanan inna Allaha sameeaun aaleemun
Thalikum waanna Allaha moohinu kaydi alkafireena
In tastaftihoo faqad jaakumu alfathu wain tantahoo fahuwa khayrun lakum wain taaoodoo naaud walan tughniya aankum fiatukum shayan walaw athurat waanna Allaha maaa almumineena
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ateeaoo Allaha warasoolahu wala tawallaw aanhu waantum tasmaaoona
Wala takoonoo kaallatheena qaloo samiana wahum la yasmaaoona
Inna sharra alddawabbi ainda Allahi alssummu albukmu allatheena la yaaqiloona
Walaw aalima Allahu feehim khayran laasmaaahum walaw asmaaahum latawallaw wahum muaridoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo istajeeboo lillahi walilrrasooli itha daaakum lima yuhyeekum waialamoo anna Allaha yahoolu bayna almari aqalbihi waannahu ilayhi tuhsharoona
Waittaqoo fitnatan la tuseebanna allatheena thalamoo minkum khassatan waialamoo anna Allaha shadeedu alaiqabi
Waothkuroo ith antum qaleelun mustadaafoona fee alardi takhafoona an yatakhattafakumu alnnasu faawakum waayyadakum binasrihi arazaqakum mina alttayyibati laaallakum tashkuroona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la takhoonoo Allaha waalrrasoola watakhoonoo amanatikum waantum taalamoona
Waialamoo annama amwalukum waawladukum fitnatun waanna Allaha aindahu ajrun aatheemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in tattaqoo Allaha yajaal lakum furqanan wayukaffir aankum sayyiatikum wayaghfir lakum waAllahu thoo lfadli alaatheemi
Waith yamkuru bika allatheena kafaroo liyuthbitooka aw yaqtulooka aw yukhrijooka wayamkuroona wayamkuru Allahu waAllahu khayru lmakireena
Waitha tutla aalayhim ayatuna qaloo qad samiana law nashao laqulna mithla hatha in hatha illa asateeru alawwaleena
Waith qaloo allahumma in kana hatha huwa alhaqqa min aindika faamtir aalayna hijaratan mina alssamai awi itina biaathabin aleemin
Wama kana Allahu liyuaaththibahum waanta feehim wama kana Allahu muaaththibahum wahum yastaghfiroona
Wama lahum alla yuaaththibahumu Allahu wahum yasuddoona aani almasjidi alharami wama kanoo awliyaahu in awliyaohu illa almuttaqoona alakinna aktharahum la yaalamoona
Wama kana salatuhum ainda albayti illa mukaan watasdiyatan fathooqoo alaathaba bima kuntum takfuroona
Inna allatheena kafaroo yunfiqoona amwalahum liyasuddoo aan sabeeli Allahi fasayunfiqoonaha thumma takoonu aalayhim hasratan thumma ughlaboona waallatheena kafaroo ila jahannama yuhsharoona
Liyameeza Allahu alkhabeetha mina alttayyibi wayajaala alkhabeetha baadahu aala baadin fayarkumahu jameeaan fayajaalahu fee jahannama laika humu alkhasiroona
Qul lillatheena kafaroo in yantahoo yughfar lahum ma qad salafa wain yaaoodoo faqad madat sunnatu alawwaleena
Waqatiloohum hatta la takoona fitnatun wayakoona alddeenu kulluhu lillahi faini intahaw fainna Allaha bima yaamaloona baseerun
Wain tawallaw faialamoo anna Allaha mawlakum niama almawla waniama alnnaseeru
Waialamoo annama ghanimtum min shayin faanna lillahi khumusahu walilrrasooli walithee alqurba waalyatama waalmasakeeni waibni alssabeeli in kuntum amantum biAllahi wama anzalna aala aabdina yawma alfurqani yawma iltaqa aljamaani waAllahu aala kulli shayin adeerun
Ith antum bialaudwati alddunya wahum bialaudwati alquswa waalrrakbu asfala minkum walaw tawaaadtum laikhtalaftum fee almeeaadi walakin liyaqdiya Allahu amran kana mafaoolan liyahlika man halaka aan bayyinatin wayahya man hayya aan bayyinatin wainna Allaha lasameeaun aleemun
Ith yureekahumu Allahu fee manamika qaleelan walaw arakahum katheeran lafashiltum walatanazaatum fee alamri walakinna Allaha sallama nnahu aaleemun bithati alssudoori
Waith yureekumoohum ithi iltaqaytum fee aayunikum qaleelan wayuqallilukum fee aayunihim liyaqdiya Allahu amran kana mafaoolan waila llahi turjaau alomooru
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha laqeetum fiatan faothbutoo waothkuroo Allaha katheeran laaallakum tuflihoona
Waateeaoo Allaha warasoolahu wala tanazaaoo fatafshaloo watathhaba reehukum waisbiroo inna Allaha maaa alssabireena
Wala takoonoo kaallatheena kharajoo min diyarihim bataran wariaa alnnasi wayasuddoona aan sabeeli Allahi waAllahu bima yaamaloona uheetun
Waith zayyana lahumu alshshaytanu aamalahum waqala la ghaliba lakumu alyawma mina alnnasi wainnee jarun lakum falamma taraati alfiatani akasa aala aaqibayhi waqala innee bareeon minkum innee ara ma la tarawna innee akhafu Allaha waAllahu shadeedu alaiqabi
Ith yaqoolu almunafiqoona waallatheena fee quloobihim maradun gharra haolai deenuhum waman yatawakkal aala Allahi fainna Allaha azeezun hakeemun
Walaw tara ith yatawaffa allatheena kafaroo almalaikatu yadriboona wujoohahum waadbarahum wathooqoo aathaba alhareeqi
Thalika bima qaddamat aydeekum waanna Allaha laysa bithallamin lilaabeedi
Kadabi ali firaawna waallatheena min qablihim kafaroo biayati Allahi faakhathahumu Allahu bithunoobihim inna Allaha qawiyyun shadeedu laiqabi
Thalika bianna Allaha lam yaku mughayyiran niamatan anaamaha aala qawmin hatta yughayyiroo ma bianfusihim waanna Allaha sameeaun aleemun
Kadabi ali firaawna waallatheena min qablihim kaththaboo biayati rabbihim faahlaknahum bithunoobihim waaghraqna ala firaawna wakullun anoo thalimeena
Inna sharra alddawabbi ainda Allahi allatheena kafaroo fahum la yuminoona
Allatheena aahadta minhum thumma yanqudoona aahdahum fee kulli marratin wahum la yattaqoona
Faimma tathqafannahum fee alharbi fasharrid bihim man khalfahum laaallahum yaththakkaroona
Waimma takhafanna min qawmin khiyanatan fainbith ilayhim aala sawain inna Allaha la yuhibbu alkhaineena
Wala yahsabanna allatheena kafaroo sabaqoo innahum la yuajizoona
Waaaiddoo lahum ma istataatum min quwwatin wamin ribati alkhayli turhiboona bihi aaduwwa Allahi waaaduwwakum waakhareena min doonihim a taalamoonahumu Allahu yaalamuhum wama tunfiqoo min shayin fee sabeeli Allahi yuwaffa ilaykum waantum la tuthlamoona
Wain janahoo lilssalmi faijnah laha watawakkal aala Allahi innahu huwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Wain yureedoo an yakhdaaooka fainna hasbaka Allahu huwa allathee ayyadaka binasrihi wabialmumineena
Waallafa bayna quloobihim law anfaqta ma fee alardi jameeaan ma allafta bayna quloobihim walakinna Allaha allafa baynahum innahu azeezun hakeemun
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu hasbuka Allahu wamani ittabaaaka mina almumineena
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu harridi almumineena aala alqitali in yakun minkum aishroona sabiroona yaghliboo miatayni wain yakun minkum miatun aghliboo alfan mina allatheena kafaroo biannahum qawmun la yafqahoona
Alana khaffafa Allahu aankum waaalima anna feekum daafan fain yakun minkum miatun sabiratun yaghliboo miatayni wain yakun minkum alfun aghliboo alfayni biithni Allahi waAllahu maaa alssabireena
Ma kana linabiyyin an yakoona lahu asra hatta yuthkhina fee alardi tureedoona aarada alddunya waAllahu yureedu alakhirata waAllahu azeezun hakeemun
Lawla kitabun mina Allahi sabaqa lamassakum feema akhathtum aathabun aatheemun
Fakuloo mimma ghanimtum halalan tayyiban waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu qul liman fee aydeekum mina alasra in yaalami Allahu fee quloobikum khayran yutikum khayran mimma okhitha minkum ayaghfir lakum waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Wain yureedoo khiyanataka faqad khanoo Allaha min qablu faamkana minhum waAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Inna allatheena amanoo wahajaroo wajahadoo biamwalihim waanfusihim fee sabeeli Allahi waallatheena awaw wanasaroo olaika baaduhum awliyao baadin waallatheena amanoo walam yuhajiroo ma lakum min walayatihim min shayin hatta yuhajiroo waini istansarookum fee alddeeni aaalaykumu alnnasru illa aala qawmin baynakum wabaynahum meethaqun waAllahu bima taamaloona baseerun
Waallatheena kafaroo baaduhum awliyao baadin illa tafaaloohu takun fitnatun fee alardi wafasadun kabeerun
Waallatheena amanoo wahajaroo wajahadoo fee sabeeli Allahi waallatheena awaw wanasaroo olaika humu almuminoona haqqan lahum maghfiratun arizqun kareemun
Waallatheena amanoo min baadu wahajaroo wajahadoo maaakum faolaika minkum waoloo alarhami baaduhum awla bibaadin fee kitabi Allahi inna llaha bikulli shayin aaleemun
Baraatun mina Allahi warasoolihi ila allatheena aahadtum mina almushrikeena
Faseehoo fee alardi arbaaata ashhurin waialamoo annakum ghayru muajizee Allahi waanna Allaha mukhzee alkafireena
Waathanun mina Allahi warasoolihi ila alnnasi yawma alhajji alakbari anna Allaha bareeon mina almushrikeena warasooluhu fain tubtum ahuwa khayrun lakum wain tawallaytum faialamoo annakum ghayru muajizee Allahi wabashshiri allatheena kafaroo biaathabin aleemin
Illa allatheena aahadtum mina almushrikeena thumma lam yanqusookum shayan walam yuthahiroo aalaykum ahadan faatimmoo ilayhim aahdahum la muddatihim inna Allaha yuhibbu almuttaqeena
Faitha insalakha alashhuru alhurumu faoqtuloo almushrikeena haythu wajadtumoohum wakhuthoohum waohsuroohum waoqaudoo lahum kulla arsadin fain taboo waaqamoo alssalata waatawoo alzzakata fakhalloo sabeelahum inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Wain ahadun mina almushrikeena istajaraka faajirhu hatta yasmaaa kalama Allahi thumma ablighhu mamanahu thalika biannahum qawmun la aalamoona
Kayfa yakoonu lilmushrikeena aahdun ainda Allahi waainda rasoolihi illa allatheena aahadtum ainda almasjidi alharami fama istaqamoo akum faistaqeemoo lahum inna Allaha yuhibbu almuttaqeena
Kayfa wain yathharoo aalaykum la yarquboo feekum illan wala thimmatan yurdoonakum biafwahihim wataba quloobuhum waaktharuhum fasiqoona
Ishtaraw biayati Allahi thamanan qaleelan fasaddoo aan sabeelihi innahum saa ma kanoo yaamaloona
La yarquboona fee muminin illan wala thimmatan waolaika humu almuatadoona
Fain taboo waaqamoo alssalata waatawoo alzzakata faikhwanukum fee alddeeni wanufassilu alayati liqawmin yaalamoona
Wain nakathoo aymanahum min baadi aahdihim wataaanoo fee deenikum faqatiloo aimmata alkufri innahum la aymana lahum laaallahum antahoona
Ala tuqatiloona qawman nakathoo aymanahum wahammoo biikhraji alrrasooli wahum badaookum awwala marratin atakhshawnahum faAllahu ahaqqu n takhshawhu in kuntum mumineena
Qatiloohum yuaaththibhumu Allahu biaydeekum wayukhzihim wayansurkum aalayhim wayashfi sudoora qawmin mumineena
Wayuthhib ghaytha quloobihim wayatoobu Allahu aala man yashao waAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Am hasibtum an tutrakoo walamma yaalami Allahu allatheena jahadoo minkum walam yattakhithoo min dooni Allahi wala rasoolihi wala lmumineena waleejatan waAllahu khabeerun bima taamaloona
Ma kana lilmushrikeena an yaamuroo masajida Allahi shahideena aala anfusihim bialkufri olaika habitat aamaluhum wafee alnnari hum halidoona
Innama yaamuru masajida Allahi man amana biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri waaqama alssalata waata alzzakata walam yakhsha illa Allaha faaasa laika an yakoonoo mina almuhtadeena
Ajaaaltum siqayata alhajji waaimarata almasjidi alharami kaman amana biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri wajahada fee sabeeli Allahi la astawoona ainda Allahi waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alththalimeena
Allatheena amanoo wahajaroo wajahadoo fee sabeeli Allahi biamwalihim waanfusihim aathamu darajatan ainda Allahi waolaika humu alfaizoona
Yubashshiruhum rabbuhum birahmatin minhu waridwanin wajannatin lahum feeha naaeemun muqeemun
Khalideena feeha abadan inna Allaha aindahu ajrun aatheemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo abaakum waikhwanakum awliyaa ini istahabboo alkufra aala aleemani waman yatawallahum minkum aolaika humu alththalimoona
Qul in kana abaokum waabnaokum waikhwanukum waazwajukum waaasheeratukum waamwalun iqtaraftumooha watijaratun takhshawna kasadaha wamasakinu tardawnaha ahabba ilaykum mina Allahi warasoolihi wajihadin fee sabeelihi fatarabbasoo hatta yatiya Allahu biamrihi waAllahu a yahdee alqawma alfasiqeena
Laqad nasarakumu Allahu fee mawatina katheeratin wayawma hunaynin ith aajabatkum kathratukum falam tughni aankum shayan wadaqat alaykumu alardu bima rahubat thumma wallaytum mudbireena
Thumma anzala Allahu sakeenatahu aala rasoolihi waaala almumineena waanzala junoodan lam tarawha waaaththaba allatheena kafaroo athalika jazao alkafireena
Thumma yatoobu Allahu min baadi thalika aala man yashao waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo innama almushrikoona najasun fala yaqraboo almasjida alharama baada aamihim hatha wain khiftum aaylatan asawfa yughneekumu Allahu min fadlihi in shaa inna Allaha aaleemun hakeemun
Qatiloo allatheena la yuminoona biAllahi wala bialyawmi alakhiri wala yuharrimoona ma harrama Allahu warasooluhu wala yadeenoona deena lhaqqi mina allatheena ootoo alkitaba hatta yuatoo aljizyata aan yadin wahum saghiroona
Waqalati alyahoodu auzayrun ibnu Allahi waqalati alnnasara almaseehu ibnu Allahi thalika qawluhum biafwahihim yudahioona qawla llatheena kafaroo min qablu qatalahumu Allahu anna yufakoona
Ittakhathoo ahbarahum waruhbanahum arbaban min dooni Allahi waalmaseeha ibna maryama wama omiroo illa liyaabudoo ilahan wahidan la laha illa huwa subhanahu aamma yushrikoona
Yureedoona an yutfioo noora Allahi biafwahihim wayaba Allahu illa an yutimma noorahu walaw kariha alkafiroona
Huwa allathee arsala rasoolahu bialhuda wadeeni alhaqqi liyuthhirahu aala alddeeni kullihi walaw kariha almushrikoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo inna katheeran mina alahbari waalrruhbani layakuloona amwala alnnasi bialbatili wayasuddoona aan sabeeli llahi waallatheena yaknizoona alththahaba waalfiddata wala yunfiqoonaha fee sabeeli Allahi fabashshirhum biaathabin aleemin
Yawma yuhma aalayha fee nari jahannama fatukwa biha jibahuhum wajunoobuhum wathuhooruhum hatha ma kanaztum lianfusikum fathooqoo ma untum taknizoona
Inna aiddata alshshuhoori ainda Allahi ithna aashara shahran fee kitabi Allahi yawma khalaqa alssamawati waalarda minha arbaaatun hurumun thalika alddeenu alqayyimu fala tathlimoo feehinna anfusakum waqatiloo almushrikeena kaffatan kama yuqatiloonakum kaffatan aialamoo anna Allaha maaa almuttaqeena
Innama alnnaseeo ziyadatun fee alkufri yudallu bihi allatheena kafaroo yuhilloonahu aaman wayuharrimoonahu aaman liyuwatioo aiddata ma arrama Allahu fayuhilloo ma harrama Allahu zuyyina lahum sooo aamalihim waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alkafireena
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ma lakum itha qeela lakumu infiroo fee sabeeli Allahi iththaqaltum ila alardi aradeetum bialhayati alddunya ina alakhirati fama mataau alhayati alddunya fee alakhirati illa qaleelun
Illa tanfiroo yuaaththibkum aathaban aleeman wayastabdil qawman ghayrakum wala tadurroohu shayan waAllahu aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Illa tansuroohu faqad nasarahu Allahu ith akhrajahu allatheena kafaroo thaniya ithnayni ith huma fee alghari ith yaqoolu lisahibihi la tahzan inna Allaha maaana faanzala Allahu sakeenatahu aalayhi waayyadahu bijunoodin lam tarawha wajaaala kalimata allatheena kafaroo lssufla wakalimatu Allahi hiya alaulya waAllahu aazeezun hakeemun
Infiroo khifafan wathiqalan wajahidoo biamwalikum waanfusikum fee sabeeli Allahi thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum taalamoona
Law kana aaradan qareeban wasafaran qasidan laittabaaooka walakin baaudat aalayhimu alshshuqqatu wasayahlifoona biAllahi lawi istataana akharajna maaakum yuhlikoona anfusahum waAllahu yaalamu innahum lakathiboona
aafa Allahu aanka lima athinta lahum hatta yatabayyana laka allatheena sadaqoo wataalama alkathibeena
La yastathinuka allatheena yuminoona biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri an yujahidoo biamwalihim waanfusihim waAllahu aaleemun bialmuttaqeena
Innama yastathinuka allatheena la yuminoona biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri wairtabat quloobuhum fahum fee raybihim yataraddadoona
Walaw aradoo alkhurooja laaaaddoo lahu auddatan walakin kariha Allahu inbiaathahum fathabbatahum waqeela oqaudoo maaa alqaaideena
Law kharajoo feekum ma zadookum illa khabalan walaawdaaoo khilalakum yabghoonakumu alfitnata wafeekum sammaaoona lahum waAllahu aleemun bialththalimeena
Laqadi ibtaghawoo alfitnata min qablu waqallaboo laka alomoora hatta jaa alhaqqu wathahara amru Allahi wahum karihoona
Waminhum man yaqoolu ithan lee wala taftinnee ala fee alfitnati saqatoo wainna jahannama lamuheetatun bialkafireena
In tusibka hasanatun tasuhum wain tusibka museebatun yaqooloo qad akhathna amrana min qablu wayatawallaw wahum farihoona
Qul lan yuseebana illa ma kataba Allahu lana huwa mawlana waaala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoona
Qul hal tarabbasoona bina illa ihda alhusnayayni wanahnu natarabbasu bikum an yuseebakumu Allahu biaathabin min aindihi aw biaydeena atarabbasoo inna maaakum mutarabbisoona
Qul anfiqoo tawaan aw karhan lan yutaqabbala minkum innakum kuntum qawman fasiqeena
Wama manaaahum an tuqbala minhum nafaqatuhum illa annahum kafaroo biAllahi wabirasoolihi wala yatoona alssalata illa wahum kusala wala unfiqoona illa wahum karihoona
Fala tuajibka amwaluhum wala awladuhum innama yureedu Allahu liyuaaththibahum biha fee alhayati alddunya watazhaqa anfusuhum wahum afiroona
Wayahlifoona biAllahi innahum laminkum wama hum minkum walakinnahum qawmun yafraqoona
Law yajidoona maljaan aw magharatin aw muddakhalan lawallaw ilayhi wahum yajmahoona
Waminhum man yalmizuka fee alssadaqati fain oatoo minha radoo wain lam yuataw minha itha hum yaskhatoona
Walaw annahum radoo ma atahumu Allahu warasooluhu waqaloo hasbuna Allahu sayuteena Allahu min fadlihi warasooluhu inna ila Allahi aghiboona
Innama alssadaqatu lilfuqarai waalmasakeeni waalaamileena aalayha waalmuallafati quloobuhum wafee alrriqabi waalgharimeena wafee abeeli Allahi waibni alssabeeli fareedatan mina Allahi waAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Waminhumu allatheena yuthoona alnnabiyya wayaqooloona huwa othunun qul othunu khayrin lakum yuminu biAllahi wayuminu lilmumineena arahmatun lillatheena amanoo minkum waallatheena yuthoona rasoola Allahi lahum aathabun aleemun
Yahlifoona biAllahi lakum liyurdookum waAllahu warasooluhu ahaqqu an yurdoohu in kanoo mumineena
Alam yaalamoo annahu man yuhadidi Allaha warasoolahu faanna lahu nara jahannama khalidan feeha thalika alkhizyu alaatheemu
Yahtharu almunafiqoona an tunazzala aalayhim sooratun tunabbiohum bima fee quloobihim quli istahzioo inna Allaha mukhrijun ma ahtharoona
Walain saaltahum layaqoolunna innama kunna nakhoodu wanalaabu qul abiAllahi waayatihi warasoolihi kuntum tastahzioona
La taatathiroo qad kafartum baada eemanikum in naafu aan taifatin minkum nuaaththib taifatan biannahum kanoo mujrimeena
Almunafiqoona waalmunafiqatu baaduhum min baadin yamuroona bialmunkari wayanhawna aani almaaroofi wayaqbidoona aydiyahum nasoo Allaha anasiyahum inna almunafiqeena humu alfasiqoona
Waaada Allahu almunafiqeena waalmunafiqati waalkuffara nara jahannama khalideena feeha hiya hasbuhum walaaanahumu Allahu walahum athabun muqeemun
Kaallatheena min qablikum kanoo ashadda minkum quwwatan waakthara amwalan waawladan faistamtaaoo bikhalaqihim faistamtaatum bikhalaqikum kama istamtaaa allatheena min qablikum bikhalaqihim wakhudtum kaallathee khadoo olaika habitat aamaluhum fee alddunya aalakhirati waolaika humu alkhasiroona
Alam yatihim nabao allatheena min qablihim qawmi noohin waaadin wathamooda waqawmi ibraheema waashabi madyana waalmutafikati atathum usuluhum bialbayyinati fama kana Allahu liyathlimahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona
Waalmuminoona waalmuminatu baaduhum awliyao baadin yamuroona bialmaaroofi wayanhawna aani almunkari wayuqeemoona alssalata wayutoona lzzakata wayuteeaoona Allaha warasoolahu olaika sayarhamuhumu Allahu inna Allaha aazeezun hakeemun
Waaada Allahu almumineena waalmuminati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wamasakina tayyibatan fee jannati aadnin aridwanun mina Allahi akbaru thalika huwa alfawzu alaatheemu
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu jahidi alkuffara waalmunafiqeena waoghluth aalayhim wamawahum jahannamu wabisa almaseeru
Yahlifoona biAllahi ma qaloo walaqad qaloo kalimata alkufri wakafaroo baada islamihim wahammoo bima lam yanaloo wama naqamoo illa an aghnahumu Allahu warasooluhu min fadlihi fain yatooboo yaku khayran lahum wain yatawallaw yuaaththibhumu Allahu aathaban aleeman fee lddunya waalakhirati wama lahum fee alardi min waliyyin wala naseerin
Waminhum man aahada Allaha lain atana min fadlihi lanassaddaqanna walanakoonanna mina alssaliheena
Falamma atahum min fadlihi bakhiloo bihi watawallaw wahum muaridoona
Faaaqabahum nifaqan fee quloobihim ila yawmi yalqawnahu bima akhlafoo Allaha ma waaadoohu wabima kanoo yakthiboona
Alam yaalamoo anna Allaha yaalamu sirrahum wanajwahum waanna Allaha aallamu alghuyoobi
Allatheena yalmizoona almuttawwiaeena mina almumineena fee alssadaqati waallatheena la yajidoona illa juhdahum fayaskharoona minhum akhira Allahu minhum walahum aathabun aleemun
Istaghfir lahum aw la tastaghfir lahum in tastaghfir lahum sabaeena marratan falan yaghfira Allahu lahum thalika biannahum kafaroo iAllahi warasoolihi waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeena
Fariha almukhallafoona bimaqaadihim khilafa rasooli Allahi wakarihoo an yujahidoo biamwalihim waanfusihim fee sabeeli Allahi waqaloo la anfiroo fee alharri qul naru jahannama ashaddu harran law kanoo yafqahoona
Falyadhakoo qaleelan walyabkoo katheeran jazaan bima kanoo yaksiboona
Fain rajaaaka Allahu ila taifatin minhum faistathanooka lilkhurooji faqul lan takhrujoo maaiya abadan walan tuqatiloo maaiya aaduwwan nnakum radeetum bialquaoodi awwala marratin faoqaudoo maaa alkhalifeena
Wala tusalli aala ahadin minhum mata abadan wala taqum aala qabrihi innahum kafaroo biAllahi warasoolihi wamatoo wahum fasiqoona
Wala tuajibka amwaluhum waawladuhum innama yureedu Allahu an yuaaththibahum biha fee alddunya watazhaqa anfusuhum wahum kafiroona
Waitha onzilat sooratun an aminoo biAllahi wajahidoo maaa rasoolihi istathanaka oloo alttawli minhum waqaloo tharna nakun maaa lqaaideena
Radoo bian yakoonoo maaa alkhawalifi watubiaa aala quloobihim fahum la yafqahoona
Lakini alrrasoolu waallatheena amanoo maaahu jahadoo biamwalihim waanfusihim waolaika lahumu alkhayratu waolaika humu almuflihoona
aaadda Allahu lahum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha thalika alfawzu alaatheemu
Wajaa almuaaththiroona mina alaarabi liyuthana lahum waqaaada allatheena kathaboo Allaha warasoolahu sayuseebu allatheena kafaroo inhum aathabun aleemun
Laysa aala aldduaafai wala aala almarda wala aala allatheena la yajidoona ma yunfiqoona harajun itha nasahoo lillahi warasoolihi ma ala almuhsineena min sabeelin waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Wala aala allatheena itha ma atawka litahmilahum qulta la ajidu ma ahmilukum aalayhi tawallaw waaayunuhum tafeedu mina alddamai hazanan lla yajidoo ma yunfiqoona
Innama alssabeelu aala allatheena yastathinoonaka wahum aghniyao radoo bian yakoonoo maaa alkhawalifi watabaaa Allahu aala quloobihim ahum la yaalamoona
Yaatathiroona ilaykum itha rajaatum ilayhim qul la taatathiroo lan numina lakum qad nabbaana Allahu min akhbarikum wasayara Allahu amalakum warasooluhu thumma turaddoona ila aalimi alghaybi waalshshahadati fayunabbiokum bima kuntum taamaloona
Sayahlifoona biAllahi lakum itha inqalabtum ilayhim lituaridoo aanhum faaaridoo aanhum innahum rijsun wamawahum jahannamu jazaan bima anoo yaksiboona
Yahlifoona lakum litardaw aanhum fain tardaw aanhum fainna Allaha la yarda aani alqawmi alfasiqeena
Alaarabu ashaddu kufran wanifaqan waajdaru alla yaalamoo hudooda ma anzala Allahu aala rasoolihi waAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Wamina alaarabi man yattakhithu ma yunfiqu maghraman wayatarabbasu bikumu alddawaira aalayhim dairatu alssawi waAllahu sameeaun aaleemun
Wamina alaarabi man yuminu biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri wayattakhithu ma yunfiqu qurubatin ainda Allahi wasalawati alrrasooli ala innaha urbatun lahum sayudkhiluhumu Allahu fee rahmatihi inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Waalssabiqoona alawwaloona mina almuhajireena waalansari waallatheena ittabaaoohum biihsanin radiya Allahu aanhum waradoo aanhu aaaadda lahum jannatin tajree tahtaha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan thalika alfawzu alaatheemu
Wamimman hawlakum mina alaarabi munafiqoona wamin ahli almadeenati maradoo aala alnnifaqi la taalamuhum nahnu naalamuhum anuaaththibuhum marratayni thumma yuraddoona ila aathabin aatheemin
Waakharoona iatarafoo bithunoobihim khalatoo aamalan salihan waakhara sayyian aasa Allahu an yatooba aalayhim inna Allaha ghafoorun aheemun
Khuth min amwalihim sadaqatan tutahhiruhum watuzakkeehim biha wasalli aalayhim inna salataka sakanun lahum waAllahu sameeaun aaleemun
Alam yaalamoo anna Allaha huwa yaqbalu alttawbata aan aibadihi wayakhuthu alssadaqati waanna Allaha huwa alttawwabu alrraheemu
Waquli iamaloo fasayara Allahu aamalakum warasooluhu waalmuminoona wasaturaddoona ila aalimi alghaybi waalshshahadati fayunabbiokum ima kuntum taamaloona
Waakharoona murjawna liamri Allahi imma yuaaththibuhum waimma yatoobu aalayhim waAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Waallatheena ittakhathoo masjidan diraran wakufran watafreeqan bayna almumineena wairsadan liman haraba Allaha warasoolahu min qablu alayahlifunna in aradna illa alhusna waAllahu yashhadu innahum lakathiboona
La taqum feehi abadan lamasjidun ossisa aala alttaqwa min awwali yawmin ahaqqu an taqooma feehi feehi rijalun yuhibboona an atatahharoo waAllahu yuhibbu almuttahhireena
Afaman assasa bunyanahu aala taqwa mina Allahi waridwanin khayrun am man assasa bunyanahu aala shafa jurufin harin fainhara bihi fee ari jahannama waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alththalimeena
La yazalu bunyanuhumu allathee banaw reebatan fee quloobihim illa an taqattaaa quloobuhum waAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Inna Allaha ishtara mina almumineena anfusahum waamwalahum bianna lahumu aljannata yuqatiloona fee sabeeli Allahi fayaqtuloona wayuqtaloona waadan aalayhi haqqan fee alttawrati waalinjeeli waalqurani waman awfa biaahdihi mina Allahi faistabshiroo bibayaikumu llathee bayaatum bihi wathalika huwa alfawzu alaatheemu
Alttaiboona alaabidoona alhamidoona alssaihoona alrrakiaoona alssajidoona alamiroona bialmaaroofi waalnnahoona aani almunkari aalhafithoona lihudoodi Allahi wabashshiri almumineena
Ma kana lilnnabiyyi waallatheena amanoo an yastaghfiroo lilmushrikeena walaw kanoo olee qurba min baadi ma tabayyana lahum annahum shabu aljaheemi
Wama kana istighfaru ibraheema liabeehi illa aan mawaidatin waaadaha iyyahu falamma tabayyana lahu annahu aaduwwun lillahi tabarraa inhu inna ibraheema laawwahun haleemun
Wama kana Allahu liyudilla qawman baada ith hadahum hatta yubayyina lahum ma yattaqoona inna Allaha bikulli shayin aaleemun
Inna Allaha lahu mulku alssamawati waalardi yuhyee wayumeetu wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseerin
Laqad taba Allahu aala alnnabiyyi waalmuhajireena waalansari allatheena ittabaaoohu fee saaati alausrati min baadi ma kada yazeeghu uloobu fareeqin minhum thumma taba aalayhim innahu bihim raoofun raheemun
Waaala alththalathati allatheena khullifoo hatta itha daqat aalayhimu alardu bima rahubat wadaqat aalayhim anfusuhum wathannoo an la aljaa mina Allahi illa ilayhi thumma taba aalayhim liyatooboo inna Allaha huwa alttawwabu alrraheemu
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha wakoonoo maaa alssadiqeena
Ma kana liahli almadeenati waman hawlahum mina alaarabi an yatakhallafoo aan rasooli Allahi wala yarghaboo bianfusihim aan nafsihi thalika biannahum la yuseebuhum thamaon wala nasabun wala makhmasatun fee sabeeli Allahi wala yataoona mawtian yagheethu alkuffara wala analoona min aaduwwin naylan illa kutiba lahum bihi aamalun salihun inna Allaha la yudeeau ajra almuhsineena
Wala yunfiqoona nafaqatan sagheeratan wala kabeeratan wala yaqtaaoona wadiyan illa kutiba lahum liyajziyahumu Allahu ahsana ma kanoo aamaloona
Wama kana almuminoona liyanfiroo kaffatan falawla nafara min kulli firqatin minhum taifatun liyatafaqqahoo fee alddeeni waliyunthiroo awmahum itha rajaaoo ilayhim laaallahum yahtharoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo qatiloo allatheena yaloonakum mina alkuffari walyajidoo feekum ghilthatan waialamoo anna Allaha maaa lmuttaqeena
Waitha ma onzilat sooratun faminhum man yaqoolu ayyukum zadathu hathihi eemanan faamma allatheena amanoo fazadathum eemanan wahum astabshiroona
Waamma allatheena fee quloobihim maradun fazadathum rijsan ila rijsihim wamatoo wahum kafiroona
Awala yarawna annahum yuftanoona fee kulli aamin marratan aw marratayni thumma la yatooboona wala hum yaththakkaroona
Waitha ma onzilat sooratun nathara baaduhum ila baadin hal yarakum min ahadin thumma insarafoo sarafa Allahu quloobahum biannahum awmun la yafqahoona
Laqad jaakum rasoolun min anfusikum aazeezun aalayhi ma aanittum hareesun aalaykum bialmumineena raoofun raheemun
Fain tawallaw faqul hasbiya Allahu la ilaha illa huwa aalayhi tawakkaltu wahuwa rabbu alaarshi alaatheemi
Aliflamra tilka ayatu alkitabi alhakeemi
Akana lilnnasi aajaban an awhayna ila rajulin minhum an anthiri alnnasa wabashshiri allatheena amanoo anna lahum qadama sidqin ainda abbihim qala alkafiroona inna hatha lasahirun mubeenun
Inna rabbakumu Allahu allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa aala alaarshi yudabbiru alamra ma min hafeeain illa min baadi ithnihi thalikumu Allahu rabbukum faoabudoohu afala tathakkaroona
Ilayhi marjiaukum jameeaan waada Allahi haqqan innahu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yuaeeduhu liyajziya allatheena amanoo waaamiloo lssalihati bialqisti waallatheena kafaroo lahum sharabun min hameemin waaathabun aleemun bima kanoo yakfuroona
Huwa allathee jaaala alshshamsa diyaan waalqamara nooran waqaddarahu manazila litaalamoo aadada alssineena waalhisaba ma khalaqa Allahu halika illa bialhaqqi yufassilu alayati liqawmin yaalamoona
Inna fee ikhtilafi allayli waalnnahari wama khalaqa Allahu fee alssamawati waalardi laayatin liqawmin yattaqoona
Inna allatheena la yarjoona liqaana waradoo bialhayati alddunya waitmaannoo biha waallatheena hum aan ayatina ghafiloona
Olaika mawahumu alnnaru bima kanoo yaksiboona
Inna allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati yahdeehim rabbuhum bieemanihim tajree min tahtihimu alanharu fee jannati alnnaaeemi
Daawahum feeha subhanaka allahumma watahiyyatuhum feeha salamun waakhiru daawahum ani alhamdu lillahi rabbi alaalameena
Walaw yuaajjilu Allahu lilnnasi alshsharra istiajalahum bialkhayri laqudiya ilayhim ajaluhum fanatharu allatheena la yarjoona liqaana ee tughyanihim yaamahoona
Waitha massa alinsana alddurru daaana lijanbihi aw qaaidan aw qaiman falamma kashafna aanhu durrahu marra kaan lam yadauna ila durrin assahu kathalika zuyyina lilmusrifeena ma kanoo yaamaloona
Walaqad ahlakna alquroona min qablikum lamma thalamoo wajaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati wama kanoo liyuminoo kathalika najzee alqawma lmujrimeena
Thumma jaaalnakum khalaifa fee alardi min baadihim linanthura kayfa taamaloona
Waitha tutla aalayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qala allatheena la yarjoona liqaana iti biquranin ghayri hatha aw baddilhu qul ma yakoonu lee n obaddilahu min tilqai nafsee in attabiau illa ma yooha ilayya innee akhafu in aasaytu rabbee aathaba yawmin aatheemin
Qul law shaa Allahu ma talawtuhu aalaykum wala adrakum bihi faqad labithtu feekum aumuran min qablihi afala taaqiloona
Faman athlamu mimmani iftara aala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba biayatihi innahu la yuflihu almujrimoona
Wayaabudoona min dooni Allahi ma la yadurruhum wala yanfaauhum wayaqooloona haolai shufaaaona ainda Allahi qul atunabbioona Allaha bima a yaalamu fee alssamawati wala fee alardi subhanahu wataaala aamma yushrikoona
Wama kana alnnasu illa ommatan wahidatan faikhtalafoo walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum feema feehi yakhtalifoona
Wayaqooloona lawla onzila aalayhi ayatun min rabbihi faqul innama alghaybu lillahi faintathiroo innee maaakum mina almuntathireena
Waitha athaqna alnnasa rahmatan min baadi darraa massathum itha lahum makrun fee ayatina quli Allahu asraau makran inna rusulana aktuboona ma tamkuroona
Huwa allathee yusayyirukum fee albarri waalbahri hatta itha kuntum fee alfulki wajarayna bihim bireehin tayyibatin wafarihoo biha jaatha reehun aasifun wajaahumu almawju min kulli makanin wathannoo annahum oheeta bihim daaawoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu alddeena lain njaytana min hathihi lanakoonanna mina alshshakireena
Falamma anjahum itha hum yabghoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi ya ayyuha alnnasu innama baghyukum aala anfusikum mataaa alhayati lddunya thumma ilayna marjiaukum fanunabbiokum bima kuntum taamaloona
Innama mathalu alhayati alddunya kamain anzalnahu mina alssamai faikhtalata bihi nabatu alardi mimma yakulu alnnasu waalanaamu hatta itha akhathati alardu zukhrufaha waizzayyanat wathanna ahluha annahum qadiroona aalayha ataha amruna laylan aw naharan fajaaalnaha aseedan kaan lam taghna bialamsi kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin yatafakkaroona
WaAllahu yadaoo ila dari alssalami wayahdee man yashao ila siratin mustaqeemin
Lillatheena ahsanoo alhusna waziyadatun wala yarhaqu wujoohahum qatarun wala thillatun olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoona
Waallatheena kasaboo alssayyiati jazao sayyiatin bimithliha watarhaquhum thillatun ma lahum mina Allahi min aasimin kaannama oghshiyat ujoohuhum qitaaan mina allayli muthliman olaika ashabu alnnari hum feeha khalidoona
Wayawma nahshuruhum jameeaan thumma naqoolu lillatheena ashrakoo makanakum antum washurakaokum fazayyalna baynahum waqala shurakaohum a kuntum iyyana taabudoona
Fakafa biAllahi shaheedan baynana wabaynakum in kunna aan aibadatikum laghafileena
Hunalika tabloo kullu nafsin ma aslafat waruddoo ila Allahi mawlahumu alhaqqi wadalla aanhum ma kanoo yaftaroona
Qul man yarzuqukum mina alssamai waalardi amman yamliku alssamaa waalabsara waman yukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti wayukhriju almayyita ina alhayyi waman yudabbiru alamra fasayaqooloona Allahu faqul afala tattaqoona
Fathalikumu Allahu rabbukumu alhaqqu famatha baada alhaqqi illa alddalalu faanna tusrafoona
Kathalika haqqat kalimatu rabbika aala allatheena fasaqoo annahum la yuminoona
Qul hal min shurakaikum man yabdao alkhalqa thumma yuaeeduhu quli Allahu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yuaeeduhu faanna tufakoona
Qul hal min shurakaikum man yahdee ila alhaqqi quli Allahu yahdee lilhaqqi afaman yahdee ila alhaqqi ahaqqu an yuttabaaa amman la ahiddee illa an yuhda fama lakum kayfa tahkumoona
Wama yattabiau aktharuhum illa thannan inna alththanna la yughnee mina alhaqqi shayan inna Allaha aaleemun bima yafaaloona
Wama kana hatha alquranu an yuftara min dooni Allahi walakin tasdeeqa allathee bayna yadayhi watafseela alkitabi la rayba feehi min abbi alaalameena
Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul fatoo bisooratin mithlihi waodaoo mani istataatum min dooni Allahi in kuntum sadiqeena
Bal kaththaboo bima lam yuheetoo biailmihi walamma yatihim taweeluhu kathalika kaththaba allatheena min qablihim faonthur kayfa kana aqibatu alththalimeena
Waminhum man yuminu bihi waminhum man la yuminu bihi warabbuka aalamu bialmufsideena
Wain kaththabooka faqul lee aamalee walakum aamalukum antum bareeoona mimma aamalu waana bareeon mimma taamaloona
Waminhum man yastamiaoona ilayka afaanta tusmiau alssumma walaw kanoo la yaaqiloona
Waminhum man yanthuru ilayka afaanta tahdee alaumya walaw kanoo la yubsiroona
Inna Allaha la yathlimu alnnasa shayan walakinna alnnasa anfusahum yathlimoona
Wayawma yahshuruhum kaan lam yalbathoo illa saaatan mina alnnahari yataaarafoona baynahum qad khasira allatheena kaththaboo biliqai llahi wama kanoo muhtadeena
Waimma nuriyannaka baada allathee naaiduhum aw natawaffayannaka failayna marjiauhum thumma Allahu shaheedun aala ma yafaaloona
Walikulli ommatin rasoolun faitha jaa rasooluhum qudiya baynahum bialqisti wahum la yuthlamoona
Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwaadu in kuntum sadiqeena
Qul la amliku linafsee darran wala nafaan illa ma shaa Allahu likulli ommatin ajalun itha jaa ajaluhum fala yastakhiroona saaatan wala astaqdimoona
Qul araaytum in atakum aathabuhu bayatan aw naharan matha yastaajilu minhu almujrimoona
Athumma itha ma waqaaa amantum bihi alana waqad kuntum bihi tastaajiloona
Thumma qeela lillatheena thalamoo thooqoo aathaba alkhuldi hal tujzawna illa bima kuntum taksiboona
Wayastanbioonaka ahaqqun huwa qul ee warabbee innahu lahaqqun wama antum bimuajizeena
Walaw anna likulli nafsin thalamat ma fee alardi laiftadat bihi waasarroo alnnadamata lamma raawoo alaathaba waqudiya baynahum ialqisti wahum la yuthlamoona
Ala inna lillahi ma fee alssamawati waalardi ala inna waada Allahi haqqun walakinna aktharahum la yaalamoona
Huwa yuhyee wayumeetu wailayhi turjaaoona
Ya ayyuha alnnasu qad jaatkum mawaithatun min rabbikum washifaon lima fee alssudoori wahudan warahmatun lilmumineena
Qul bifadli Allahi wabirahmatihi fabithalika falyafrahoo huwa khayrun mimma yajmaaoona
Qul araaytum ma anzala Allahu lakum min rizqin fajaaaltum minhu haraman wahalalan qul allahu athina lakum am aala Allahi taftaroona
Wama thannu allatheena yaftaroona aala Allahi alkathiba yawma alqiyamati inna Allaha lathoo fadlin aala alnnasi walakinna aktharahum la ashkuroona
Wama takoonu fee shanin wama tatloo minhu min quranin wala taamaloona min aamalin illa kunna aalaykum shuhoodan ith tufeedoona feehi wama yaazubu aan rabbika min mithqali tharratin fee alardi wala fee alssamai wala asghara min thalika wala akbara illa fee kitabin ubeenun
Ala inna awliyaa Allahi la khawfun aalayhim wala hum yahzanoona
Allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoona
Lahumu albushra fee alhayati alddunya wafee alakhirati la tabdeela likalimati Allahi thalika huwa alfawzu alaatheemu
Wala yahzunka qawluhum inna alaizzata lillahi jameeaan huwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Ala inna lillahi man fee alssamawati waman fee alardi wama yattabiau allatheena yadaoona min dooni Allahi shurakaa in yattabiaoona illa lththanna wain hum illa yakhrusoona
Huwa allathee jaaala lakumu allayla litaskunoo feehi waalnnahara mubsiran inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yasmaaoona
Qaloo ittakhatha Allahu waladan subhanahu huwa alghaniyyu lahu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi in aindakum min sultanin bihatha taqooloona aala Allahi ma la taalamoona
Qul inna allatheena yaftaroona aala Allahi alkathiba la yuflihoona
Mataaun fee alddunya thumma ilayna marjiauhum thumma nutheequhumu alaathaba alshshadeeda bima kanoo yakfuroona
Waotlu aalayhim nabaa noohin ith qala liqawmihi ya qawmi in kana kabura aalaykum maqamee watathkeeree biayati Allahi faaala Allahi awakkaltu faajmiaoo amrakum washurakaakum thumma la yakun amrukum aalaykum ghummatan thumma iqdoo ilayya wala tunthirooni
Fain tawallaytum fama saaltukum min ajrin in ajriya illa aala Allahi waomirtu an akoona mina almuslimeena
Fakaththaboohu fanajjaynahu waman maaahu fee alfulki wajaaalnahum khalaifa waaghraqna allatheena kaththaboo biayatina faonthur kayfa ana aaqibatu almunthareena
Thumma baaathna min baadihi rusulan ila qawmihim fajaoohum bialbayyinati fama kanoo liyuminoo bima kaththaboo bihi min qablu kathalika atbaau aala quloobi almuatadeena
Thumma baaathna min baadihim moosa waharoona ila firaawna wamalaihi biayatina faistakbaroo wakanoo qawman mujrimeena
Falamma jaahumu alhaqqu min aindina qaloo inna hatha lasihrun mubeenun
Qala moosa ataqooloona lilhaqqi lamma jaakum asihrun hatha wala yuflihu alssahiroona
Qaloo ajitana litalfitana aamma wajadna aalayhi abaana watakoona lakuma alkibriyao fee alardi wama nahnu lakuma bimumineena
Waqala firaawnu itoonee bikulli sahirin aaleemin
Falamma jaa alssaharatu qala lahum moosa alqoo ma antum mulqoona
Falamma alqaw qala moosa ma jitum bihi alssihru inna Allaha sayubtiluhu inna Allaha la yuslihu aamala almufsideena
Wayuhiqqu Allahu alhaqqa bikalimatihi walaw kariha almujrimoona
Fama amana limoosa illa thurriyyatun min qawmihi aala khawfin min firaawna wamalaihim an yaftinahum wainna firaawna laaalin fee alardi ainnahu lamina almusrifeena
Waqala moosa ya qawmi in kuntum amantum biAllahi faaalayhi tawakkaloo in kuntum muslimeena
Faqaloo aala Allahi tawakkalna rabbana la tajaalna fitnatan lilqawmi alththalimeena
Wanajjina birahmatika mina alqawmi alkafireena
Waawhayna ila moosa waakheehi an tabawwaa liqawmikuma bimisra buyootan waijaaloo buyootakum qiblatan waaqeemoo alssalata wabashshiri lmumineena
Waqala moosa rabbana innaka atayta firaawna wamalaahu zeenatan waamwalan fee alhayati alddunya rabbana liyudilloo aan sabeelika rabbana tmis aala amwalihim waoshdud aala quloobihim fala yuminoo hatta yarawoo alaathaba alaleema
Qala qad ojeebat daawatukuma faistaqeema wala tattabiaanni sabeela allatheena la yaalamoona
Wajawazna bibanee israeela albahra faatbaaahum firaawnu wajunooduhu baghyan waaadwan hatta itha adrakahu algharaqu qala amantu annahu a ilaha illa allathee amanat bihi banoo israeela waana mina almuslimeena
Alana waqad aasayta qablu wakunta mina almufsideena
Faalyawma nunajjeeka bibadanika litakoona liman khalfaka ayatan wainna katheeran mina alnnasi aan ayatina laghafiloona
Walaqad bawwana banee israeela mubawwaa sidqin warazaqnahum mina alttayyibati fama ikhtalafoo hatta jaahumu alailmu inna rabbaka yaqdee aynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoona
Fain kunta fee shakkin mimma anzalnna ilayka faisali allatheena yaqraoona alkitaba min qablika laqad jaaka alhaqqu min rabbika fala akoonanna mina almumtareena
Wala takoonanna mina allatheena kaththaboo biayati Allahi fatakoona mina alkhasireena
Inna allatheena haqqat aalayhim kalimatu rabbika la yuminoona
Walaw jaathum kullu ayatin hatta yarawoo alaathaba alaleema
Falawla kanat qaryatun amanat fanafaaaha eemanuha illa qawma yoonusa lamma amanoo kashafna aanhum aathaba alkhizyi fee alhayati lddunya wamattaanahum ila heenin
Walaw shaa rabbuka laamana man fee alardi kulluhum jameeaan afaanta tukrihu alnnasa hatta yakoonoo mumineena
Wama kana linafsin an tumina illa biithni Allahi wayajaalu alrrijsa aala allatheena la yaaqiloona
Quli onthuroo matha fee alssamawati waalardi wama tughnee alayatu waalnnuthuru aan qawmin la yuminoona
Fahal yantathiroona illa mithla ayyami allatheena khalaw min qablihim qul faintathiroo innee maaakum mina almuntathireena
Thumma nunajjee rusulana waallatheena amanoo kathalika haqqan aalayna nunjee almumineena
Qul ya ayyuha alnnasu in kuntum fee shakkin min deenee fala aabudu allatheena taabudoona min dooni Allahi walakin aabudu Allaha llathee yatawaffakum waomirtu an akoona mina almumineena
Waan aqim wajhaka lilddeeni haneefan wala takoonanna mina almushrikeena
Wala tadau min dooni Allahi ma la yanfaauka wala yadurruka fain faaalta fainnaka ithan mina alththalimeena
Wain yamsaska Allahu bidurrin fala kashifa lahu illa huwa wain yuridka bikhayrin fala radda lifadlihi yuseebu bihi man yashao min ibadihi wahuwa alghafooru alrraheemu
Qul ya ayyuha alnnasu qad jaakumu alhaqqu min rabbikum famani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu aalayha ama ana aalaykum biwakeelin
Waittabia ma yooha ilayka waisbir hatta yahkuma Allahu wahuwa khayru alhakimeena
Aliflamra kitabun ohkimat ayatuhu thumma fussilat min ladun hakeemin khabeerin
Alla taabudoo illa Allaha innanee lakum minhu natheerun wabasheerun
Waani istaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi yumattiakum mataaan hasanan ila ajalin musamman wayuti kulla thee fadlin fadlahu wain awallaw fainee akhafu aalaykum aathaba yawmin kabeerin
Ila Allahi marjiaukum wahuwa aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Ala innahum yathnoona sudoorahum liyastakhfoo minhu ala heena yastaghshoona thiyabahum yaalamu ma yusirroona wama yualinoona innahu aleemun bithati alssudoori
Wama min dabbatin fee alardi illa aala Allahi rizquha wayaalamu mustaqarraha wamustawdaaaha kullun fee kitabin mubeenin
Wahuwa allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda fee sittati ayyamin wakana aarshuhu aala almai liyabluwakum ayyukum ahsanu aamalan walain ulta innakum mabaoothoona min baadi almawti layaqoolanna allatheena kafaroo in hatha illa sihrun mubeenun
Walain akhkharna aanhumu alaathaba ila ommatin maadoodatin layaqoolunna ma yahbisuhu ala yawma yateehim laysa masroofan aanhum wahaqa ihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Walain athaqna alinsana minna rahmatan thumma nazaanaha minhu innahu layaoosun kafoorun
Walain athaqnahu naamaa baada darraa massathu layaqoolanna thahaba alssayyiatu aannee innahu lafarihun fakhoorun
Illa allatheena sabaroo waaamiloo alssalihati olaika lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeerun
Falaaallaka tarikun baada ma yooha ilayka wadaiqun bihi sadruka an yaqooloo lawla onzila aalayhi kanzun aw jaa maaahu malakun innama nta natheerun waAllahu aala kulli shayin wakeelun
Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul fatoo biaashri suwarin mithlihi muftarayatin waodaoo mani istataatum min dooni Allahi in kuntum sadiqeena
Fai llam yastajeeboo lakum faialamoo annama onzila biailmi Allahi waan la ilaha illa huwa fahal antum muslimoona
Man kana yureedu alhayata alddunya wazeenataha nuwaffi ilayhim aamalahum feeha wahum feeha la yubkhasoona
Olaika allatheena laysa lahum fee alakhirati illa alnnaru wahabita ma sanaaoo feeha wabatilun ma kanoo yaamaloona
Afaman kana aala bayyinatin min rabbihi wayatloohu shahidun minhu wamin qablihi kitabu moosa imaman warahmatan olaika yuminoona bihi waman yakfur bihi mina alahzabi faalnnaru mawaiduhu fala taku fee miryatin minhu innahu alhaqqu min rabbika walakinna akthara alnnasi la uminoona
Waman athlamu mimmani iftara aala Allahi kathiban olaika yuaradoona aala rabbihim wayaqoolu alashhadu haolai allatheena kathaboo aala abbihim ala laanatu Allahi aala alththalimeena
Allatheena yasuddoona aan sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha aiwajan wahum bialakhirati hum kafiroona
Olaika lam yakoonoo muajizeena fee alardi wama kana lahum min dooni Allahi min awliyaa yudaaafu lahumu alaathabu ma kanoo yastateeaoona lssamaa wama kanoo yubsiroona
Olaika allatheena khasiroo anfusahum wadalla aanhum ma kanoo yaftaroona
La jarama annahum fee alakhirati humu alakhsaroona
Inna allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alsalihati waakhbatoo ila rabbihim olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoona
Mathalu alfareeqayni kaalaama waalasammi waalbaseeri waalssameeai hal yastawiyani mathalan afala tathakkaroona
Walaqad arsalna noohan ila qawmihi innee lakum natheerun mubeenun
An la taabudoo illa Allaha innee akhafu aalaykum aathaba yawmin aleemin
Faqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi ma naraka illa basharan mithlana wama naraka ittabaaaka illa allatheena hum arathiluna adiya alrrayi wama nara lakum aalayna min fadlin bal nathunnukum kathibeena
Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu aala bayyinatin min rabbee waatanee rahmatan min aindihi faaummiyat aalaykum anulzimukumooha waantum aha karihoona
Waya qawmi la asalukum aalayhi malan in ajriya illa aala Allahi wama ana bitaridi allatheena amanoo innahum mulaqoo rabbihim walakinnee rakum qawman tajhaloona
Waya qawmi man yansurunee mina Allahi in taradtuhum afala tathakkaroona
Wala aqoolu lakum aindee khazainu Allahi wala aalamu alghayba wala aqoolu innee malakun wala aqoolu lillatheena tazdaree aayunukum lan utiyahumu Allahu khayran Allahu aalamu bima fee anfusihim innee ithan lamina alththalimeena
Qaloo ya noohu qad jadaltana faaktharta jidalana fatina bima taaiduna in kunta mina alssadiqeena
Qala innama yateekum bihi Allahu in shaa wama antum bimuajizeena
Wala yanfaaukum nushee in aradtu an ansaha lakum in kana Allahu yureedu an yughwiyakum huwa rabbukum wailayhi turjaaoona
Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul ini iftaraytuhu faaalayya ijramee waana bareeon mimma tujrimoona
Waoohiya ila noohin annahu lan yumina min qawmika illa man qad amana fala tabtais bima kanoo yafaaloona
Waisnaai alfulka biaayunina wawahyina wala tukhatibnee fee allatheena thalamoo innahum mughraqoona
Wayasnaau alfulka wakullama marra aalayhi malaon min qawmihi sakhiroo minhu qala in taskharoo minna fainna naskharu minkum kama askharoona
Fasawfa taalamoona man yateehi aathabun yukhzeehi wayahillu aalayhi aathabun muqeemun
Hatta itha jaa amruna wafara alttannooru qulna ihmil feeha min kullin zawjayni ithnayni waahlaka illa man sabaqa aalayhi alqawlu waman mana wama amana maaahu illa qaleelun
Waqala irkaboo feeha bismi Allahi majraha wamursaha inna rabbee laghafoorun raheemun
Wahiya tajree bihim fee mawjin kaaljibali wanada noohunu ibnahu wakana fee maazilin ya bunayya irkab maaana wala takun maaa alkafireena
Qala saawee ila jabalin yaasimunee mina almai qala la aasima alyawma min amri Allahi illa man rahima wahala baynahuma almawju fakana ina almughraqeena
Waqeela ya ardu iblaaee maaki waya samao aqliaee wagheeda almao waqudiya alamru waistawat aala aljoodiyyi waqeela buadan lilqawmi lththalimeena
Wanada noohun rabbahu faqala rabbi inna ibnee min ahlee wainna waadaka alhaqqu waanta ahkamu alhakimeena
Qala ya noohu innahu laysa min ahlika innahu aamalun ghayru salihin fala tasalni ma laysa laka bihi ailmun innee aaithuka an takoona ina aljahileena
Qala rabbi innee aaoothu bika an asalaka ma laysa lee bihi ailmun wailla taghfir lee watarhamnee akun mina alkhasireena
Qeela ya noohu ihbit bisalamin minna wabarakatin aalayka waaala omamin mimman maaaka waomamun sanumattiauhum thumma yamassuhum minna athabun aleemun
Tilka min anbai alghaybi nooheeha ilayka ma kunta taalamuha anta wala qawmuka min qabli hatha faisbir inna alaaqibata lilmuttaqeena
Waila aadin akhahum hoodan qala ya qawmi oabudoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu in antum illa muftaroona
Ya qawmi la asalukum aalayhi ajran in ajriya illa aala allathee fataranee afala taaqiloona
Waya qawmi istaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi yursili alssamaa aalaykum midraran wayazidkum quwwatan ila quwwatikum wala atawallaw mujrimeena
Qaloo ya hoodu ma jitana bibayyinatin wama nahnu bitarikee alihatina aan qawlika wama nahnu laka bimumineena
In naqoolu illa iataraka baadu alihatina bisooin qala innee oshhidu Allaha waishhadoo annee bareeon mimma tushrikoona
Min doonihi fakeedoonee jameeaan thumma la tunthirooni
Innee tawakkaltu aala Allahi rabbee warabbikum ma min dabbatin illa huwa akhithun binasiyatiha inna rabbee aala siratin mustaqeemin
Fain tawallaw faqad ablaghtukum ma orsiltu bihi ilaykum wayastakhlifu rabbee qawman ghayrakum wala tadurroonahu shayan inna rabbee aala ulli shayin hafeethun
Walamma jaa amruna najjayna hoodan waallatheena amanoo maaahu birahmatin minna wanajjaynahum min aathabin ghaleethin
Watilka aadun jahadoo biayati rabbihim waaasaw rusulahu waittabaaoo amra kulli jabbarin aaneedin
Waotbiaoo fee hathihi alddunya laanatan wayawma alqiyamati ala inna aadan kafaroo rabbahum ala buadan liaadin qawmi hoodin
Waila thamooda akhahum salihan qala ya qawmi oabudoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu huwa anshaakum mina alardi waistaamarakum eeha faistaghfiroohu thumma tooboo ilayhi inna rabbee qareebun mujeebun
Qaloo ya salihu qad kunta feena marjuwwan qabla hatha atanhana an naabuda ma yaabudu abaona wainnana lafee shakkin mimma tadaoona layhi mureebun
Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu aala bayyinatin min rabbee waatanee minhu rahmatan faman yansurunee mina Allahi in aasaytuhu fama azeedoonanee ghayra takhseerin
Waya qawmi hathihi naqatu Allahi lakum ayatan fatharooha takul fee ardi Allahi wala tamassooha bisooin fayakhuthakum aathabun qareebun
Faaaqarooha faqala tamattaaoo fee darikum thalathata ayyamin thalika waadun ghayru makthoobin
Falamma jaa amruna najjayna salihan waallatheena amanoo maaahu birahmatin minna wamin khizyi yawmiithin inna rabbaka huwa alqawiyyu laazeezu
Waakhatha allatheena thalamoo alssayhatu faasbahoo fee diyarihim jathimeena
Kaan lam yaghnaw feeha ala inna thamooda kafaroo rabbahum ala buadan lithamooda
Walaqad jaat rusuluna ibraheema bialbushra qaloo salaman qala salamun fama labitha an jaa biaijlin haneethin
Falamma raa aydiyahum la tasilu ilayhi nakirahum waawjasa minhum kheefatan qaloo la takhaf inna orsilna ila qawmi lootin
Waimraatuhu qaimatun fadahikat fabashsharnaha biishaqa wamin warai ishaqa yaaqooba
Qalat ya waylata aalidu waana aajoozun wahatha baalee shaykhan inna hatha lashayon aajeebun
Qaloo ataajabeena min amri Allahi rahmatu Allahi wabarakatuhu aalaykum ahla albayti innahu hameedun majeedun
Falamma thahaba aan ibraheema alrrawau wajaathu albushra yujadiluna fee qawmi lootin
Inna ibraheema lahaleemun awwahun muneebun
Ya ibraheemu aarid aan hatha innahu qad jaa amru rabbika wainnahum ateehim aathabun ghayru mardoodin
Walamma jaat rusuluna lootan seea bihim wadaqa bihim tharaan waqala hatha yawmun aaseebun
Wajaahu qawmuhu yuhraaoona ilayhi wamin qablu kanoo yaamaloona alssayyiati qala ya qawmi haolai banatee hunna atharu lakum faittaqoo llaha wala tukhzooni fee dayfee alaysa minkum rajulun rasheedun
Qaloo laqad aalimta ma lana fee banatika min haqqin wainnaka lataalamu ma nureedu
Qala law anna lee bikum quwwatan aw awee ila ruknin shadeedin
Qaloo ya lootu inna rusulu rabbika lan yasiloo ilayka faasri biahlika biqitain mina allayli wala yaltafit minkum ahadun illa imraataka nnahu museebuha ma asabahum inna mawaidahumu alssubhu alaysa alssubhu biqareebin
Falamma jaa amruna jaaalna aaliyaha safilaha waamtarna aalayha hijaratan min sijjeelin mandoodin
Musawwamatan ainda rabbika wama hiya mina alththalimeena bibaaeedin
Waila madyana akhahum shuaayban qala ya qawmi oabudoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu wala tanqusoo almikyala waalmeezana innee rakum bikhayrin wainnee akhafu aalaykum aathaba yawmin muheetin
Waya qawmi awfoo almikyala waalmeezana bialqisti wala tabkhasoo alnnasa ashyaahum wala taathaw fee alardi mufsideena
Baqiyyatu Allahi khayrun lakum in kuntum mumineena wama ana aalaykum bihafeethin
Qaloo ya shuaaybu asalatuka tamuruka an natruka ma yaabudu abaona aw an nafaala fee amwalina ma nashao innaka laanta alhaleemu lrrasheedu
Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu aala bayyinatin min rabbee warazaqanee minhu rizqan hasanan wama oreedu an okhalifakum ila ma anhakum anhu in oreedu illa alislaha ma istataatu wama tawfeeqee illa biAllahi aalayhi tawakkaltu wailayhi oneebu
Waya qawmi la yajrimannakum shiqaqee an yuseebakum mithlu ma asaba qawma noohin aw qawma hoodin aw qawma salihin wama qawmu lootin inkum bibaaeedin
Waistaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi inna rabbee raheemun wadoodun
Qaloo ya shuaaybu ma nafqahu katheeran mimma taqoolu wainna lanaraka feena daaeefan walawla rahtuka larajamnaka wama anta aalayna iaazeezin
Qala ya qawmi arahtee aaazzu aalaykum mina Allahi waittakhathtumoohu waraakum thihriyyan inna rabbee bima taamaloona muheetun
Waya qawmi iamaloo aala makanatikum innee aamilun sawfa taalamoona man yateehi aathabun yukhzeehi waman huwa kathibun wairtaqiboo inne aaakum raqeebun
Walamma jaa amruna najjayna shuaayban waallatheena amanoo maaahu birahmatin minna waakhathati allatheena thalamoo alssayhatu faasbahoo ee diyarihim jathimeena
Kaan lam yaghnaw feeha ala buadan limadyana kama baaidat thamoodu
Walaqad arsalna moosa biayatina wasultanin mubeenin
Ila firaawna wamalaihi faittabaaoo amra firaawna wama amru firaawna birasheedin
Yaqdumu qawmahu yawma alqiyamati faawradahumu alnnara wabisa alwirdu almawroodu
Waotbiaoo fee hathihi laanatan wayawma alqiyamati bisa alrrifdu almarfoodu
Thalika min anbai alqura naqussuhu aalayka minha qaimun wahaseedun
Wama thalamnahum walakin thalamoo anfusahum fama aghnat aanhum alihatuhumu allatee yadaoona min dooni Allahi min shayin lamma jaa amru abbika wama zadoohum ghayra tatbeebin
Wakathalika akhthu rabbika itha akhatha alqura wahiya thalimatun inna akhthahu aleemun shadeedun
Inna fee thalika laayatan liman khafa aathaba alakhirati thalika yawmun majmooaun lahu alnnasu wathalika yawmun mashhoodun
Wama nuakhkhiruhu illa liajalin maadoodin
Yawma yati la takallamu nafsun illa biithnihi faminhum shaqiyyun wasaaeedin
Faamma allatheena shaqoo fafee alnnari lahum feeha zafeerun washaheequn
Khalideena feeha ma damati alssamawatu waalardu illa ma shaa rabbuka inna rabbaka faaalun lima yureedu
Waamma allatheena suaidoo fafee aljannati khalideena feeha ma damati alssamawatu waalardu illa ma shaa rabbuka aataan ghayra majthoothin
Fala taku fee miryatin mimma yaabudu haolai ma yaabudoona illa kama yaabudu abaohum min qablu wainna lamuwaffoohum naseebahum ghayra anqoosin
Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba faikhtulifa feehi walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum wainnahum lafee shakkin minhu ureebun
Wainna kullan lamma layuwaffiyannahum rabbuka aamalahum innahu bima yaamaloona khabeerun
Faistaqim kama omirta waman taba maaaka wala tatghaw innahu bima taamaloona baseerun
Wala tarkanoo ila allatheena thalamoo fatamassakumu alnnaru wama lakum min dooni Allahi min awliyaa thumma la tunsaroona
Waaqimi alssalata tarafayi alnnahari wazulafan mina allayli inna alhasanati yuthhibna alssayyiati thalika thikra lilththakireena
Waisbir fainna Allaha la yudeeau ajra almuhsineena
Falawla kana mina alqurooni min qablikum oloo baqiyyatin yanhawna aani alfasadi fee alardi illa qaleelan mimman anjayna minhum aittabaaa allatheena thalamoo ma otrifoo feehi wakanoo mujrimeena
Wama kana rabbuka liyuhlika alqura bithulmin waahluha muslihoona
Walaw shaa rabbuka lajaaala alnnasa ommatan wahidatan wala yazaloona mukhtalifeena
Illa man rahima rabbuka walithalika khalaqahum watammat kalimatu rabbika laamlaanna jahannama mina aljinnati waalnnasi ajmaaeena
Wakullan naqussu aalayka min anbai alrrusuli ma nuthabbitu bihi fuadaka wajaaka fee hathihi alhaqqu wamawaithatun wathikra lilmumineena
Waqul lillatheena la yuminoona iamaloo aala makanatikum inna aamiloona
Waintathiroo inna muntathiroona
Walillahi ghaybu alssamawati waalardi wailayhi yurjaau alamru kulluhu faoabudhu watawakkal aalayhi wama rabbuka bighafilin aamma aamaloona
Aliflamra tilka ayatu alkitabi almubeenu
Inna anzalnahu quranan aarabiyyan laaallakum taaqiloona
Nahnu naqussu aalayka ahsana alqasasi bima awhayna ilayka hatha alqurana wain kunta min qablihi lamina alghafileena
Ith qala yoosufu liabeehi ya abati innee raaytu ahada aashara kawkaban waalshshamsa waalqamara raaytuhum lee sajideena
Qala ya bunayya la taqsus ruyaka aala ikhwatika fayakeedoo laka kaydan inna alshshaytana lilinsani aaduwwun mubeenun
Wakathalika yajtabeeka rabbuka wayuaallimuka min taweeli alahadeethi wayutimmu niamatahu aalayka waaala ali yaaqooba kama atammaha aala bawayka min qablu ibraheema waishaqa inna rabbaka aaleemun hakeemun
Laqad kana fee yoosufa waikhwatihi ayatun lilssaileena
Ith qaloo layoosufu waakhoohu ahabbu ila abeena minna wanahnu ausbatun inna abana lafee dalalin mubeenin
Oqtuloo yoosufa awi itrahoohu ardan yakhlu lakum wajhu abeekum watakoonoo min baadihi qawman saliheena
Qala qailun minhum la taqtuloo yoosufa waalqoohu fee ghayabati aljubbi yaltaqithu baadu alssayyarati in kuntum faaileena
Qaloo ya abana ma laka la tamanna aala yoosufa wainna lahu lanasihoona
Arsilhu maaana ghadan yartaa wayalaab wainna lahu lahafithoona
Qala innee layahzununee an thathhaboo bihi waakhafu an yakulahu alththibu waantum aanhu ghafiloona
Qaloo lain akalahu alththibu wanahnu ausbatun inna ithan lakhasiroona
Falamma thahaboo bihi waajmaaoo an yajaaloohu fee ghayabati aljubbi waawhayna ilayhi latunabiannahum biamrihim hatha wahum la ashauroona
Wajaoo abahum aishaan yabkoona
Qaloo ya abana inna thahabna nastabiqu watarakna yoosufa ainda mataaina faakalahu alththibu wama anta bimuminin lana walaw kunna adiqeena
Wajaoo aala qameesihi bidamin kathibin qala bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amran fasabrun jameelun waAllahu almustaaanu aala ma tasifoona
Wajaat sayyaratun faarsaloo waridahum faadla dalwahu qala ya bushra hatha ghulamun waasarroohu bidaaatan waAllahu aaleemun bima aamaloona
Washarawhu bithamanin bakhsin darahima maadoodatin wakanoo feehi mina alzzahideena
Waqala allathee ishtarahu min misra liimraatihi akrimee mathwahu aasa an yanfaaana aw nattakhithahu waladan wakathalika makkanna iyoosufa fee alardi walinuaallimahu min taweeli alahadeethi waAllahu ghalibun aala amrihi walakinna akthara alnnasi la yaalamoona
Walamma balagha ashuddahu ataynahu hukman waailman wakathalika najzee almuhsineena
Warawadathu allatee huwa fee baytiha aan nafsihi waghallaqati alabwaba waqalat hayta laka qala maaatha Allahi innahu rabbee ahsana athwaya innahu la yuflihu alththalimoona
Walaqad hammat bihi wahamma biha lawla an raa burhana rabbihi kathalika linasrifa aanhu alssooa waalfahshaa innahu min aibadina lmukhlaseena
Waistabaqa albaba waqaddat qameesahu min duburin waalfaya sayyidaha lada albabi qalat ma jazao man arada biahlika sooan illa an yusjana w aathabun aleemun
Qala hiya rawadatnee aan nafsee washahida shahidun min ahliha in kana qameesuhu qudda min qubulin fasadaqat wahuwa mina alkathibeena
Wain kana qameesuhu qudda min duburin fakathabat wahuwa mina alssadiqeena
Falamma raa qameesahu qudda min duburin qala innahu min kaydikunna inna kaydakunna aatheemun
Yoosufu aarid aan hatha waistaghfiree lithanbiki innaki kunti mina alkhatieena
Waqala niswatun fee almadeenati imraatu alaazeezi turawidu fataha aan nafsihi qad shaghafaha hubban inna lanaraha fee dalalin mubeenin
Falamma samiaat bimakrihinna arsalat ilayhinna waaatadat lahunna muttakaan waatat kulla wahidatin minhunna sikkeenan waqalati okhruj alayhinna falamma raaynahu akbarnahu waqattaana aydiyahunna waqulna hasha lillahi ma hatha basharan in hatha illa malakun kareemun
Qalat fathalikunna allathee lumtunnanee feehi walaqad rawadtuhu aan nafsihi faistasama walain lam yafaal ma amuruhu layusjananna alayakoonan mina alssaghireena
Qala rabbi alssijnu ahabbu ilayya mimma yadaoonanee ilayhi wailla tasrif aannee kaydahunna asbu ilayhinna waakun mina aljahileena
Faistajaba lahu rabbuhu fasarafa aanhu kaydahunna innahu huwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Thumma bada lahum min baadi ma raawoo alayati layasjununnahu hatta heenin
Wadakhala maaahu alssijna fatayani qala ahaduhuma innee aranee aasiru khamran waqala alakharu innee aranee ahmilu fawqa rasee khubzan akulu alttayru minhu nabbina bitaweelihi inna naraka mina almuhsineena
Qala la yateekuma taaamun turzaqanihi illa nabbatukuma bitaweelihi qabla an yatiyakuma thalikuma mimma aallamanee rabbee innee taraktu illata qawmin la yuminoona biAllahi wahum bialakhirati hum kafiroona
Waittabaatu millata abaee ibraheema waishaqa wayaaqooba ma kana lana an nushrika biAllahi min shayin thalika min fadli Allahi aalayna aaala alnnasi walakinna akthara alnnasi la yashkuroona
Ya sahibayi alssijni aarbabun mutafarriqoona khayrun ami Allahu alwahidu alqahharu
Ma taabudoona min doonihi illa asmaan sammaytumooha antum waabaokum ma anzala Allahu biha min sultanin ini alhukmu illa lillahi amara lla taabudoo illa iyyahu thalika alddeenu alqayyimu walakinna akthara alnnasi la yaalamoona
Ya sahibayi alssijni amma ahadukuma fayasqee rabbahu khamran waamma alakharu fayuslabu fatakulu alttayru min rasihi qudiya alamru llathee feehi tastaftiyani
Waqala lillathee thanna annahu najin minhuma othkurnee ainda rabbika faansahu alshshaytanu thikra rabbihi falabitha fee alssijni bidaa ineena
Waqala almaliku innee ara sabaa baqaratin simanin yakuluhunna sabaun aijafun wasabaa sunbulatin khudrin waokhara yabisatin ya ayyuha lmalao aftoonee fee ruyaya in kuntum lilrruya taaburoona
Qaloo adghathu ahlamin wama nahnu bitaweeli alahlami biaalimeena
Waqala allathee naja minhuma waiddakara baada ommatin ana onabbiokum bitaweelihi faarsilooni
Yoosufu ayyuha alssiddeequ aftina fee sabai baqaratin simanin yakuluhunna sabaun aijafun wasabai sunbulatin khudrin waokhara yabisatin aaallee arjiau ila alnnasi laaallahum yaalamoona
Qala tazraaoona sabaa sineena daaban fama hasadtum fatharoohu fee sunbulihi illa qaleelan mimma takuloona
Thumma yatee min baadi thalika sabaun shidadun yakulna ma qaddamtum lahunna illa qaleelan mimma tuhsinoona
Thumma yatee min baadi thalika aamun feehi yughathu alnnasu wafeehi yaasiroona
Waqala almaliku itoonee bihi falamma jaahu alrrasoolu qala irjia ila rabbika faisalhu ma balu alnniswati allatee qattaana aydiyahunna nna rabbee bikaydihinna aaleemun
Qala ma khatbukunna ith rawadtunna yoosufa aan nafsihi qulna hasha lillahi ma aalimna aalayhi min sooin qalati imraatu alaazeezi alana ashasa alhaqqu ana rawadtuhu aan nafsihi wainnahu lamina alssadiqeena
Thalika liyaalama annee lam akhunhu bialghaybi waanna Allaha la yahdee kayda alkhaineena
Wama obarrio nafsee inna alnnafsa laammaratun bialssooi illa ma rahima rabbee inna rabbee ghafoorun raheemun
Waqala almaliku itoonee bihi astakhlishu linafsee falamma kallamahu qala innaka alyawma ladayna makeenun ameenun
Qala ijaalnee aala khazaini alardi innee hafeethun aaleemun
Wakathalika makanna liyoosufa fee alardi yatabawwao minha haythu yashao nuseebu birahmatina man nashao wala nudeeau ajra almuhsineena
Walaajru alakhirati khayrun lillatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoona
Wajaa ikhwatu yoosufa fadakhaloo aalayhi faaarafahum wahum lahu munkiroona
Walamma jahhazahum bijahazihim qala itoonee biakhin lakum min abeekum ala tarawna annee oofee alkayla waana khayru almunzileena
Fain lam tatoonee bihi fala kayla lakum aindee wala taqrabooni
Qaloo sanurawidu aanhu abahu wainna lafaailoona
Waqala lifityanihi ijaaloo bidaaatahum fee rihalihim laaallahum yaarifoonaha itha inqalaboo ila ahlihim laaallahum yarjiaoona
Falamma rajaaoo ila abeehim qaloo ya abana muniaa minna alkaylu faarsil maaana akhana naktal wainna lahu lahafithoona
Qala hal amanukum aalayhi illa kama amintukum aala akheehi min qablu faAllahu khayrun hafithan wahuwa arhamu alrrahimeena
Walamma fatahoo mataaahum wajadoo bidaaatahum ruddat ilayhim qaloo ya abana ma nabghee hathihi bidaaatuna ruddat ilayna wanameeru hlana wanahfathu akhana wanazdadu kayla baaeerin thalika kaylun yaseerun
Qala lan orsilahu maaakum hatta tutooni mawthiqan mina Allahi latatunnanee bihi illa an yuhata bikum falamma atawhu mawthiqahum qala llahu aala ma naqoolu wakeelun
Waqala ya baniyya la tadkhuloo min babin wahidin waodkhuloo min abwabin mutafarriqatin wama oghnee aankum mina Allahi min shayin ini lhukmu illa lillahi aalayhi tawakkaltu waaalayhi falyatawakkali almutawakkiloona
Walamma dakhaloo min haythu amarahum aboohum ma kana yughnee aanhum mina Allahi min shayin illa hajatan fee nafsi yaaqooba qadaha ainnahu lathoo ailmin lima aallamnahu walakinna akthara alnnasi la yaalamoona
Walamma dakhaloo aala yoosufa awa ilayhi akhahu qala innee ana akhooka fala tabtais bima kanoo yaamaloona
Falamma jahhazahum bijahazihim jaaala alssiqayata fee rahli akheehi thumma aththana muaththinun ayyatuha alaeeru innakum lasariqoona
Qaloo waaqbaloo aalayhim matha tafqidoona
Qaloo nafqidu suwaaa almaliki waliman jaa bihi himlu baaeerin waana bihi zaaeemun
Qaloo taAllahi laqad aalimtum ma jina linufsida fee alardi wama kunna sariqeena
Qaloo fama jazaohu in kuntum kathibeena
Qaloo jazaohu man wujida fee rahlihi fahuwa jazaohu kathalika najzee alththalimeena
Fabadaa biawaiyatihim qabla wiaai akheehi thumma istakhrajaha min wiaai akheehi kathalika kidna liyoosufa ma kana liyakhutha akhahu fee eeni almaliki illa an yashaa Allahu narfaau darajatin man nashao wafawqa kulli thee ailmin aaleemun
Qaloo in yasriq faqad saraqa akhun lahu min qablu faasarraha yoosufu fee nafsihi walam yubdiha lahum qala antum sharrun makanan aAllahu aalamu bima tasifoona
Qaloo ya ayyuha alaazeezu inna lahu aban shaykhan kabeeran fakhuth ahadana makanahu inna naraka mina almuhsineena
Qala maaatha Allahi an nakhutha illa man wajadna mataaana aindahu inna ithan lathalimoona
Falamma istayasoo minhu khalasoo najiyyan qala kabeeruhum alam taalamoo anna abakum qad akhatha aalaykum mawthiqan mina Allahi wamin ablu ma farrattum fee yoosufa falan abraha alarda hatta yathana lee abee aw yahkuma Allahu lee wahuwa khayru alhakimeena
Irjiaoo ila abeekum faqooloo ya abana inna ibnaka saraqa wama shahidna illa bima aalimna wama kunna lilghaybi hafitheena
Waisali alqaryata allatee kunna feeha waalaeera allatee aqbalna feeha wainna lasadiqoona
Qala bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amran fasabrun jameelun aasa Allahu an yatiyanee bihim jameeaan innahu huwa alaaleemu alhakeemu
Watawalla aanhum waqala ya asafa aala yoosufa waibyaddat aaynahu mina alhuzni fahuwa katheemun
Qaloo taAllahi taftao tathkuru yoosufa hatta takoona haradan aw takoona mina alhalikeena
Qala innama ashkoo baththee wahuznee ila Allahi waaalamu mina Allahi ma la taalamoona
Ya baniyya ithhaboo fatahassasoo min yoosufa waakheehi wala tayasoo min rawhi Allahi innahu la yayasu min rawhi Allahi illa alqawmu lkafiroona
Falamma dakhaloo aalayhi qaloo ya ayyuha alaazeezu massana waahlana alddurru wajina bibidaaatin muzjatin faawfi lana alkayla watasaddaq alayna inna Allaha yajzee almutasaddiqeena
Qala hal aalimtum ma faaaltum biyoosufa waakheehi ith antum jahiloona
Qaloo ainnaka laanta yoosufa qala ana yoosufu wahatha akhee qad manna Allahu aalayna innahu man yattaqi wayasbir fainna Allaha la udeeau ajra almuhsineena
Qaloo taAllahi laqad atharaka Allahu aalayna wain kunna lakhatieena
Qala la tathreeba aalaykumu alyawma yaghfiru Allahu lakum wahuwa arhamu alrrahimeena
Ithhaboo biqameesee hatha faalqoohu aala wajhi abee yati baseeran watoonee biahlikum ajmaaeena
Walamma fasalati alaeeru qala aboohum innee laajidu reeha yoosufa lawla an tufannidooni
Qaloo taAllahi innaka lafee dalalika alqadeemi
Falamma an jaa albasheeru alqahu aala wajhihi fairtadda baseeran qala alam aqul lakum innee aalamu mina Allahi ma la taalamoona
Qaloo ya abana istaghfir lana thunoobana inna kunna khatieena
Qala sawfa astaghfiru lakum rabbee innahu huwa alghafooru alrraheemu
Falamma dakhaloo aala yoosufa awa ilayhi abawayhi waqala odkhuloo misra in shaa Allahu amineena
Warafaaa abawayhi aala alaarshi wakharroo lahu sujjadan waqala ya abati hatha taweelu ruyaya min qablu qad jaaalaha rabbee haqqan waqad ahsana bee ith akhrajanee mina alssijni wajaa bikum mina albadwi min baadi an nazagha alshshaytanu baynee wabayna ikhwatee inna rabbee ateefun lima yashao innahu huwa alaaleemu alhakeemu
Rabbi qad ataytanee mina almulki waaallamtanee min taweeli alahadeethi fatira alssamawati waalardi anta waliyyee fee alddunya aalakhirati tawaffanee musliman waalhiqnee bialssaliheena
Thalika min anbai alghaybi nooheehi ilayka wama kunta ladayhim ith ajmaaoo amrahum wahum yamkuroona
Wama aktharu alnnasi walaw harasta bimumineena
Wama tasaluhum aalayhi min ajrin in huwa illa thikrun lilaalameena
Wakaayyin min ayatin fee alssamawati waalardi yamurroona aalayha wahum aanha muaridoona
Wama yuminu aktharuhum biAllahi illa wahum mushrikoona
Afaaminoo an tatiyahum ghashiyatun min aathabi Allahi aw tatiyahumu alssaaatu baghtatan wahum la yashauroona
Qul hathihi sabeelee adaoo ila Allahi aala baseeratin ana wamani ittabaaanee wasubhana Allahi wama ana mina almushrikeena
Wama arsalna min qablika illa rijalan noohee ilayhim min ahli alqura afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu llatheena min qablihim waladaru alakhirati khayrun lillatheena ittaqaw afala taaqiloona
Hatta itha istayasa alrrusulu wathannoo annahum qad kuthiboo jaahum nasruna fanujjiya man nashao wala yuraddu basuna aani alqawmi lmujrimeena
Laqad kana fee qasasihim aibratun liolee alalbabi ma kana hadeethan yuftara walakin tasdeeqa allathee bayna yadayhi watafseela kulli hayin wahudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoona
Aliflammeemra tilka ayatu alkitabi waallathee onzila ilayka min rabbika alhaqqu walakinna akthara alnnasi la yuminoona
Allahu allathee rafaaa alssamawati bighayri aamadin tarawnaha thumma istawa aala alaarshi wasakhkhara alshshamsa waalqamara kullun ajree liajalin musamman yudabbiru alamra yufassilu alayati laaallakum biliqai rabbikum tooqinoona
Wahuwa allathee madda alarda wajaaala feeha rawasiya waanharan wamin kulli alththamarati jaaala feeha zawjayni ithnayni yughshee llayla alnnahara inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroona
Wafee alardi qitaaun mutajawiratun wajannatun min aanabin wazaraun wanakheelun sinwanun waghayru sinwanin yusqa bimain wahidin anufaddilu baadaha aala baadin fee alokuli inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yaaqiloona
Wain taajab faaajabun qawluhum aitha kunna turaban ainna lafee khalqin jadeedin olaika allatheena kafaroo birabbihim waolaika alaghlalu ee aanaqihim waolaika ashabu alnnari hum feeha khalidoona
Wayastaajiloonaka bialssayyiati qabla alhasanati waqad khalat min qablihimu almathulatu wainna rabbaka lathoo maghfiratin lilnnasi aala hulmihim wainna rabbaka lashadeedu alaiqabi
Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lawla onzila aalayhi ayatun min rabbihi innama anta munthirun walikulli qawmin hadin
Allahu yaalamu ma tahmilu kullu ontha wama tagheedu alarhamu wama tazdadu wakullu shayin aindahu bimiqdarin
aalimu alghaybi waalshshahadati alkabeeru almutaaali
Sawaon minkum man asarra alqawla waman jahara bihi waman huwa mustakhfin biallayli wasaribun bialnnahari
Lahu muaaqqibatun min bayni yadayhi wamin khalfihi yahfathoonahu min amri Allahi inna Allaha la yughayyiru ma biqawmin hatta ughayyiroo ma bianfusihim waitha arada Allahu biqawmin sooan fala maradda lahu wama lahum min doonihi min walin
Huwa allathee yureekumu albarqa khawfan watamaaan wayunshio alssahaba alththiqala
Wayusabbihu alrraadu bihamdihi waalmalaikatu min kheefatihi wayursilu alssawaaiqa fayuseebu biha man yashao wahum yujadiloona fee llahi wahuwa shadeedu almihali
Lahu daawatu alhaqqi waallatheena yadaoona min doonihi la yastajeeboona lahum bishayin illa kabasiti kaffayhi ila almai liyablugha fahu ama huwa bibalighihi wama duaao alkafireena illa fee dalalin
Walillahi yasjudu man fee alssamawati waalardi tawaan wakarhan wathilaluhum bialghuduwwi waalasali
Qul man rabbu alssamawati waalardi quli Allahu qul afaittakhathtum min doonihi awliyaa la yamlikoona lianfusihim nafaan wala darran qul hal yastawee alaama waalbaseeru am hal tastawee alththulumatu waalnnooru am jaaaloo lillahi shurakaa khalaqoo kakhalqihi fatashabaha lkhalqu aalayhim quli Allahu khaliqu kulli shayin wahuwa alwahidu alqahharu
Anzala mina alssamai maan fasalat awdiyatun biqadariha faihtamala alssaylu zabadan rabiyan wamimma yooqidoona aalayhi fee alnnari ibtighaa hilyatin aw mataain zabadun mithluhu kathalika yadribu Allahu alhaqqa waalbatila faamma alzzabadu fayathhabu jufaan waamma ma anfaau alnnasa fayamkuthu fee alardi kathalika yadribu Allahu alamthala
Lillatheena istajaboo lirabbihimu alhusna waallatheena lam yastajeeboo lahu law anna lahum ma fee alardi jameeaan wamithlahu maaahu aiftadaw bihi olaika lahum sooo alhisabi wamawahum jahannamu wabisa almihadu
Afaman yaalamu annama onzila ilayka min rabbika alhaqqu kaman huwa aama innama yatathakkaru oloo alalbabi
Allatheena yoofoona biaahdi Allahi wala yanqudoona almeethaqa
Waallatheena yasiloona ma amara Allahu bihi an yoosala wayakhshawna rabbahum wayakhafoona sooa alhisabi
Waallatheena sabaroo ibtighaa wajhi rabbihim waaqamoo alssalata waanfaqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran waaalaniyatan wayadraoona ialhasanati alssayyiata olaika lahum auqba alddari
Jannatu aadnin yadkhuloonaha waman salaha min abaihim waazwajihim wathurriyyatihim waalmalaikatu yadkhuloona aalayhim min kulli babin
Salamun aalaykum bima sabartum faniama auqba alddari
Waallatheena yanqudoona aahda Allahi min baadi meethaqihi wayaqtaaoona ma amara Allahu bihi an yoosala wayufsidoona fee alardi olaika ahumu allaanatu walahum sooo alddari
Allahu yabsutu alrrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru wafarihoo bialhayati alddunya wama alhayatu alddunya fee alakhirati illa mataaun
Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lawla onzila aalayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul inna Allaha yudillu man yashao wayahdee ilayhi man anaba
Allatheena amanoo watatmainnu quloobuhum bithikri Allahi ala bithikri Allahi tatmainnu alquloobu
Allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati tooba lahum wahusnu maabin
Kathalika arsalnaka fee ommatin qad khalat min qabliha omamun litatluwa aalayhimu allathee awhayna ilayka wahum yakfuroona bialrrahmani ul huwa rabbee la ilaha illa huwa aalayhi tawakkaltu wailayhi matabi
Walaw anna quranan suyyirat bihi aljibalu aw quttiaat bihi alardu aw kullima bihi almawta bal lillahi alamru jameeaan afalam yayasi allatheena amanoo an law yashao Allahu lahada alnnasa jameeaan wala yazalu allatheena kafaroo tuseebuhum bima sanaaoo qariaatun aw ahullu qareeban min darihim hatta yatiya waadu Allahi inna Allaha la yukhlifu almeeaada
Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika faamlaytu lillatheena kafaroo thumma akhathtuhum fakayfa kana aiqabi
Afaman huwa qaimun aala kulli nafsin bima kasabat wajaaaloo lillahi shurakaa qul sammoohum am tunabbioonahu bima la yaalamu fee alardi m bithahirin mina alqawli bal zuyyina lillatheena kafaroo makruhum wasuddoo aani alssabeeli waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min hadin
Lahum aathabun fee alhayati alddunya walaaathabu alakhirati ashaqqu wama lahum mina Allahi min waqin
