Mathalu aljannati allatee wuaida almuttaqoona tajree min tahtiha alanharu okuluha daimun wathilluha tilka auqba allatheena ittaqaw aauqba alkafireena alnnaru
Waallatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yafrahoona bima onzila ilayka wamina alahzabi man yunkiru baadahu qul innama omirtu an aabuda Allaha ala oshrika bihi ilayhi adaoo wailayhi maabi
Wakathalika anzalnahu hukman aarabiyyan walaini ittabaata ahwaahum baada ma jaaka mina alailmi ma laka mina Allahi min waliyyin wala aqin
Walaqad arsalna rusulan min qablika wajaaalna lahum azwajan wathurriyyatan wama kana lirasoolin an yatiya biayatin illa biithni Allahi ikulli ajalin kitabun
Yamhoo Allahu ma yashao wayuthbitu waaindahu ommu alkitabi
Wain ma nuriyannaka baada allathee naaiduhum aw natawaffayannaka fainnama aalayka albalaghu waaalayna alhisabu
Awalam yaraw anna natee alarda nanqusuha min atrafiha waAllahu yahkumu la muaaqqiba lihukmihi wahuwa sareeau alhisabi
Waqad makara allatheena min qablihim falillahi almakru jameeaan yaalamu ma taksibu kullu nafsin wasayaalamu alkuffaru liman auqba lddari
Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lasta mursalan qul kafa biAllahi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum waman aindahu ailmu alkitabi
Aliflamra kitabun anzalnahu ilayka litukhrija alnnasa mina alththulumati ila alnnoori biithni rabbihim ila sirati alaazeezi alhameedi
Allahi allathee lahu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wawaylun lilkafireena min aathabin shadeedin
Allatheena yastahibboona alhayata alddunya aala alakhirati wayasuddoona aan sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha aiwajan olaika fee dalalin aaeedin
Wama arsalna min rasoolin illa bilisani qawmihi liyubayyina lahum fayudillu Allahu man yashao wayahdee man yashao wahuwa alaazeezu lhakeemu
Walaqad arsalna moosa biayatina an akhrij qawmaka mina alththulumati ila alnnoori wathakkirhum biayyami Allahi inna fee thalika aayatin likulli sabbarin shakoorin
Waith qala moosa liqawmihi othkuroo niamata Allahi aalaykum ith anjakum min ali firaawna yasoomoonakum sooa alaathabi wayuthabbihoona bnaakum wayastahyoona nisaakum wafee thalikum balaon min rabbikum aatheemun
Waith taaththana rabbukum lain shakartum laazeedannakum walain kafartum inna aathabee lashadeedun
Waqala moosa in takfuroo antum waman fee alardi jameeaan fainna Allaha laghaniyyun hameedun
Alam yatikum nabao allatheena min qablikum qawmi noohin waaadin wathamooda waallatheena min baadihim la yaalamuhum illa Allahu jaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati faraddoo aydiyahum fee afwahihim waqaloo inna kafarna bima orsiltum bihi wainna lafee shakkin mimma tadaoonana layhi mureebun
Qalat rusuluhum afee Allahi shakkun fatiri alssamawati waalardi yadaookum liyaghfira lakum min thunoobikum wayuakhkhirakum ila ajalin usamman qaloo in antum illa basharun mithluna tureedoona an tasuddoona aamma kana yaabudu abaona fatoona bisultanin mubeenin
Qalat lahum rusuluhum in nahnu illa basharun mithlukum walakinna Allaha yamunnu aala man yashao min aibadihi wama kana lana an atiyakum bisultanin illa biithni Allahi waaala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoona
Wama lana alla natawakkala aala Allahi waqad hadana subulana walanasbiranna aala ma athaytumoona waaala Allahi falyatawakkali lmutawakkiloona

Wama thalika aala Allahi biaazeezin

Waqala alshshaytanu lamma qudiya alamru inna Allaha waaadakum waada alhaqqi wawaaadtukum faakhlaftukum wama kana liya aalaykum min sultanin illa an daaawtukum faistajabtum lee fala taloomoonee waloomoo anfusakum ma ana bimusrikhikum wama antum bimusrikhiyya innee afartu bima ashraktumooni min qablu inna alththalimeena lahum aathabun aleemun
Waodkhila allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha biithni rabbihim tahiyyatuhum eeha salamun
Alam tara kayfa daraba Allahu mathalan kalimatan tayyibatan kashajaratin tayyibatin asluha thabitun wafarauha fee alssamai

Jahannama yaslawnaha wabisa alqararu
Wajaaaloo lillahi andadan liyudilloo aan sabeelihi qul tamattaaoo fainna maseerakum ila alnnari
Qul liaibadiya allatheena amanoo yuqeemoo alssalata wayunfiqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran waaalaniyatan min qabli an yatiya yawmun la ayaun feehi wala khilalun
Allahu allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda waanzala mina alssamai maan faakhraja bihi mina alththamarati rizqan lakum wasakhkhara akumu alfulka litajriya fee albahri biamrihi wasakhkhara lakumu alanhara
Wasakhkhara lakumu alshshamsa waalqamara daibayni wasakhkhara lakumu allayla waalnnahara
Waatakum min kulli ma saaltumoohu wain taauddoo niamata Allahi la tuhsooha inna alinsana lathaloomun kaffarun
Waith qala ibraheemu rabbi ijaal hatha albalada aminan waojnubnee wabaniyya an naabuda alasnama
Rabbi innahunna adlalna katheeran mina alnnasi faman tabiaanee fainnahu minnee waman aasanee fainnaka ghafoorun raheemun
Rabbana innee askantu min thurriyyatee biwadin ghayri thee zarain ainda baytika almuharrami rabbana liyuqeemoo alssalata faijaal fidatan mina alnnasi tahwee ilayhim waorzuqhum mina alththamarati laaallahum yashkuroona
Rabbana innaka taalamu ma nukhfee wama nualinu wama yakhfa aala Allahi min shayin fee alardi wala fee alssamai
Alhamdu lillahi allathee wahaba lee aala alkibari ismaaeela waishaqa inna rabbee lasameeau aldduaai
Rabbi ijaalnee muqeema alssalati wamin thurriyyatee rabbana wtaqabbal duaai
Rabbana ighfir lee waliwalidayya walilmumineena yawma yaqoomu alhisabu
Wala tahsabanna Allaha ghafilan aamma yaamalu alththalimoona innama yuakhkhiruhum liyawmin tashkhasu feehi alabsaru

Yunbitu lakum bihi alzzaraa waalzzaytoona waalnnakheela waalaanaba wamin kulli alththamarati inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin atafakkaroona

WaAllahu yaalamu ma tusirroona wama tualinoona
Waallatheena yadaoona min dooni Allahi la yakhluqoona shayan wahum yukhlaqoona
Amwatun ghayru ahyain wama yashauroona ayyana yubaathoona
Ilahukum ilahun wahidun faallatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati quloobuhum munkiratun wahum mustakbiroona
La jarama anna Allaha yaalamu ma yusirroona wama yualinoona innahu la yuhibbu almustakbireena
Waitha qeela lahum matha anzala rabbukum qaloo asateeru alawwaleena
Liyahmiloo awzarahum kamilatan yawma alqiyamati wamin awzari allatheena yudilloonahum bighayri ailmin ala saa ma yaziroona
Qad makara allatheena min qablihim faata Allahu bunyanahum mina alqawaaidi fakharra aalayhimu alssaqfu min fawqihim waatahumu alaathabu in haythu la yashauroona
Thumma yawma alqiyamati yukhzeehim wayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum tushaqqoona feehim qala allatheena ootoo alailma inna lkhizya alyawma waalssooa aala alkafireena
Allatheena tatawaffahumu almalaikatu thalimee anfusihim faalqawoo alssalama ma kunna naamalu min sooin bala inna Allaha aaleemun bima untum taamaloona
Faodkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha falabisa mathwa almutakabbireena
Waqeela lillatheena ittaqaw matha anzala rabbukum qaloo khayran lillatheena ahsanoo fee hathihi alddunya hasanatun waladaru alakhirati hayrun walaniama daru almuttaqeena
Jannatu aadnin yadkhuloonaha tajree min tahtiha alanharu lahum feeha ma yashaoona kathalika yajzee Allahu almuttaqeena
Allatheena tatawaffahumu almalaikatu tayyibeena yaqooloona salamun aalaykumu odkhuloo aljannata bima kuntum taamaloona
Hal yanthuroona illa an tatiyahumu almalaikatu aw yatiya amru rabbika kathalika faaala allatheena min qablihim wama thalamahumu Allahu alakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona
Faasabahum sayyiatu ma aamiloo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Waqala allatheena ashrakoo law shaa Allahu ma aabadna min doonihi min shayin nahnu wala abaona wala harramna min doonihi min shayin athalika faaala allatheena min qablihim fahal aala alrrusuli illa albalaghu almubeenu
Walaqad baaathna fee kulli ommatin rasoolan ani oabudoo Allaha waijtaniboo alttaghoota faminhum man hada Allahu waminhum man haqqat alayhi alddalalatu faseeroo fee alardi faonthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu almukaththibeena
In tahris aala hudahum fainna Allaha la yahdee man yudillu wama lahum min nasireena
Waaqsamoo biAllahi jahda aymanihim la yabaathu Allahu man yamootu bala waadan aalayhi haqqan walakinna akthara alnnasi la yaalamoona
Liyubayyina lahumu allathee yakhtalifoona feehi waliyaalama allatheena kafaroo annahum kanoo kathibeena
Innama qawluna lishayin itha aradnahu an naqoola lahu kun fayakoonu
Waallatheena hajaroo fee Allahi min baadi ma thulimoo lanubawwiannahum fee alddunya hasanatan walaajru alakhirati akbaru law kanoo aalamoona
Allatheena sabaroo waaala rabbihim yatawakkaloona
Wama arsalna min qablika illa rijalan noohee ilayhim faisaloo ahla alththikri in kuntum la taalamoona
Bialbayyinati waalzzuburi waanzalna ilayka alththikra litubayyina lilnnasi ma nuzzila ilayhim walaaallahum yatafakkaroona
Afaamina allatheena makaroo alssayyiati an yakhsifa Allahu bihimu alarda aw yatiyahumu alaathabu min haythu la yashauroona
Aw yakhuthahum fee taqallubihim fama hum bimuajizeena
Aw yakhuthahum aala takhawwufin fainna rabbakum laraoofun raheemun
Awa lam yaraw ila ma khalaqa Allahu min shayin yatafayyao thilaluhu aani alyameeni waalshshamaili sujjadan lillahi wahum dakhiroona
Walillahi yasjudu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi min dabbatin waalmalaikatu wahum la yastakbiroona
Yakhafoona rabbahum min fawqihim wayafaaloona ma yumaroona
Waqala Allahu la tattakhithoo ilahayni ithnayni innama huwa ilahun wahidun faiyyaya fairhabooni
Walahu ma fee alssamawati waalardi walahu alddeenu wasiban afaghayra Allahi tattaqoona
Wama bikum min niamatin famina Allahi thumma itha massakumu alddurru failayhi tajaroona
Thumma itha kashafa alddurra aankum itha fareequn minkum birabbihim yushrikoona
Liyakfuroo bima ataynahum fatamattaaoo fasawfa taalamoona
Wayajaaloona lima la yaalamoona naseeban mimma razaqnahum taAllahi latusalunna aamma kuntum taftaroona
Wayajaaloona lillahi albanati subhanahu walahum ma yashtahoona
Waitha bushshira ahaduhum bialontha thalla wajhuhu muswaddan wahuwa katheemun
Yatawara mina alqawmi min sooi ma bushshira bihi ayumsikuhu aala hoonin am yadussuhu fee altturabi ala saa ma yahkumoona
Lillatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati mathalu alssawi walillahi almathalu alaala wahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Walaw yuakhithu Allahu alnnasa bithulmihim ma taraka aalayha min dabbatin walakin yuakhkhiruhum ila ajalin musamman faitha jaa ajaluhum a yastakhiroona saaatan wala yastaqdimoona
Wayajaaloona lillahi ma yakrahoona watasifu alsinatuhumu alkathiba anna lahumu alhusna la jarama anna lahumu alnnara waannahum ufratoona
TaAllahi laqad arsalna ila omamin min qablika fazayyana lahumu alshshaytanu aamalahum fahuwa waliyyuhumu alyawma walahum aathabun leemun
Wama anzalna aalayka alkitaba illa litubayyina lahumu allathee ikhtalafoo feehi wahudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoona
WaAllahu anzala mina alssamai maan faahya bihi alarda baada mawtiha inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yasmaaoona
Wainna lakum fee alanaami laaibratan nusqeekum mimma fee butoonihi min bayni farthin wadamin labanan khalisan saighan lilshsharibeena
Wamin thamarati alnnakheeli waalaanabi tattakhithoona minhu sakaran warizqan hasanan inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yaaqiloona
Waawha rabbuka ila alnnahli ani ittakhithee mina aljibali buyootan wamina alshshajari wamimma yaarishoona
Thumma kulee min kulli alththamarati faoslukee subula rabbiki thululan yakhruju min butooniha sharabun mukhtalifun alwanuhu feehi hifaon lilnnasi inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yatafakkaroona
WaAllahu khalaqakum thumma yatawaffakum waminkum man yuraddu ila arthali alaumuri likay la yaalama baada ailmin shayan inna Allaha aleemun qadeerun
WaAllahu faddala baadakum aala baadin fee alrrizqi fama allatheena fuddiloo biraddee rizqihim aala ma malakat aymanuhum fahum feehi awaon afabiniamati Allahi yajhadoona
WaAllahu jaaala lakum min anfusikum azwajan wajaaala lakum min azwajikum baneena wahafadatan warazaqakum mina alttayyibati fabialbatili yuminoona wabiniamati Allahi hum yakfuroona
Wayaabudoona min dooni Allahi ma la yamliku lahum rizqan mina alssamawati waalardi shayan wala yastateeaoona
Fala tadriboo lillahi alamthala inna Allaha yaalamu waantum la taalamoona
Daraba Allahu mathalan aabdan mamlookan la yaqdiru aala shayin waman razaqnahu minna rizqan hasanan fahuwa yunfiqu minhu sirran ajahran hal yastawoona alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la yaalamoona
Wadaraba Allahu mathalan rajulayni ahaduhuma abkamu la yaqdiru aala shayin wahuwa kallun aala mawlahu aynama yuwajjihhu la yati ikhayrin hal yastawee huwa waman yamuru bialaadli wahuwa aala siratin mustaqeemin
Walillahi ghaybu alssamawati waalardi wama amru alssaaati illa kalamhi albasari aw huwa aqrabu inna Allaha aala kulli shayin qadeerun
WaAllahu akhrajakum min butooni ommahatikum la taalamoona shayan wajaaala lakumu alssamaa waalabsara waalafidata laaallakum tashkuroona
Alam yaraw ila alttayri musakhkharatin fee jawwi alssamai ma yumsikuhunna illa Allahu inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoona
WaAllahu jaaala lakum min buyootikum sakanan wajaaala lakum min juloodi alanaami buyootan tastakhiffoonaha yawma thaanikum wayawma qamatikum wamin aswafiha waawbariha waashaariha athathan wamataaan ila heenin
WaAllahu jaaala lakum mimma khalaqa thilalan wajaaala lakum mina aljibali aknanan wajaaala lakum sarabeela taqeekumu alharra asarabeela taqeekum basakum kathalika yutimmu niamatahu aalaykum laaallakum tuslimoona
Fain tawallaw fainnama aalayka albalaghu almubeenu
Yaarifoona niamata Allahi thumma yunkiroonaha waaktharuhumu alkafiroona
Wayawma nabaathu min kulli ommatin shaheedan thumma la yuthanu lillatheena kafaroo wala hum yustaataboona
Waitha raa allatheena thalamoo alaathaba fala yukhaffafu aanhum wala hum yuntharoona
Waitha raa allatheena ashrakoo shurakaahum qaloo rabbana haolai shurakaona allatheena kunna nadaoo min doonika faalqaw ilayhimu alqawla nnakum lakathiboona
Waalqaw ila Allahi yawmaithin alssalama wadalla aanhum ma kanoo yaftaroona
Allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo aan sabeeli Allahi zidnahum aathaban fawqa alaathabi bima kanoo yufsidoona
Wayawma nabaathu fee kulli ommatin shaheedan aalayhim min anfusihim wajina bika shaheedan aala haolai wanazzalna aalayka alkitaba ibyanan likulli shayin wahudan warahmatan wabushra lilmuslimeena
Inna Allaha yamuru bialaadli waalihsani waeetai thee alqurba wayanha aani alfahshai waalmunkari waalbaghyi yaaithukum laaallakum athakkaroona
Waawfoo biaahdi Allahi itha aahadtum wala tanqudoo alaymana baada tawkeediha waqad jaaaltumu Allaha aalaykum kafeelan inna Allaha aalamu ma tafaaloona
Wala takoonoo kaallatee naqadat ghazlaha min baadi quwwatin ankathan tattakhithoona aymanakum dakhalan baynakum an takoona ommatun hiya rba min ommatin innama yablookumu Allahu bihi walayubayyinanna lakum yawma alqiyamati ma kuntum feehi takhtalifoona
Walaw shaa Allahu lajaaalakum ommatan wahidatan walakin yudillu man yashao wayahdee man yashao walatusalunna aamma kuntum taamaloona
Wala tattakhithoo aymanakum dakhalan baynakum fatazilla qadamun baada thubootiha watathooqoo alssooa bima sadadtum aan sabeeli Allahi alakum aathabun aatheemun
Wala tashtaroo biaahdi Allahi thamanan qaleelan innama ainda Allahi huwa khayrun lakum in kuntum taalamoona
Ma aindakum yanfadu wama ainda Allahi baqin walanajziyanna allatheena sabaroo ajrahum biahsani ma kanoo yaamaloona
Man aamila salihan min thakarin aw ontha wahuwa muminun falanuhyiyannahu hayatan tayyibatan walanajziyannahum ajrahum biahsani ma kanoo aamaloona
Faitha qarata alqurana faistaaith biAllahi mina alshshaytani alrrajeemi
Innahu laysa lahu sultanun aala allatheena amanoo waaala rabbihim yatawakkaloona
Innama sultanuhu aala allatheena yatawallawnahu waallatheena hum bihi mushrikoona
Waitha baddalna ayatan makana ayatin waAllahu aalamu bima yunazzilu qaloo innama anta muftarin bal aktharuhum la yaalamoona
Qul nazzalahu roohu alqudusi min rabbika bialhaqqi liyuthabbita allatheena amanoo wahudan wabushra lilmuslimeena
Walaqad naalamu annahum yaqooloona innama yuaallimuhu basharun lisanu allathee yulhidoona ilayhi aajamiyyun wahatha lisanun aarabiyyun ubeenun
Inna allatheena la yuminoona biayati Allahi la yahdeehimu Allahu walahum aathabun aleemun
Innama yaftaree alkathiba allatheena la yuminoona biayati Allahi waolaika humu alkathiboona
Man kafara biAllahi min baadi eemanihi illa man okriha waqalbuhu mutmainnun bialeemani walakin man sharaha bialkufri sadran faaalayhim hadabun mina Allahi walahum aathabun aatheemun
Thalika biannahumu istahabboo alhayata alddunya aala alakhirati waanna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alkafireena
Olaika allatheena tabaaa Allahu aala quloobihim wasamaihim waabsarihim waolaika humu alghafiloona
La jarama annahum fee alakhirati humu alkhasiroona
Thumma inna rabbaka lillatheena hajaroo min baadi ma futinoo thumma jahadoo wasabaroo inna rabbaka min baadiha laghafoorun raheemun
Yawma tatee kullu nafsin tujadilu aan nafsiha watuwaffa kullu nafsin ma aamilat wahum la yuthlamoona
Wadaraba Allahu mathalan qaryatan kanat aminatan mutmainnatan yateeha rizquha raghadan min kulli makanin fakafarat bianaumi Allahi aathaqaha Allahu libasa aljooai waalkhawfi bima kanoo yasnaaoona
Walaqad jaahum rasoolun minhum fakaththaboohu faakhathahumu alaathabu wahum thalimoona
Fakuloo mimma razaqakumu Allahu halalan tayyiban waoshkuroo niamata Allahi in kuntum iyyahu taabudoona
Innama harrama aalaykumu almaytata waalddama walahma alkhinzeeri wama ohilla lighayri Allahi bihi famani idturra ghayra baghin wala adin fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Wala taqooloo lima tasifu alsinatukumu alkathiba hatha halalun wahatha haramun litaftaroo aala Allahi alkathiba inna allatheena aftaroona aala Allahi alkathiba la yuflihoona
Mataaun qaleelun walahum aathabun aleemun
Waaala allatheena hadoo harramna ma qasasna aalayka min qablu wama thalamnahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona
Thumma inna rabbaka lillatheena aamiloo alssooa bijahalatin thumma taboo min baadi thalika waaslahoo inna rabbaka min baadiha aghafoorun raheemun
Inna ibraheema kana ommatan qanitan lillahi haneefan walam yaku mina almushrikeena
Shakiran lianaumihi ijtabahu wahadahu ila siratin mustaqeemin
Waataynahu fee alddunya hasanatan wainnahu fee alakhirati lamina alssaliheena
Thumma awhayna ilayka ani ittabia millata ibraheema haneefan wama kana mina almushrikeena
Innama juaila alssabtu aala allatheena ikhtalafoo feehi wainna rabbaka layahkumu baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi akhtalifoona
Odau ila sabeeli rabbika bialhikmati waalmawaithati alhasanati wajadilhum biallatee hiya ahsanu inna rabbaka huwa aalamu biman dalla an sabeelihi wahuwa aalamu bialmuhtadeena
Wain aaqabtum faaaqiboo bimithli ma aooqibtum bihi walain sabartum lahuwa khayrun lilssabireena
Waisbir wama sabruka illa biAllahi wala tahzan aalayhim wala taku fee dayqin mimma yamkuroona
Inna Allaha maaa allatheena ittaqaw waallatheena hum muhsinoona
Subhana allathee asra biaabdihi laylan mina almasjidi alharami ila almasjidi alaqsa allathee barakna hawlahu linuriyahu min ayatina nnahu huwa alssameeau albaseeru
Waatayna moosa alkitaba wajaaalnahu hudan libanee israeela alla tattakhithoo min doonee wakeelan
Thurriyyata man hamalna maaa noohin innahu kana aabdan shakooran
Waqadayna ila banee israeela fee alkitabi latufsidunna fee alardi marratayni walataalunna auluwwan kabeeran
Faitha jaa waadu oolahuma baaathna aalaykum aibadan lana olee basin shadeedin fajasoo khilala alddiyari wakana waadan mafaoolan
Thumma radadna lakumu alkarrata aalayhim waamdadnakum biamwalin wabaneena wajaaalnakum akthara nafeeran
In ahsantum ahsantum lianfusikum wain asatum falaha faitha jaa waadu alakhirati liyasoooo wujoohakum waliyadkhuloo almasjida kama akhaloohu awwala marratin waliyutabbiroo ma aalaw tatbeeran
aasa rabbukum an yarhamakum wain audtum audna wajaaalna jahannama lilkafireena haseeran
Inna hatha alqurana yahdee lillatee hiya aqwamu wayubashshiru almumineena allatheena yaamaloona alssalihati anna lahum ajran kabeeran
Waanna allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati aatadna lahum aathaban aleeman
Wayadau alinsanu bialshsharri duaaahu bialkhayri wakana alinsanu aajoolan
Wajaaalna allayla waalnnahara ayatayni famahawna ayata allayli wajaaalna ayata alnnahari mubsiratan litabtaghoo fadlan min rabbikum alitaalamoo aadada alssineena waalhisaba wakulla shayin fassalnahu tafseelan
Wakulla insanin alzamnahu tairahu fee aunuqihi wanukhriju lahu yawma alqiyamati kitaban yalqahu manshooran
Iqra kitabaka kafa binafsika alyawma aalayka haseeban
Mani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu aalayha wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra wama kunna uaaththibeena hatta nabaatha rasoolan
Waitha aradna an nuhlika qaryatan amarna mutrafeeha fafasaqoo feeha fahaqqa aalayha alqawlu fadammarnaha tadmeeran
Wakam ahlakna mina alqurooni min baadi noohin wakafa birabbika bithunoobi aibadihi khabeeran baseeran
Man kana yureedu alaajilata aajjalna lahu feeha ma nashao liman nureedu thumma jaaalna lahu jahannama yaslaha mathmooman madhooran
Waman arada alakhirata wasaaa laha saayaha wahuwa muminun faolaika kana saayuhum mashkooran
Kullan numiddu haolai wahaolai min aatai rabbika wama kana aatao rabbika mahthooran
Onthur kayfa faddalna baadahum aala baadin walalakhiratu akbaru darajatin waakbaru tafdeelan
La tajaal maaa Allahi ilahan akhara fataqauda mathmooman makhthoolan
Waqada rabbuka alla taabudoo illa iyyahu wabialwalidayni ihsanan imma yablughanna aindaka alkibara ahaduhuma aw kilahuma fala taqul ahuma offin wala tanharhuma waqul lahuma qawlan kareeman
Waikhfid lahuma janaha alththulli mina alrrahmati waqul rabbi irhamhuma kama rabbayanee sagheeran
Rabbukum aalamu bima fee nufoosikum in takoonoo saliheena fainnahu kana lilawwabeena ghafooran
Waati tha alqurba haqqahu waalmiskeena waibna alssabeeli wala tubaththir tabtheeran
Inna almubaththireena kanoo ikhwana alshshayateeni wakana alshshaytanu lirabbihi kafooran
Waimma tuaridanna aanhumu ibtighaa rahmatin min rabbika tarjooha faqul lahum qawlan maysooran
Wala tajaal yadaka maghloolatan ila aunuqika wala tabsutha kulla albasti fataqauda malooman mahsooran
Inna rabbaka yabsutu alrrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru innahu kana biaibadihi khabeeran baseeran
Wala taqtuloo awladakum khashyata imlaqin nahnu narzuquhum waiyyakum inna qatlahum kana khitan kabeeran
Wala taqraboo alzzina innahu kana fahishatan wasaa sabeelan
Wala taqtuloo alnnafsa allatee harrama Allahu illa bialhaqqi waman qutila mathlooman faqad jaaalna liwaliyyihi sultanan fala yusrif fee lqatli innahu kana mansooran
Wala taqraboo mala alyateemi illa biallatee hiya ahsanu hatta yablugha ashuddahu waawfoo bialaahdi inna alaahda kana masoolan
Waawfoo alkayla itha kiltum wazinoo bialqistasi almustaqeemi thalika khayrun waahsanu taweelan
Wala taqfu ma laysa laka bihi ailmun inna alssamaa waalbasara waalfuada kullu olaika kana aanhu masoolan
Wala tamshi fee alardi marahan innaka lan takhriqa alarda walan tablugha aljibala toolan
Kullu thalika kana sayyiohu ainda rabbika makroohan
Thalika mimma awha ilayka rabbuka mina alhikmati wala tajaal maaa Allahi ilahan akhara fatulqa fee jahannama malooman madhooran
Afaasfakum rabbukum bialbaneena waittakhatha mina almalaikati inathan innakum lataqooloona qawlan aatheeman
Walaqad sarrafna fee hatha alqurani liyaththakkaroo wama yazeeduhum illa nufooran
Qul law kana maaahu alihatun kama yaqooloona ithan laibtaghaw ila thee alaarshi sabeelan
Subhanahu wataaala aamma yaqooloona auluwwan kabeeran
Tusabbihu lahu alssamawatu alssabau waalardu waman feehinna wain min shayin illa yusabbihu bihamdihi walakin la tafqahoona tasbeehahum nnahu kana haleeman ghafooran
Waitha qarata alqurana jaaalna baynaka wabayna allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati hijaban mastooran
Wajaaalna aala quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee athanihim waqran waitha thakarta rabbaka fee alqurani wahdahu wallaw aala dbarihim nufooran
Nahnu aalamu bima yastamiaoona bihi ith yastamiaoona ilayka waith hum najwa ith yaqoolu alththalimoona in tattabiaoona illa rajulan ashooran
Onthur kayfa daraboo laka alamthala fadalloo fala yastateeaoona sabeelan
Waqaloo aitha kunna aithaman warufatan ainna lamabaoothoona khalqan jadeedan
Qul koonoo hijaratan aw hadeedan
Aw khalqan mimma yakburu fee sudoorikum fasayaqooloona man yuaeeduna quli allathee fatarakum awwala marratin fasayunghidoona ilayka uoosahum wayaqooloona mata huwa qul aasa an yakoona qareeban
Yawma yadaookum fatastajeeboona bihamdihi watathunnoona in labithtum illa qaleelan
Waqul liaibadee yaqooloo allatee hiya ahsanu inna alshshaytana yanzaghu baynahum inna alshshaytana kana lilinsani aaduwwan mubeenan
Rabbukum aalamu bikum in yasha yarhamkum aw in yasha yuaaththibkum wama arsalnaka aalayhim wakeelan
Warabbuka aalamu biman fee alssamawati waalardi walaqad faddalna baada alnnabiyyeena aala baadin waatayna dawooda zabooran
Quli odau allatheena zaaamtum min doonihi fala yamlikoona kashfa alddurri aankum wala tahweelan
Olaika allatheena yadaoona yabtaghoona ila rabbihimu alwaseelata ayyuhum aqrabu wayarjoona rahmatahu wayakhafoona aathabahu inna athaba rabbika kana mahthooran
Wain min qaryatin illa nahnu muhlikooha qabla yawmi alqiyamati aw muaaththibooha aathaban shadeedan kana thalika fee alkitabi mastooran
Wama manaaana an nursila bialayati illa an kaththaba biha alawwaloona waatayna thamooda alnnaqata mubsiratan fathalamoo biha wama ursilu bialayati illa takhweefan
Waith qulna laka inna rabbaka ahata bialnnasi wama jaaalna alrruya allatee araynaka illa fitnatan lilnnasi waalshshajarata almalaoonata ee alqurani wanukhawwifuhum fama yazeeduhum illa tughyanan kabeeran
Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa qala aasjudu liman khalaqta teenan
Qala araaytaka hatha allathee karramta aalayya lain akhkhartani ila yawmi alqiyamati laahtanikanna thurriyyatahu illa qaleelan
Qala ithhab faman tabiaaka minhum fainna jahannama jazaokum jazaan mawfooran
Waistafziz mani istataata minhum bisawtika waajlib aalayhim bikhaylika warajlika washarikhum fee alamwali waalawladi waaidhum wama aaiduhumu alshshaytanu illa ghurooran
Inna aibadee laysa laka aalayhim sultanun wakafa birabbika wakeelan
Rabbukumu allathee yuzjee lakumu alfulka fee albahri litabtaghoo min fadlihi innahu kana bikum raheeman
Waitha massakumu alddurru fee albahri dalla man tadaoona illa iyyahu falamma najjakum ila albarri aaradtum wakana alinsanu kafooran
Afaamintum an yakhsifa bikum janiba albarri aw yursila aalaykum hasiban thumma la tajidoo lakum wakeelan
Am amintum an yuaeedakum feehi taratan okhra fayursila aalaykum qasifan mina alrreehi fayughriqakum bima kafartum thumma la tajidoo akum aalayna bihi tabeeaan
Walaqad karramna banee adama wahamalnahum fee albarri waalbahri warazaqnahum mina alttayyibati wafaddalnahum aala katheerin mimman halaqna tafdeelan
Yawma nadaoo kulla onasin biimamihim faman ootiya kitabahu biyameenihi faolaika yaqraoona kitabahum wala yuthlamoona fateelan
Waman kana fee hathihi aama fahuwa fee alakhirati aama waadallu sabeelan
Wain kadoo layaftinoonaka aani allathee awhayna ilayka litaftariya aalayna ghayrahu waithan laittakhathooka khaleelan
Walawla an thabbatnaka laqad kidta tarkanu ilayhim shayan qaleelan
Ithan laathaqnaka diafa alhayati wadiafa almamati thumma la tajidu laka aalayna naseeran
Wain kadoo layastafizzoonaka mina alardi liyukhrijooka minha waithan la yalbathoona khilafaka illa qaleelan
Sunnata man qad arsalna qablaka min rusulina wala tajidu lisunnatina tahweelan
Aqimi alssalata lidulooki alshshamsi ila ghasaqi allayli waqurana alfajri inna qurana alfajri kana mashhoodan
Wamina allayli fatahajjad bihi nafilatan laka aasa an yabaathaka rabbuka maqaman mahmoodan
Waqul rabbi adkhilnee mudkhala sidqin waakhrijnee mukhraja sidqin waijaal lee min ladunka sultanan naseeran
Waqul jaa alhaqqu wazahaqa albatilu inna albatila kana zahooqan
Wanunazzilu mina alqurani ma huwa shifaon warahmatun lilmumineena wala yazeedu alththalimeena illa khasaran
Waitha anaamna aala alinsani aarada wanaa bijanibihi waitha massahu alshsharru kana yaoosan
Qul kullun yaamalu aala shakilatihi farabbukum aalamu biman huwa ahda sabeelan
Wayasaloonaka aani alrroohi quli alrroohu min amri rabbee wama ooteetum mina alailmi illa qaleelan
Walain shina lanathhabanna biallathee awhayna ilayka thumma la tajidu laka bihi aalayna wakeelan
Illa rahmatan min rabbika inna fadlahu kana aalayka kabeeran
Qul laini ijtamaaati alinsu waaljinnu aala an yatoo bimithli hatha alqurani la yatoona bimithlihi walaw kana baaduhum libaadin thaheeran
Walaqad sarrafna lilnnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin faaba aktharu alnnasi illa kufooran
Waqaloo lan numina laka hatta tafjura lana mina alardi yanbooaan
Aw takoona laka jannatun min nakheelin waainabin fatufajjira alanhara khilalaha tafjeeran
Aw tusqita alssamaa kama zaaamta aalayna kisafan aw tatiya biAllahi waalmalaikati qabeelan
Aw yakoona laka baytun min zukhrufin aw tarqa fee alssamai walan numina liruqiyyika hatta tunazzila aalayna kitaban naqraohu qul ubhana rabbee hal kuntu illa basharan rasoolan
Wama manaaa alnnasa an yuminoo ith jaahumu alhuda illa an qaloo abaaatha Allahu basharan rasoolan
Qul law kana fee alardi malaikatun yamshoona mutmainneena lanazzalna aalayhim mina alssamai malakan rasoolan
Qul kafa biAllahi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum innahu kana biaibadihi khabeeran baseeran
Waman yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadi waman yudlil falan tajida lahum awliyaa min doonihi wanahshuruhum yawma alqiyamati aala wujoohihim umyan wabukman wasumman mawahum jahannamu kullama khabat zidnahum saaeeran
Thalika jazaohum biannahum kafaroo biayatina waqaloo aitha kunna aithaman warufatan ainna lamabaoothoona khalqan jadeedan
Awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda qadirun aala an yakhluqa mithlahum wajaaala lahum ajalan la rayba feehi aaba alththalimoona illa kufooran
Qul law antum tamlikoona khazaina rahmati rabbee ithan laamsaktum khashyata alinfaqi wakana alinsanu qatooran
Walaqad atayna moosa tisaa ayatin bayyinatin faisal banee israeela ith jaahum faqala lahu firaawnu innee laathunnuka ya moosa mashooran
Qala laqad aalimta ma anzala haolai illa rabbu alssamawati waalardi basaira wainnee laathunnuka ya firaawnu mathbooran
Faarada an yastafizzahum mina alardi faaghraqnahu waman maaahu jameeaan
Waqulna min baadihi libanee israeela oskunoo alarda faitha jaa waadu alakhirati jina bikum lafeefan
Wabialhaqqi anzalnahu wabialhaqqi nazala wama arsalnaka illa mubashshiran wanatheeran
Waquranan faraqnahu litaqraahu aala alnnasi aala mukthin wanazzalnahu tanzeelan
Qul aminoo bihi aw la tuminoo inna allatheena ootoo alailma min qablihi itha yutla aalayhim yakhirroona lilathqani sujjadan
Wayaqooloona subhana rabbina in kana waadu rabbina lamafaoolan
Wayakhirroona lilathqani yabkoona wayazeeduhum khushooaan
Quli odaoo Allaha awi odaoo alrrahmana ayyan ma tadaoo falahu alasmao alhusna wala tajhar bisalatika wala tukhafit biha waibtaghi bayna halika sabeelan
Waquli alhamdu lillahi allathee lam yattakhith waladan walam yakun lahu shareekun fee almulki walam yakun lahu waliyyun mina alththulli akabbirhu takbeeran
Alhamdu lillahi allathee anzala aala aabdihi alkitaba walam yajaal lahu aiwajan
Qayyiman liyunthira basan shadeedan min ladunhu wayubashshira almumineena allatheena yaamaloona alssalihati anna lahum ajran hasanan
Makitheena feehi abadan
Wayunthira allatheena qaloo ittakhatha Allahu waladan
Ma lahum bihi min ailmin wala liabaihim kaburat kalimatan takhruju min afwahihim in yaqooloona illa kathiban
Falaaallaka bakhiaun nafsaka aala atharihim in lam yuminoo bihatha alhadeethi asafan
Inna jaaalna ma aala alardi zeenatan laha linabluwahum ayyuhum ahsanu aamalan
Wainna lajaailoona ma aalayha saaeedan juruzan
Am hasibta anna ashaba alkahfi waalrraqeemi kanoo min ayatina aajaban
Ith awa alfityatu ila alkahfi faqaloo rabbana atina min ladunka rahmatan wahayyi lana min amrina rashadan
Fadarabna aala athanihim fee alkahfi sineena aadadan
Thumma baaathnahum linaalama ayyu alhizbayni ahsa lima labithoo amadan
Nahnu naqussu aalayka nabaahum bialhaqqi innahum fityatun amanoo birabbihim wazidnahum hudan
Warabatna aala quloobihim ith qamoo faqaloo rabbuna rabbu alssamawati waalardi lan nadauwa min doonihi ilahan laqad qulna ithan shatatan
Haolai qawmuna ittakhathoo min doonihi alihatan lawla yatoona aalayhim bisultanin bayyinin faman athlamu mimmani iftara aala Allahi athiban
Waithi iatazaltumoohum wama yaabudoona illa Allaha fawoo ila alkahfi yanshur lakum rabbukum min rahmatihi wayuhayyi lakum min amrikum irfaqan
Watara alshshamsa itha talaaat tazawaru aan kahfihim thata alyameeni waitha gharabat taqriduhum thata alshshimali wahum fee fajwatin inhu thalika min ayati Allahi man yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadi waman yudlil falan tajida lahu waliyyan murshidan
Watahsabuhum ayqathan wahum ruqoodun wanuqallibuhum thata alyameeni wathata alshshimali wakalbuhum basitun thiraaayhi bialwaseedi lawi ttalaata aalayhim lawallayta minhum firaran walamulita minhum ruaban
Wakathalika baaathnahum liyatasaaloo baynahum qala qailun minhum kam labithtum qaloo labithna yawman aw baada yawmin qaloo rabbukum aalamu bima labithtum faibaathoo ahadakum biwariqikum hathihi ila almadeenati falyanthur ayyuha azka taaaman falyatikum birizqin minhu alyatalattaf wala yushairanna bikum ahadan
Innahum in yathharoo aalaykum yarjumookum aw yuaeedookum fee millatihim walan tuflihoo ithan abadan
Wakathalika aatharna aalayhim liyaalamoo anna waada Allahi haqqun waanna alsaaata la rayba feeha ith yatanazaaoona baynahum amrahum aqaloo ibnoo aalayhim bunyanan rabbuhum aalamu bihim qala allatheena ghalaboo aala amrihim lanattakhithanna aalayhim masjidan
Sayaqooloona thalathatun rabiauhum kalbuhum wayaqooloona khamsatun sadisuhum kalbuhum rajman bialghaybi wayaqooloona sabaatun wathaminuhum kalbuhum qul rabbee aalamu biaiddatihim ma yaalamuhum illa qaleelun fala tumari feehim illa miraan thahiran wala tastafti eehim minhum ahadan
Wala taqoolanna lishayin innee faailun thalika ghadan
Illa an yashaa Allahu waothkur rabbaka itha naseeta waqul aasa an yahdiyani rabbee liaqraba min hatha rashadan
Walabithoo fee kahfihim thalatha miatin sineena waizdadoo tisaan
Quli Allahu aalamu bima labithoo lahu ghaybu alssamawati waalardi absir bihi waasmia ma lahum min doonihi min waliyyin wala yushriku ee hukmihi ahadan
Waotlu ma oohiya ilayka min kitabi rabbika la mubaddila likalimatihi walan tajida min doonihi multahadan
Waisbir nafsaka maaa allatheena yadaoona rabbahum bialghadati waalaashiyyi yureedoona wajhahu wala taadu aaynaka aanhum tureedu zeenata lhayati alddunya wala tutia man aghfalna qalbahu aan thikrina waittabaaa hawahu wakana amruhu furutan
Waquli alhaqqu min rabbikum faman shaa falyumin waman shaa falyakfur inna aatadna lilththalimeena naran ahata bihim suradiquha wain astagheethoo yughathoo bimain kaalmuhli yashwee alwujooha bisa alshsharabu wasaat murtafaqan
Inna allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati inna la nudeeau ajra man ahsana aamalan
Olaika lahum jannatu aadnin tajree min tahtihimu alanharu yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin wayalbasoona thiyaban khudran min undusin waistabraqin muttakieena feeha aala alaraiki niama alththawabu wahasunat murtafaqan
Waidrib lahum mathalan rajulayni jaaalna liahadihima jannatayni min aanabin wahafafnahuma binakhlin wajaaalna baynahuma zaraan
Kilta aljannatayni atat okulaha walam tathlim minhu shayan wafajjarna khilalahuma naharan
Wakana lahu thamarun faqala lisahibihi wahuwa yuhawiruhu ana aktharu minka malan waaaazzu nafaran
Wadakhala jannatahu wahuwa thalimun linafsihi qala ma athunnu an tabeeda hathihi abadan
Wama athunnu alssaaata qaimatan walain rudidtu ila rabbee laajidanna khayran minha munqalaban
Qala lahu sahibuhu wahuwa yuhawiruhu akafarta biallathee khalaqaka min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma sawwaka rajulan
Lakinna huwa Allahu rabbee wala oshriku birabbee ahadan
Walawla ith dakhalta jannataka qulta ma shaa Allahu la quwwata illa biAllahi in tarani ana aqalla minka malan wawaladan
Faaasa rabbee an yutiyani khayran min jannatika wayursila aalayha husbanan mina alssamai fatusbiha saaeedan zalaqan
Aw yusbiha maoha ghawran falan tastateeaa lahu talaban
Waoheeta bithamarihi faasbaha yuqallibu kaffayhi aala ma anfaqa feeha wahiya khawiyatun aala aurooshiha wayaqoolu ya laytanee lam shrik birabbee ahadan
Walam takun lahu fiatun yansuroonahu min dooni Allahi wama kana muntasiran
Hunalika alwalayatu lillahi alhaqqi huwa khayrun thawaban wakhayrun auqban
Waidrib lahum mathala alhayati alddunya kamain anzalnahu mina alssamai faikhtalata bihi nabatu alardi faasbaha hasheeman tathroohu lrriyahu wakana Allahu aala kulli shayin muqtadiran
Almalu waalbanoona zeenatu alhayati alddunya waalbaqiyatu alssalihatu khayrun ainda rabbika thawaban wakhayrun amalan
Wayawma nusayyiru aljibala watara alarda barizatan wahasharnahum falam nughadir minhum ahadan
Waauridoo aala rabbika saffan laqad jitumoona kama khalaqnakum awwala marratin bal zaaamtum allan najaala lakum mawaidan
Wawudiaa alkitabu fatara almujrimeena mushfiqeena mimma feehi wayaqooloona ya waylatana ma lihatha alkitabi la yughadiru sagheeratan ala kabeeratan illa ahsaha wawajadoo ma aamiloo hadiran wala yathlimu rabbuka ahadan
Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa kana mina aljinni fafasaqa aan amri rabbihi afatattakhithoonahu athurriyyatahu awliyaa min doonee wahum lakum aaduwwun bisa lilththalimeena badalan
Ma ashhadtuhum khalqa alssamawati waalardi wala khalqa anfusihim wama kuntu muttakhitha almudilleena aadudan
Wayawma yaqoolu nadoo shurakaiya allatheena zaaamtum fadaaawhum falam yastajeeboo lahum wajaaalna baynahum mawbiqan
Waraa almujrimoona alnnara fathannoo annahum muwaqiaooha walam yajidoo aanha masrifan
Walaqad sarrafna fee hatha alqurani lilnnasi min kulli mathalin wakana alinsanu akthara shayin jadalan
Wama manaaa alnnasa an yuminoo ith jaahumu alhuda wayastaghfiroo rabbahum illa an tatiyahum sunnatu alawwaleena aw yatiyahumu alaathabu ubulan
Wama nursilu almursaleena illa mubashshireena wamunthireena wayujadilu allatheena kafaroo bialbatili liyudhidoo bihi alhaqqa aittakhathoo ayatee wama onthiroo huzuwan
Waman athlamu mimman thukkira biayati rabbihi faaarada aanha wanasiya ma qaddamat yadahu inna jaaalna aala quloobihim akinnatan an afqahoohu wafee athanihim waqran wain tadauhum ila alhuda falan yahtadoo ithan abadan
Warabbuka alghafooru thoo alrrahmati law yuakhithuhum bima kasaboo laaajjala lahumu alaathaba bal lahum mawaidun lan yajidoo min oonihi mawilan
Watilka alqura ahlaknahum lamma thalamoo wajaaalna limahlikihim mawaidan
Waith qala moosa lifatahu la abrahu hatta ablugha majmaaa albahrayni aw amdiya huquban
Falamma balagha majmaaa baynihima nasiya hootahuma faittakhatha sabeelahu fee albahri saraban
Falamma jawaza qala lifatahu atina ghadaana laqad laqeena min safarina hatha nasaban
Qala araayta ith awayna ila alssakhrati fainnee naseetu alhoota wama ansaneehu illa alshshaytanu an athkurahu waittakhatha sabeelahu ee albahri aajaban
Qala thalika ma kunna nabghi fairtadda aala atharihima qasasan
Fawajada aabdan min aibadina ataynahu rahmatan min aindina waaallamnahu min ladunna ailman
Qala lahu moosa hal attabiauka aala an tuaallimani mimma aullimta rushdan
Qala innaka lan tastateeaa maaiya sabran
Wakayfa tasbiru aala ma lam tuhit bihi khubran
Qala satajidunee in shaa Allahu sabiran wala aasee laka amran
Qala faini ittabaatanee fala tasalnee aan shayin hatta ohditha laka minhu thikran
Faintalaqa hatta itha rakiba fee alssafeenati kharaqaha qala akharaqtaha litughriqa ahlaha laqad jita shayan imran
Qala alam aqul innaka lan tastateeaa maaiya sabran
Qala la tuakhithnee bima naseetu wala turhiqnee min amree ausran
Faintalaqa hatta itha laqiya ghulaman faqatalahu qala aqatalta nafsan zakiyyatan bighayri nafsin laqad jita shayan nukran
Qala alam aqul laka innaka lan tastateeaa maaiya sabran
Qala in saaltuka aan shayin baadaha fala tusahibnee qad balaghta min ladunnee authran
Faintalaqa hatta itha ataya ahla qaryatin istataama ahlaha faabaw an yudayyifoohuma fawajada feeha jidaran yureedu an yanqadda aaqamahu qala law shita laittakhathta aalayhi ajran
Qala hatha firaqu baynee wabaynika saonabbioka bitaweeli ma lam tastatia aalayhi sabran
Amma alssafeenatu fakanat limasakeena yaamaloona fee albahri faaradtu an aaeebaha wakana waraahum malikun yakhuthu kulla safeenatin hasban
Waamma alghulamu fakana abawahu muminayni fakhasheena an yurhiqahuma tughyanan wakufran
Faaradna an yubdilahuma rabbuhuma khayran minhu zakatan waaqraba ruhman
Waamma aljidaru fakana lighulamayni yateemayni fee almadeenati wakana tahtahu kanzun lahuma wakana aboohuma salihan faarada rabbuka an ablugha ashuddahuma wayastakhrija kanzahuma rahmatan min rabbika wama faaaltuhu aan amree thalika taweelu ma lam tastia aalayhi sabran
Wayasaloonaka aan thee alqarnayni qul saatloo aalaykum minhu thikran
Inna makkanna lahu fee alardi waataynahu min kulli shayin sababan
Faatbaaa sababan
Hatta itha balagha maghriba alshshamsi wajadaha taghrubu fee aaynin hamiatin wawajada aindaha qawman qulna ya tha alqarnayni imma an uaaththiba waimma an tattakhitha feehim husnan
Qala amma man thalama fasawfa nuaaththibuhu thumma yuraddu ila rabbihi fayuaaththibuhu aathaban nukran
Waamma man amana waaamila salihan falahu jazaan alhusna wasanaqoolu lahu min amrina yusran
Thumma atbaaa sababan
Hatta itha balagha matliaa alshshamsi wajadaha tatluau aala qawmin lam najaal lahum min dooniha sitran
Kathalika waqad ahatna bima ladayhi khubran
Thumma atbaaa sababan
Hatta itha balagha bayna alssaddayni wajada min doonihima qawman la yakadoona yafqahoona qawlan
Qaloo ya tha alqarnayni inna yajooja wamajooja mufsidoona fee alardi fahal najaalu laka kharjan aala an tajaala baynana wabaynahum addan
Qala ma makkannee feehi rabbee khayrun faaaeenoonee biquwwatin ajaal baynakum wabaynahum radman
Atoonee zubara alhadeedi hatta itha sawa bayna alsadafayni qala onfukhoo hatta itha jaaalahu naran qala atoonee ofrigh aalayhi qitran
Fama istaaoo an yathharoohu wama istataaoo lahu naqban
Qala hatha rahmatun min rabbee faitha jaa waadu rabbee jaaalahu dakkaa wakana waadu rabbee haqqan
Watarakna baadahum yawmaithin yamooju fee baadin wanufikha fee alssoori fajamaanahum jamaan
Waaaradna jahannama yawmaithin lilkafireena aardan
Allatheena kanat aayunuhum fee ghitain aan thikree wakanoo la yastateeaoona samaan
Afahasiba allatheena kafaroo an yattakhithoo aibadee min doonee awliyaa inna aatadna jahannama lilkafireena nuzulan
Qul hal nunabbiokum bialakhsareena aamalan
Allatheena dalla saayuhum fee alhayati alddunya wahum yahsaboona annahum yuhsinoona sunaan
Olaika allatheena kafaroo biayati rabbihim waliqaihi fahabitat aamaluhum fala nuqeemu lahum yawma alqiyamati waznan
Thalika jazaohum jahannamu bima kafaroo waittakhathoo ayatee warusulee huzuwan
Inna allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati kanat lahum jannatu alfirdawsi nuzulan
Khalideena feeha la yabghoona aanha hiwalan
Qul law kana albahru midadan likalimati rabbee lanafida albahru qabla an tanfada kalimatu rabbee walaw jina bimithlihi madadan
Qul innama ana basharun mithlukum yooha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun faman kana yarjoo liqaa rabbihi falyaamal aamalan salihan ala yushrik biaibadati rabbihi ahadan
Kafhayaaaynsad
Thikru rahmati rabbika aabdahu zakariyya
Ith nada rabbahu nidaan khafiyyan
Qala rabbi innee wahana alaathmu minnee waishtaaala alrrasu shayban walam akun biduaaika rabbi shaqiyyan
Wainnee khiftu almawaliya min waraee wakanati imraatee aaqiran fahab lee min ladunka waliyyan
Yarithunee wayarithu min ali yaaqooba waijaalhu rabbi radiyyan
Ya zakariyya inna nubashshiruka bighulamin ismuhu yahya lam najaal lahu min qablu samiyyan
Qala rabbi anna yakoonu lee ghulamun wakanati imraatee aaqiran waqad balaghtu mina alkibari aitiyyan
Qala kathalika qala rabbuka huwa aalayya hayyinun waqad khalaqtuka min qablu walam taku shayan
Qala rabbi ijaal lee ayatan qala ayatuka alla tukallima alnnasa thalatha layalin sawiyyan
Fakharaja aala qawmihi mina almihrabi faawha ilayhim an sabbihoo bukratan waaashiyyan
Ya yahya khuthi alkitaba biquwwatin waataynahu alhukma sabiyyan
Wahananan min ladunna wazakatan wakana taqiyyan
Wabarran biwalidayhi walam yakun jabbaran aasiyyan
Wasalamun aalayhi yawma wulida wayawma yamootu wayawma yubaathu hayyan
Waothkur fee alkitabi maryama ithi intabathat min ahliha makanan sharqiyyan
Faittakhathat min doonihim hijaban faarsalna ilayha roohana fatamaththala laha basharan sawiyyan
Qalat innee aaoothu bialrrahmani minka in kunta taqiyyan
Qala innama ana rasoolu rabbiki liahaba laki ghulaman zakiyyan
Qalat anna yakoonu lee ghulamun walam yamsasnee basharun walam aku baghiyyan
Qala kathaliki qala rabbuki huwa aalayya hayyinun walinajaalahu ayatan lilnnasi warahmatan minna wakana amran maqdiyyan
Fahamalathu faintabathat bihi makanan qasiyyan
Faajaaha almakhadu ila jithai alnnakhlati qalat ya laytanee mittu qabla hatha wakuntu nasyan mansiyyan
Fanadaha min tahtiha alla tahzanee qad jaaala rabbuki tahtaki sariyyan
Wahuzzee ilayki bijithai alnnakhlati tusaqit aalayki rutaban janiyyan
Fakulee waishrabee waqarree aaynan faimma tarayinna mina albashari ahadan faqoolee innee nathartu lilrrahmani sawman falan okallima lyawma insiyyan
Faatat bihi qawmaha tahmiluhu qaloo ya maryamu laqad jiti shayan fariyyan
Ya okhta haroona ma kana abooki imraa sawin wama kanat ommuki baghiyyan
Faasharat ilayhi qaloo kayfa nukallimu man kana fee almahdi sabiyyan
Qala innee aabdu Allahi ataniya alkitaba wajaaalanee nabiyyan
Wajaaalanee mubarakan ayna ma kuntu waawsanee bialssalati waalzzakati ma dumtu hayyan
Wabarran biwalidatee walam yajaalnee jabbaran shaqiyyan
Waalssalamu aalayya yawma wulidtu wayawma amootu wayawma obaathu hayyan
Thalika aeesa ibnu maryama qawla alhaqqi allathee feehi yamtaroona
Ma kana lillahi an yattakhitha min waladin subhanahu itha qada amran fainnama yaqoolu lahu kun fayakoonu
Wainna Allaha rabbee warabbukum faoabudoohu hatha siratun mustaqeemun
Faikhtalafa alahzabu min baynihim fawaylun lillatheena kafaroo min mashhadi yawmin aatheemin
Asmia bihim waabsir yawma yatoonana lakini alththalimoona alyawma fee dalalin mubeenin
Waanthirhum yawma alhasrati ith qudiya alamru wahum fee ghaflatin wahum la yuminoona
Inna nahnu narithu alarda waman aalayha wailayna yurjaaoona
Waothkur fee alkitabi ibraheema innahu kana siddeeqan nabiyyan
Ith qala liabeehi ya abati lima taabudu ma la yasmaau wala yubsiru wala yughnee aanka shayan
Ya abati innee qad jaanee mina alailmi ma lam yatika faittabianee ahdika siratan sawiyyan
Ya abati la taabudi alshshaytana inna alshshaytana kana lilrrahmani aasiyyan
Ya abati innee akhafu an yamassaka aathabun mina alrrahmani fatakoona lilshshyatani waliyyan
Qala araghibun anta aan alihatee ya ibraheemu lain lam tantahi laarjumannaka waohjurnee maliyyan
Qala salamun aalayka saastaghfiru laka rabbee innahu kana bee hafiyyan
Waaatazilukum wama tadaoona min dooni Allahi waadaoo rabbee aasa alla akoona biduaai rabbee shaqiyyan
Falamma iatazalahum wama yaabudoona min dooni Allahi wahabna lahu ishaqa wayaaqooba wakullan jaaalna nabiyyan
Wawahabna lahum min rahmatina wajaaalna lahum lisana sidqin aaliyyan
Waothkur fee alkitabi moosa innahu kana mukhlasan wakana rasoolan nabiyyan
Wanadaynahu min janibi alttoori alaymani waqarrabnahu najiyyan
Wawahabna lahu min rahmatina akhahu haroona nabiyyan
Waothkur fee alkitabi ismaaeela innahu kana sadiqa alwaadi wakana rasoolan nabiyyan
Wakana yamuru ahlahu bialssalati waalzzakati wakana ainda rabbihi mardiyyan
Waothkur fee alkitabi idreesa innahu kana siddeeqan nabiyyan
Warafaanahu makanan aaliyyan
Olaika allatheena anaama Allahu aalayhim mina alnnabiyyeena min thurriyyati adama wamimman hamalna maaa noohin wamin thurriyyati braheema waisraeela wamimman hadayna waijtabayna itha tutla aalayhim ayatu alrrahmani kharroo sujjadan wabukiyyan
Fakhalafa min baadihim khalfun adaaoo alssalata waittabaaoo alshshahawati fasawfa yalqawna ghayyan
Illa man taba waamana waaamila salihan faolaika yadkhuloona aljannata wala yuthlamoona shayan
Jannati aadnin allatee waaada alrrahmanu aibadahu bialghaybi innahu kana waaduhu matiyyan
La yasmaaoona feeha laghwan illa salaman walahum rizquhum feeha bukratan waaashiyyan
Tilka aljannatu allatee noorithu min aibadina man kana taqiyyan
Wama natanazzalu illa biamri rabbika lahu ma bayna aydeena wama khalfana wama bayna thalika wama kana rabbuka nasiyyan
Rabbu alssamawati waalardi wama baynahuma faoabudhu waistabir liaibadatihi hal taalamu lahu samiyyan
Wayaqoolu alinsanu aitha ma mittu lasawfa okhraju hayyan
Awala yathkuru alinsanu anna khalaqnahu min qablu walam yaku shayan
Fawarabbika lanahshurannahum waalshshayateena thumma lanuhdirannahum hawla jahannama jithiyyan
Thumma lananziaanna min kulli sheeaatin ayyuhum ashaddu aala alrrahmani aitiyyan
Thumma lanahnu aalamu biallatheena hum awla biha siliyyan
Wain minkum illa wariduha kana aala rabbika hatman maqdiyyan
Thumma nunajjee allatheena ittaqaw wanatharu alththalimeena feeha jithiyyan
Waitha tutla aalayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qala allatheena kafaroo lillatheena amanoo ayyu alfareeqayni khayrun maqaman waahsanu nadiyyan
Wakam ahlakna qablahum min qarnin hum ahsanu athathan wariyan
Qul man kana fee alddalalati falyamdud lahu alrrahmanu maddan hatta itha raaw ma yooaadoona imma alaathaba waimma alssaaata asayaalamoona man huwa sharrun makanan waadaafu jundan
Wayazeedu Allahu allatheena ihtadaw hudan waalbaqiyatu alssalihatu khayrun ainda rabbika thawaban wakhayrun maraddan
Afaraayta allathee kafara biayatina waqala laootayanna malan wawaladan
Attalaaa alghayba ami ittakhatha ainda alrrahmani aahdan
Kalla sanaktubu ma yaqoolu wanamuddu lahu mina alaathabi maddan
Wanarithuhu ma yaqoolu wayateena fardan
Waittakhathoo min dooni Allahi alihatan liyakoonoo lahum aizzan
Kalla sayakfuroona biaibadatihim wayakoonoona aalayhim diddan
Alam tara anna arsalna alshshayateena aala alkafireena taozzuhum azzan
Fala taajal aalayhim innama naauddu lahum aaddan
Yawma nahshuru almuttaqeena ila alrrahmani wafdan
Wanasooqu almujrimeena ila jahannama wirdan
La yamlikoona alshshafaaata illa mani ittakhatha ainda alrrahmani aahdan
Waqaloo ittakhatha alrrahmanu waladan
Laqad jitum shayan iddan
Takadu alssamawatu yatafattarna minhu watanshaqqu alardu watakhirru aljibalu haddan
An daaaw lilrrahmani waladan
Wama yanbaghee lilrrahmani an yattakhitha waladan
In kullu man fee alssamawati waalardi illa atee alrrahmani aabdan
Laqad ahsahum waaaddahum aaddan
Wakulluhum ateehi yawma alqiyamati fardan
Inna allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati sayajaalu lahumu alrrahmanu wuddan
Fainnama yassarnahu bilisanika litubashshira bihi almuttaqeena watunthira bihi qawman luddan

Taha
Ma anzalna aalayka alqurana litashqa
Illa tathkiratan liman yakhsha
Tanzeelan mimman khalaqa alarda waalssamawati alaula
Alrrahmanu aala alaarshi istawa
Lahu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wama baynahuma wama tahta alththara
Wain tajhar bialqawli fainnahu yaalamu alssirra waakhfa
Allahu la ilaha illa huwa lahu alasmao alhusna
Wahal ataka hadeethu moosa
Ith raa naran faqala liahlihi omkuthoo innee anastu naran laaallee ateekum minha biqabasin aw ajidu aala alnnari hudan
Falamma ataha noodiya ya moosa
Innee ana rabbuka faikhlaa naalayka innaka bialwadi almuqaddasi tuwan
Waana ikhtartuka faistamia lima yooha
Innanee ana Allahu la ilaha illa ana faoabudnee waaqimi alssalata lithikree
Inna alssaaata atiyatun akadu okhfeeha litujza kullu nafsin bima tasaa
Fala yasuddannaka aanha man la yuminu biha waittabaaa hawahu fatarda
Wama tilka biyameenika ya moosa
Qala hiya aasaya atawakkao aalayha waahushshu biha aala ghanamee waliya feeha maaribu okhra
Qala alqiha ya moosa
Faalqaha faitha hiya hayyatun tasaa
Qala khuthha wala takhaf sanuaeeduha seerataha aloola
Waodmum yadaka ila janahika takhruj baydaa min ghayri sooin ayatan okhra
Linuriyaka min ayatina alkubra
Ithhab ila firaawna innahu tagha
Qala rabbi ishrah lee sadree
Wayassir lee amree
Waohlul auqdatan min lisanee
Yafqahoo qawlee
Waijaal lee wazeeran min ahlee
Haroona akhee
Oshdud bihi azree
Waashrikhu fee amree
Kay nusabbihaka katheeran
Wanathkuraka katheeran
Innaka kunta bina baseeran
Qala qad ooteeta sulaka ya moosa
Walaqad mananna aalayka marratan okhra
Ith awhayna ila ommika ma yooha
Ani iqthifeehi fee alttabooti faiqthifeehi fee alyammi falyulqihi alyammu bialssahili yakhuthhu aaduwwun lee waaaduwwun lahu waalqaytu alayka mahabbatan minnee walitusnaaa aala aaynee
Ith tamshee okhtuka fataqoolu hal adullukum aala man yakfuluhu farajaanaka ila ommika kay taqarra aaynuha wala tahzana waqatalta nafsan anajjaynaka mina alghammi wafatannaka futoonan falabithta sineena fee ahli madyana thumma jita aala qadarin ya moosa
Waistanaatuka linafsee
Ithhab anta waakhooka biayatee wala taniya fee thikree
Ithhaba ila firaawna innahu tagha
Faqoola lahu qawlan layyinan laaallahu yatathakkaru aw yakhsha
Qala rabbana innana nakhafu an yafruta aalayna aw an yatgha
Qala la takhafa innanee maaakuma asmaau waara
Fatiyahu faqoola inna rasoola rabbika faarsil maaana banee israeela wala tuaaththibhum qad jinaka biayatin min rabbika waalssalamu aala ani ittabaaa alhuda
Inna qad oohiya ilayna anna alaathaba aala man kaththaba watawalla
Qala faman rabbukuma ya moosa
Qala rabbuna allathee aata kulla shayin khalqahu thumma hada
Qala fama balu alqurooni aloola
Qala ailmuha ainda rabbee fee kitabin la yadillu rabbee wala yansa
Allathee jaaala lakumu alarda mahdan wasalaka lakum feeha subulan waanzala mina alssamai maan faakhrajna bihi azwajan min nabatin shatta
Kuloo wairaaw anaamakum inna fee thalika laayatin liolee alnnuha
Minha khalaqnakum wafeeha nuaeedukum waminha nukhrijukum taratan okhra
Walaqad araynahu ayatina kullaha fakaththaba waaba
Qala ajitana litukhrijana min ardina bisihrika ya moosa
Falanatiyannaka bisihrin mithlihi faijaal baynana wabaynaka mawaidan la nukhlifuhu nahnu wala anta makanan suwan
Qala mawaidukum yawmu alzzeenati waan yuhshara alnnasu duhan
Fatawalla firaawnu fajamaaa kaydahu thumma ata
Qala lahum moosa waylakum la taftaroo aala Allahi kathiban fayushitakum biaathabin waqad khaba mani iftara
Fatanazaaoo amrahum baynahum waasarroo alnnajwa
Qaloo in hathani lasahirani yureedani an yukhrijakum min ardikum bisihrihima wayathhaba bitareeqatikumu almuthla
Faajmiaoo kaydakum thumma itoo saffan waqad aflaha alyawma mani istaala
Qaloo ya moosa imma an tulqiya waimma an nakoona awwala man alqa
Qala bal alqoo faitha hibaluhum waaisiyyuhum yukhayyalu ilayhi min sihrihim annaha tasaa
Faawjasa fee nafsihi kheefatan moosa
Qulna la takhaf innaka anta alaala
Waalqi ma fee yameenika talqaf ma sanaaoo innama sanaaoo kaydu sahirin wala yuflihu alssahiru haythu ata
Faolqiya alssaharatu sujjadan qaloo amanna birabbi haroona wamoosa
Qala amantum lahu qabla an athana lakum innahu lakabeerukumu allathee aallamakumu alssihra falaoqattiaanna aydiyakum waarjulakum min hilafin walaosallibannakum fee juthooai alnnakhli walataalamunna ayyuna ashaddu aathaban waabqa
Qaloo lan nuthiraka aala ma jaana mina albayyinati waallathee fatarana faiqdi ma anta qadin innama taqdee hathihi alhayata alddunya
Inna amanna birabbina liyaghfira lana khatayana wama akrahtana aalayhi mina alssihri waAllahu khayrun waabqa
Innahu man yati rabbahu mujriman fainna lahu jahannama la yamootu feeha wala yahya
Waman yatihi muminan qad aamila alssalihati faolaika lahumu alddarajatu alaula
Jannatu aadnin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wathalika jazao man tazakka
Walaqad awhayna ila moosa an asri biaibadee faidrib lahum tareeqan fee albahri yabasan la takhafu darakan wala takhsha
Faatbaaahum firaawnu bijunoodihi faghashiyahum mina alyammi ma ghashiyahum
Waadalla firaawnu qawmahu wama hada
Ya banee israeela qad anjaynakum min aaduwwikum wawaaadnakum janiba alttoori alaymana wanazzalna aalaykumu almanna waalssalwa
Kuloo min tayyibati ma razaqnakum wala tatghaw feehi fayahilla aalaykum ghadabee waman yahlil aalayhi ghadabee faqad hawa
Wainnee laghaffarun liman taba waamana waaamila salihan thumma ihtada
Wama aajalaka aan qawmika ya moosa
Qala hum olai aala atharee waaajiltu ilayka rabbi litarda
Qala fainna qad fatanna qawmaka min baadika waadallahumu alssamiriyyu
Farajaaa moosa ila qawmihi ghadbana asifan qala ya qawmi alam yaaidkum rabbukum waadan hasanan afatala aalaykumu alaahdu am aradtum an ahilla aalaykum ghadabun min rabbikum faakhlaftum mawaidee
Qaloo ma akhlafna mawaidaka bimalkina walakinna hummilna awzaran min zeenati alqawmi faqathafnaha fakathalika alqa alssamiriyyu
Faakhraja lahum aijlan jasadan lahu khuwarun faqaloo hatha ilahukum wailahu moosa fanasiya
Afala yarawna alla yarjiau ilayhim qawlan wala yamliku lahum darran wala nafaan
Walaqad qala lahum haroonu min qablu ya qawmi innama futintum bihi wainna rabbakumu alrrahmanu faittabiaoonee waateeaoo amree
Qaloo lan nabraha aalayhi aakifeena hatta yarjiaa ilayna moosa
Qala ya haroonu ma manaaaka ith raaytahum dalloo
Alla tattabiaani afaaasayta amree
Qala ya bna omma la takhuth bilihyatee wala birasee innee khasheetu an taqoola farraqta bayna banee israeela walam tarqub qawlee
Qala fama khatbuka ya samiriyyu
Qala basurtu bima lam yabsuroo bihi faqabadtu qabdatan min athari alrrasooli fanabathtuha wakathalika sawwalat lee nafsee
Qala faithhab fainna laka fee alhayati an taqoola la misasa wainna laka mawaidan lan tukhlafahu waonthur ila ilahika allathee thalta alayhi aakifan lanuharriqannahu thumma lanansifannahu fee alyammi nasfan
Innama ilahukumu Allahu allathee la ilaha illa huwa wasiaa kulla shayin ailman
Kathalika naqussu aalayka min anbai ma qad sabaqa waqad ataynaka min ladunna thikran
Man aarada aanhu fainnahu yahmilu yawma alqiyamati wizran
Khalideena feehi wasaa lahum yawma alqiyamati himlan
Yawma yunfakhu fee alssoori wanahshuru almujrimeena yawmaithin zurqan
Yatakhafatoona baynahum in labithtum illa aashran
Nahnu aalamu bima yaqooloona ith yaqoolu amthaluhum tareeqatan in labithtum illa yawman
Wayasaloonaka aani aljibali faqul yansifuha rabbee nasfan
Fayatharuha qaaan safsafan
La tara feeha aiwajan wala amtan
Yawmaithin yattabiaoona alddaaiya la aiwaja lahu wakhashaaati alaswatu lilrrahmani fala tasmaau illa hamsan
Yawmaithin la tanfaau alshshafaaatu illa man athina lahu alrrahmanu waradiya lahu qawlan
Yaalamu ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum wala yuheetoona bihi ailman
Waaanati alwujoohu lilhayyi alqayyoomi waqad khaba man hamala thulman
Waman yaamal mina alssalihati wahuwa muminun fala yakhafu thulman wala hadman
Wakathalika anzalnahu quranan aarabiyyan wasarrafna feehi mina alwaaeedi laaallahum yattaqoona aw yuhdithu lahum thikran
Fataaala Allahu almaliku alhaqqu wala taajal bialqurani min qabli an yuqda ilayka wahyuhu waqul rabbi zidnee ailman
Walaqad aahidna ila adama min qablu fanasiya walam najid lahu aazman
Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa aba
Faqulna ya adamu inna hatha aaduwwun laka walizawjika fala yukhrijannakuma mina aljannati fatashqa
Inna laka alla tajooaa feeha wala taara
Waannaka la tathmao feeha wala tadha
Fawaswasa ilayhi alshshaytanu qala ya adamu hal adulluka aala shajarati alkhuldi wamulkin la yabla
Faakala minha fabadat lahuma sawatuhuma watafiqa yakhsifani aalayhima min waraqi aljannati waaasa adamu rabbahu faghawa
Thumma ijtabahu rabbuhu fataba aalayhi wahada
Qala ihbita minha jameeaan baadukum libaadin aaduwwun faimma yatiyannakum minnee hudan famani ittabaaa hudaya fala yadillu wala yashqa
Waman aarada aan thikree fainna lahu maaeeshatan dankan wanahshuruhu yawma alqiyamati aaman
Qala rabbi lima hashartanee aama waqad kuntu baseeran
Qala kathalika atatka ayatuna fanaseetaha wakathalika alyawma tunsa
Wakathalika najzee man asrafa walam yumin biayati rabbihi walaaathabu alakhirati ashaddu waabqa
Afalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakna qablahum mina alqurooni yamshoona fee masakinihim inna fee thalika laayatin liolee alnnuha
Walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika lakana lizaman waajalun musamman
Faisbir aala ma yaqooloona wasabbih bihamdi rabbika qabla tulooai alshshamsi waqabla ghuroobiha wamin anai allayli fasabbih waatrafa lnnahari laaallaka tarda
Wala tamuddanna aaynayka ila ma mattaana bihi azwajan minhum zahrata alhayati alddunya linaftinahum feehi warizqu rabbika khayrun waabqa
Wamur ahlaka bialssalati waistabir aalayha la nasaluka rizqan nahnu narzuquka waalaaqibatu lilttaqwa
Waqaloo lawla yateena biayatin min rabbihi awalam tatihim bayyinatu ma fee alssuhufi aloola
Walaw anna ahlaknahum biaathabin min qablihi laqaloo rabbana lawla arsalta ilayna rasoolan fanattabiaa ayatika min qabli an nathilla anakhza
Qul kullun mutarabbisun fatarabbasoo fasataalamoona man ashabu alssirati alssawiyyi wamani ihtada
Iqtaraba lilnnasi hisabuhum wahum fee ghaflatin muaridoona
Ma yateehim min thikrin min rabbihim muhdathin illa istamaaoohu wahum yalaaboona
Lahiyatan quloobuhum waasarroo alnnajwa allatheena thalamoo hal hatha illa basharun mithlukum afatatoona alssihra waantum tubsiroona
Qala rabbee yaalamu alqawla fee alssamai waalardi wahuwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Bal qaloo adghathu ahlamin bali iftarahu bal huwa shaairun falyatina biayatin kama orsila alawwaloona
Ma amanat qablahum min qaryatin ahlaknaha afahum yuminoona
Wama arsalna qablaka illa rijalan noohee ilayhim faisaloo ahla alththikri in kuntum la taalamoona
Wama jaaalnahum jasadan la yakuloona alttaaama wama kanoo khalideena
Thumma sadaqnahumu alwaada faanjaynahum waman nashao waahlakna almusrifeena
Laqad anzalna ilaykum kitaban feehi thikrukum afala taaqiloona
Wakam qasamna min qaryatin kanat thalimatan waanshana baadaha qawman akhareena
Falamma ahassoo basana itha hum minha yarkudoona
La tarkudoo wairjiaoo ila ma otriftum feehi wamasakinikum laaallakum tusaloona
Qaloo ya waylana inna kunna thalimeena
Fama zalat tilka daawahum hatta jaaalnahum haseedan khamideena
Wama khalaqna alssamaa waalarda wama baynahuma laaibeena
Law aradna an nattakhitha lahwan laittakhathnahu min ladunna in kunna faaileena
Bal naqthifu bialhaqqi aala albatili fayadmaghuhu faitha huwa zahiqun walakumu alwaylu mimma tasifoona
Walahu man fee alssamawati waalardi waman aindahu la yastakbiroona aan aibadatihi wala yastahsiroona
Yusabbihoona allayla waalnnahara la yafturoona
Ami ittakhathoo alihatan mina alardi hum yunshiroona
Law kana feehima alihatun illa Allahu lafasadata fasubhana Allahi rabbi alaarshi aamma yasifoona
La yusalu aamma yafaalu wahum yusaloona
Ami ittakhathoo min doonihi alihatan qul hatoo burhanakum hatha thikru man maaiya wathikru man qablee bal aktharuhum la yaalamoona lhaqqa fahum muaridoona
Wama arsalna min qablika min rasoolin illa noohee ilayhi annahu la ilaha illa ana faoabudooni
Waqaloo ittakhatha alrrahmanu waladan subhanahu bal aibadun mukramoona
La yasbiqoonahu bialqawli wahum biamrihi yaamaloona
Yaalamu ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum wala yashfaaoona illa limani irtada wahum min khashyatihi mushfiqoona
Waman yaqul minhum innee ilahun min doonihi fathalika najzeehi jahannama kathalika najzee alththalimeena
Awalam yara allatheena kafaroo anna alssamawati waalarda kanata ratqan fafataqnahuma wajaaalna mina almai kulla shayin hayyin afala uminoona
Wajaaalna fee alardi rawasiya an tameeda bihim wajaaalna feeha fijajan subulan laaallahum yahtadoona
Wajaaalna alssamaa saqfan mahfoothan wahum aan ayatiha muaridoona
Wahuwa allathee khalaqa allayla waalnnahara waalshshamsa waalqamara kullun fee falakin yasbahoona
Wama jaaalna libasharin min qablika alkhulda afain mitta fahumu alkhalidoona
Kullu nafsin thaiqatu almawti wanablookum bialshsharri waalkhayri fitnatan wailayna turjaaoona
Waitha raaka allatheena kafaroo in yattakhithoonaka illa huzuwan ahatha allathee yathkuru alihatakum wahum bithikri alrrahmani hum afiroona
Khuliqa alinsanu min aajalin saoreekum ayatee fala tastaajiloona
Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwaadu in kuntum sadiqeena
Law yaalamu allatheena kafaroo heena la yakuffoona aan wujoohihimu alnnara wala aan thuhoorihim wala hum yunsaroona
Bal tateehim baghtatan fatabhatuhum fala yastateeaoona raddaha wala hum yuntharoona
Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika fahaqa biallatheena sakhiroo minhum ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Qul man yaklaokum biallayli waalnnahari mina alrrahmani bal hum aan thikri rabbihim muaridoona
Am lahum alihatun tamnaauhum min doonina la yastateeaoona nasra anfusihim wala hum minna yushaboona
Bal mattaana haolai waabaahum hatta tala aalayhimu alaumuru afala yarawna anna natee alarda nanqusuha min atrafiha afahumu alghaliboona
Qul innama onthirukum bialwahyi wala yasmaau alssummu aldduaaa itha ma yuntharoona
Walain massathum nafhatun min aathabi rabbika layaqoolunna ya waylana inna kunna thalimeena
Wanadaau almawazeena alqista liyawmi alqiyamati fala tuthlamu nafsun shayan wain kana mithqala habbatin min khardalin atayna biha akafa bina hasibeena
Walaqad atayna moosa waharoona alfurqana wadiyaan wathikran lilmuttaqeena
Allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bialghaybi wahum mina alssaaati mushfiqoona
Wahatha thikrun mubarakun anzalnahu afaantum lahu munkiroona
Walaqad atayna ibraheema rushdahu min qablu wakunna bihi aalimeena
Ith qala liabeehi waqawmihi ma hathihi alttamatheelu allatee antum laha aakifoona
Qaloo wajadna abaana laha aabideena
Qala laqad kuntum antum waabaokum fee dalalin mubeenin
Qaloo ajitana bialhaqqi am anta mina allaaibeena
Qala bal rabbukum rabbu alssamawati waalardi allathee fatarahunna waana aala thalikum mina alshshahideena
WataAllahi laakeedanna asnamakum baada an tuwalloo mudbireena
Fajaaalahum juthathan illa kabeeran lahum laaallahum ilayhi yarjiaoona
Qaloo man faaala hatha bialihatina innahu lamina alththalimeena
Qaloo samiana fatan yathkuruhum yuqalu lahu ibraheemu
Qaloo fatoo bihi aala aayuni alnnasi laaallahum yashhadoona
Qaloo aanta faaalta hatha bialihatina ya ibraheemu
Qala bal faaalahu kabeeruhum hatha faisaloohum in kanoo yantiqoona
Farajaaoo ila anfusihim faqaloo innakum antumu alththalimoona
Thumma nukisoo aala ruoosihim laqad aalimta ma haolai yantiqoona
Qala afataabudoona min dooni Allahi ma la yanfaaukum shayan wala yadurrukum
Offin lakum walima taabudoona min dooni Allahi afala taaqiloona
Qaloo harriqoohu waonsuroo alihatakum in kuntum faaileena
Qulna ya naru koonee bardan wasalaman aala ibraheema
Waaradoo bihi kaydan fajaaalnahumu alakhsareena
Wanajjaynahu walootan ila alardi allatee barakna feeha lilaalameena
Wawahabna lahu ishaqa wayaaqooba nafilatan wakullan jaaalna saliheena
Wajaaalnahum aimmatan yahdoona biamrina waawhayna ilayhim fiala alkhayrati waiqama alssalati waeetaa alzzakati wakanoo lana aabideena
Walootan ataynahu hukman waailman wanajjaynahu mina alqaryati allatee kanat taamalu alkhabaitha innahum kanoo qawma sawin fasiqeena
Waadkhalnahu fee rahmatina innahu mina alssaliheena
Wanoohan ith nada min qablu faistajabna lahu fanajjaynahu waahlahu mina alkarbi alaatheemi
Wanasarnahu mina alqawmi allatheena kaththaboo biayatina innahum kanoo qawma sawin faaghraqnahum ajmaaeena
Wadawooda wasulaymana ith yahkumani fee alharthi ith nafashat feehi ghanamu alqawmi wakunna lihukmihim shahideena
Fafahhamnaha sulaymana wakullan atayna hukman waailman wasakhkharna maaa dawooda aljibala yusabbihna waalttayra wakunna faaileena
Waaallamnahu sanaata laboosin lakum lituhsinakum min basikum fahal antum shakiroona
Walisulaymana alrreeha aasifatan tajree biamrihi ila alardi allatee barakna feeha wakunna bikulli shayin aalimeena
Wamina alshshayateeni man yaghoosoona lahu wayaamaloona aamalan doona thalika wakunna lahum hafitheena
Waayyooba ith nada rabbahu annee massaniya alddurru waanta arhamu alrrahimeena
Faistajabna lahu fakashafna ma bihi min durrin waataynahu ahlahu wamithlahum maaahum rahmatan min aindina wathikra lilaabideena
Waismaaeela waidreesa watha alkifli kullun mina alssabireena
Waadkhalnahum fee rahmatina innahum mina alssaliheena
Watha alnnooni ith thahaba mughadiban fathanna an lan naqdira aalayhi fanada fee alththulumati an la ilaha illa anta subhanaka innee untu mina alththalimeena
Faistajabna lahu wanajjaynahu mina alghammi wakathalika nunjee almumineena
Wazakariyya ith nada rabbahu rabbi la tatharnee fardan waanta khayru alwaritheena
Faistajabna lahu wawahabna lahu yahya waaslahna lahu zawjahu innahum kanoo yusariaoona fee alkhayrati wayadaoonana raghaban warahaban akanoo lana khashiaeena
Waallatee ahsanat farjaha fanafakhna feeha min roohina wajaaalnaha waibnaha ayatan lilaalameena
Inna hathihi ommatukum ommatan wahidatan waana rabbukum faoabudooni
Wataqattaaoo amrahum baynahum kullun ilayna rajiaoona
Faman yaamal mina alssalihati wahuwa muminun fala kufrana lisaayihi wainna lahu katiboona
Waharamun aala qaryatin ahlaknaha annahum la yarjiaoona
Hatta itha futihat yajooju wamajooju wahum min kulli hadabin yansiloona
Waiqtaraba alwaadu alhaqqu faitha hiya shakhisatun absaru allatheena kafaroo ya waylana qad kunna fee ghaflatin min hatha bal kunna halimeena
Innakum wama taabudoona min dooni Allahi hasabu jahannama antum laha waridoona
Law kana haolai alihatan ma waradooha wakullun feeha khalidoona
Lahum feeha zafeerun wahum feeha la yasmaaoona
Inna allatheena sabaqat lahum minna alhusna olaika aanha mubaadoona
La yasmaaoona haseesaha wahum fee ma ishtahat anfusuhum khalidoona
La yahzunuhumu alfazaau alakbaru watatalaqqahumu almalaikatu hatha yawmukumu allathee kuntum tooaadoona
Yawma natwee alssamaa katayyi alssijlli lilkutubi kama badana awwala khalqin nuaeeduhu waadan aalayna inna kunna faaileena
Walaqad katabna fee alzzaboori min baadi alththikri anna alarda yarithuha aibadiya alssalihoona
Inna fee hatha labalaghan liqawmin aabideena
Wama arsalnaka illa rahmatan lilaalameena
Qul innama yooha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun fahal antum muslimoona
Fain tawallaw faqul athantukum aala sawain wain adree aqareebun am baaeedun ma tooaadoona
Innahu yaalamu aljahra mina alqawli wayaalamu ma taktumoona
Wain adree laaallahu fitnatun lakum wamataaun ila heenin
Qala rabbi ohkum bialhaqqi warabbuna alrrahmanu almustaaanu aala ma tasifoona
Ya ayyuha alnnasu ittaqoo rabbakum inna zalzalata alssaaati shayon aatheemun
Yawma tarawnaha tathhalu kullu murdiaatin aamma ardaaat watadaau kullu thati hamlin hamlaha watara alnnasa sukara wama hum bisukara alakinna aathaba Allahi shadeedun
Wamina alnnasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri ailmin wayattabiau kulla shaytanin mareedin
Kutiba aalayhi annahu man tawallahu faannahu yudilluhu wayahdeehi ila aathabi alssaaeeri
Ya ayyuha alnnasu in kuntum fee raybin mina albaathi fainna khalaqnakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma min aalaqatin thumma min mudghatin mukhallaqatin waghayri mukhallaqatin linubayyina lakum wanuqirru fee alarhami ma nashao ila ajalin musamman thumma nukhrijukum tiflan thumma litablughoo ashuddakum waminkum man yutawaffa waminkum man yuraddu ila arthali alaumuri likayla yaalama min baadi ailmin hayan watara alarda hamidatan faitha anzalna aalayha almaa ihtazzat warabat waanbatat min kulli zawjin baheejin
Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waannahu yuhyee almawta waannahu aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Waanna alssaaata atiyatun la rayba feeha waanna Allaha yabaathu man fee alquboori
Wamina alnnasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri ailmin wala hudan wala kitabin muneerin
Thaniya aitfihi liyudilla aan sabeeli Allahi lahu fee alddunya khizyun wanutheequhu yawma alqiyamati aathaba alhareeqi
Thalika bima qaddamat yadaka waanna Allaha laysa bithallamin lilaabeedi
Wamina alnnasi man yaabudu Allaha aala harfin fain asabahu khayrun itmaanna bihi wain asabathu fitnatun inqalaba aala wajhihi khasira lddunya waalakhirata thalika huwa alkhusranu almubeenu
Yadaoo min dooni Allahi ma la yadurruhu wama la yanfaauhu thalika huwa alddalalu albaaeedu
Yadaoo laman darruhu aqrabu min nafaihi labisa almawla walabisa alaasheeru
Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu inna Allaha yafaalu ma yureedu
Man kana yathunnu an lan yansurahu Allahu fee alddunya waalakhirati falyamdud bisababin ila alssamai thumma liyaqtaa falyanthur hal uthhibanna kayduhu ma yagheethu
Wakathalika anzalnahu ayatin bayyinatin waanna Allaha yahdee man yureedu
Inna allatheena amanoo waallatheena hadoo waalssabieena waalnnasara waalmajoosa waallatheena ashrakoo inna Allaha yafsilu baynahum awma alqiyamati inna Allaha aala kulli shayin shaheedun
Alam tara anna Allaha yasjudu lahu man fee alssamawati waman fee alardi waalshshamsu waalqamaru waalnnujoomu waaljibalu waalshshajaru waalddawabbu wakatheerun mina alnnasi wakatheerun haqqa aalayhi alaathabu waman yuhini Allahu fama lahu min mukrimin inna Allaha yafaalu a yashao
Hathani khasmani ikhtasamoo fee rabbihim faallatheena kafaroo quttiaat lahum thiyabun min narin yusabbu min fawqi ruoosihimu alhameemu
Yusharu bihi ma fee butoonihim waaljuloodu
Walahum maqamiau min hadeedin
Kullama aradoo an yakhrujoo minha min ghammin oaeedoo feeha wathooqoo aathaba alhareeqi
Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu yuhallawna feeha min asawira min hahabin waluluan walibasuhum feeha hareerun
Wahudoo ila alttayyibi mina alqawli wahudoo ila sirati alhameedi
Inna allatheena kafaroo wayasuddoona aan sabeeli Allahi waalmasjidi alharami allathee jaaalnahu lilnnasi sawaan alaakifu feehi waalbadi aman yurid feehi biilhadin bithulmin nuthiqhu min aathabin aleemin
Waith bawwana liibraheema makana albayti an la tushrik bee shayan watahhir baytiya lilttaifeena waalqaimeena waalrrukkaai alssujoodi
Waaththin fee alnnasi bialhajji yatooka rijalan waaala kulli damirin yateena min kulli fajjin aameeqin
Liyashhadoo manafiaa lahum wayathkuroo isma Allahi fee ayyamin maaloomatin aala ma razaqahum min baheemati alanaami fakuloo minha aataimoo albaisa alfaqeera
Thumma lyaqdoo tafathahum walyoofoo nuthoorahum walyattawwafoo bialbayti alaateeqi
Thalika waman yuaaththim hurumati Allahi fahuwa khayrun lahu ainda rabbihi waohillat lakumu alanaamu illa ma yutla aalaykum faijtaniboo lrrijsa mina alawthani waijtaniboo qawla alzzoori
Hunafaa lillahi ghayra mushrikeena bihi waman yushrik biAllahi fakaannama kharra mina alssamai fatakhtafuhu alttayru aw tahwee bihi lrreehu fee makanin saheeqin
Thalika waman yuaaththim shaaaira Allahi fainnaha min taqwa alquloobi
Lakum feeha manafiau ila ajalin musamman thumma mahilluha ila albayti alaateeqi
Walikulli ommatin jaaalna mansakan liyathkuroo isma Allahi aala ma razaqahum min baheemati alanaami failahukum ilahun wahidun falahu slimoo wabashshiri almukhbiteena
Allatheena itha thukira Allahu wajilat quloobuhum waalssabireena aala ma asabahum waalmuqeemee alssalati wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona
Waalbudna jaaalnaha lakum min shaaairi Allahi lakum feeha khayrun faothkuroo isma Allahi aalayha sawaffa faitha wajabat junoobuha akuloo minha waataimoo alqaniaa waalmuatarra kathalika sakhkharnaha lakum laaallakum tashkuroona
Lan yanala Allaha luhoomuha wala dimaoha walakin yanaluhu alttaqwa minkum kathalika sakhkharaha lakum litukabbiroo Allaha aala ma adakum wabashshiri almuhsineena
Inna Allaha yudafiau aani allatheena amanoo inna Allaha la yuhibbu kulla khawwanin kafoorin
Othina lillatheena yuqataloona biannahum thulimoo wainna Allaha aala nasrihim laqadeerun
Allatheena okhrijoo min diyarihim bighayri haqqin illa an yaqooloo rabbuna Allahu walawla dafau Allahi alnnasa baadahum bibaadin lahuddimat sawamiau wabiyaaun wasalawatun wamasajidu yuthkaru feeha ismu Allahi katheeran walayansuranna Allahu man yansuruhu inna llaha laqawiyyun aazeezun
Allatheena in makkannahum fee alardi aqamoo alssalata waatawoo alzzakata waamaroo bialmaaroofi wanahaw aani almunkari walillahi aqibatu alomoori
Wain yukaththibooka faqad kaththabat qablahum qawmu noohin waaadun wathamoodu
Waqawmu ibraheema waqawmu lootin
Waashabu madyana wakuththiba moosa faamlaytu lilkafireena thumma akhathtuhum fakayfa kana nakeeri
Fakaayyin min qaryatin ahlaknaha wahiya thalimatun fahiya khawiyatun aala aurooshiha wabirin muaattalatin waqasrin masheedin
Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fatakoona lahum quloobun yaaqiloona biha aw athanun yasmaaoona biha fainnaha la taama alabsaru walakin taama lquloobu allatee fee alssudoori
Wayastaajiloonaka bialaathabi walan yukhlifa Allahu waadahu wainna yawman ainda rabbika kaalfi sanatin mimma taauddoona
Wakaayyin min qaryatin amlaytu laha wahiya thalimatun thumma akhathtuha wailayya almaseeru
Qul ya ayyuha alnnasu innama ana lakum natheerun mubeenun
Faallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareemun
Waallatheena saaaw fee ayatina muaajizeena olaika ashabu aljaheemi
Wama arsalna min qablika min rasoolin wala nabiyyin illa itha tamanna alqa alshshaytanu fee omniyyatihi fayansakhu Allahu ma yulqee lshshaytanu thumma yuhkimu Allahu ayatihi waAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Liyajaala ma yulqee alshshaytanu fitnatan lillatheena fee quloobihim maradun waalqasiyati quloobuhum wainna alththalimeena lafee hiqaqin baaeedin
Waliyaalama allatheena ootoo alailma annahu alhaqqu min rabbika fayuminoo bihi fatukhbita lahu quloobuhum wainna Allaha lahadi llatheena amanoo ila siratin mustaqeemin
Wala yazalu allatheena kafaroo fee miryatin minhu hatta tatiyahumu alssaaatu baghtatan aw yatiyahum aathabu yawmin aaqeemin
Almulku yawmaithin lillahi yahkumu baynahum faallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati fee jannati alnnaaeemi
Waallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina faolaika lahum aathabun muheenun
Waallatheena hajaroo fee sabeeli Allahi thumma qutiloo aw matoo layarzuqannahumu Allahu rizqan hasanan wainna Allaha lahuwa khayru lrraziqeena
Layudkhilannahum mudkhalan yardawnahu wainna Allaha laaaleemun haleemun
Thalika waman aaqaba bimithli ma aooqiba bihi thumma bughiya aalayhi layansurannahu Allahu inna Allaha laaafuwwun ghafoorun
Thalika bianna Allaha yooliju allayla fee alnnahari wayooliju alnnahara fee allayli waanna Allaha sameeaun baseerun
Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waanna ma yadaoona min doonihi huwa albatilu waanna Allaha huwa alaaliyyu alkabeeru
Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina alssamai maan fatusbihu alardu mukhdarratan inna Allaha lateefun khabeerun
Lahu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wainna Allaha lahuwa alghaniyyu alhameedu
Alam tara anna Allaha sakhkhara lakum ma fee alardi waalfulka tajree fee albahri biamrihi wayumsiku alssamaa an taqaaa aala alardi illa iithnihi inna Allaha bialnnasi laraoofun raheemun
Wahuwa allathee ahyakum thumma yumeetukum thumma yuhyeekum inna alinsana lakafoorun
Likulli ommatin jaaalna mansakan hum nasikoohu fala yunaziaunnaka fee alamri waodau ila rabbika innaka laaala hudan mustaqeemin
Wain jadalooka faquli Allahu aalamu bima taamaloona
Allahu yahkumu baynakum yawma alqiyamati feema kuntum feehi takhtalifoona
Alam taalam anna Allaha yaalamu ma fee alssamai waalardi inna thalika fee kitabin inna thalika aala Allahi yaseerun
Wayaabudoona min dooni Allahi ma lam yunazzil bihi sultanan wama laysa lahum bihi ailmun wama lilththalimeena min naseerin
Waitha tutla aalayhim ayatuna bayyinatin taarifu fee wujoohi allatheena kafaroo almunkara yakadoona yastoona biallatheena yatloona alayhim ayatina qul afaonabbiokum bisharrin min thalikum alnnaru waaadaha Allahu allatheena kafaroo wabisa almaseeru
Ya ayyuha alnnasu duriba mathalun faistamiaoo lahu inna allatheena tadaoona min dooni Allahi lan yakhluqoo thubaban walawi ijtamaaoo ahu wain yaslubuhumu alththubabu shayan la yastanqithoohu minhu daaufa alttalibu waalmatloobu
Ma qadaroo Allaha haqqa qadrihi inna Allaha laqawiyyun aazeezun
Allahu yastafee mina almalaikati rusulan wamina alnnasi inna Allaha sameeaun baseerun
Yaalamu ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum waila Allahi turjaau alomooru
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo irkaaoo waosjudoo waoabudoo rabbakum waifaaloo alkhayra laaallakum tuflihoona
Wajahidoo fee Allahi haqqa jihadihi huwa ijtabakum wama jaaala aalaykum fee alddeeni min harajin millata abeekum ibraheema huwa sammakumu almuslimeena min qablu wafee hatha liyakoona alrrasoolu shaheedan aalaykum watakoonoo shuhadaa aala alnnasi faaqeemoo lssalata waatoo alzzakata waiatasimoo biAllahi huwa mawlakum faniama almawla waniama alnnaseeru

Allatheena hum fee salatihim khashiaoona
Waallatheena hum aani allaghwi muaridoona
Waallatheena hum lilzzakati faailoona
Waallatheena hum lifuroojihim hafithoona
Illa aala azwajihim aw ma malakat aymanuhum fainnahum ghayru maloomeena
