Waallatheena hum liamanatihim waaahdihim raaoona
Waallatheena hum aala salawatihim yuhafithoona
Olaika humu alwarithoona
Allatheena yarithoona alfirdawsa hum feeha khalidoona
Walaqad khalaqna alinsana min sulalatin min teenin
Thumma jaaalnahu nutfatan fee qararin makeenin
Thumma khalaqna alnnutfata aalaqatan fakhalaqna alaalaqata mudghatan fakhalaqna almudghata aithaman fakasawna alaithama lahman thumma nshanahu khalqan akhara fatabaraka Allahu ahsanu alkhaliqeena
Thumma innakum baada thalika lamayyitoona
Thumma innakum yawma alqiyamati tubaathoona
Walaqad khalaqna fawqakum sabaa taraiqa wama kunna aani alkhalqi ghafileena
Waanzalna mina alssamai maan biqadarin faaskannahu fee alardi wainna aala thahabin bihi laqadiroona
Faanshana lakum bihi jannatin min nakheelin waaanabin lakum feeha fawakihu katheeratun waminha takuloona
Washajaratan takhruju min toori saynaa tanbutu bialdduhni wasibghin lilakileena
Wainna lakum fee alanaami laaibratan nusqeekum mimma fee butooniha walakum feeha manafiau katheeratun waminha takuloona
Waaalayha waaala alfulki tuhmaloona
Walaqad arsalna noohan ila qawmihi faqala ya qawmi oabudoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaqoona
Faqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi ma hatha illa basharun mithlukum yureedu an yatafaddala aalaykum walaw shaa Allahu aanzala malaikatan ma samiana bihatha fee abaina alawwaleena
In huwa illa rajulun bihi jinnatun fatarabbasoo bihi hatta heenin
Qala rabbi onsurnee bima kaththabooni
Faawhayna ilayhi ani isnaai alfulka biaayunina wawahyina faitha jaa amruna wafara alttannooru faosluk feeha min kullin zawjayni thnayni waahlaka illa man sabaqa aalayhi alqawlu minhum wala tukhatibnee fee allatheena thalamoo innahum mughraqoona
Faitha istawayta anta waman maaaka aala alfulki faquli alhamdu lillahi allathee najjana mina alqawmi alththalimeena
Waqul rabbi anzilnee munzalan mubarakan waanta khayru almunzileena
Inna fee thalika laayatin wain kunna lamubtaleena
Thumma anshana min baadihim qarnan akhareena
Faarsalna feehim rasoolan minhum ani oabudoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaqoona

Waallatheena hum biayati rabbihim yuminoona

Olaika yusariaoona fee alkhayrati wahum laha sabiqoona

Hatta itha akhathna mutrafeehim bialaathabi itha hum yajaroona
La tajaroo alyawma innakum minna la tunsaroona
Qad kanat ayatee tutla aalaykum fakuntum aala aaqabikum tankisoona
Mustakbireena bihi samiran tahjuroona
Afalam yaddabbaroo alqawla am jaahum ma lam yati abaahumu alawwaleena
Am lam yaarifoo rasoolahum fahum lahu munkiroona
Am yaqooloona bihi jinnatun bal jaahum bialhaqqi waaktharuhum lilhaqqi karihoona
Walawi ittabaaa alhaqqu ahwaahum lafasadati alssamawatu waalardu waman feehinna bal ataynahum bithikrihim fahum aan thikrihim muaridoona
Am tasaluhum kharjan fakharaju rabbika khayrun wahuwa khayru alrraziqeena
Wainnaka latadaoohum ila siratin mustaqeemin
Wainna allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati aani alssirati lanakiboona
Walaw rahimnahum wakashafna ma bihim min durrin lalajjoo fee tughyanihim yaamahoona
Walaqad akhathnahum bialaathabi fama istakanoo lirabbihim wama yatadarraaoona
Hatta itha fatahna aalayhim baban tha aathabin shadeedin itha hum feehi mublisoona
Wahuwa allathee anshaa lakumu alssamaa waalabsara waalafidata qaleelan ma tashkuroona
Wahuwa allathee tharaakum fee alardi wailayhi tuhsharoona

Qul limani alardu waman feeha in kuntum taalamoona
Sayaqooloona lillahi qul afala tathakkaroona
Qul man rabbu alssamawati alssabai warabbu alaarshi alaatheemi
Sayaqooloona lillahi qul afala tattaqoona
Qul man biyadihi malakootu kulli shayin wahuwa yujeeru wala yujaru aalayhi in kuntum taalamoona
Sayaqooloona lillahi qul faanna tusharoona

Idfaa biallatee hiya ahsanu alssayyiata nahnu aalamu bima yasifoona
Waqul rabbi aaoothu bika min hamazati alshshayateeni
Waaaoothu bika rabbi an yahdurooni
Hatta itha jaa ahadahumu almawtu qala rabbi irjiaooni
Laaallee aamalu salihan feema taraktu kalla innaha kalimatun huwa qailuha wamin waraihim barzakhun ila yawmi yubaathoona
Faitha nufikha fee alssoori fala ansaba baynahum yawmaithin wala yatasaaloona
Faman thaqulat mawazeenuhu faolaika humu almuflihoona
Waman khaffat mawazeenuhu faolaika allatheena khasiroo anfusahum fee jahannama khalidoona
Talfahu wujoohahumu alnnaru wahum feeha kalihoona
Alam takun ayatee tutla aalaykum fakuntum biha tukaththiboona
Qaloo rabbana ghalabat aalayna shiqwatuna wakunna qawman dalleena
Rabbana akhrijna minha fain audna fainna thalimoona
Qala ikhsaoo feeha wala tukallimooni
Innahu kana fareequn min aibadee yaqooloona rabbana amanna faighfir lana wairhamna waanta khayru alrrahimeena
Faittakhathtumoohum sikhriyyan hatta ansawkum thikree wakuntum minhum tadhakoona
Innee jazaytuhumu alyawma bima sabaroo annahum humu alfaizoona
Qala kam labithtum fee alardi aadada sineena
Qaloo labithna yawman aw baada yawmin faisali alaaddeena
Qala in labithtum illa qaleelan law annakum kuntum taalamoona
Afahasibtum annama khalaqnakum aabathan waannakum ilayna la turjaaoona
Fataaala Allahu almaliku alhaqqu la ilaha illa huwa rabbu alaarshi alkareemi
Waman yadau maaa Allahi ilahan akhara la burhana lahu bihi fainnama hisabuhu ainda rabbihi innahu la yuflihu alkafiroona
Waqul rabbi ighfir wairham waanta khayru alrrahimeena
Sooratun anzalnaha wafaradnaha waanzalna feeha ayatin bayyinatin laaallakum tathakkaroona
Alzzaniyatu waalzzanee faijlidoo kulla wahidin minhuma miata jaldatin wala takhuthkum bihima rafatun fee deeni Allahi in kuntum uminoona biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri walyashhad aathabahuma taifatun mina almumineena
Alzzanee la yankihu illa zaniyatan aw mushrikatan waalzzaniyatu la yankihuha illa zanin aw mushrikun wahurrima thalika aala almumineena
Waallatheena yarmoona almuhsanati thumma lam yatoo biarbaaati shuhadaa faijlidoohum thamaneena jaldatan wala taqbaloo lahum shahadatan badan waolaika humu alfasiqoona
Illa allatheena taboo min baadi thalika waaslahoo fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Waallatheena yarmoona azwajahum walam yakun lahum shuhadao illa anfusuhum fashahadatu ahadihim arbaau shahadatin biAllahi innahu lamina lssadiqeena
Waalkhamisatu anna laanata Allahi aalayhi in kana mina alkathibeena
Wayadrao aanha alaathaba an tashhada arbaaa shahadatin biAllahi innahu lamina alkathibeena
Waalkhamisata anna ghadaba Allahi aalayha in kana mina alssadiqeena
Walawla fadlu Allahi aalaykum warahmatuhu waanna Allaha tawwabun hakeemun
Inna allatheena jaoo bialifki ausbatun minkum la tahsaboohu sharran lakum bal huwa khayrun lakum likulli imriin minhum ma iktasaba mina lithmi waallathee tawalla kibrahu minhum lahu aathabun aatheemun
Lawla ith samiatumoohu thanna almuminoona waalmuminatu bianfusihim khayran waqaloo hatha ifkun mubeenun
Lawla jaoo aalayhi biarbaaati shuhadaa faith lam yatoo bialshshuhadai faolaika ainda Allahi humu alkathiboona
Walawla fadlu Allahi aalaykum warahmatuhu fee alddunya waalakhirati lamassakum fee ma afadtum feehi aathabun aatheemun
Ith talaqqawnahu bialsinatikum wataqooloona biafwahikum ma laysa lakum bihi ailmun watahsaboonahu hayyinan wahuwa ainda Allahi aatheemun
Walawla ith samiatumoohu qultum ma yakoonu lana an natakallama bihatha subhanaka hatha buhtanun aatheemun
Yaaithukumu Allahu an taaoodoo limithlihi abadan in kuntum mumineena
Wayubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati waAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Inna allatheena yuhibboona an tasheeaa alfahishatu fee allatheena amanoo lahum aathabun aleemun fee alddunya waalakhirati waAllahu aalamu waantum la taalamoona
Walawla fadlu Allahi aalaykum warahmatuhu waanna Allaha raoofun raheemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattabiaoo khutuwati alshshaytani waman yattabia khutuwati alshshaytani fainnahu yamuru bialfahshai waalmunkari walawla fadlu Allahi aalaykum warahmatuhu ma zaka minkum min ahadin abadan walakinna Allaha yuzakkee man yashao waAllahu ameeaun aaleemun
Wala yatali oloo alfadli minkum waalssaaati an yutoo olee alqurba waalmasakeena waalmuhajireena fee sabeeli Allahi walyaafoo alyasfahoo ala tuhibboona an yaghfira Allahu lakum waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Inna allatheena yarmoona almuhsanati alghafilati almuminati luainoo fee alddunya waalakhirati walahum aathabun aatheemun
Yawma tashhadu aalayhim alsinatuhum waaydeehim waarjuluhum bima kanoo yaamaloona
Yawmaithin yuwaffeehimu Allahu deenahumu alhaqqa wayaalamoona anna Allaha huwa alhaqqu almubeenu
Alkhabeethatu lilkhabeetheena waalkhabeethoona lilkhabeethati waalttayyibatu lilttayyibeena waalttayyiboona lilttayyibati olaika ubarraoona mimma yaqooloona lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tadkhuloo buyootan ghayra buyootikum hatta tastanisoo watusallimoo aala ahliha thalikum khayrun lakum aaallakum tathakkaroona
Fain lam tajidoo feeha ahadan fala tadkhulooha hatta yuthana lakum wain qeela lakumu irjiaoo fairjiaoo huwa azka lakum waAllahu bima aamaloona aaleemun
Laysa aalaykum junahun an tadkhuloo buyootan ghayra maskoonatin feeha mataaun lakum waAllahu yaalamu ma tubdoona wama taktumoona
Qul lilmumineena yaghuddoo min absarihum wayahfathoo furoojahum thalika azka lahum inna Allaha khabeerun bima yasnaaoona
Waqul lilmuminati yaghdudna min absarihinna wayahfathna furoojahunna wala yubdeena zeenatahunna illa ma thahara minha walyadribna bikhumurihinna aala juyoobihinna wala yubdeena zeenatahunna illa libuaoolatihinna aw abaihinna aw abai buaoolatihinna aw abnaihinna aw abnai buaoolatihinna aw ikhwanihinna aw banee ikhwanihinna aw banee akhawatihinna aw nisaihinna aw ma malakat aymanuhunna awi alttabiaeena ghayri olee alirbati mina alrrijali awi alttifli allatheena lam yathharoo aala aawrati alnnisai wala yadribna biarjulihinna iyualama ma yukhfeena min zeenatihinna watooboo ila Allahi jameeaan ayyuha almuminoona laaallakum tuflihoona
Waankihoo alayama minkum waalssaliheena min aibadikum waimaikum in yakoonoo fuqaraa yughnihimu Allahu min fadlihi waAllahu wasiaun aleemun
Walyastaafifi allatheena la yajidoona nikahan hatta yughniyahumu Allahu min fadlihi waallatheena yabtaghoona alkitaba mimma malakat aymanukum fakatiboohum in aalimtum feehim khayran waatoohum min mali Allahi allathee atakum wala tukrihoo fatayatikum aala albighai in radna tahassunan litabtaghoo aarada alhayati alddunya waman yukrihhunna fainna Allaha min baadi ikrahihinna ghafoorun raheemun
Walaqad anzalna ilaykum ayatin mubayyinatin wamathalan mina allatheena khalaw min qablikum wamawaithatan lilmuttaqeena
Allahu nooru alssamawati waalardi mathalu noorihi kamishkatin feeha misbahun almisbahu fee zujajatin alzzujajatu kaannaha kawkabun durriyyun yooqadu min shajaratin mubarakatin zaytoonatin la sharqiyyatin wala gharbiyyatin yakadu zaytuha yudeeo walaw lam tamsashu arun noorun aala noorin yahdee Allahu linoorihi man yashao wayadribu Allahu alamthala lilnnasi waAllahu bikulli shayin aaleemun
Fee buyootin athina Allahu an turfaaa wayuthkara feeha ismuhu yusabbihu lahu feeha bialghuduwwi waalasali
Rijalun la tulheehim tijaratun wala bayaun aan thikri Allahi waiqami alssalati waeetai alzzakati yakhafoona yawman tataqallabu feehi lquloobu waalabsaru
Liyajziyahumu Allahu ahsana ma aamiloo wayazeedahum min fadlihi waAllahu yarzuqu man yashao bighayri hisabin
Waallatheena kafaroo aamaluhum kasarabin biqeeaatin yahsabuhu alththamanu maan hatta itha jaahu lam yajidhu shayan wawajada Allaha indahu fawaffahu hisabahu waAllahu sareeau alhisabi
Aw kathulumatin fee bahrin lujjiyyin yaghshahu mawjun min fawqihi mawjun min fawqihi sahabun thulumatun baaduha fawqa baadin itha khraja yadahu lam yakad yaraha waman lam yajaali Allahu lahu nooran fama lahu min noorin
Alam tara anna Allaha yusabbihu lahu man fee alssamawati waalardi waalttayru saffatin kullun qad aalima salatahu watasbeehahu waAllahu aleemun bima yafaaloona
Walillahi mulku alssamawati waalardi waila Allahi almaseeru
Alam tara anna Allaha yuzjee sahaban thumma yuallifu baynahu thumma yajaaluhu rukaman fatara alwadqa yakhruju min khilalihi wayunazzilu ina alssamai min jibalin feeha min baradin fayuseebu bihi man yashao wayasrifuhu aan man yashao yakadu sana barqihi yathhabu bialabsari
Yuqallibu Allahu allayla waalnnahara inna fee thalika laaibratan liolee alabsari
WaAllahu khalaqa kulla dabbatin min main faminhum man yamshee aala batnihi waminhum man yamshee aala rijlayni waminhum man yamshee aala rbaain yakhluqu Allahu ma yashao inna Allaha aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Laqad anzalna ayatin mubayyinatin waAllahu yahdee man yashao ila siratin mustaqeemin
Wayaqooloona amanna biAllahi wabialrrasooli waataana thumma yatawalla fareequn minhum min baadi thalika wama olaika bialmumineena
Waitha duaoo ila Allahi warasoolihi liyahkuma baynahum itha fareequn minhum muaridoona
Wain yakun lahumu alhaqqu yatoo ilayhi muthaineena
Afee quloobihim maradun ami irtaboo am yakhafoona an yaheefa Allahu aalayhim warasooluhu bal olaika humu alththalimoona
Innama kana qawla almumineena itha duaoo ila Allahi warasoolihi liyahkuma baynahum an yaqooloo samiana waataana waolaika humu lmuflihoona
Waman yutiai Allaha warasoolahu wayakhsha Allaha wayattaqhi faolaika humu alfaizoona
Waaqsamoo biAllahi jahda aymanihim lain amartahum layakhrujunna qul la tuqsimoo taaatun maaroofatun inna Allaha khabeerun bima aamaloona
Qul ateeaoo Allaha waateeaoo alrrasoola fain tawallaw fainnama aalayhi ma hummila waaalaykum ma hummiltum wain tuteeaoohu tahtadoo wama ala alrrasooli illa albalaghu almubeena
Waaada Allahu allatheena amanoo minkum waaamiloo alssalihati layastakhlifannahum fee alardi kama istakhlafa allatheena min qablihim walayumakkinanna lahum deenahumu allathee irtada lahum walayubaddilannahum min baadi khawfihim amnan yaabudoonanee la yushrikoona bee hayan waman kafara baada thalika faolaika humu alfasiqoona
Waaqeemoo alssalata waatoo alzzakata waateeaoo alrrasoola laaallakum turhamoona
La tahsabanna allatheena kafaroo muajizeena fee alardi wamawahumu alnnaru walabisa almaseeru
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo liyastathinkumu allatheena malakat aymanukum waallatheena lam yablughoo alhuluma minkum thalatha marratin min qabli salati alfajri waheena tadaaoona thiyabakum mina alththaheerati wamin baadi salati alaishai thalathu aawratin lakum laysa aalaykum wala aalayhim junahun baadahunna tawwafoona aalaykum baadukum aala baadin kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati waAllahu aleemun hakeemun
Waitha balagha alatfalu minkumu alhuluma falyastathinoo kama istathana allatheena min qablihim kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakum ayatihi aAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Waalqawaaidu mina alnnisai allatee la yarjoona nikahan falaysa aalayhinna junahun an yadaana thiyabahunna ghayra mutabarrijatin izeenatin waan yastaafifna khayrun lahunna waAllahu sameeaun aaleemun
Laysa aala alaama harajun wala aala alaaraji harajun wala aala almareedi harajun wala aala anfusikum an takuloo min buyootikum aw buyooti abaikum aw buyooti ommahatikum aw buyooti ikhwanikum aw buyooti akhawatikum aw buyooti aamamikum aw buyooti aammatikum aw buyooti akhwalikum aw buyooti khalatikum aw ma malaktum mafatihahu aw sadeeqikum laysa aalaykum junahun an takuloo jameeaan aw ashtatan faitha dakhaltum buyootan fasallimoo aala anfusikum tahiyyatan min aindi Allahi mubarakatan tayyibatan kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakumu layati laaallakum taaqiloona
Innama almuminoona allatheena amanoo biAllahi warasoolihi waitha kanoo maaahu aala amrin jamiain lam yathhaboo hatta yastathinoohu inna allatheena yastathinoonaka olaika allatheena yuminoona biAllahi warasoolihi faitha istathanooka libaadi shanihim fathan liman shita inhum waistaghfir lahumu Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
La tajaaloo duaaa alrrasooli baynakum kaduaai baadikum baadan qad yaalamu Allahu allatheena yatasallaloona minkum liwathan falyahthari llatheena yukhalifoona aan amrihi an tuseebahum fitnatun aw yuseebahum aathabun aleemun
Ala inna lillahi ma fee alssamawati waalardi qad yaalamu ma antum aalayhi wayawma yurjaaoona ilayhi fayunabbiohum bima aamiloo waAllahu ikulli shayin aaleemun
Tabaraka allathee nazzala alfurqana aala aabdihi liyakoona lilaalameena natheeran
Allathee lahu mulku alssamawati waalardi walam yattakhith waladan walam yakun lahu shareekun fee almulki wakhalaqa kulla shayin aqaddarahu taqdeeran
Waittakhathoo min doonihi alihatan la yakhluqoona shayan wahum yukhlaqoona wala yamlikoona lianfusihim darran wala nafaan wala amlikoona mawtan wala hayatan wala nushooran
Waqala allatheena kafaroo in hatha illa ifkun iftarahu waaaanahu aalayhi qawmun akharoona faqad jaoo thulman wazooran
Waqaloo asateeru alawwaleena iktatabaha fahiya tumla aalayhi bukratan waaseelan
Qul anzalahu allathee yaalamu alssirra fee alssamawati waalardi innahu kana ghafooran raheeman
Waqaloo mali hatha alrrasooli yakulu alttaaama wayamshee fee alaswaqi lawla onzila ilayhi malakun fayakoona maaahu natheeran
Aw yulqa ilayhi kanzun aw takoonu lahu jannatun yakulu minha waqala alththalimoona in tattabiaoona illa rajulan mashooran
Onthur kayfa daraboo laka alamthala fadalloo fala yastateeaoona sabeelan
Tabaraka allathee in shaa jaaala laka khayran min thalika jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu wayajaal laka qusooran
Bal kaththaboo bialssaaati waaatadna liman kaththaba bialssaaati saaeeran
Itha raathum min makanin baaeedin samiaoo laha taghayyuthan wazafeeran
Waitha olqoo minha makanan dayyiqan muqarraneena daaaw hunalika thubooran
La tadaoo alyawma thubooran wahidan waodaoo thubooran katheeran
Qul athalika khayrun am jannatu alkhuldi allatee wuaida almuttaqoona kanat lahum jazaan wamaseeran
Lahum feeha ma yashaoona khalideena kana aala rabbika waadan masoolan
Wayawma yahshuruhum wama yaabudoona min dooni Allahi fayaqoolu aantum adlaltum aibadee haolai am hum dalloo alssabeela
Qaloo subhanaka ma kana yanbaghee lana an nattakhitha min doonika min awliyaa walakin mattaatahum waabaahum hatta nasoo alththikra akanoo qawman booran
Faqad kaththabookum bima taqooloona fama tastateeaoona sarfan wala nasran waman yathlim minkum nuthiqhu aathaban kabeeran
Wama arsalna qablaka mina almursaleena illa innahum layakuloona alttaaama wayamshoona fee alaswaqi wajaaalna baadakum libaadin fitnatan tasbiroona wakana rabbuka baseeran
Waqala allatheena la yarjoona liqaana lawla onzila aalayna almalaikatu aw nara rabbana laqadi istakbaroo fee anfusihim waaataw autuwwan abeeran
Yawma yarawna almalaikata la bushra yawmaithin lilmujrimeena wayaqooloona hijran mahjooran
Waqadimna ila ma aamiloo min aamalin fajaaalnahu habaan manthooran
Ashabu aljannati yawmaithin khayrun mustaqarran waahsanu maqeelan
Wayawma tashaqqaqu alssamao bialghamami wanuzzila almalaikatu tanzeelan
Almulku yawmaithin alhaqqu lilrrahmani wakana yawman aala alkafireena aaseeran
Wayawma yaaaddu alththalimu aala yadayhi yaqoolu ya laytanee ittakhathtu maaa alrrasooli sabeelan
Ya waylata laytanee lam attakhith fulanan khaleelan
Laqad adallanee aani alththikri baada ith jaanee wakana alshshaytanu lilinsani khathoolan
Waqala alrrasoolu ya rabbi inna qawmee ittakhathoo hatha alqurana mahjooran
Wakathalika jaaalna likulli nabiyyin aaduwwan mina almujrimeena wakafa birabbika hadiyan wanaseeran
Waqala allatheena kafaroo lawla nuzzila aalayhi alquranu jumlatan wahidatan kathalika linuthabbita bihi fuadaka warattalnahu tarteelan
Wala yatoonaka bimathalin illa jinaka bialhaqqi waahsana tafseeran
Allatheena yuhsharoona aala wujoohihim ila jahannama olaika sharrun makanan waadallu sabeelan
Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba wajaaalna maaahu akhahu haroona wazeeran
Faqulna ithhaba ila alqawmi allatheena kaththaboo biayatina fadammarnahum tadmeeran
Waqawma noohin lamma kaththaboo alrrusula aghraqnahum wajaaalnahum lilnnasi ayatan waaatadna lilththalimeena aathaban aleeman
Waaadan wathamooda waashaba alrrassi waquroonan bayna thalika katheeran
Wakullan darabna lahu alamthala wakullan tabbarna tatbeeran
Walaqad ataw aala alqaryati allatee omtirat matara alssawi afalam yakoonoo yarawnaha bal kanoo la yarjoona nushooran
Waitha raawka in yattakhithoonaka illa huzuwan ahatha allathee baaatha Allahu rasoolan
In kada layudilluna aan alihatina lawla an sabarna aalayha wasawfa yaalamoona heena yarawna alaathaba man adallu sabeelan
Araayta mani ittakhatha ilahahu hawahu afaanta takoonu aalayhi wakeelan
Am tahsabu anna aktharahum yasmaaoona aw yaaqiloona in hum illa kaalanaami bal hum adallu sabeelan
Alam tara ila rabbika kayfa madda alththilla walaw shaa lajaaalahu sakinan thumma jaaalna alshshamsa aalayhi daleelan
Thumma qabadnahu ilayna qabdan yaseeran
Wahuwa allathee jaaala lakumu allayla libasan waalnnawma subatan wajaaala alnnahara nushooran
Wahuwa allathee arsala alrriyaha bushran bayna yaday rahmatihi waanzalna mina alssamai maan tahooran
Linuhyiya bihi baldatan maytan wanusqiyahu mimma khalaqna anaaman waanasiyya katheeran
Walaqad sarrafnahu baynahum liyaththakkaroo faaba aktharu alnnasi illa kufooran
Walaw shina labaaathna fee kulli qaryatin natheeran
Fala tutiai alkafireena wajahidhum bihi jihadan kabeeran
Wahuwa allathee maraja albahrayni hatha aathbun furatun wahatha milhun ojajun wajaaala baynahuma barzakhan wahijran mahjooran
Wahuwa allathee khalaqa mina almai basharan fajaaalahu nasaban wasihran wakana rabbuka qadeeran
Wayaabudoona min dooni Allahi ma la yanfaauhum wala yadurruhum wakana alkafiru aala rabbihi thaheeran
Wama arsalnaka illa mubashshiran wanatheeran
Qul ma asalukum aalayhi min ajrin illa man shaa an yattakhitha ila rabbihi sabeelan
Watawakkal aala alhayyi allathee la yamootu wasabbih bihamdihi wakafa bihi bithunoobi aibadihi khabeeran
Allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda wama baynahuma fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa aala alaarshi alrrahmanu faisal bihi khabeeran
Waitha qeela lahumu osjudoo lilrrahmani qaloo wama alrrahmanu anasjudu lima tamuruna wazadahum nufooran
Tabaraka allathee jaaala fee alssamai buroojan wajaaala feeha sirajan waqamaran muneeran
Wahuwa allathee jaaala allayla waalnnahara khilfatan liman arada an yaththakkara aw arada shukooran
Waaibadu alrrahmani allatheena yamshoona aala alardi hawnan waitha khatabahumu aljahiloona qaloo salaman
Waallatheena yabeetoona lirabbihim sujjadan waqiyaman
Waallatheena yaqooloona rabbana isrif aanna aathaba jahannama inna aathabaha kana gharaman
Innaha saat mustaqarran wamuqaman
Waallatheena itha anfaqoo lam yusrifoo walam yaqturoo wakana bayna thalika qawaman
Waallatheena la yadaoona maaa Allahi ilahan akhara wala yaqtuloona alnnafsa allatee harrama Allahu illa bialhaqqi wala yaznoona waman afaal thalika yalqa athaman
Yudaaaf lahu alaathabu yawma alqiyamati wayakhlud feehi muhanan
Illa man taba waamana waaamila aamalan salihan faolaika yubaddilu Allahu sayyiatihim hasanatin wakana Allahu ghafooran raheeman
Waman taba waaamila salihan fainnahu yatoobu ila Allahi mataban
Waallatheena la yashhadoona alzzoora waitha marroo biallaghwi marroo kiraman
Waallatheena itha thukkiroo biayati rabbihim lam yakhirroo aalayha summan waaumyanan
Waallatheena yaqooloona rabbana hab lana min azwajina wathurriyyatina qurrata aayunin waijaalna lilmuttaqeena imaman
Olaika yujzawna alghurfata bima sabaroo wayulaqqawna feeha tahiyyatan wasalaman
Khalideena feeha hasunat mustaqarran wamuqaman

Laaallaka bakhiaun nafsaka alla yakoonoo mumineena
