Thikra wama kunna thalimeena
Wama tanazzalat bihi alshshayateenu
Wama yanbaghee lahum wama yastateeaoona
Innahum aani alssamai lamaazooloona
Fala tadau maaa Allahi ilahan akhara fatakoona mina almuaaththabeena
Waanthir aasheerataka alaqrabeena
Waikhfid janahaka limani ittabaaaka mina almumineena
Fain aasawka faqul innee bareeon mimma taamaloona
Watawakkal aala alaazeezi alrraheemi
Allathee yaraka heena taqoomu
Wataqallubaka fee alssajideena
Innahu huwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Hal onabbiokum aala man tanazzalu alshshayateenu
Tanazzalu aala kulli affakin atheemin
Yulqoona alssamaa waaktharuhum kathiboona
Waalshshuaarao yattabiauhumu alghawoona
Alam tara annahum fee kulli wadin yaheemoona
Waannahum yaqooloona ma la yafaaloona
Illa allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati wathakaroo Allaha katheeran waintasaroo min baadi ma thulimoo wasayaalamu allatheena halamoo ayya munqalabin yanqaliboona
Taseen tilka ayatu alqurani wakitabin mubeenin
Hudan wabushra lilmumineena
Allatheena yuqeemoona alssalata wayutoona alzzakata wahum bialakhirati hum yooqinoona
Inna allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati zayyanna lahum aamalahum fahum yaamahoona
Olaika allatheena lahum sooo alaathabi wahum fee alakhirati humu alakhsaroona
Wainnaka latulaqqa alqurana min ladun hakeemin aaleemin
Ith qala moosa liahlihi innee anastu naran saateekum minha bikhabarin aw ateekum bishihabin qabasin laaallakum tastaloona
Falamma jaaha noodiya an boorika man fee alnnari waman hawlaha wasubhana Allahi rabbi alaalameena
Ya moosa innahu ana Allahu alaazeezu alhakeemu
Waalqi aasaka falamma raaha tahtazzu kaannaha jannun walla mudbiran walam yuaaqqib ya moosa la takhaf innee la yakhafu ladayya lmursaloona
Illa man thalama thumma baddala husnan baada sooin fainnee ghafoorun raheemun
Waadkhil yadaka fee jaybika takhruj baydaa min ghayri sooin fee tisai ayatin ila firaawna waqawmihi innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeena
Falamma jaathum ayatuna mubsiratan qaloo hatha sihrun mubeenun
Wajahadoo biha waistayqanatha anfusuhum thulman waauluwwan faonthur kayfa kana aaqibatu almufsideena
Walaqad atayna dawooda wasulaymana ailman waqala alhamdu lillahi allathee faddalana aala katheerin min aibadihi almumineena
Wawaritha sulaymanu dawooda waqala ya ayyuha alnnasu aullimna mantiqa alttayri waooteena min kulli shayin inna hatha lahuwa alfadlu lmubeenu
Wahushira lisulaymana junooduhu mina aljinni waalinsi waalttayri fahum yoozaaoona
Hatta itha ataw aala wadi alnnamli qalat namlatun ya ayyuha alnnamlu odkhuloo masakinakum la yahtimannakum sulaymanu wajunooduhu wahum a yashauroona
Fatabassama dahikan min qawliha waqala rabbi awzianee an ashkura niamataka allatee anaamta aalayya waaala walidayya waan aamala salihan ardahu waadkhilnee birahmatika fee aibadika alssaliheena
Watafaqqada alttayra faqala ma liya la ara alhudhuda am kana mina alghaibeena
Laoaaththibannahu aathaban shadeedan aw laathbahannahu aw layatiyannee bisultanin mubeenin
Famakatha ghayra baaeedin faqala ahattu bima lam tuhit bihi wajituka min sabain binabain yaqeenin
Innee wajadtu imraatan tamlikuhum waootiyat min kulli shayin walaha aarshun aatheemun
Wajadtuha waqawmaha yasjudoona lilshshamsi min dooni Allahi wazayyana lahumu alshshaytanu aamalahum fasaddahum aani alssabeeli fahum la ahtadoona
Alla yasjudoo lillahi allathee yukhriju alkhabaa fee alssamawati waalardi wayaalamu ma tukhfoona wama tualinoona
Allahu la ilaha illa huwa rabbu alaarshi alaatheemi
Qala sananthuru asadaqta am kunta mina alkathibeena
Ithhab bikitabee hatha faalqih ilayhim thumma tawalla aanhum faonthur matha yarjiaoona
Qalat ya ayyuha almalao innee olqiya ilayya kitabun kareemun
Innahu min sulaymana wainnahu bismi Allahi alrrahmani alrraheemi
Alla taaloo aalayya watoonee muslimeena
Qalat ya ayyuha almalao aftoonee fee amree ma kuntu qatiaatan amran hatta tashhadoona
Qaloo nahnu oloo quwwatin waoloo basin shadeedin waalamru ilayki faonthuree matha tamureena
Qalat inna almulooka itha dakhaloo qaryatan afsadooha wajaaaloo aaizzata ahliha athillatan wakathalika yafaaloona
Wainnee mursilatun ilayhim bihadiyyatin fanathiratun bima yarjiau almursaloona
Falamma jaa sulaymana qala atumiddoonani bimalin fama ataniya Allahu khayrun mimma atakum bal antum bihadiyyatikum tafrahoona
Irjia ilayhim falanatiyannahum bijunoodin la qibala lahum biha walanukhrijannahum minha athillatan wahum saghiroona
Qala ya ayyuha almalao ayyukum yateenee biaarshiha qabla an yatoonee muslimeena
Qala aifreetun mina aljinni ana ateeka bihi qabla an taqooma min maqamika wainne aalayhi laqawiyyun ameenun
Qala allathee aindahu ailmun mina alkitabi ana ateeka bihi qabla an yartadda ilayka tarfuka falamma raahu mustaqirran aindahu qala hatha min fadli rabbee liyabluwanee aashkuru am akfuru waman shakara fainnama yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fainna rabbee ghaniyyun areemun
Qala nakkiroo laha aarshaha nanthur atahtadee am takoonu mina allatheena la yahtadoona
Falamma jaat qeela ahakatha aarshuki qalat kaannahu huwa waooteena alailma min qabliha wakunna muslimeena
Wasaddaha ma kanat taabudu min dooni Allahi innaha kanat min qawmin kafireena
Qeela laha odkhulee alssarha falamma raathu hasibathu lujjatan wakashafat aan saqayha qala innahu sarhun mumarradun min qawareera qalat abbi innee thalamtu nafsee waaslamtu maaa sulaymana lillahi rabbi alaalameena
Walaqad arsalna ila thamooda akhahum salihan ani oabudoo Allaha faitha hum fareeqani yakhtasimoona
Qala ya qawmi lima tastaajiloona bialssayyiati qabla alhasanati lawla tastaghfiroona Allaha laaallakum turhamoona
Qaloo ittayyarna bika wabiman maaaka qala tairukum ainda Allahi bal antum qawmun tuftanoona
Wakana fee almadeenati tisaatu rahtin yufsidoona fee alardi wala yuslihoona
Qaloo taqasamoo biAllahi lanubayyitannahu waahlahu thumma lanaqoolanna liwaliyyihi ma shahidna mahlika ahlihi wainna lasadiqoona
Wamakaroo makran wamakarna makran wahum la yashauroona
Faonthur kayfa kana aaqibatu makrihim anna dammarnahum waqawmahum ajmaaeena
Fatilka buyootuhum khawiyatan bima thalamoo inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yaalamoona
Waanjayna allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoona
Walootan ith qala liqawmihi atatoona alfahishata waantum tubsiroona
Ainnakum latatoona alrrijala shahwatan min dooni alnnisai bal antum qawmun tajhaloona
Fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo akhrijoo ala lootin min qaryatikum innahum onasun yatatahharoona
Faanjaynahu waahlahu illa imraatahu qaddarnaha mina alghabireena
Waamtarna aalayhim mataran fasaa mataru almunthareena
Quli alhamdu lillahi wasalamun aala aibadihi allatheena istafa allahu khayrun amma yushrikoona
Amman khalaqa alssamawati waalarda waanzala lakum mina alssamai maan faanbatna bihi hadaiqa thata bahjatin ma kana lakum an tunbitoo hajaraha ailahun maaa Allahi bal hum qawmun yaadiloona
Amman jaaala alarda qararan wajaaala khilalaha anharan wajaaala laha rawasiya wajaaala bayna albahrayni hajizan ailahun maaa Allahi bal ktharuhum la yaalamoona
Amman yujeebu almudtarra itha daaahu wayakshifu alssooa wayajaalukum khulafaa alardi ailahun maaa Allahi qaleelan ma tathakkaroona
Amman yahdeekum fee thulumati albarri waalbahri waman yursilu alrriyaha bushran bayna yaday rahmatihi ailahun maaa Allahi taaala Allahu amma yushrikoona
Amman yabdao alkhalqa thumma yuaeeduhu waman yarzuqukum mina alssamai waalardi ailahun maaa Allahi qul hatoo burhanakum in kuntum adiqeena
Qul la yaalamu man fee alssamawati waalardi alghayba illa Allahu wama yashauroona ayyana yubaathoona
Bali iddaraka ailmuhum fee alakhirati bal hum fee shakkin minha bal hum minha aamoona
Waqala allatheena kafaroo aitha kunna turaban waabaona ainna lamukhrajoona
Laqad wuaidna hatha nahnu waabaona min qablu in hatha illa asateeru alawwaleena
Qul seeroo fee alardi faonthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu almujrimeena
Wala tahzan aalayhim wala takun fee dayqin mimma yamkuroona
Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwaadu in kuntum sadiqeena
Qul aasa an yakoona radifa lakum baadu allathee tastaajiloona
Wainna rabbaka lathoo fadlin aala alnnasi walakinna aktharahum la yashkuroona
Wainna rabbaka layaalamu ma tukinnu sudooruhum wama yualinoona
Wama min ghaibatin fee alssamai waalardi illa fee kitabin mubeenin
Inna hatha alqurana yaqussu aala banee israeela akthara allathee hum feehi yakhtalifoona
Wainnahu lahudan warahmatun lilmumineena
Inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum bihukmihi wahuwa alaazeezu alaaleemu
Fatawakkal aala Allahi innaka aala alhaqqi almubeeni
Innaka la tusmiau almawta wala tusmiau alssumma aldduaaa itha wallaw mudbireena
Wama anta bihadee alaumyi aan dalalatihim in tusmiau illa man yuminu biayatina fahum muslimoona
Waitha waqaaa alqawlu aalayhim akhrajna lahum dabbatan mina alardi tukallimuhum anna alnnasa kanoo biayatina la yooqinoona
Wayawma nahshuru min kulli ommatin fawjan mimman yukaththibu biayatina fahum yoozaaoona
Hatta itha jaoo qala akaththabtum biayatee walam tuheetoo biha ailman ammatha kuntum taamaloona
Wawaqaaa alqawlu aalayhim bima thalamoo fahum la yantiqoona
Alam yaraw anna jaaalna allayla liyaskunoo feehi waalnnahara mubsiran inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoona
Wayawma yunfakhu fee alssoori fafaziaa man fee alssamawati waman fee alardi illa man shaa Allahu wakullun atawhu dakhireena
Watara aljibala tahsabuha jamidatan wahiya tamurru marra alssahabi sunaa Allahi allathee atqana kulla shayin innahu khabeerun bima afaaloona
Man jaa bialhasanati falahu khayrun minha wahum min fazaain yawmaithin aminoona
Waman jaa bialssayyiati fakubbat wujoohuhum fee alnnari hal tujzawna illa ma kuntum taamaloona
Innama omirtu an aabuda rabba hathihi albaldati allathee harramaha walahu kullu shayin waomirtu an akoona mina almuslimeena
Waan atluwa alqurana famani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla faqul innama ana mina almunthireena
Waquli alhamdu lillahi sayureekum ayatihi fataarifoonaha wama rabbuka bighafilin aamma taamaloona
Taseenmeem
Tilka ayatu alkitabi almubeeni
Natloo aalayka min nabai moosa wafiraawna bialhaqqi liqawmin yuminoona
Inna firaawna aala fee alardi wajaaala ahlaha shiyaaan yastadaifu taifatan minhum yuthabbihu abnaahum wayastahyee nisaahum innahu kana ina almufsideena
Wanureedu an namunna aala allatheena istudaifoo fee alardi wanajaalahum aimmatan wanajaalahumu alwaritheena
Wanumakkina lahum fee alardi wanuriya firaawna wahamana wajunoodahuma minhum ma kanoo yahtharoona
Waawhayna ila ommi moosa an ardiaeehi faitha khifti aalayhi faalqeehi fee alyammi wala takhafee wala tahzanee inna raddoohu ilayki ajaailoohu mina almursaleena
Failtaqatahu alu firaawna liyakoona lahum aaduwwan wahazanan inna firaawna wahamana wajunoodahuma kanoo khatieena
Waqalati imraatu firaawna qurratu aaynin lee walaka la taqtuloohu aasa an yanfaaana aw nattakhithahu waladan wahum la yashauroona
Waasbaha fuadu ommi moosa farighan in kadat latubdee bihi lawla an rabatna aala qalbiha litakoona mina almumineena
Waqalat liokhtihi qusseehi fabasurat bihi aan junubin wahum la yashauroona
Waharramna aalayhi almaradiaa min qablu faqalat hal adullukum aala ahli baytin yakfuloonahu lakum wahum lahu nasihoona
Faradadnahu ila ommihi kay taqarra aaynuha wala tahzana walitaalama anna waada Allahi haqqun walakinna aktharahum la yaalamoona
Walamma balagha ashuddahu waistawa ataynahu hukman waailman wakathalika najzee almuhsineena
Wadakhala almadeenata aala heeni ghaflatin min ahliha fawajada feeha rajulayni yaqtatilani hatha min sheeaatihi wahatha min aaduwwihi faistaghathahu allathee min sheeaatihi aala allathee min aaduwwihi fawakazahu moosa faqada aalayhi qala hatha min aamali alshshaytani nnahu aaduwwun mudillun mubeenun
Qala rabbi innee thalamtu nafsee faighfir lee faghafara lahu innahu huwa alghafooru alrraheemu
Qala rabbi bima anaamta aalayya falan akoona thaheeran lilmujrimeena
Faasbaha fee almadeenati khaifan yataraqqabu faitha allathee istansarahu bialamsi yastasrikhuhu qala lahu moosa innaka laghawiyyun ubeenun
Falamma an arada an yabtisha biallathee huwa aaduwwun lahuma qala ya moosa atureedu an taqtulanee kama qatalta nafsan bialamsi in ureedu illa an takoona jabbaran fee alardi wama tureedu an takoona mina almusliheena
Wajaa rajulun min aqsa almadeenati yasaa qala ya moosa inna almalaa yatamiroona bika liyaqtulooka faokhruj innee laka mina alnnasiheena
Fakharaja minha khaifan yataraqqabu qala rabbi najjinee mina alqawmi alththalimeena
Walamma tawajjaha tilqaa madyana qala aasa rabbee an yahdiyanee sawaa alssabeeli
Walamma warada maa madyana wajada aalayhi ommatan mina alnnasi yasqoona wawajada min doonihimu imraatayni tathoodani qala ma khatbukuma alata la nasqee hatta yusdira alrriaao waaboona shaykhun kabeerun
Fasaqa lahuma thumma tawalla ila alththilli faqala rabbi innee lima anzalta ilayya min khayrin faqeerun
Fajaathu ihdahuma tamshee aala istihyain qalat inna abee yadaooka liyajziyaka ajra ma saqayta lana falamma jaahu waqassa aalayhi lqasasa qala la takhaf najawta mina alqawmi alththalimeena
Qalat ihdahuma ya abati istajirhu inna khayra mani istajarta alqawiyyu alameenu
Qala innee oreedu an onkihaka ihda ibnatayya hatayni aala an tajuranee thamaniya hijajin fain atmamta aashran famin aindika wama oreedu n ashuqqa aalayka satajidunee in shaa Allahu mina alssaliheena
Qala thalika baynee wabaynaka ayyama alajalayni qadaytu fala audwana aalayya waAllahu aala ma naqoolu wakeelun
Falamma qada moosaalajala wasara biahlihi anasa min janibi alttoori naran qala liahlihi omkuthoo innee anastu naran laaallee ateekum inha bikhabarin aw jathwatin mina alnnari laaallakum tastaloona
Falamma ataha noodiya min shatii alwadi alaymani fee albuqaati almubarakati mina alshshajarati an ya moosa innee ana Allahu rabbu laalameena
Waan alqi aasaka falamma raaha tahtazzu kaannaha jannun walla mudbiran walam yuaaqqib ya moosa aqbil wala takhaf innaka mina alamineena
Osluk yadaka fee jaybika takhruj baydaa min ghayri sooin waodmum ilayka janahaka mina alrrahbi fathanika burhanani min rabbika ila iraawna wamalaihi innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeena
Qala rabbi innee qataltu minhum nafsan faakhafu an yaqtulooni
Waakhee haroonu huwa afsahu minnee lisanan faarsilhu maaiya ridan yusaddiqunee innee akhafu an yukaththibooni
Qala sanashuddu aadudaka biakheeka wanajaalu lakuma sultanan fala yasiloona ilaykuma biayatina antuma wamani ittabaaakuma alghaliboona
Falamma jaahum moosa biayatina bayyinatin qaloo ma hatha illa sihrun muftaran wama samiana bihatha fee abaina alawwaleena
Waqala moosa rabbee aalamu biman jaa bialhuda min aindihi waman takoonu lahu aaqibatu alddari innahu la yuflihu alththalimoona
Waqala firaawnu ya ayyuha almalao ma aalimtu lakum min ilahin ghayree faawqid lee ya hamanu aala altteeni faijaal lee sarhan laaallee ttaliau ila ilahi moosa wainnee laathunnuhu mina alkathibeena
Waistakbara huwa wajunooduhu fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wathannoo annahum ilayna la yurjaaoona
Faakhathnahu wajunoodahu fanabathnahum fee alyammi faonthur kayfa kana aaqibatu alththalimeena
Wajaaalnahum aimmatan yadaoona ila alnnari wayawma alqiyamati la yunsaroona
Waatbaanahum fee hathihi alddunya laanatan wayawma alqiyamati hum mina almaqbooheena
Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba min baadi ma ahlakna alquroona aloola basaira lilnnasi wahudan warahmatan laaallahum yatathakkaroona
Wama kunta bijanibi algharbiyyi ith qadayna ila moosa alamra wama kunta mina alshshahideena
Walakinna anshana quroonan fatatawala aalayhimu alaumuru wama kunta thawiyan fee ahli madyana tatloo aalayhim ayatina walakinna kunna ursileena
Wama kunta bijanibi alttoori ith nadayna walakin rahmatan min rabbika litunthira qawman ma atahum min natheerin min qablika laaallahum atathakkaroona
Walawla an tuseebahum museebatun bima qaddamat aydeehim fayaqooloo rabbana lawla arsalta ilayna rasoolan fanattabiaa ayatika wanakoona ina almumineena
Falamma jaahumu alhaqqu min aindina qaloo lawla ootiya mithla ma ootiya moosa awalam yakfuroo bima ootiya moosa min qablu qaloo sihrani athahara waqaloo inna bikullin kafiroona
Qul fatoo bikitabin min aindi Allahi huwa ahda minhuma attabiahu in kuntum sadiqeena
Fain lam yastajeeboo laka faialam annama yattabiaoona ahwaahum waman adallu mimmani ittabaaa hawahu bighayri hudan mina Allahi inna llaha la yahdee alqawma alththalimeena
Walaqad wassalna lahumu alqawla laaallahum yatathakkaroona
Allatheena ataynahumu alkitaba min qablihi hum bihi yuminoona
Waitha yutla aalayhim qaloo amanna bihi innahu alhaqqu min rabbina inna kunna min qablihi muslimeena
Olaika yutawna ajrahum marratayni bima sabaroo wayadraoona bialhasanati alssayyiata wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona
Waitha samiaoo allaghwa aaradoo aanhu waqaloo lana aamaluna walakum aamalukum salamun aalaykum la nabtaghee aljahileena
Innaka la tahdee man ahbabta walakinna Allaha yahdee man yashao wahuwa aalamu bialmuhtadeena
Waqaloo in nattabiai alhuda maaaka nutakhattaf min ardina awalam numakkin lahum haraman aminan yujba ilayhi thamaratu kulli shayin izqan min ladunna walakinna aktharahum la yaalamoona
Wakam ahlakna min qaryatin batirat maaeeshataha fatilka masakinuhum lam tuskan min baadihim illa qaleelan wakunna nahnu alwaritheena
Wama kana rabbuka muhlika alqura hatta yabaatha fee ommiha rasoolan yatloo aalayhim ayatina wama kunna muhlikee alqura illa waahluha halimoona
Wama ooteetum min shayin famataau alhayati alddunya wazeenatuha wama ainda Allahi khayrun waabqa afala taaqiloona
Afaman waaadnahu waadan hasanan fahuwa laqeehi kaman mattaanahu mataaa alhayati alddunya thumma huwa yawma alqiyamati mina almuhdareena
Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum tazaumoona
Qala allatheena haqqa aalayhimu alqawlu rabbana haolai allatheena aghwayna aghwaynahum kama ghawayna tabarrana ilayka ma kanoo iyyana aabudoona
Waqeela odaoo shurakaakum fadaaawhum falam yastajeeboo lahum waraawoo alaathaba law annahum kanoo yahtadoona
Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu matha ajabtumu almursaleena
Faaamiyat aalayhimu alanbao yawmaithin fahum la yatasaaloona
Faamma man taba waamana waaamila salihan faaasa an yakoona mina almufliheena
Warabbuka yakhluqu ma yashao wayakhtaru ma kana lahumu alkhiyaratu subhana Allahi wataaala aamma yushrikoona
Warabbuka yaalamu ma tukinnu sudooruhum wama yualinoona
Wahuwa Allahu la ilaha illa huwa lahu alhamdu fee aloola waalakhirati walahu alhukmu wailayhi turjaaoona
Qul araaytum in jaaala Allahu aalaykumu allayla sarmadan ila yawmi alqiyamati man ilahun ghayru Allahi yateekum bidiyain afala asmaaoona
Qul araaytum in jaaala Allahu aalaykumu alnnahara sarmadan ila yawmi alqiyamati man ilahun ghayru Allahi yateekum bilaylin taskunoona eehi afala tubsiroona
Wamin rahmatihi jaaala lakumu allayla waalnnahara litaskunoo feehi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi walaaallakum tashkuroona
Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum tazaumoona
Wanazaana min kulli ommatin shaheedan faqulna hatoo burhanakum faaalimoo anna alhaqqa lillahi wadalla aanhum ma kanoo yaftaroona
Inna qaroona kana min qawmi moosa fabagha aalayhim waataynahu mina alkunoozi ma inna mafatihahu latanooo bialausbati olee alquwwati ith ala lahu qawmuhu la tafrah inna Allaha la yuhibbu alfariheena
Waibtaghi feema ataka Allahu alddara alakhirata wala tansa naseebaka mina alddunya waahsin kama ahsana Allahu ilayka wala tabghi lfasada fee alardi inna Allaha la yuhibbu almufsideena
Qala innama ooteetuhu aala ailmin aindee awalam yaalam anna Allaha qad ahlaka min qablihi mina alqurooni man huwa ashaddu minhu uwwatan waaktharu jamaan wala yusalu aan thunoobihimu almujrimoona
Fakharaja aala qawmihi fee zeenatihi qala allatheena yureedoona alhayata alddunya ya layta lana mithla ma ootiya qaroonu innahu lathoo aththin aatheemin
Waqala allatheena ootoo alailma waylakum thawabu Allahi khayrun liman amana waaamila salihan wala yulaqqaha illa alssabiroona
Fakhasafna bihi wabidarihi alarda fama kana lahu min fiatin yansuroonahu min dooni Allahi wama kana mina almuntasireena
Waasbaha allatheena tamannaw makanahu bialamsi yaqooloona waykaanna Allaha yabsutu alrrizqa liman yashao min aibadihi wayaqdiru lawla n manna Allahu aalayna lakhasafa bina waykaannahu la yuflihu alkafiroona
Tilka alddaru alakhiratu najaaluha lillatheena la yureedoona auluwwan fee alardi wala fasadan waalaaqibatu lilmuttaqeena
Man jaa bialhasanati falahu khayrun minha waman jaa bialssayyiati fala yujza allatheena aamiloo alssayyiati illa ma kanoo yaamaloona
Inna allathee farada aalayka alqurana laradduka ila maaadin qul rabbee aalamu man jaa bialhuda waman huwa fee dalalin mubeenin
Wama kunta tarjoo an yulqa ilayka alkitabu illa rahmatan min rabbika fala takoonanna thaheeran lilkafireena
Wala yasuddunnaka aan ayati Allahi baada ith onzilat ilayka waodau ila rabbika wala takoonanna mina almushrikeena
Wala tadau maaa Allahi ilahan akhara la ilaha illa huwa kullu shayin halikun illa wajhahu lahu alhukmu wailayhi turjaaoona
Aliflammeem
Ahasiba alnnasu an yutrakoo an yaqooloo amanna wahum la yuftanoona
Walaqad fatanna allatheena min qablihim falayaalamanna Allahu allatheena sadaqoo walayaalamanna alkathibeena
Am hasiba allatheena yaamaloona alssayyiati an yasbiqoona saa ma yahkumoona
Man kana yarjoo liqaa Allahi fainna ajala Allahi laatin wahuwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Waman jahada fainnama yujahidu linafsihi inna Allaha laghaniyyun aani alaalameena
Waallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati lanukaffiranna aanhum sayyiatihim walanajziyannahum ahsana allathee kanoo yaamaloona
Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi husnan wain jahadaka litushrika bee ma laysa laka bihi ailmun fala tutiahuma ilayya marjiaukum aonabbiokum bima kuntum taamaloona
Waallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati lanudkhilannahum fee alssaliheena
Wamina alnnasi man yaqoolu amanna biAllahi faitha oothiya fee Allahi jaaala fitnata alnnasi kaaathabi Allahi walain jaa nasrun min abbika layaqoolunna inna kunna maaakum awalaysa Allahu biaalama bima fee sudoori alaalameena
Walayaalamanna Allahu allatheena amanoo walayaalamanna almunafiqeena
Waqala allatheena kafaroo lillatheena amanoo ittabiaoo sabeelana walnahmil khatayakum wama hum bihamileena min khatayahum min shayin nnahum lakathiboona
Walayahmilunna athqalahum waathqalan maaa athqalihim walayusalunna yawma alqiyamati aamma kanoo yaftaroona
Walaqad arsalna noohan ila qawmihi falabitha feehim alfa sanatin illa khamseena aaman faakhathahumu alttoofanu wahum thalimoona
Faanjaynahu waashaba alssafeenati wajaaalnaha ayatan lilaalameena
Waibraheema ith qala liqawmihi oabudoo Allaha waittaqoohu thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum taalamoona
Innama taabudoona min dooni Allahi awthanan watakhluqoona ifkan inna allatheena taabudoona min dooni Allahi la yamlikoona lakum rizqan aibtaghoo ainda Allahi alrrizqa waoabudoohu waoshkuroo lahu ilayhi turjaaoona
Wain tukaththiboo faqad kaththaba omamun min qablikum wama aala alrrasooli illa albalaghu almubeenu
Awalam yaraw kayfa yubdio Allahu alkhalqa thumma yuaeeduhu inna thalika aala Allahi yaseerun
Qul seeroo fee alardi faonthuroo kayfa badaa alkhalqa thumma Allahu yunshio alnnashata alakhirata inna Allaha aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Yuaaththibu man yashao wayarhamu man yashao wailayhi tuqlaboona
Wama antum bimuajizeena fee alardi wala fee alssamai wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseerin
Waallatheena kafaroo biayati Allahi waliqaihi olaika yaisoo min rahmatee waolaika lahum aathabun aleemun
Fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo oqtuloohu aw harriqoohu faanjahu Allahu mina alnnari inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoona
Waqala innama ittakhathtum min dooni Allahi awthanan mawaddata baynikum fee alhayati alddunya thumma yawma alqiyamati yakfuru baadukum ibaadin wayalaanu baadukum baadan wamawakumu alnnaru wama lakum min nasireena
Faamana lahu lootun waqala innee muhajirun ila rabbee innahu huwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Wawahabna lahu ishaqa wayaaqooba wajaaalna fee thurriyyatihi alnnubuwwata waalkitaba waataynahu ajrahu fee alddunya wainnahu fee lakhirati lamina alssaliheena
Walootan ith qala liqawmihi innakum latatoona alfahishata ma sabaqakum biha min ahadin mina alaalameena
Ainnakum latatoona alrrijala wataqtaaoona alssabeela watatoona fee nadeekumu almunkara fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo itina iaathabi Allahi in kunta mina alssadiqeena
Qala rabbi onsurnee aala alqawmi almufsideena
Walamma jaat rusuluna ibraheema bialbushra qaloo inna muhlikoo ahli hathihi alqaryati inna ahlaha kanoo thalimeena
Qala inna feeha lootan qaloo nahnu aalamu biman feeha lanunajjiyannahu waahlahu illa imraatahu kanat mina alghabireena
Walamma an jaat rusuluna lootan seea bihim wadaqa bihim tharaan waqaloo la takhaf wala tahzan inna munajjooka waahlaka illa imraataka anat mina alghabireena
Inna munziloona aala ahli hathihi alqaryati rijzan mina alssamai bima kanoo yafsuqoona
Walaqad tarakna minha ayatan bayyinatan liqawmin yaaqiloona
Waila madyana akhahum shuaayban faqala ya qawmi oabudoo Allaha waorjoo alyawma alakhira wala taathaw fee alardi mufsideena
Fakaththaboohu faakhathathumu alrrajfatu faasbahoo fee darihim jathimeena
Waaadan wathamooda waqad tabayyana lakum min masakinihim wazayyana lahumu alshshaytanu aamalahum fasaddahum aani alssabeeli wakanoo ustabsireena
Waqaroona wafiraawna wahamana walaqad jaahum moosa bialbayyinati faistakbaroo fee alardi wama kanoo sabiqeena
Fakullan akhathna bithanbihi faminhum man arsalna aalayhi hasiban waminhum man akhathathu alssayhatu waminhum man khasafna bihi alarda aminhum man aghraqna wama kana Allahu liyathlimahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona
Mathalu allatheena ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi awliyaa kamathali alaankabooti ittakhathat baytan wainna awhana albuyooti labaytu laankabooti law kanoo yaalamoona
Inna Allaha yaalamu ma yadaoona min doonihi min shayin wahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Watilka alamthalu nadribuha lilnnasi wama yaaqiluha illa alaalimoona
Khalaqa Allahu alssamawati waalarda bialhaqqi inna fee thalika laayatan lilmumineena
Otlu ma oohiya ilayka mina alkitabi waaqimi alssalata inna alssalata tanha aani alfahshai waalmunkari walathikru Allahi akbaru waAllahu aalamu ma tasnaaoona
Wala tujadiloo ahla alkitabi illa biallatee hiya ahsanu illa allatheena thalamoo minhum waqooloo amanna biallathee onzila ilayna aonzila ilaykum wailahuna wailahukum wahidun wanahnu lahu muslimoona
Wakathalika anzalna ilayka alkitaba faallatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yuminoona bihi wamin haolai man yuminu bihi wama yajhadu biayatina lla alkafiroona
Wama kunta tatloo min qablihi min kitabin wala takhuttuhu biyameenika ithan lairtaba almubtiloona
Bal huwa ayatun bayyinatun fee sudoori allatheena ootoo alailma wama yajhadu biayatina illa alththalimoona
Waqaloo lawla onzila aalayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul innama alayatu ainda Allahi wainnama ana natheerun mubeenun
Awalam yakfihim anna anzalna aalayka alkitaba yutla aalayhim inna fee thalika larahmatan wathikra liqawmin yuminoona
Qul kafa biAllahi baynee wabaynakum shaheedan yaalamu ma fee alssamawati waalardi waallatheena amanoo bialbatili wakafaroo biAllahi laika humu alkhasiroona
Wayastaajiloonaka bialaathabi walawla ajalun musamman lajaahumu alaathabu walayatiyannahum baghtatan wahum la yashauroona
Yastaajiloonaka bialaathabi wainna jahannama lamuheetatun bialkafireena
Yawma yaghshahumu alaathabu min fawqihim wamin tahti arjulihim wayaqoolu thooqoo ma kuntum taamaloona
Ya aibadiya allatheena amanoo inna ardee wasiaatun faiyyaya faoabudooni
Kullu nafsin thaiqatu almawti thumma ilayna turjaaoona
Waallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati lanubawwiannahum mina aljannati ghurafan tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha niama jru alaamileena
Allatheena sabaroo waaala rabbihim yatawakkaloona
Wakaayyin min dabbatin la tahmilu rizqaha Allahu yarzuquha waiyyakum wahuwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Walain saaltahum man khalaqa alssamawati waalarda wasakhkhara alshshamsa waalqamara layaqoolunna Allahu faanna yufakoona
Allahu yabsutu alrrizqa liman yashao min aibadihi wayaqdiru lahu inna Allaha bikulli shayin aaleemun
Walain saaltahum man nazzala mina alssamai maan faahya bihi alarda min baadi mawtiha layaqoolunna Allahu quli alhamdu lillahi bal ktharuhum la yaaqiloona
Wama hathihi alhayatu alddunya illa lahwun walaaibun wainna alddara alakhirata lahiya alhayawanu law kanoo yaalamoona
Faitha rakiboo fee alfulki daaawoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu alddeena falamma najjahum ila albarri itha hum yushrikoona
Liyakfuroo bima ataynahum waliyatamattaaoo fasawfa yaalamoona
Awalam yaraw anna jaaalna haraman aminan wayutakhattafu alnnasu min hawlihim afabialbatili yuminoona wabiniamati Allahi yakfuroona
Waman athlamu mimmani iftara aala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba bialhaqqi lamma jaahu alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilkafireena
Waallatheena jahadoo feena lanahdiyannahum subulana wainna Allaha lamaaa almuhsineena
Aliflammeem
Ghulibati alrroomu
Fee adna alardi wahum min baadi ghalabihim sayaghliboona
Fee bidai sineena lillahi alamru min qablu wamin baadu wayawmaithin yafrahu almuminoona
Binasri Allahi yansuru man yashao wahuwa alaazeezu alrraheemu
Waada Allahi la yukhlifu Allahu waadahu walakinna akthara alnnasi la yaalamoona
Yaalamoona thahiran mina alhayati alddunya wahum aani alakhirati hum ghafiloona
Awalam yatafakkaroo fee anfusihim ma khalaqa Allahu alssamawati waalarda wama baynahuma illa bialhaqqi waajalin musamman wainna atheeran mina alnnasi biliqai rabbihim lakafiroona
Awalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu allatheena min qablihim kanoo ashadda minhum quwwatan waatharoo alarda aaamarooha akthara mimma aamarooha wajaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati fama kana Allahu liyathlimahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona
Thumma kana aaqibata allatheena asaoo alssooa an kaththaboo biayati Allahi wakanoo biha yastahzioona
Allahu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yuaeeduhu thumma ilayhi turjaaoona
Wayawma taqoomu alssaaatu yublisu almujrimoona
Walam yakun lahum min shurakaihim shufaaao wakanoo bishurakaihim kafireena
Wayawma taqoomu alssaaatu yawmaithin yatafarraqoona
Faamma allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati fahum fee rawdatin yuhbaroona
Waamma allatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina waliqai alakhirati faolaika fee alaathabi muhdaroona
Fasubhana Allahi heena tumsoona waheena tusbihoona
Walahu alhamdu fee alssamawati waalardi waaashiyyan waheena tuthhiroona
Yukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti wayukhriju almayyita mina alhayyi wayuhyee alarda baada mawtiha wakathalika tukhrajoona
Wamin ayatihi an khalaqakum min turabin thumma itha antum basharun tantashiroona
Wamin ayatihi an khalaqa lakum min anfusikum azwajan litaskunoo ilayha wajaaala baynakum mawaddatan warahmatan inna fee thalika aayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroona
Wamin ayatihi khalqu alssamawati waalardi waikhtilafu alsinatikum waalwanikum inna fee thalika laayatin lilaalimeena
Wamin ayatihi manamukum biallayli waalnnahari waibtighaokum min fadlihi inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yasmaaoona
Wamin ayatihi yureekumu albarqa khawfan watamaaan wayunazzilu mina alssamai maan fayuhyee bihi alarda baada mawtiha inna fee thalika aayatin liqawmin yaaqiloona
Wamin ayatihi an taqooma alssamao waalardu biamrihi thumma itha daaakum daawatan mina alardi itha antum takhrujoona
Walahu man fee alssamawati waalardi kullun lahu qanitoona
Wahuwa allathee yabdao alkhalqa thumma yuaeeduhu wahuwa ahwanu aalayhi walahu almathalu alaala fee alssamawati waalardi wahuwa laazeezu alhakeemu
Daraba lakum mathalan min anfusikum hal lakum mi mma malakat aymanukum min shurakaa fee ma razaqnakum faantum feehi sawaon akhafoonahum kakheefatikum anfusakum kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin yaaqiloona
Bali ittabaaa allatheena thalamoo ahwaahum bighayri ailmin faman yahdee man adalla Allahu wama lahum min nasireena
Faaqim wajhaka lilddeeni haneefan fitrata Allahi allatee fatara alnnasa aalayha la tabdeela likhalqi Allahi thalika alddeenu alqayyimu alakinna akthara alnnasi la yaalamoona
Muneebeena ilayhi waittaqoohu waaqeemoo alssalata wala takoonoo mina almushrikeena
Mina allatheena farraqoo deenahum wakanoo shiyaaan kullu hizbin bima ladayhim farihoona
Waitha massa alnnasa durrun daaaw rabbahum muneebeena ilayhi thumma itha athaqahum minhu rahmatan itha fareequn minhum birabbihim ushrikoona
Liyakfuroo bima ataynahum fatamattaaoo fasawfa taalamoona
Am anzalna aalayhim sultanan fahuwa yatakallamu bima kanoo bihi yushrikoona
Waitha athaqna alnnasa rahmatan farihoo biha wain tusibhum sayyiatun bima qaddamat aydeehim itha hum yaqnatoona
Awalam yaraw anna Allaha yabsutu alrrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoona
Faati tha alqurba haqqahu waalmiskeena waibna alssabeeli thalika khayrun lillatheena yureedoona wajha Allahi waolaika humu almuflihoona
Wama ataytum min riban liyarbuwa fee amwali alnnasi fala yarboo ainda Allahi wama ataytum min zakatin tureedoona wajha Allahi faolaika umu almudaifoona
Allahu allathee khalaqakum thumma razaqakum thumma yumeetukum thumma yuhyeekum hal min shurakaikum man yafaalu min thalikum min shayin ubhanahu wataaala aamma yushrikoona
Thahara alfasadu fee albarri waalbahri bima kasabat aydee alnnasi liyutheeqahum baada allathee aamiloo laaallahum yarjiaoona
Qul seeroo fee alardi faonthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu allatheena min qablu kana aktharuhum mushrikeena
Faaqim wajhaka lilddeeni alqayyimi min qabli an yatiya yawmun la maradda lahu mina Allahi yawmaithin yassaddaaoona
Man kafara faaalayhi kufruhu waman aamila salihan falianfusihim yamhadoona
Liyajziya allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati min fadlihi innahu la yuhibbu alkafireena
Wamin ayatihi an yursila alrriyaha mubashshiratin waliyutheeqakum min rahmatihi walitajriya alfulku biamrihi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi alaaallakum tashkuroona
Walaqad arsalna min qablika rusulan ila qawmihim fajaoohum bialbayyinati faintaqamna mina allatheena ajramoo wakana haqqan aalayna asru almumineena
Allahu allathee yursilu alrriyaha fatutheeru sahaban fayabsutuhu fee alssamai kayfa yashao wayajaaluhu kisafan fatara alwadqa yakhruju in khilalihi faitha asaba bihi man yashao min aibadihi itha hum yastabshiroona
Wain kanoo min qabli an yunazzala aalayhim min qablihi lamubliseena
Faonthur ila athari rahmati Allahi kayfa yuhyee alarda baada mawtiha inna thalika lamuhyee almawta wahuwa aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Walain arsalna reehan faraawhu musfarran lathalloo min baadihi yakfuroona
Fainnaka la tusmiau almawta wala tusmiau alssumma aldduaaa itha wallaw mudbireena
Wama anta bihadi alaumyi aan dalalatihim in tusmiau illa man yuminu biayatina fahum muslimoona
Allahu allathee khalaqakum min daafin thumma jaaala min baadi daafin quwwatan thumma jaaala min baadi quwwatin daafan washaybatan akhluqu ma yashao wahuwa alaaleemu alqadeeru
Wayawma taqoomu alssaaatu yuqsimu almujrimoona ma labithoo ghayra saaatin kathalika kanoo yufakoona
Waqala allatheena ootoo alailma waaleemana laqad labithtum fee kitabi Allahi ila yawmi albaathi fahatha yawmu albaathi walakinnakum untum la taalamoona
Fayawmaithin la yanfaau allatheena thalamoo maathiratuhum wala hum yustaataboona
Walaqad darabna lilnnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin walain jitahum biayatin layaqoolanna allatheena kafaroo in antum illa ubtiloona
Kathalika yatbaau Allahu aala quloobi allatheena la yaalamoona
Faisbir inna waada Allahi haqqun wala yastakhiffannaka allatheena la yooqinoona
Aliflammeem
Tilka ayatu alkitabi alhakeemi
Hudan warahmatan lilmuhsineena
Allatheena yuqeemoona alssalata wayutoona alzzakata wahum bialakhirati hum yooqinoona
Olaika aala hudan min rabbihim waolaika humu almuflihoona
Wamina alnnasi man yashtaree lahwa alhadeethi liyudilla aan sabeeli Allahi bighayri ailmin wayattakhithaha huzuwan olaika lahum athabun muheenun
Waitha tutla aalayhi ayatuna walla mustakbiran kaan lam yasmaaha kaanna fee othunayhi waqran fabashshirhu biaathabin aleemin
Inna allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati lahum jannatu alnnaaeemi
Khalideena feeha waada Allahi haqqan wahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Khalaqa alssamawati bighayri aamadin tarawnaha waalqa fee alardi rawasiya an tameeda bikum wabaththa feeha min kulli dabbatin waanzalna ina alssamai maan faanbatna feeha min kulli zawjin kareemin
Hatha khalqu Allahi faaroonee matha khalaqa allatheena min doonihi bali alththalimoona fee dalalin mubeenin
Walaqad atayna luqmana alhikmata ani oshkur lillahi waman yashkur fainnama yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fainna Allaha ghaniyyun ameedun
Waith qala luqmanu liibnihi wahuwa yaaithuhu ya bunayya la tushrik biAllahi inna alshshirka lathulmun aatheemun
Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi hamalathu ommuhu wahnan aala wahnin wafisaluhu fee aamayni ani oshkur lee waliwalidayka ilayya almaseeru
Wain jahadaka aala an tushrika bee ma laysa laka bihi ailmun fala tutiahuma wasahibhuma fee alddunya maaroofan waittabia sabeela man naba ilayya thumma ilayya marjiaukum faonabbiokum bima kuntum taamaloona
Ya bunayya innaha in taku mithqala habbatin min khardalin fatakun fee sakhratin aw fee alssamawati aw fee alardi yati biha Allahu inna llaha lateefun khabeerun
Ya bunayya aqimi alssalata wamur bialmaaroofi wainha aani almunkari waisbir aala ma asabaka inna thalika min aazmi alomoori
Wala tusaair khaddaka lilnnasi wala tamshi fee alardi marahan inna Allaha la yuhibbu kulla mukhtalin fakhoorin
Waiqsid fee mashyika waoghdud min sawtika inna ankara alaswati lasawtu alhameeri
Alam taraw anna Allaha sakhkhara lakum ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi waasbagha aalaykum niaamahu thahiratan wabatinatan wamina lnnasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri ailmin wala hudan wala kitabin muneerin
Waitha qeela lahumu ittabiaoo ma anzala Allahu qaloo bal nattabiau ma wajadna aalayhi abaana awalaw kana alshshaytanu yadaoohum ila athabi alssaaeeri
Waman yuslim wajhahu ila Allahi wahuwa muhsinun faqadi istamsaka bialaurwati alwuthqa waila Allahi aaqibatu alomoori
Waman kafara fala yahzunka kufruhu ilayna marjiauhum fanunabbiohum bima aamiloo inna Allaha aaleemun bithati alssudoori
Numattiauhum qaleelan thumma nadtarruhum ila aathabin ghaleethin
Walain saaltahum man khalaqa alssamawati waalarda layaqoolunna Allahu quli alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la yaalamoona
Lillahi ma fee alssamawati waalardi inna Allaha huwa alghaniyyu alhameedu
Walaw annama fee alardi min shajaratin aqlamun waalbahru yamudduhu min baadihi sabaatu abhurin ma nafidat kalimatu Allahi inna Allaha azeezun hakeemun
Ma khalqukum wala baathukum illa kanafsin wahidatin inna Allaha sameeaun baseerun
Alam tara anna Allaha yooliju allayla fee alnnahari wayooliju alnnahara fee allayli wasakhkhara alshshamsa waalqamara kullun yajree ila jalin musamman waanna Allaha bima taamaloona khabeerun
Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waanna ma yadaoona min doonihi albatilu waanna Allaha huwa alaaliyyu alkabeeru
Alam tara anna alfulka tajree fee albahri biniamati Allahi liyuriyakum min ayatihi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoorin
Waitha ghashiyahum mawjun kaalththulali daaawoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu alddeena falamma najjahum ila albarri faminhum muqtasidun wama ajhadu biayatina illa kullu khattarin kafoorin
Ya ayyuha alnnasu ittaqoo rabbakum waikhshaw yawman la yajzee walidun aan waladihi wala mawloodun huwa jazin aan walidihi shayan inna aada Allahi haqqun fala taghurrannakumu alhayatu alddunya wala yaghurrannakum biAllahi algharooru
Inna Allaha aindahu ailmu alssaaati wayunazzilu alghaytha wayaalamu ma fee alarhami wama tadree nafsun matha taksibu ghadan wama tadree afsun biayyi ardin tamootu inna Allaha aaleemun khabeerun
Aliflammeem
Tanzeelu alkitabi la rayba feehi min rabbi alaalameena
Am yaqooloona iftarahu bal huwa alhaqqu min rabbika litunthira qawman ma atahum min natheerin min qablika laaallahum yahtadoona
Allahu allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda wama baynahuma fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa aala alaarshi ma lakum min doonihi min aliyyin wala shafeeain afala tatathakkaroona
Yudabbiru alamra mina alssamai ila alardi thumma yaaruju ilayhi fee yawmin kana miqdaruhu alfa sanatin mimma taauddoona
Thalika aalimu alghaybi waalshshahadati alaazeezu alrraheemu
Allathee ahsana kulla shayin khalaqahu wabadaa khalqa alinsani min teenin
Thumma jaaala naslahu min sulalatin min main maheenin
Thumma sawwahu wanafakha feehi min roohihi wajaaala lakumu alssamaa waalabsara waalafidata qaleelan ma tashkuroona
Waqaloo aitha dalalna fee alardi ainna lafee khalqin jadeedin bal hum biliqai rabbihim kafiroona
Qul yatawaffakum malaku almawti allathee wukkila bikum thumma ila rabbikum turjaaoona
Walaw tara ithi almujrimoona nakisoo ruoosihim ainda rabbihim rabbana absarna wasamiana faarjiana naamal salihan inna mooqinoona
Walaw shina laatayna kulla nafsin hudaha walakin haqqa alqawlu minnee laamlaanna jahannama mina aljinnati waalnnasi ajmaaeena
Fathooqoo bima naseetum liqaa yawmikum hatha inna naseenakum wathooqoo aathaba alkhuldi bima kuntum taamaloona
Innama yuminu biayatina allatheena itha thukkiroo biha kharroo sujjadan wasabbahoo bihamdi rabbihim wahum la yastakbiroona
Tatajafa junoobuhum aani almadajiai yadaoona rabbahum khawfan watamaaan wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona
Fala taalamu nafsun ma okhfiya lahum min qurrati aayunin jazaan bima kanoo yaamaloona
Afaman kana muminan kaman kana fasiqan la yastawoona
Amma allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati falahum jannatu almawa nuzulan bima kanoo yaamaloona
Waamma allatheena fasaqoo famawahumu alnnaru kullama aradoo an yakhrujoo minha oaeedoo feeha waqeela lahum thooqoo aathaba alnnari llathee kuntum bihi tukaththiboona
Walanutheeqannahum mina alaathabi aladna doona alaathabi alakbari laaallahum yarjiaoona
Waman athlamu mimman thukkira biayati rabbihi thumma aarada aanha inna mina almujrimeena muntaqimoona
Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba fala takun fee miryatin min liqaihi wajaaalnahu hudan libanee israeela
Wajaaalna minhum aimmatan yahdoona biamrina lamma sabaroo wakanoo biayatina yooqinoona
Inna rabbaka huwa yafsilu baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoona
Awalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakna min qablihim mina alqurooni yamshoona fee masakinihim inna fee thalika laayatin afala yasmaaoona
Awalam yaraw anna nasooqu almaa ila alardi aljuruzi fanukhriju bihi zaraan takulu minhu anaamuhum waanfusuhum afala yubsiroona
Wayaqooloona mata hatha alfathu in kuntum sadiqeena
Qul yawma alfathi la yanfaau allatheena kafaroo eemanuhum wala hum yuntharoona
Faaarid aanhum waintathir innahum muntathiroona
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu ittaqi Allaha wala tutiai alkafireena waalmunafiqeena inna Allaha kana aaleeman hakeeman
Waittabia ma yooha ilayka min rabbika inna Allaha kana bima taamaloona khabeeran
Watawakkal aala Allahi wakafa biAllahi wakeelan
Ma jaaala Allahu lirajulin min qalbayni fee jawfihi wama jaaala azwajakumu allaee tuthahiroona minhunna ommahatikum wama jaaala daiyaakum abnaakum thalikum qawlukum biafwahikum waAllahu yaqoolu alhaqqa wahuwa yahdee alssabeela
Odaoohum liabaihim huwa aqsatu ainda Allahi fain lam taalamoo abaahum faikhwanukum fee alddeeni wamawaleekum walaysa aalaykum junahun eema akhtatum bihi walakin ma taaammadat quloobukum wakana Allahu ghafooran raheeman
Alnnabiyyu awla bialmumineena min anfusihim waazwajuhu ommahatuhum waoloo alarhami baaduhum awla bibaadin fee kitabi Allahi mina lmumineena waalmuhajireena illa an tafaaloo ila awliyaikum maaroofan kana thalika fee alkitabi mastooran
Waith akhathna mina alnnabiyyeena meethaqahum waminka wamin noohin waibraheema wamoosa waaeesa ibni maryama waakhathna minhum meethaqan haleethan
Liyasala alssadiqeena aan sidqihim waaaadda lilkafireena aathaban aleeman
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo othkuroo niamata Allahi aalaykum ith jaatkum junoodun faarsalna aalayhim reehan wajunoodan lam tarawha akana Allahu bima taamaloona baseeran
Ith jaookum min fawqikum wamin asfala minkum waith zaghati alabsaru wabalaghati alquloobu alhanajira watathunnoona biAllahi alththunoona
Hunalika ibtuliya almuminoona wazulziloo zilzalan shadeedan
Waith yaqoolu almunafiqoona waallatheena fee quloobihim maradun ma waaadana Allahu warasooluhu illa ghurooran
Waith qalat taifatun minhum ya ahla yathriba la muqama lakum fairjiaoo wayastathinu fareequn minhumu alnnabiyya yaqooloona inna uyootana aawratun wama hiya biaawratin in yureedoona illa firaran
Walaw dukhilat aalayhim min aqtariha thumma suiloo alfitnata laatawha wama talabbathoo biha illa yaseeran
Walaqad kanoo aahadoo Allaha min qablu la yuwalloona aladbara wakana aahdu Allahi masoolan
Qul lan yanfaaakumu alfiraru in farartum mina almawti awi alqatli waithan la tumattaaoona illa qaleelan
Qul man tha allathee yaasimukum mina Allahi in arada bikum sooan aw arada bikum rahmatan wala yajidoona lahum min dooni Allahi waliyyan ala naseeran
Qad yaalamu Allahu almuaawwiqeena minkum waalqaileena liikhwanihim halumma ilayna wala yatoona albasa illa qaleelan
Ashihhatan aalaykum faitha jaa alkhawfu raaytahum yanthuroona ilayka tadooru aayunuhum kaallathee yughsha aalayhi mina almawti faitha thahaba alkhawfu salaqookum bialsinatin hidadin ashihhatan aala alkhayri olaika lam yuminoo faahbata Allahu aamalahum wakana thalika ala Allahi yaseeran
Yahsaboona alahzaba lam yathhaboo wain yati alahzabu yawaddoo law annahum badoona fee alaarabi yasaloona aan anbaikum walaw kanoo eekum ma qataloo illa qaleelan
Laqad kana lakum fee rasooli Allahi oswatun hasanatun liman kana yarjoo Allaha waalyawma alakhira wathakara Allaha katheeran
Walamma raa almuminoona alahzaba qaloo hatha ma waaadana Allahu warasooluhu wasadaqa Allahu warasooluhu wama zadahum illa eemanan atasleeman
Mina almumineena rijalun sadaqoo ma aahadoo Allaha aalayhi faminhum man qada nahbahu waminhum man yantathiru wama baddaloo tabdeelan
Liyajziya Allahu alssadiqeena bisidqihim wayuaaththiba almunafiqeena in shaa aw yatooba aalayhim inna Allaha kana ghafooran raheeman
Waradda Allahu allatheena kafaroo bighaythihim lam yanaloo khayran wakafa Allahu almumineena alqitala wakana Allahu qawiyyan aazeezan
Waanzala allatheena thaharoohum min ahli alkitabi min sayaseehim waqathafa fee quloobihimu alrruaba fareeqan taqtuloona watasiroona areeqan
Waawrathakum ardahum wadiyarahum waamwalahum waardan lam tataooha wakana Allahu aala kulli shayin qadeeran
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu qul liazwajika in kuntunna turidna alhayata alddunya wazeenataha fataaalayna omattiakunna waosarrihkunna sarahan ameelan
Wain kuntunna turidna Allaha warasoolahu waalddara alakhirata fainna Allaha aaadda lilmuhsinati minkunna ajran aatheeman
Ya nisaa alnnabiyyi man yati minkunna bifahishatin mubayyinatin yudaaaf laha alaathabu diafayni wakana thalika aala Allahi yaseeran
Waman yaqnut minkunna lillahi warasoolihi wataamal salihan nutiha ajraha marratayni waaatadna laha rizqan kareeman
Ya nisaa alnnabiyyi lastunna kaahadin mina alnnisai ini ittaqaytunna fala takhdaana bialqawli fayatmaaa allathee fee qalbihi maradun aqulna qawlan maaroofan
Waqarna fee buyootikunna wala tabarrajna tabarruja aljahiliyyati aloola waaqimna alssalata waateena alzzakata waatiana Allaha arasoolahu innama yureedu Allahu liyuthhiba aankumu alrrijsa ahla albayti wayutahhirakum tatheeran
Waothkurna ma yutla fee buyootikunna min ayati Allahi waalhikmati inna Allaha kana lateefan khabeeran
Inna almuslimeena waalmuslimati waalmumineena waalmuminati waalqaniteena waalqanitati waalssadiqeena waalssadiqati waalssabireena waalssabirati waalkhashiaeena waalkhashiaati waalmutasaddiqeena waalmutasaddiqati waalssaimeena waalssaimati waalhafitheena furoojahum aalhafithati waalththakireena Allaha katheeran waalththakirati aaadda Allahu lahum maghfiratan waajran aatheeman
Wama kana limuminin wala muminatin itha qada Allahu warasooluhu amran an yakoona lahumu alkhiyaratu min amrihim waman yaasi Allaha arasoolahu faqad dalla dalalan mubeenan
Waith taqoolu lillathee anaama Allahu aalayhi waanaamta aalayhi amsik aalayka zawjaka waittaqi Allaha watukhfee fee nafsika ma Allahu mubdeehi watakhsha alnnasa waAllahu ahaqqu an takhshahu falamma qada zaydun minha wataran zawwajnakaha likay la yakoona aala almumineena arajun fee azwaji adaiyaihim itha qadaw minhunna wataran wakana amru Allahi mafaoolan
Ma kana aala alnnabiyyi min harajin feema farada Allahu lahu sunnata Allahi fee allatheena khalaw min qablu wakana amru Allahi qadaran aqdooran
Allatheena yuballighoona risalati Allahi wayakhshawnahu wala yakhshawna ahadan illa Allaha wakafa biAllahi haseeban
Ma kana muhammadun aba ahadin min rijalikum walakin rasoola Allahi wakhatama alnnabiyyeena wakana Allahu bikulli shayin aaleeman
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo othkuroo Allaha thikran katheeran
Wasabbihoohu bukratan waaseelan
Huwa allathee yusallee aalaykum wamalaikatuhu liyukhrijakum mina alththulumati ila alnnoori wakana bialmumineena raheeman
Tahiyyatuhum yawma yalqawnahu salamun waaaadda lahum ajran kareeman
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu inna arsalnaka shahidan wamubashshiran wanatheeran
Wadaaiyan ila Allahi biithnihi wasirajan muneeran
Wabashshiri almumineena bianna lahum mina Allahi fadlan kabeeran
Wala tutiai alkafireena waalmunafiqeena wadaa athahum watawakkal aala Allahi wakafa biAllahi wakeelan
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha nakahtumu almuminati thumma tallaqtumoohunna min qabli an tamassoohunna fama lakum aalayhinna min iddatin taataddoonaha famattiaoohunna wasarrihoohunna sarahan jameelan
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu inna ahlalna laka azwajaka allatee atayta ojoorahunna wama malakat yameenuka mimma afaa Allahu aalayka wabanati aammika wabanati aammatika wabanati khalika wabanati khalatika allatee hajarna maaaka waimraatan muminatan in wahabat nafsaha lilnnabiyyi in arada alnnabiyyu an yastankihaha khalisatan laka min dooni almumineena qad aalimna ma faradna aalayhim fee azwajihim wama alakat aymanuhum likayla yakoona aalayka harajun wakana Allahu ghafooran raheeman
Turjee man tashao minhunna watuwee ilayka man tashao wamani ibtaghayta mimman aazalta fala junaha aalayka thalika adna an taqarra ayunuhunna wala yahzanna wayardayna bima ataytahunna kulluhunna waAllahu yaalamu ma fee quloobikum wakana Allahu aaleeman haleeman
La yahillu laka alnnisao min baadu wala an tabaddala bihinna min azwajin walaw aajabaka husnuhunna illa ma malakat yameenuka wakana llahu aala kulli shayin raqeeban
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tadkhuloo buyoota alnnabiyyi illa an yuthana lakum ila taaamin ghayra nathireena inahu walakin itha duaeetum faodkhuloo faitha taaimtum faintashiroo wala mustaniseena lihadeethin inna thalikum kana yuthee alnnabiyya fayastahyee minkum waAllahu la yastahyee mina alhaqqi waitha saaltumoohunna mataaan faisaloohunna min warai hijabin thalikum atharu liquloobikum waquloobihinna wama kana lakum an tuthoo rasoola Allahi wala an tankihoo azwajahu min baadihi abadan inna thalikum kana ainda Allahi atheeman
In tubdoo shayan aw tukhfoohu fainna Allaha kana bikulli shayin aaleeman
La junaha aalayhinna fee abaihinna wala abnaihinna wala ikhwanihinna wala abnai ikhwanihinna wala abnai akhawatihinna wala nisaihinna ala ma malakat aymanuhunna waittaqeena Allaha inna Allaha kana aala kulli shayin shaheedan
Inna Allaha wamalaikatahu yusalloona aala alnnabiyyi ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo salloo aalayhi wasallimoo tasleeman
Inna allatheena yuthoona Allaha warasoolahu laaanahumu Allahu fee alddunya waalakhirati waaaadda lahum aathaban muheenan
Waallatheena yuthoona almumineena waalmuminati bighayri ma iktasaboo faqadi ihtamaloo buhtanan waithman mubeenan
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu qul liazwajika wabanatika wanisai almumineena yudneena aalayhinna min jalabeebihinna thalika adna an yuarafna fala uthayna wakana Allahu ghafooran raheeman
Lain lam yantahi almunafiqoona waallatheena fee quloobihim maradun waalmurjifoona fee almadeenati lanughriyannaka bihim thumma la ujawiroonaka feeha illa qaleelan
Malaooneena aynama thuqifoo okhithoo waquttiloo taqteelan
Sunnata Allahi fee allatheena khalaw min qablu walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeelan
Yasaluka alnnasu aani alssaaati qul innama ailmuha ainda Allahi wama yudreeka laaalla alssaaata takoonu qareeban
Inna Allaha laaana alkafireena waaaadda lahum saaeeran
Khalideena feeha abadan la yajidoona waliyyan wala naseeran
Yawma tuqallabu wujoohuhum fee alnnari yaqooloona ya laytana ataana Allaha waataana alrrasoola
Waqaloo rabbana inna ataana sadatana wakubaraana faadalloona alssabeela
Rabbana atihim diafayni mina alaathabi wailaanhum laanan kabeeran
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la takoonoo kaallatheena athaw moosa fabarraahu Allahu mimma qaloo wakana ainda Allahi wajeehan
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha waqooloo qawlan sadeedan
Yuslih lakum aamalakum wayaghfir lakum thunoobakum waman yutiai Allaha warasoolahu faqad faza fawzan aatheeman
Inna aaradna alamanata aala alssamawati waalardi waaljibali faabayna an yahmilnaha waashfaqna minha wahamalaha alinsanu innahu kana halooman jahoolan
Liyuaaththiba Allahu almunafiqeena waalmunafiqati waalmushrikeena waalmushrikati wayatooba Allahu aala almumineena waalmuminati wakana llahu ghafooran raheeman
Alhamdu lillahi allathee lahu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi walahu alhamdu fee alakhirati wahuwa alhakeemu alkhabeeru
Yaalamu ma yaliju fee alardi wama yakhruju minha wama yanzilu mina alssamai wama yaaruju feeha wahuwa alrraheemu alghafooru
Waqala allatheena kafaroo la tateena alssaaatu qul bala warabbee latatiyannakum aalimi alghaybi la yaazubu aanhu mithqalu tharratin fee lssamawati wala fee alardi wala asgharu min thalika wala akbaru illa fee kitabin mubeenin
Liyajziya allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati olaika lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareemun
Waallatheena saaaw fee ayatina muaajizeena olaika lahum aathabun min rijzin aleemin
Wayara allatheena ootoo alailma allathee onzila ilayka min rabbika huwa alhaqqa wayahdee ila sirati alaazeezi alhameedi
Waqala allatheena kafaroo hal nadullukum aala rajulin yunabbiokum itha muzziqtum kulla mumazzaqin innakum lafee khalqin jadeedin
Aftara aala Allahi kathiban am bihi jinnatun bali allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati fee alaathabi waalddalali albaaeedi
Afalam yaraw ila ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum mina alssamai waalardi in nasha nakhsif bihimu alarda aw nusqit aalayhim kisafan mina lssamai inna fee thalika laayatan likulli aabdin muneebin
Walaqad atayna dawooda minna fadlan ya jibalu awwibee maaahu waalttayra waalanna lahu alhadeeda
Ani iamal sabighatin waqaddir fee alssardi waiamaloo salihan innee bima taamaloona baseerun
Walisulaymana alrreeha ghuduwwuha shahrun warawahuha shahrun waasalna lahu aayna alqitri wamina aljinni man yaamalu bayna yadayhi iithni rabbihi waman yazigh minhum aan amrina nuthiqhu min aathabi alssaaeeri
Yaamaloona lahu ma yashao min mahareeba watamatheela wajifanin kaaljawabi waqudoorin rasiyatin iamaloo ala dawooda shukran waqaleelun in aibadiya alshshakooru
Falamma qadayna aalayhi almawta ma dallahum aala mawtihi illa dabbatu alardi takulu minsaatahu falamma kharra tabayyanati aljinnu an aw kanoo yaalamoona alghayba ma labithoo fee alaathabi almuheeni
Laqad kana lisabain fee maskanihim ayatun jannatani aan yameenin washimalin kuloo min rizqi rabbikum waoshkuroo lahu baldatun ayyibatun warabbun ghafoorun
Faaaradoo faarsalna aalayhim sayla alaarimi wabaddalnahum bijannatayhim jannatayni thawatay okulin khamtin waathlin washayin min sidrin aleelin
Thalika jazaynahum bima kafaroo wahal nujazee illa alkafoora
Wajaaalna baynahum wabayna alqura allatee barakna feeha quran thahiratan waqaddarna feeha alssayra seeroo feeha layaliya waayyaman mineena
Faqaloo rabbana baaid bayna asfarina wathalamoo anfusahum fajaaalnahum ahadeetha wamazzaqnahum kulla mumazzaqin inna fee thalika aayatin likulli sabbarin shakoorin
Walaqad saddaqa aalayhim ibleesu thannahu faittabaaoohu illa fareeqan mina almumineena
Wama kana lahu aalayhim min sultanin illa linaalama man yuminu bialakhirati mimman huwa minha fee shakkin warabbuka aala kulli shayin afeethun
Quli odaoo allatheena zaaamtum min dooni Allahi la yamlikoona mithqala tharratin fee alssamawati wala fee alardi wama lahum feehima min hirkin wama lahu minhum min thaheerin
Wala tanfaau alshshafaaatu aindahu illa liman athina lahu hatta itha fuzziaa aan quloobihim qaloo matha qala rabbukum qaloo alhaqqa ahuwa alaaliyyu alkabeeru
Qul man yarzuqukum mina alssamawati waalardi quli Allahu wainna aw iyyakum laaala hudan aw fee dalalin mubeenin
Qul la tusaloona aamma ajramna wala nusalu aamma taamaloona
Qul yajmaau baynana rabbuna thumma yaftahu baynana bialhaqqi wahuwa alfattahu alaaleemu
Qul arooniya allatheena alhaqtum bihi shurakaa kalla bal huwa Allahu alaazeezu alhakeemu
Wama arsalnaka illa kaffatan lilnnasi basheeran wanatheeran walakinna akthara alnnasi la yaalamoona
Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwaadu in kuntum sadiqeena
Qul lakum meeaadu yawmin la tastakhiroona aanhu saaatan wala tastaqdimoona
Waqala allatheena kafaroo lan numina bihatha alqurani wala biallathee bayna yadayhi walaw tara ithi alththalimoona mawqoofoona ainda abbihim yarjiau baaduhum ila baadin alqawla yaqoolu allatheena istudaifoo lillatheena istakbaroo lawla antum lakunna mumineena
Qala allatheena istakbaroo lillatheena istudaifoo anahnu sadadnakum aani alhuda baada ith jaakum bal kuntum mujrimeena
Waqala allatheena istudaifoo lillatheena istakbaroo bal makru allayli waalnnahari ith tamuroonana an nakfura biAllahi wanajaala lahu andadan waasarroo alnnadamata lamma raawoo alaathaba wajaaalna alaghlala fee aanaqi allatheena kafaroo hal yujzawna illa ma kanoo aamaloona
Wama arsalna fee qaryatin min natheerin illa qala mutrafooha inna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroona
Waqaloo nahnu aktharu amwalan waawladan wama nahnu bimuaaththabeena
Qul inna rabbee yabsutu alrrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru walakinna akthara alnnasi la yaalamoona
Wama amwalukum wala awladukum biallatee tuqarribukum aindana zulfa illa man amana waaamila salihan faolaika lahum jazao alddiafi bima amiloo wahum fee alghurufati aminoona
Waallatheena yasaawna fee ayatina muaajizeena olaika fee alaathabi muhdaroona
Qul inna rabbee yabsutu alrrizqa liman yashao min aibadihi wayaqdiru lahu wama anfaqtum min shayin fahuwa yukhlifuhu wahuwa khayru lrraziqeena
Wayawma yahshuruhum jameeaan thumma yaqoolu lilmalaikati ahaolai iyyakum kanoo yaabudoona
Qaloo subhanaka anta waliyyuna min doonihim bal kanoo yaabudoona aljinna aktharuhum bihim muminoona
Faalyawma la yamliku baadukum libaadin nafaan wala darran wanaqoolu lillatheena thalamoo thooqoo aathaba alnnari allatee kuntum biha ukaththiboona
Waitha tutla aalayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qaloo ma hatha illa rajulun yureedu an yasuddakum aamma kana yaabudu abaokum waqaloo ma hatha lla ifkun muftaran waqala allatheena kafaroo lilhaqqi lamma jaahum in hatha illa sihrun mubeenun
Wama ataynahum min kutubin yadrusoonaha wama arsalna ilayhim qablaka min natheerin
Wakaththaba allatheena min qablihim wama balaghoo miashara ma ataynahum fakaththaboo rusulee fakayfa kana nakeeri
Qul innama aaithukum biwahidatin an taqoomoo lillahi mathna wafurada thumma tatafakkaroo ma bisahibikum min jinnatin in huwa illa atheerun lakum bayna yaday aathabin shadeedin
Qul ma saaltukum min ajrin fahuwa lakum in ajriya illa aala Allahi wahuwa aala kulli shayin shaheedun
Qul inna rabbee yaqthifu bialhaqqi aallamu alghuyoobi
Qul jaa alhaqqu wama yubdio albatilu wama yuaeedu
Qul in dalaltu fainnama adillu aala nafsee waini ihtadaytu fabima yoohee ilayya rabbee innahu sameeaun qareebun
Walaw tara ith faziaoo fala fawta waokhithoo min makanin qareebin
Waqaloo amanna bihi waanna lahumu alttanawushu min makanin baaeedin
Waqad kafaroo bihi min qablu wayaqthifoona bialghaybi min makanin baaeedin
Waheela baynahum wabayna ma yashtahoona kama fuaila biashyaaihim min qablu innahum kanoo fee shakkin mureebin
Alhamdu lillahi fatiri alssamawati waalardi jaaili almalaikati rusulan olee ajnihatin mathna wathulatha warubaaa yazeedu fee alkhalqi a yashao inna Allaha aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Ma yaftahi Allahu lilnnasi min rahmatin fala mumsika laha wama yumsik fala mursila lahu min baadihi wahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Ya ayyuha alnnasu othkuroo niamata Allahi aalaykum hal min khaliqin ghayru Allahi yarzuqukum mina alssamai waalardi la ilaha illa huwa aanna tufakoona
Wain yukaththibooka faqad kuththibat rusulun min qablika waila Allahi turjaau alomooru
Ya ayyuha alnnasu inna waada Allahi haqqun fala taghurrannakumu alhayatu alddunya wala yaghurrannakum biAllahi algharooru
Inna alshshaytana lakum aaduwwun faittakhithoohu aaduwwan innama yadaoo hizbahu liyakoonoo min ashabi alssaaeeri
Allatheena kafaroo lahum aathabun shadeedun waallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeerun
Afaman zuyyina lahu sooo aamalihi faraahu hasanan fainna Allaha yudillu man yashao wayahdee man yashao fala tathhab nafsuka aalayhim asaratin inna Allaha aaleemun bima yasnaaoona
WaAllahu allathee arsala alrriyaha fatutheeru sahaban fasuqnahu ila baladin mayyitin faahyayna bihi alarda baada mawtiha kathalika lnnushooru
Man kana yureedu alaizzata falillahi alaizzatu jameeaan ilayhi yasaadu alkalimu alttayyibu waalaamalu alssalihu yarfaauhu waallatheena amkuroona alssayyiati lahum aathabun shadeedun wamakru olaika huwa yabooru
WaAllahu khalaqakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma jaaalakum azwajan wama tahmilu min ontha wala tadaau illa biailmihi wama uaammaru min muaammarin wala yunqasu min aumurihi illa fee kitabin inna thalika aala Allahi yaseerun
Wama yastawee albahrani hatha aathbun furatun saighun sharabuhu wahatha milhun ojajun wamin kullin takuloona lahman tariyyan atastakhrijoona hilyatan talbasoonaha watara alfulka feehi mawakhira litabtaghoo min fadlihi walaaallakum tashkuroona
Yooliju allayla fee alnnahari wayooliju alnnahara fee allayli wasakhkhara alshshamsa waalqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman halikumu Allahu rabbukum lahu almulku waallatheena tadaoona min doonihi ma yamlikoona min qitmeerin
In tadaoohum la yasmaaoo duaaakum walaw samiaoo ma istajaboo lakum wayawma alqiyamati yakfuroona bishirkikum wala yunabbioka mithlu habeerin
Ya ayyuha alnnasu antumu alfuqarao ila Allahi waAllahu huwa alghaniyyu alhameedu
In yasha yuthhibkum wayati bikhalqin jadeedin
Wama thalika aala Allahi biaazeezin
Wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra wain tadau muthqalatun ila himliha la yuhmal minhu shayon walaw kana tha qurba innama tunthiru llatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bialghaybi waaqamoo alssalata waman tazakka fainnama yatazakka linafsihi waila Allahi almaseeru
Wama yastawee alaama waalbaseeru
Wala alththulumatu wala alnnooru
Wala alththillu wala alharooru
Wama yastawee alahyao wala alamwatu inna Allaha yusmiau man yashao wama anta bimusmiain man fee alquboori
In anta illa natheerun
Inna arsalnaka bialhaqqi basheeran wanatheeran wain min ommatin illa khala feeha natheerun
Wain yukaththibooka faqad kaththaba allatheena min qablihim jaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati wabialzzuburi wabialkitabi almuneeri
Thumma akhathtu allatheena kafaroo fakayfa kana nakeeri
Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina alssamai maan faakhrajna bihi thamaratin mukhtalifan alwanuha wamina aljibali judadun beedun wahumrun ukhtalifun alwanuha wagharabeebu soodun
Wamina alnnasi waalddawabbi waalanaami mukhtalifun alwanuhu kathalika innama yakhsha Allaha min aibadihi alaulamao inna Allaha aazeezun hafoorun
Inna allatheena yatloona kitaba Allahi waaqamoo alssalata waanfaqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran waaalaniyatan yarjoona tijaratan lan taboora
Liyuwaffiyahum ojoorahum wayazeedahum min fadlihi innahu ghafoorun shakoorun
Waallathee awhayna ilayka mina alkitabi huwa alhaqqu musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi inna Allaha biaibadihi lakhabeerun baseerun
Thumma awrathna alkitaba allatheena istafayna min aibadina faminhum thalimun linafsihi waminhum muqtasidun waminhum sabiqun ialkhayrati biithni Allahi thalika huwa alfadlu alkabeeru
Jannatu aadnin yadkhuloonaha yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin waluluan walibasuhum feeha hareerun
Waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee athhaba aanna alhazana inna rabbana laghafoorun shakoorun
Allathee ahallana dara almuqamati min fadlihi la yamassuna feeha nasabun wala yamassuna feeha lughoobun
Waallatheena kafaroo lahum naru jahannama la yuqda aalayhim fayamootoo wala yukhaffafu aanhum min aathabiha kathalika najzee kulla afoorin
Wahum yastarikhoona feeha rabbana akhrijna naamal salihan ghayra allathee kunna naamalu awalam nuaammirkum ma yatathakkaru feehi man athakkara wajaakumu alnnatheeru fathooqoo fama lilththalimeena min naseerin
Inna Allaha aalimu ghaybi alssamawati waalardi innahu aaleemun bithati alssudoori
Huwa allathee jaaalakum khalaifa fee alardi faman kafara faaalayhi kufruhu wala yazeedu alkafireena kufruhum ainda rabbihim illa maqtan ala yazeedu alkafireena kufruhum illa khasaran
Qul araaytum shurakaakumu allatheena tadaoona min dooni Allahi aroonee matha khalaqoo mina alardi am lahum shirkun fee alssamawati am taynahum kitaban fahum aala bayyinatin minhu bal in yaaidu alththalimoona baaduhum baadan illa ghurooran
Inna Allaha yumsiku alssamawati waalarda an tazoola walain zalata in amsakahuma min ahadin min baadihi innahu kana haleeman ghafooran
Waaqsamoo biAllahi jahda aymanihim lain jaahum natheerun layakoonunna ahda min ihda alomami falamma jaahum natheerun ma zadahum illa ufooran
Istikbaran fee alardi wamakra alssayyii wala yaheequ almakru alssayyio illa biahlihi fahal yanthuroona illa sunnata alawwaleena falan ajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeelan walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tahweelan
Awalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu allatheena min qablihim wakanoo ashadda minhum quwwatan wama kana Allahu iyuajizahu min shayin fee alssamawati wala fee alardi innahu kana aaleeman qadeeran
Walaw yuakhithu Allahu alnnasa bima kasaboo ma taraka aala thahriha min dabbatin walakin yuakhkhiruhum ila ajalin musamman faitha jaa jaluhum fainna Allaha kana biaibadihi baseeran

Inna jaaalna fee aanaqihim aghlalan fahiya ila alathqani fahum muqmahoona
Wajaaalna min bayni aydeehim saddan wamin khalfihim saddan faaghshaynahum fahum la yubsiroona
Wasawaon aalayhim aanthartahum am lam tunthirhum la yuminoona
Innama tunthiru mani ittabaaa alththikra wakhashiya alrrahmana bialghaybi fabashshirhu bimaghfiratin waajrin kareemin
Inna nahnu nuhyee almawta wanaktubu ma qaddamoo waatharahum wakulla shayin ahsaynahu fee imamin mubeenin
Waidrib lahum mathalan ashaba alqaryati ith jaaha almursaloona
Ith arsalna ilayhimu ithnayni fakaththaboohuma faaazzazna bithalithin faqaloo inna ilaykum mursaloona
Qaloo ma antum illa basharun mithluna wama anzala alrrahmanu min shayin in antum illa takthiboona
Qaloo rabbuna yaalamu inna ilaykum lamursaloona
Wama aalayna illa albalaghu almubeenu
Qaloo inna tatayyarna bikum lain lam tantahoo lanarjumannakum walayamassannakum minna aathabun aleemun
Qaloo tairukum maaakum ain thukkirtum bal antum qawmun musrifoona
Wajaa min aqsa almadeenati rajulun yasaa qala ya qawmi ittabiaoo almursaleena
Ittabiaoo man la yasalukum ajran wahum muhtadoona
Wama liya la aabudu allathee fataranee wailayhi turjaaoona
Aattakhithu min doonihi alihatan in yuridni alrrahmanu bidurrin la tughni aannee shafaaatuhum shayan wala yunqithooni
Innee ithan lafee dalalin mubeenin
Innee amantu birabbikum faismaaooni
Qeela odkhuli aljannata qala ya layta qawmee yaalamoona
Bima ghafara lee rabbee wajaaalanee mina almukrameena
Wama anzalna aala qawmihi min baadihi min jundin mina alssamai wama kunna munzileena
In kanat illa sayhatan wahidatan faitha hum khamidoona
Ya hasratan aala alaibadi ma yateehim min rasoolin illa kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Alam yaraw kam ahlakna qablahum mina alqurooni annahum ilayhim la yarjiaoona
Wain kullun lamma jameeaun ladayna muhdaroona
Waayatun lahumu alardu almaytatu ahyaynaha waakhrajna minha habban faminhu yakuloona
Wajaaalna feeha jannatin min nakheelin waaanabin wafajjarna feeha mina alauyooni
Liyakuloo min thamarihi wama aamilathu aydeehim afala yashkuroona
Subhana allathee khalaqa alazwaja kullaha mimma tunbitu alardu wamin anfusihim wamimma la yaalamoona
Waayatun lahumu allaylu naslakhu minhu alnnahara faitha hum muthlimoona
Waalshshamsu tajree limustaqarrin laha thalika taqdeeru alaazeezi alaaleemi
Waalqamara qaddarnahu manazila hatta aada kaalaurjooni alqadeemi
La alshshamsu yanbaghee laha an tudrika alqamara wala allaylu sabiqu alnnahari wakullun fee falakin yasbahoona
Waayatun lahum anna hamalna thurriyyatahum fee alfulki almashhooni
Wakhalaqna lahum min mithlihi ma yarkaboona
Wain nasha nughriqhum fala sareekha lahum wala hum yunqathoona

Ajaaala alalihata ilahan wahidan inna hatha lashayon aujabun

Am aindahum khazainu rahmati rabbika alaazeezi alwahhabi

Isbir aala ma yaqooloona waothkur aabdana dawooda tha alaydi innahu awwabun
Inna sakhkharna aljibala maaahu yusabbihna bialaashiyyi waalishraqi
Waalttayra mahshooratan kullun lahu awwabun
Washadadna mulkahu waataynahu alhikmata wafasla alkhitabi
Wahal ataka nabao alkhasmi ith tasawwaroo almihraba
Ith dakhaloo aala dawooda fafaziaa minhum qaloo la takhaf khasmani bagha baaduna aala baadin faohkum baynana bialhaqqi wala tushtit aihdina ila sawai alssirati
Inna hatha akhee lahu tisaun watisaoona naajatan waliya naajatun wahidatun faqala akfilneeha waaazzanee fee alkhitabi
Qala laqad thalamaka bisuali naajatika ila niaajihi wainna katheeran mina alkhulatai layabghee baaduhum aala baadin illa allatheena manoo waaamiloo alssalihati waqaleelun ma hum wathanna dawoodu annama fatannahu faistaghfara rabbahu wakharra rakiaan waanaba
Faghafarna lahu thalika wainna lahu aindana lazulfa wahusna maabin
Ya dawoodu inna jaaalnaka khaleefatan fee alardi faohkum bayna alnnasi bialhaqqi wala tattabiai alhawa fayudillaka aan sabeeli Allahi nna allatheena yadilloona aan sabeeli Allahi lahum aathabun shadeedun bima nasoo yawma alhisabi
Wama khalaqna alssamaa waalarda wama baynahuma batilan thalika thannu allatheena kafaroo fawaylun lillatheena kafaroo mina alnnari
Am najaalu allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati kaalmufsideena fee alardi am najaalu almuttaqeena kaalfujjari

Antum aanhu muaridoona

Ith qala rabbuka lilmalaikati innee khaliqun basharan min teenin

Fasajada almalaikatu kulluhum ajmaaoona

Qala fainnaka mina almunthareena
