Qul ma asalukum aalayhi min ajrin wama ana mina almutakallifeena
In huwa illa thikrun lilaalameena
Walataalamunna nabaahu baada heenin
Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi alaazeezi alhakeemi
Inna anzalna ilayka alkitaba bialhaqqi faoabudi Allaha mukhlisan lahu alddeena
Ala lillahi alddeenu alkhalisu waallatheena ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa ma naabuduhum illa liyuqarriboona ila Allahi zulfa inna llaha yahkumu baynahum fee ma hum feehi yakhtalifoona inna Allaha la yahdee man huwa kathibun kaffarun
Law arada Allahu an yattakhitha waladan laistafa mimma yakhluqu ma yashao subhanahu huwa Allahu alwahidu alqahharu
Khalaqa alssamawati waalarda bialhaqqi yukawwiru allayla aala alnnahari wayukawwiru alnnahara aala allayli wasakhkhara alshshamsa aalqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman ala huwa alaazeezu alghaffaru
Khalaqakum min nafsin wahidatin thumma jaaala minha zawjaha waanzala lakum mina alanaami thamaniyata azwajin yakhluqukum fee butooni ommahatikum khalqan min baadi khalqin fee thulumatin thalathin thalikumu Allahu rabbukum lahu almulku la ilaha illa huwa faanna usrafoona
In takfuroo fainna Allaha ghaniyyun aankum wala yarda liaibadihi alkufra wain tashkuroo yardahu lakum wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra humma ila rabbikum marjiaukum fayunabbiokum bima kuntum taamaloona innahu aaleemun bithati alssudoori
Waitha massa alinsana durrun daaa rabbahu muneeban ilayhi thumma itha khawwalahu niamatan minhu nasiya ma kana yadaoo ilayhi min qablu ajaaala lillahi andadan liyudilla aan sabeelihi qul tamattaa bikufrika qaleelan innaka min ashabi alnnari
Amman huwa qanitun anaa allayli sajidan waqaiman yahtharu alakhirata wayarjoo rahmata rabbihi qul hal yastawee allatheena yaalamoona aallatheena la yaalamoona innama yatathakkaru oloo alalbabi
Qul ya aibadi allatheena amanoo ittaqoo rabbakum lillatheena ahsanoo fee hathihi alddunya hasanatun waardu Allahi wasiaatun innama uwaffa alssabiroona ajrahum bighayri hisabin
Qul innee omirtu an aabuda Allaha mukhlisan lahu alddeena
Waomirtu lian akoona awwala almuslimeena
Qul innee akhafu in aasaytu rabbee aathaba yawmin aatheemin
Quli Allaha aabudu mukhlisan lahu deenee
Faoabudoo ma shitum min doonihi qul inna alkhasireena allatheena khasiroo anfusahum waahleehim yawma alqiyamati ala thalika huwa lkhusranu almubeenu
Lahum min fawqihim thulalun mina alnnari wamin tahtihim thulalun thalika yukhawwifu Allahu bihi aibadahu ya aibadi faittaqooni
Waallatheena ijtanaboo alttaghoota an yaabudooha waanaboo ila Allahi lahumu albushra fabashshir aibadi
Allatheena yastamiaoona alqawla fayattabiaoona ahsanahu olaika allatheena hadahumu Allahu waolaika hum oloo alalbabi
Afaman haqqa aalayhi kalimatu alaathabi afaanta tunqithu man fee alnnari
Lakini allatheena ittaqaw rabbahum lahum ghurafun min fawqiha ghurafun mabniyyatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu waada Allahi la yukhlifu llahu almeeaada
Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina alssamai maan fasalakahu yanabeeaa fee alardi thumma yukhriju bihi zaraan mukhtalifan alwanuhu thumma aheeju fatarahu musfarran thumma yajaaluhu hutaman inna fee thalika lathikra liolee alalbabi
Afaman sharaha Allahu sadrahu lilislami fahuwa aala noorin min rabbihi fawaylun lilqasiyati quloobuhum min thikri Allahi olaika fee alalin mubeenin
Allahu nazzala ahsana alhadeethi kitaban mutashabihan mathaniya taqshaairru minhu juloodu allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum thumma taleenu ulooduhum waquloobuhum ila thikri Allahi thalika huda Allahi yahdee bihi man yashao waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min hadin
Afaman yattaqee biwajhihi sooa alaathabi yawma alqiyamati waqeela lilththalimeena thooqoo ma kuntum taksiboona
Kaththaba allatheena min qablihim faatahumu alaathabu min haythu la yashauroona
Faathaqahumu Allahu alkhizya fee alhayati alddunya walaaathabu alakhirati akbaru law kanoo yaalamoona
Walaqad darabna lilnnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin laaallahum yatathakkaroona
Quranan aarabiyyan ghayra thee aiwajin laaallahum yattaqoona
Daraba Allahu mathalan rajulan feehi shurakao mutashakisoona warajulan salaman lirajulin hal yastawiyani mathalan alhamdu lillahi bal ktharuhum la yaalamoona
Innaka mayyitun wainnahum mayyitoona
Thumma innakum yawma alqiyamati ainda rabbikum takhtasimoona
Faman athlamu mimman kathaba aala Allahi wakaththaba bialssidqi ith jaahu alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilkafireena
Waallathee jaa bialssidqi wasaddaqa bihi olaika humu almuttaqoona
Lahum ma yashaoona ainda rabbihim thalika jazao almuhsineena
Liyukaffira Allahu aanhum aswaa allathee aamiloo wayajziyahum ajrahum biahsani allathee kanoo yaamaloona
Alaysa Allahu bikafin aabdahu wayukhawwifoonaka biallatheena min doonihi waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min hadin
Waman yahdi Allahu fama lahu min mudillin alaysa Allahu biaazeezin thee intiqamin
Walain saaltahum man khalaqa alssamawati waalarda layaqoolunna Allahu qul afaraaytum ma tadaoona min dooni Allahi in aradaniya Allahu bidurrin hal hunna kashifatu durrihi aw aradanee birahmatin hal hunna mumsikatu rahmatihi qul hasbiya Allahu aalayhi yatawakkalu lmutawakkiloona
Qul ya qawmi iamaloo aala makanatikum innee aamilun fasawfa taalamoona
Man yateehi aathabun yukhzeehi wayahillu aalayhi aathabun muqeemun
Inna anzalna aalayka alkitaba lilnnasi bialhaqqi famani ihtada falinafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu aalayha wama anta aalayhim iwakeelin
Allahu yatawaffa alanfusa heena mawtiha waallatee lam tamut fee manamiha fayumsiku allatee qada aalayha almawta wayursilu alokhra ila jalin musamman inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroona
Ami ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi shufaaaa qul awalaw kanoo la yamlikoona shayan wala yaaqiloona
Qul lillahi alshshafaaatu jameeaan lahu mulku alssamawati waalardi thumma ilayhi turjaaoona
Waitha thukira Allahu wahdahu ishmaazzat quloobu allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati waitha thukira allatheena min doonihi itha hum astabshiroona
Quli allahumma fatira alssamawati waalardi aalima alghaybi waalshshahadati anta tahkumu bayna aibadika fee ma kanoo feehi yakhtalifoona
Walaw anna lillatheena thalamoo ma fee alardi jameeaan wamithlahu maaahu laiftadaw bihi min sooi alaathabi yawma alqiyamati wabada ahum mina Allahi ma lam yakoonoo yahtasiboona
Wabada lahum sayyiatu ma kasaboo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Faitha massa alinsana durrun daaana thumma itha khawwalnahu niamatan minna qala innama ooteetuhu aala ailmin bal hiya fitnatun alakinna aktharahum la yaalamoona
Qad qalaha allatheena min qablihim fama aghna aanhum ma kanoo yaksiboona
Faasabahum sayyiatu ma kasaboo waallatheena thalamoo min haolai sayuseebuhum sayyiatu ma kasaboo wama hum bimuajizeena
Awalam yaalamoo anna Allaha yabsutu alrrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoona
Qul ya aibadiya allatheena asrafoo aala anfusihim la taqnatoo min rahmati Allahi inna Allaha yaghfiru alththunooba jameeaan innahu huwa lghafooru alrraheemu
Waaneeboo ila rabbikum waaslimoo lahu min qabli an yatiyakumu alaathabu thumma la tunsaroona
Waittabiaoo ahsana ma onzila ilaykum min rabbikum min qabli an yatiyakumu alaathabu baghtatan waantum la tashauroona
An taqoola nafsun ya hasrata aala ma farrattu fee janbi Allahi wain kuntu lamina alssakhireena
Aw taqoola law anna Allaha hadanee lakuntu mina almuttaqeena
Aw taqoola heena tara alaathaba law anna lee karratan faakoona mina almuhsineena
Bala qad jaatka ayatee fakaththabta biha waistakbarta wakunta mina alkafireena
Wayawma alqiyamati tara allatheena kathaboo aala Allahi wujoohuhum muswaddatun alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilmutakabbireena
Wayunajjee Allahu allatheena ittaqaw bimafazatihim la yamassuhumu alssooo wala hum yahzanoona
Allahu khaliqu kulli shayin wahuwa aala kulli shayin wakeelun
Lahu maqaleedu alssamawati waalardi waallatheena kafaroo biayati Allahi olaika humu alkhasiroona
Qul afaghayra Allahi tamuroonnee aabudu ayyuha aljahiloona
Walaqad oohiya ilayka waila allatheena min qablika lain ashrakta layahbatanna aamaluka walatakoonanna mina alkhasireena
Bali Allaha faoabud wakun mina alshshakireena
Wama qadaroo Allaha haqqa qadrihi waalardu jameeaan qabdatuhu yawma alqiyamati waalssamawatu matwiyyatun biyameenihi subhanahu wataaala amma yushrikoona
Wanufikha fee alssoori fasaaiqa man fee alssamawati waman fee alardi illa man shaa Allahu thumma nufikha feehi okhra faitha hum qiyamun anthuroona
Waashraqati alardu binoori rabbiha wawudiaa alkitabu wajeea bialnnabiyyeena waalshshuhadai waqudiya baynahum bialhaqqi wahum la uthlamoona
Wawuffiyat kullu nafsin ma aamilat wahuwa aalamu bima yafaaloona
Waseeqa allatheena kafaroo ila jahannama zumaran hatta itha jaooha futihat abwabuha waqala lahum khazanatuha alam yatikum rusulun minkum yatloona aalaykum ayati rabbikum wayunthiroonakum liqaa yawmikum hatha qaloo bala walakin haqqat kalimatu alaathabi aala lkafireena
Qeela odkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha fabisa mathwa almutakabbireena
Waseeqa allatheena ittaqaw rabbahum ila aljannati zumaran hatta itha jaooha wafutihat abwabuha waqala lahum khazanatuha salamun alaykum tibtum faodkhulooha khalideena
Waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee sadaqana waadahu waawrathana alarda natabawwao mina aljannati haythu nashao faniama ajru alaamileena
Watara almalaikata haffeena min hawli alaarshi yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim waqudiya baynahum bialhaqqi waqeela alhamdu lillahi rabbi laalameena
Hameem
Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi alaazeezi alaaleemi
Ghafiri alththanbi waqabili alttawbi shadeedi alaiqabi thee alttawli la ilaha illa huwa ilayhi almaseeru
Ma yujadilu fee ayati Allahi illa allatheena kafaroo fala yaghrurka taqallubuhum fee albiladi
Kaththabat qablahum qawmu noohin waalahzabu min baadihim wahammat kullu ommatin birasoolihim liyakhuthoohu wajadaloo bialbatili iyudhidoo bihi alhaqqa faakhathtuhum fakayfa kana aiqabi
Wakathalika haqqat kalimatu rabbika aala allatheena kafaroo annahum ashabu alnnari
Allatheena yahmiloona alaarsha waman hawlahu yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim wayuminoona bihi wayastaghfiroona lillatheena amanoo rabbana asiata kulla shayin rahmatan waailman faighfir lillatheena taboo waittabaaoo sabeelaka waqihim aathaba aljaheemi
Rabbana waadkhilhum jannati aadnin allatee waaadtahum waman salaha min abaihim waazwajihim wathurriyyatihim innaka anta alaazeezu lhakeemu
Waqihimu alssayyiati waman taqi alssayyiati yawmaithin faqad rahimtahu wathalika huwa alfawzu alaatheemu
Inna allatheena kafaroo yunadawna lamaqtu Allahi akbaru min maqtikum anfusakum ith tudaawna ila aleemani fatakfuroona
Qaloo rabbana amattana ithnatayni waahyaytana ithnatayni faiatarafna bithunoobina fahal ila khuroojin min sabeelin
Thalikum biannahu itha duaiya Allahu wahdahu kafartum wain yushrak bihi tuminoo faalhukmu lillahi alaaliyyi alkabeeri
Huwa allathee yureekum ayatihi wayunazzilu lakum mina alssamai rizqan wama yatathakkaru illa man yuneebu
Faodaoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu alddeena walaw kariha alkafiroona
Rafeeau alddarajati thoo alaarshi yulqee alrrooha min amrihi aala man yashao min aibadihi liyunthira yawma alttalaqi
Yawma hum barizoona la yakhfa aala Allahi minhum shayon limani almulku alyawma lillahi alwahidi alqahhari
Alyawma tujza kullu nafsin bima kasabat la thulma alyawma inna Allaha sareeau alhisabi
Waanthirhum yawma alazifati ithi alquloobu lada alhanajiri kathimeena ma lilththalimeena min hameemin wala shafeeain yutaau
Yaalamu khainata alaayuni wama tukhfee alssudooru
WaAllahu yaqdee bialhaqqi waallatheena yadaoona min doonihi la yaqdoona bishayin inna Allaha huwa alssameeau albaseeru
Awa lam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu allatheena kanoo min qablihim kanoo hum ashadda minhum quwwatan waatharan ee alardi faakhathahumu Allahu bithunoobihim wama kana lahum mina Allahi min waqin
Thalika biannahum kanat tateehim rusuluhum bialbayyinati fakafaroo faakhathahumu Allahu innahu qawiyyun shadeedu alaiqabi
Walaqad arsalna moosa biayatina wasultanin mubeenin
Ila firaawna wahamana waqaroona faqaloo sahirun kaththabun
Falamma jaahum bialhaqqi min aindina qaloo oqtuloo abnaa allatheena amanoo maaahu waistahyoo nisaahum wama kaydu alkafireena illa fee alalin
Waqala firaawnu tharoonee aqtul moosa walyadau rabbahu innee akhafu an yubaddila deenakum aw an yuthhira fee alardi alfasada
Waqala moosa innee authtu birabbee warabbikum min kulli mutakabbirin la yuminu biyawmi alhisabi
Waqala rajulun muminun min ali firaawna yaktumu eemanahu ataqtuloona rajulan an yaqoola rabbiyya Allahu waqad jaakum bialbayyinati min rabbikum wain yaku kathiban faaalayhi kathibuhu wain yaku sadiqan yusibkum baadu allathee yaaidukum inna Allaha la yahdee man huwa usrifun kaththabun
Ya qawmi lakumu almulku alyawma thahireena fee alardi faman yansuruna min basi Allahi in jaana qala firaawnu ma oreekum illa ma ara ama ahdeekum illa sabeela alrrashadi
Waqala allathee amana ya qawmi innee akhafu aalaykum mithla yawmi alahzabi
Mithla dabi qawmi noohin waaadin wathamooda waallatheena min baadihim wama Allahu yureedu thulman lilaibadi
Waya qawmi innee akhafu aalaykum yawma alttanadi
Yawma tuwalloona mudbireena ma lakum mina Allahi min aasimin waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min hadin
Walaqad jaakum yoosufu min qablu bialbayyinati fama ziltum fee shakkin mimma jaakum bihi hatta itha halaka qultum lan yabaatha Allahu in baadihi rasoolan kathalika yudillu Allahu man huwa musrifun murtabun
Allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi bighayri sultanin atahum kabura maqtan ainda Allahi waainda allatheena amanoo kathalika yatbaau llahu aala kulli qalbi mutakabbirin jabbarin
Waqala firaawnu ya hamanu ibni lee sarhan laaallee ablughu alasbaba
Asbaba alssamawati faattaliaa ila ilahi moosa wainnee laathunnuhu kathiban wakathalika zuyyina lifiraawna sooo aamalihi wasudda aani lssabeeli wama kaydu firaawna illa fee tababin
Waqala allathee amana ya qawmi ittabiaooni ahdikum sabeela alrrashadi
Ya qawmi innama hathihi alhayatu alddunya mataaun wainna alakhirata hiya daru alqarari
Man aamila sayyiatan fala yujza illa mithlaha waman aamila salihan min thakarin aw ontha wahuwa muminun faolaika yadkhuloona aljannata urzaqoona feeha bighayri hisabin
Waya qawmi ma lee adaookum ila alnnajati watadaoonanee ila alnnari
Tadaoonanee liakfura biAllahi waoshrika bihi ma laysa lee bihi ailmun waana adaookum ila alaazeezi alghaffari
La jarama annama tadaoonanee ilayhi laysa lahu daawatun fee alddunya wala fee alakhirati waanna maraddana ila Allahi waanna lmusrifeena hum ashabu alnnari
Fasatathkuroona ma aqoolu lakum waofawwidu amree ila Allahi inna Allaha baseerun bialaibadi
Fawaqahu Allahu sayyiati ma makaroo wahaqa biali firaawna sooo alaathabi
Alnnaru yuaradoona aalayha ghuduwwan waaashiyyan wayawma taqoomu alssaaatu adkhiloo ala firaawna ashadda alaathabi
Waith yatahajjoona fee alnnari fayaqoolu aldduaafao lillatheena istakbaroo inna kunna lakum tabaaan fahal antum mughnoona aanna aseeban mina alnnari
Qala allatheena istakbaroo inna kullun feeha inna Allaha qad hakama bayna alaibadi
Waqala allatheena fee alnnari likhazanati jahannama odaoo rabbakum yukhaffif aanna yawman mina alaathabi
Qaloo awalam taku tateekum rusulukum bialbayyinati qaloo bala qaloo faodaoo wama duaao alkafireena illa fee dalalin
Inna lanansuru rusulana waallatheena amanoo fee alhayati alddunya wayawma yaqoomu alashhadu
Yawma la yanfaau alththalimeena maathiratuhum walahumu allaanatu walahum sooo alddari
Walaqad atayna moosa alhuda waawrathna banee israeela alkitaba
Hudan wathikra liolee alalbabi
Faisbir inna waada Allahi haqqun waistaghfir lithanbika wasabbih bihamdi rabbika bialaashiyyi waalibkari
Inna allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi bighayri sultanin atahum in fee sudoorihim illa kibrun ma hum bibaligheehi faistaaith iAllahi innahu huwa alssameeau albaseeru
Lakhalqu alssamawati waalardi akbaru min khalqi alnnasi walakinna akthara alnnasi la yaalamoona
Wama yastawee alaama waalbaseeru waallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati wala almuseeo qaleelan ma tatathakkaroona
Inna alssaaata laatiyatun la rayba feeha walakinna akthara alnnasi la yuminoona
Waqala rabbukumu odaoonee astajib lakum inna allatheena yastakbiroona aan aibadatee sayadkhuloona jahannama dakhireena
Allahu allathee jaaala lakumu allayla litaskunoo feehi waalnnahara mubsiran inna Allaha lathoo fadlin aala alnnasi walakinna akthara lnnasi la yashkuroona
Thalikumu Allahu rabbukum khaliqu kulli shayin la ilaha illa huwa faanna tufakoona
Kathalika yufaku allatheena kanoo biayati Allahi yajhadoona
Allahu allathee jaaala lakumu alarda qararan waalssamaa binaan wasawwarakum faahsana suwarakum warazaqakum mina alttayyibati thalikumu llahu rabbukum fatabaraka Allahu rabbu alaalameena
Huwa alhayyu la ilaha illa huwa faodaoohu mukhliseena lahu alddeena alhamdu lillahi rabbi alaalameena
Qul innee nuheetu an aabuda allatheena tadaoona min dooni Allahi lamma jaaniya albayyinatu min rabbee waomirtu an oslima lirabbi laalameena
Huwa allathee khalaqakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma min aalaqatin thumma yukhrijukum tiflan thumma litablughoo ashuddakum humma litakoonoo shuyookhan waminkum man yutawaffa min qablu walitablughoo ajalan musamman walaaallakum taaqiloona
Huwa allathee yuhyee wayumeetu faitha qada amran fainnama yaqoolu lahu kun fayakoonu
Alam tara ila allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi anna yusrafoona
Allatheena kaththaboo bialkitabi wabima arsalna bihi rusulana fasawfa yaalamoona
Ithi alaghlalu fee aanaqihim waalssalasilu yushaboona
Fee alhameemi thumma fee alnnari yusjaroona
Thumma qeela lahum ayna ma kuntum tushrikoona
Min dooni Allahi qaloo dalloo aanna bal lam nakun nadaoo min qablu shayan kathalika yudillu Allahu alkafireena
Thalikum bima kuntum tafrahoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wabima kuntum tamrahoona
Odkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha fabisa mathwa almutakabbireena
Faisbir inna waada Allahi haqqun faimma nuriyannaka baada allathee naaiduhum aw natawaffayannaka failayna yurjaaoona
Walaqad arsalna rusulan min qablika minhum man qasasna aalayka waminhum man lam naqsus aalayka wama kana lirasoolin an yatiya biayatin lla biithni Allahi faitha jaa amru Allahi qudiya bialhaqqi wakhasira hunalika almubtiloona
Allahu allathee jaaala lakumu alanaama litarkaboo minha waminha takuloona
Walakum feeha manafiau walitablughoo aalayha hajatan fee sudoorikum waaalayha waaala alfulki tuhmaloona
Wayureekum ayatihi faayya ayati Allahi tunkiroona
Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu allatheena min qablihim kanoo akthara minhum waashadda quwwatan waatharan ee alardi fama aghna aanhum ma kanoo yaksiboona
Falamma jaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati farihoo bima aindahum mina alailmi wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Falamma raaw basana qaloo amanna biAllahi wahdahu wakafarna bima kunna bihi mushrikeena
Falam yaku yanfaauhum eemanuhum lamma raaw basana sunnata Allahi allatee qad khalat fee aibadihi wakhasira hunalika alkafiroona
Hameem
Tanzeelun mina alrrahmani alrraheemi
Kitabun fussilat ayatuhu quranan aarabiyyan liqawmin yaalamoona
Basheeran wanatheeran faaarada aktharuhum fahum la yasmaaoona
Waqaloo quloobuna fee akinnatin mimma tadaoona ilayhi wafee athanina waqrun wamin baynina wabaynika hijabun faiamal innana aamiloona
Qul innama ana basharun mithlukum yooha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun faistaqeemoo ilayhi waistaghfiroohu wawaylun ilmushrikeena
Allatheena la yutoona alzzakata wahum bialakhirati hum kafiroona
Inna allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati lahum ajrun ghayru mamnoonin
Qul ainnakum latakfuroona biallathee khalaqa alarda fee yawmayni watajaaloona lahu andadan thalika rabbu alaalameena
Wajaaala feeha rawasiya min fawqiha wabaraka feeha waqaddara feeha aqwataha fee arbaaati ayyamin sawaan lilssaileena
Thumma istawa ila alssamai wahiya dukhanun faqala laha walilardi itiya tawaan aw karhan qalata atayna taiaeena
Faqadahunna sabaa samawatin fee yawmayni waawha fee kulli samain amraha wazayyanna alssamaa alddunya bimasabeeha wahifthan thalika aqdeeru alaazeezi alaaleemi
Fain aaradoo fuqul anthartukum saaiqatan mithla saaiqati aadin wathamooda
Ith jaathumu alrrusulu min bayni aydeehim wamin khalfihim alla taabudoo illa Allaha qaloo law shaa rabbuna laanzala malaikatan fainna ima orsiltum bihi kafiroona
Faamma aadun faistakbaroo fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi waqaloo man ashaddu minna quwwatan awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqahum uwa ashaddu minhum quwwatan wakanoo biayatina yajhadoona
Faarsalna aalayhim reehan sarsaran fee ayyamin nahisatin linutheeqahum aathaba alkhizyi fee alhayati alddunya walaaathabu alakhirati khza wahum la yunsaroona
Waamma thamoodu fahadaynahum faistahabboo alaama aala alhuda faakhathathum saaiqatu alaathabi alhooni bima kanoo yaksiboona
Wanajjayna allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoona
Wayawma yuhsharu aadao Allahi ila alnnari fahum yoozaaoona
Hatta itha ma jaooha shahida aalayhim samauhum waabsaruhum wajulooduhum bima kanoo yaamaloona
Waqaloo lijuloodihim lima shahidtum aalayna qaloo antaqana Allahu allathee antaqa kulla shayin wahuwa khalaqakum awwala marratin ailayhi turjaaoona
Wama kuntum tastatiroona an yashhada aalaykum samaukum wala absarukum wala juloodukum walakin thanantum anna Allaha la yaalamu atheeran mimma taamaloona
Wathalikum thannukumu allathee thanantum birabbikum ardakum faasbahtum mina alkhasireena
Fain yasbiroo faalnnaru mathwan lahum wain yastaatiboo fama hum mina almuatabeena
Waqayyadna lahum quranaa fazayyanoo lahum ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum wahaqqa aalayhimu alqawlu fee omamin qad khalat min qablihim ina aljinni waalinsi innahum kanoo khasireena
Waqala allatheena kafaroo la tasmaaoo lihatha alqurani wailghaw feehi laaallakum taghliboona
Falanutheeqanna allatheena kafaroo aathaban shadeedan walanajziyannahum aswaa allathee kanoo yaamaloona
Thalika jazao aadai Allahi alnnaru lahum feeha daru alkhuldi jazaan bima kanoo biayatina yajhadoona
Waqala allatheena kafaroo rabbana arina allathayni adallana mina aljinni waalinsi najaalhuma tahta aqdamina liyakoona mina alasfaleena
Inna allatheena qaloo rabbuna Allahu thumma istaqamoo tatanazzalu aalayhimu almalaikatu alla takhafoo wala tahzanoo waabshiroo ialjannati allatee kuntum tooaadoona
Nahnu awliyaokum fee alhayati alddunya wafee alakhirati walakum feeha ma tashtahee anfusukum walakum feeha ma taddaaoona
Nuzulan min ghafoorin raheemin
Waman ahsanu qawlan mimman daaa ila Allahi waaamila salihan waqala innanee mina almuslimeena
Wala tastawee alhasanatu wala alssayyiatu idfaa biallatee hiya ahsanu faitha allathee baynaka wabaynahu aadawatun kaannahu waliyyun ameemun
Wama yulaqqaha illa allatheena sabaroo wama yulaqqaha illa thoo haththin aatheemin
Waimma yanzaghannaka mina alshshaytani nazghun faistaaith biAllahi innahu huwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Wamin ayatihi allaylu waalnnaharu waalshshamsu waalqamaru la tasjudoo lilshshamsi wala lilqamari waosjudoo lillahi alathee khalaqahunna n kuntum iyyahu taabudoona
Faini istakbaroo faallatheena ainda rabbika yusabbihoona lahu biallayli waalnnahari wahum la yasamoona
Wamin ayatihi annaka tara alarda khashiaatan faitha anzalna aalayha almaa ihtazzat warabat inna allathee ahyaha lamuhyee almawta innahu ala kulli shayin qadeerun
Inna allatheena yulhidoona fee ayatina la yakhfawna aalayna afaman yulqa fee alnnari khayrun am man yatee aminan yawma alqiyamati amaloo ma shitum innahu bima taamaloona baseerun
Inna allatheena kafaroo bialththikri lamma jaahum wainnahu lakitabun aazeezun
La yateehi albatilu min bayni yadayhi wala min khalfihi tanzeelun min hakeemin hameedin
Ma yuqalu laka illa ma qad qeela lilrrusuli min qablika inna rabbaka lathoo maghfiratin wathoo aiqabin aleemin
Walaw jaaalnahu quranan aajamiyyan laqaloo lawla fussilat ayatuhu aaajamiyyun waaarabiyyun qul huwa lillatheena amanoo hudan washifaon aallatheena la yuminoona fee athanihim waqrun wahuwa aalayhim aaman olaika yunadawna min makanin baaeedin
Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba faikhtulifa feehi walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum wainnahum lafee shakkin minhu ureebin
Man aamila salihan falinafsihi waman asaa faaalayha wama rabbuka bithallamin lilaabeedi
Ilayhi yuraddu ailmu alssaaati wama takhruju min thamaratin min akmamiha wama tahmilu min ontha wala tadaau illa biailmihi wayawma unadeehim ayna shurakaee qaloo athannaka ma minna min shaheedin
Wadalla aanhum ma kanoo yadaoona min qablu wathannoo ma lahum min maheesin
La yasamu alinsanu min duaai alkhayri wain massahu alshsharru fayaoosun qanootun
Walain athaqnahu rahmatan minna min baadi darraa massathu layaqoolanna hatha lee wama athunnu alssaaata qaimatan walain rujiatu ila abbee inna lee aindahu lalhusna falanunabbianna allatheena kafaroo bima aamiloo walanutheeqannahum min aathabin ghaleethin
Waitha anaamna aala alinsani aarada wanaa bijanibihi waitha massahu alshsharru fathoo duaain aareedin
Qul araaytum in kana min aindi Allahi thumma kafartum bihi man adallu mimman huwa fee shiqaqin baaeedin
Sanureehim ayatina fee alafaqi wafee anfusihim hatta yatabayyana lahum annahu alhaqqu awalam yakfi birabbika annahu aala kulli shayin haheedun
Ala innahum fee miryatin min liqai rabbihim ala innahu bikulli shayin muheetun
Hameem
aaynseenqaf
Kathalika yoohee ilayka waila allatheena min qablika Allahu alaazeezu alhakeemu
Lahu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wahuwa alaaliyyu alaatheemu
Takadu alssamawatu yatafattarna min fawqihinna waalmalaikatu yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim wayastaghfiroona liman fee alardi ala inna llaha huwa alghafooru alrraheemu
Waallatheena ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa Allahu hafeethun aalayhim wama anta aalayhim biwakeelin
Wakathalika awhayna ilayka quranan aarabiyyan litunthira omma alqura waman hawlaha watunthira yawma aljamai la rayba feehi fareequn fee ljannati wafareequn fee alssaaeeri
Walaw shaa Allahu lajaaalahum ommatan wahidatan walakin yudkhilu man yashao fee rahmatihi waalththalimoona ma lahum min waliyyin wala aseerin
Ami ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa faAllahu huwa alwaliyyu wahuwa yuhyee almawta wahuwa aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Wama ikhtalaftum feehi min shayin fahukmuhu ila Allahi thalikumu Allahu rabbee aalayhi tawakkaltu wailayhi oneebu
Fatiru alssamawati waalardi jaaala lakum min anfusikum azwajan wamina alanaami azwajan yathraokum feehi laysa kamithlihi shayon wahuwa lssameeau albaseeru
Lahu maqaleedu alssamawati waalardi yabsutu alrrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru innahu bikulli shayin aaleemun
Sharaaa lakum mina alddeeni ma wassa bihi noohan waallathee awhayna ilayka wama wassayna bihi ibraheema wamoosa waaeesa an aqeemoo alddeena wala tatafarraqoo feehi kabura aala almushrikeena ma tadaoohum ilayhi Allahu yajtabee ilayhi man yashao wayahdee ilayhi man uneebu
Wama tafarraqoo illa min baadi ma jaahumu alailmu baghyan baynahum walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika ila ajalin musamman laqudiya aynahum wainna allatheena oorithoo alkitaba min baadihim lafee shakkin minhu mureebin
Falithalika faodau waistaqim kama omirta wala tattabia ahwaahum waqul amantu bima anzala Allahu min kitabin waomirtu liaadila baynakum llahu rabbuna warabbukum lana aamaluna walakum aamalukum la hujjata baynana wabaynakumu Allahu yajmaau baynana wailayhi almaseeru
Waallatheena yuhajjoona fee Allahi min baadi ma istujeeba lahu hujjatuhum dahidatun ainda rabbihim waaalayhim ghadabun walahum aathabun hadeedun
Allahu allathee anzala alkitaba bialhaqqi waalmeezani wama yudreeka laaalla alssaaata qareebun
Yastaajilu biha allatheena la yuminoona biha waallatheena amanoo mushfiqoona minha wayaalamoona annaha alhaqqu ala inna allatheena umaroona fee alssaaati lafee dalalin baaeedin
Allahu lateefun biaibadihi yarzuqu man yashao wahuwa alqawiyyu alaazeezu
Man kana yureedu hartha alakhirati nazid lahu fee harthihi waman kana yureedu hartha alddunya nutihi minha wama lahu fee alakhirati min aseebin
Am lahum shurakao sharaaoo lahum mina alddeeni ma lam yathan bihi Allahu walawla kalimatu alfasli laqudiya baynahum wainna lththalimeena lahum aathabun aleemun
Tara alththalimeena mushfiqeena mimma kasaboo wahuwa waqiaun bihim waallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati fee rawdati aljannati ahum ma yashaoona ainda rabbihim thalika huwa alfadlu alkabeeru
Thalika allathee yubashshiru Allahu aibadahu allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati qul la asalukum aalayhi ajran illa almawaddata fee lqurba waman yaqtarif hasanatan nazid lahu feeha husnan inna Allaha ghafoorun shakoorun
Am yaqooloona iftara aala Allahi kathiban fain yashai Allahu yakhtim aala qalbika wayamhu Allahu albatila wayuhiqqu alhaqqa ikalimatihi innahu aaleemun bithati alssudoori
Wahuwa allathee yaqbalu alttawbata aan aibadihi wayaafoo aani alssayyiati wayaalamu ma tafaaloona
Wayastajeebu allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati wayazeeduhum min fadlihi waalkafiroona lahum aathabun shadeedun
Walaw basata Allahu alrrizqa liaibadihi labaghaw fee alardi walakin yunazzilu biqadarin ma yashao innahu biaibadihi khabeerun baseerun
Wahuwa allathee yunazzilu alghaytha min baadi ma qanatoo wayanshuru rahmatahu wahuwa alwaliyyu alhameedu
Wamin ayatihi khalqu alssamawati waalardi wama baththa feehima min dabbatin wahuwa aala jamaihim itha yashao qadeerun
Wama asabakum min museebatin fabima kasabat aydeekum wayaafoo aan katheerin
Wama antum bimuajizeena fee alardi wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseerin
Wamin ayatihi aljawari fee albahri kaalaalami
In yasha yuskini alrreeha fayathlalna rawakida aala thahrihi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoorin
Aw yoobiqhunna bima kasaboo wayaafu aan katheerin
Wayaalama allatheena yujadiloona fee ayatina ma lahum min maheesin
Fama ooteetum min shayin famataau alhayati alddunya wama ainda Allahi khayrun waabqa lillatheena amanoo waaala rabbihim yatawakkaloona
Waallatheena yajtaniboona kabaira alithmi waalfawahisha waitha ma ghadiboo hum yaghfiroona
Waallatheena istajaboo lirabbihim waaqamoo alssalata waamruhum shoora baynahum wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona
Waallatheena itha asabahumu albaghyu hum yantasiroona
Wajazao sayyiatin sayyiatun mithluha faman aafa waaslaha faajruhu aala Allahi innahu la yuhibbu alththalimeena
Walamani intasara baada thulmihi faolaika ma aalayhim min sabeelin
Innama alssabeelu aala allatheena yathlimoona alnnasa wayabghoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi olaika lahum aathabun aleemun
Walaman sabara waghafara inna thalika lamin aazmi alomoori
Waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min waliyyin min baadihi watara alththalimeena lamma raawoo alaathaba yaqooloona hal ila maraddin min abeelin
Watarahum yuaradoona aalayha khashiaeena mina alththulli yanthuroona min tarfin khafiyyin waqala allatheena amanoo inna alkhasireena llatheena khasiroo anfusahum waahleehim yawma alqiyamati ala inna alththalimeena fee aathabin muqeemin
Wama kana lahum min awliyaa yansuroonahum min dooni Allahi waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min sabeelin
Istajeeboo lirabbikum min qabli an yatiya yawmun la maradda lahu mina Allahi ma lakum min maljain yawmaithin wama lakum min nakeerin
Fain aaradoo fama arsalnaka aalayhim hafeethan in aalayka illa albalaghu wainna itha athaqna alinsana minna rahmatan fariha biha wain usibhum sayyiatun bima qaddamat aydeehim fainna alinsana kafoorun
Lillahi mulku alssamawati waalardi yakhluqu ma yashao yahabu liman yashao inathan wayahabu liman yashao alththukoora
Aw yuzawwijuhum thukranan wainathan wayajaalu man yashao aaqeeman innahu aaleemun qadeerun
Wama kana libasharin an yukallimahu Allahu illa wahyan aw min warai hijabin aw yursila rasoolan fayoohiya biithnihi ma yashao innahu aliyyun hakeemun
Wakathalika awhayna ilayka roohan min amrina ma kunta tadree ma alkitabu wala aleemanu walakin jaaalnahu nooran nahdee bihi man nashao in aibadina wainnaka latahdee ila siratin mustaqeemin
Sirati Allahi allathee lahu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi ala ila Allahi taseeru alomooru
Hameem
Waalkitabi almubeeni
Inna jaaalnahu quranan aarabiyyan laaallakum taaqiloona
Wainnahu fee ommi alkitabi ladayna laaaliyyun hakeemun
Afanadribu aankumu alththikra safhan an kuntum qawman musrifeena
Wakam arsalna min nabiyyin fee alawwaleena
Wama yateehim min nabiyyin illa kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Faahlakna ashadda minhum batshan wamada mathalu alawwaleena
Walain saaltahum man khalaqa alssamawati waalarda layaqoolunna khalaqahunna alaazeezu alaaleemu
Allathee jaaala lakumu alarda mahdan wajaaala lakum feeha subulan laaallakum tahtadoona
Waallathee nazzala mina alssamai maan biqadarin faansharna bihi baldatan maytan kathalika tukhrajoona
Waallathee khalaqa alazwaja kullaha wajaaala lakum mina alfulki waalanaami ma tarkaboona
Litastawoo aala thuhoorihi thumma tathkuroo niamata rabbikum itha istawaytum aalayhi wataqooloo subhana allathee sakhkhara lana hatha ama kunna lahu muqrineena
Wainna ila rabbina lamunqaliboona
Wajaaaloo lahu min aibadihi juzan inna alinsana lakafoorun mubeenun
Ami ittakhatha mimma yakhluqu banatin waasfakum bialbaneena
Waitha bushshira ahaduhum bima daraba lilrrahmani mathalan thalla wajhuhu muswaddan wahuwa katheemun
Awaman yunashshao fee alhilyati wahuwa fee alkhisami ghayru mubeenin
Wajaaaloo almalaikata allatheena hum aibadu alrrahmani inathan ashahidoo khalqahum satuktabu shahadatuhum wayusaloona
Waqaloo law shaa alrrahmanu ma aabadnahum ma lahum bithalika min ailmin in hum illa yakhrusoona
Am ataynahum kitaban min qablihi fahum bihi mustamsikoona
Bal qaloo inna wajadna abaana aala ommatin wainna aala atharihim muhtadoona
Wakathalika ma arsalna min qablika fee qaryatin min natheerin illa qala mutrafooha inna wajadna abaana aala ommatin wainna aala tharihim muqtadoona
Qala awalaw jitukum biahda mimma wajadtum aalayhi abaakum qaloo inna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroona
Faintaqamna minhum faonthur kayfa kana aaqibatu almukaththibeena
Waith qala ibraheemu liabeehi waqawmihi innanee baraon mimma taabudoona
Illa allathee fataranee fainnahu sayahdeeni
Wajaaalaha kalimatan baqiyatan fee aaqibihi laaallahum yarjiaoona
Bal mattaatu haolai waabaahum hatta jaahumu alhaqqu warasoolun mubeenun
Walamma jaahumu alhaqqu qaloo hatha sihrun wainna bihi kafiroona
Waqaloo lawla nuzzila hatha alquranu aala rajulin mina alqaryatayni aatheemun
Ahum yaqsimoona rahmata rabbika nahnu qasamna baynahum maaeeshatahum fee alhayati alddunya warafaana baadahum fawqa baadin darajatin iyattakhitha baaduhum baadan sukhriyyan warahmatu rabbika khayrun mimma yajmaaoona
Walawla an yakoona alnnasu ommatan wahidatan lajaaalna liman yakfuru bialrrahmani libuyootihim suqufan min fiddatin wamaaarija aalayha athharoona
Walibuyootihim abwaban wasururan aalayha yattakioona
Wazukhrufan wain kullu thalika lamma mataau alhayati alddunya waalakhiratu ainda rabbika lilmuttaqeena
Waman yaashu aan thikri alrrahmani nuqayyid lahu shaytanan fahuwa lahu qareenun
Wainnahum layasuddoonahum aani alssabeeli wayahsaboona annahum muhtadoona
Hatta itha jaana qala ya layta baynee wabaynaka buada almashriqayni fabisa alqareenu
Walan yanfaaakumu alyawma ith thalamtum annakum fee alaathabi mushtarikoona
Afaanta tusmiau alssumma aw tahdee alaumya waman kana fee dalalin mubeenin
Faimma nathhabanna bika fainna minhum muntaqimoona
Aw nuriyannaka allathee waaadnahum fainna aalayhim muqtadiroona
Faistamsik biallathee oohiya ilayka innaka aala siratin mustaqeemin
Wainnahu lathikrun laka waliqawmika wasawfa tusaloona
Waisal man arsalna min qablika min rusulina ajaaalna min dooni alrrahmani alihatan yuabadoona
Walaqad arsalna moosa biayatina ila firaawna wamalaihi faqala innee rasoolu rabbi alaalameena
Falamma jaahum biayatina itha hum minha yadhakoona
Wama nureehim min ayatin illa hiya akbaru min okhtiha waakhathnahum bialaathabi laaallahum yarjiaoona
Waqaloo ya ayyuha alsahiru odau lana rabbaka bima aahida aindaka innana lamuhtadoona
Falamma kashafna aanhumu alaathaba itha hum yankuthoona
Wanada firaawnu fee qawmihi qala ya qawmi alaysa lee mulku misra wahathihi alanharu tajree min tahtee afala tubsiroona
Am ana khayrun min hatha allathee huwa maheenun wala yakadu yubeenu
Falawla olqiya aalayhi aswiratun min thahabin aw jaa maaahu almalaikatu muqtarineena
Faistakhaffa qawmahu faataaoohu innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeena
Falamma asafoona intaqamna minhum faaghraqnahum ajmaaeena
Fajaaalnahum salafan wamathalan lilakhireena
Walamma duriba ibnu maryama mathalan itha qawmuka minhu yasiddoona
Waqaloo aalihatuna khayrun am huwa ma daraboohu laka illa jadalan bal hum qawmun khasimoona
In huwa illa aabdun anaamna aalayhi wajaaalnahu mathalan libanee israeela
Walaw nashao lajaaalna minkum malaikatan fee alardi yakhlufoona
Wainnahu laailmun lilssaaati fala tamtarunna biha waittabiaooni hatha siratun mustaqeemun
Wala yasuddannakumu alshshaytanu innahu lakum aaduwwun mubeenun
Walamma jaa aeesa bialbayyinati qala qad jitukum bialhikmati waliobayyina lakum baada allathee takhtalifoona feehi faittaqoo Allaha aateeaooni
Inna Allaha huwa rabbee warabbukum faoabudoohu hatha siratun mustaqeemun
Faikhtalafa alahzabu min baynihim fawaylun lillatheena thalamoo min aathabi yawmin aleemin
Hal yanthuroona illa alssaaata an tatiyahum baghtatan wahum la yashauroona
Alakhillao yawmaithin baaduhum libaadin aaduwwun illa almuttaqeena
Ya aibadi la khawfun aalaykumu alyawma wala antum tahzanoona
Allatheena amanoo biayatina wakanoo muslimeena
Odkhuloo aljannata antum waazwajukum tuhbaroona
Yutafu aalayhim bisihafin min thahabin waakwabin wafeeha ma tashtaheehi alanfusu watalaththu alaayunu waantum feeha khalidoona
Watilka aljannatu allatee oorithtumooha bima kuntum taamaloona
Lakum feeha fakihatun katheeratun minha takuloona
Inna almujrimeena fee aathabi jahannama khalidoona
La yufattaru aanhum wahum feehi mublisoona
Wama thalamnahum walakin kanoo humu alththalimeena
Wanadaw ya maliku liyaqdi aalayna rabbuka qala innakum makithoona
Laqad jinakum bialhaqqi walakinna aktharakum lilhaqqi karihoona
Am abramoo amran fainna mubrimoona
Am yahsaboona anna la nasmaau sirrahum wanajwahum bala warusuluna ladayhim yaktuboona
Qul in kana lilrrahmani waladun faana awwalu alaabideena
Subhana rabbi alssamawati waalardi rabbi alaarshi aamma yasifoona
Fatharhum yakhoodoo wayalaaboo hatta yulaqoo yawmahumu allathee yooaadoona
Wahuwa allathee fee alssamai ilahun wafee alardi ilahun wahuwa alhakeemu alaaleemu
Watabaraka allathee lahu mulku alssamawati waalardi wama baynahuma waaindahu ailmu alssaaati wailayhi turjaaoona
Wala yamliku allatheena yadaoona min doonihi alshshafaaata illa man shahida bialhaqqi wahum yaalamoona
Walain saaltahum man khalaqahum layaqoolunna Allahu faanna yufakoona
Waqeelihi yarabbi inna haolai qawmun la yuminoona
Faisfah aanhum waqul salamun fasawfa yaalamoona
Hameem
Waalkitabi almubeeni
Inna anzalnahu fee laylatin mubarakatin inna kunna munthireena
Feeha yufraqu kullu amrin hakeemin
Amran min aindina inna kunna mursileena
Rahmatan min rabbika innahu huwa alssameeau alaaleemu
Rabbi alssamawati waalardi wama baynahuma in kuntum mooqineena
La ilaha illa huwa yuhyee wayumeetu rabbukum warabbu abaikumu alawwaleena
Bal hum fee shakkin yalaaboona
Fairtaqib yawma tatee alssamao bidukhanin mubeenin
Yaghsha alnnasa hatha aathabun aleemun
Rabbana ikshif aanna alaathaba inna muminoona
Anna lahumu alththikra waqad jaahum rasoolun mubeenun
Thumma tawallaw aanhu waqaloo muaallamun majnoonun
Inna kashifoo alaathabi qaleelan innakum aaidoona
Yawma nabtishu albatshata alkubra inna muntaqimoona
Walaqad fatanna qablahum qawma firaawna wajaahum rasoolun kareemun
An addoo ilayya aibada Allahi innee lakum rasoolun ameenun
Waan la taaloo aala Allahi innee ateekum bisultanin mubeenin
Wainnee authtu birabbee warabbikum an tarjumooni
Wain lam tuminoo lee faiatazilooni
Fadaaa rabbahu anna haolai qawmun mujrimoona
Faasri biaibadee laylan innakum muttabaaoona
Waotruki albahra rahwan innahum jundun mughraqoona
Kam tarakoo min jannatin waauyoonin
Wazurooain wamaqamin kareemin
Wanaamatin kanoo feeha fakiheena
Kathalika waawrathnaha qawman akhareena
Fama bakat aalayhimu alssamao waalardu wama kanoo munthareena
Walaqad najjayna banee israeela mina alaathabi almuheeni
Min firaawna innahu kana aaliyan mina almusrifeena
Walaqadi ikhtarnahum aala ailmin aala alaalameena
Waataynahum mina alayati ma feehi balaon mubeenun
Inna haolai layaqooloona
In hiya illa mawtatuna aloola wama nahnu bimunshareena
Fatoo biabaina in kuntum sadiqeena
Ahum khayrun am qawmu tubbaain waallatheena min qablihim ahlaknahum innahum kanoo mujrimeena
Wama khalaqna alssamawati waalarda wama baynahuma laaibeena
Ma khalaqnahuma illa bialhaqqi walakinna aktharahum la yaalamoona
Inna yawma alfasli meeqatuhum ajmaaeena
Yawma la yughnee mawlan aan mawlan shayan wala hum yunsaroona
Illa man rahima Allahu innahu huwa alaazeezu alrraheemu
Inna shajarata alzzaqqoomi
Taaamu alatheemi
Kaalmuhli yaghlee fee albutooni
Kaghalyi alhameemi
Khuthoohu faiatiloohu ila sawai aljaheemi
Thumma subboo fawqa rasihi min aathabi alhameemi
Thuq innaka anta alaazeezu alkareemu
Inna hatha ma kuntum bihi tamtaroona
Inna almuttaqeena fee maqamin ameenin
Fee jannatin waauyoonin
Yalbasoona min sundusin waistabraqin mutaqabileena
Kathalika wazawwajnahum bihoorin aeenin
Yadaoona feeha bikulli fakihatin amineena
La yathooqoona feeha almawta illa almawtata aloola wawaqahum aathaba aljaheemi
Fadlan min rabbika thalika huwa alfawzu alaatheemu
Fainnama yassarnahu bilisanika laaallahum yatathakkaroona
Fairtaqib innahum murtaqiboona
Hameem
Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi alaazeezi alhakeemi
Inna fee alssamawati waalardi laayatin lilmumineena
Wafee khalqikum wama yabuththu min dabbatin ayatun liqawmin yooqinoona
Waikhtilafi allayli waalnnahari wama anzala Allahu mina alssamai min rizqin faahya bihi alarda baada mawtiha watasreefi alrriyahi yatun liqawmin yaaqiloona
Tilka ayatu Allahi natlooha aalayka bialhaqqi fabiayyi hadeethin baada Allahi waayatihi yuminoona
Waylun likulli affakin atheemin
Yasmaau ayati Allahi tutla aalayhi thumma yusirru mustakbiran kaan lam yasmaaha fabashshirhu biaathabin aleemin
Waitha aalima min ayatina shayan ittakhathaha huzuwan olaika lahum aathabun muheenun
Min waraihim jahannamu wala yughnee aanhum ma kasaboo shayan wala ma ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi awliyaa walahum aathabun aatheemun
Hatha hudan waallatheena kafaroo biayati rabbihim lahum aathabun min rijzin aleemin
Allahu allathee sakhkhara lakumu albahra litajriya alfulku feehi biamrihi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi walaaallakum tashkuroona
Wasakhkhara lakum ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi jameeaan minhu inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroona
Qul lillatheena amanoo yaghfiroo lillatheena la yarjoona ayyama Allahi liyajziya qawman bima kanoo yaksiboona
Man aamila salihan falinafsihi waman asaa faaalayha thumma ila rabbikum turjaaoona
Walaqad atayna banee israeela alkitaba waalhukma waalnnubuwwata warazaqnahum mina alttayyibati wafaddalnahum aala alaalameena
Waataynahum bayyinatin mina alamri fama ikhtalafoo illa min baadi ma jaahumu alailmu baghyan baynahum inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum awma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoona
Thumma jaaalnaka aala shareeaatin mina alamri faittabiaha wala tattabia ahwaa allatheena la yaalamoona
Innahum lan yughnoo aanka mina Allahi shayan wainna alththalimeena baaduhum awliyao baadin waAllahu waliyyu almuttaqeena
Hatha basairu lilnnasi wahudan warahmatun liqawmin yooqinoona
Am hasiba allatheena ijtarahoo alssayyiati an najaalahum kaallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati sawaan mahyahum wamamatuhum saa ma ahkumoona
Wakhalaqa Allahu alssamawati waalarda bialhaqqi walitujza kullu nafsin bima kasabat wahum la yuthlamoona
Afaraayta mani ittakhatha ilahahu hawahu waadallahu Allahu aala ailmin wakhatama aala samaihi waqalbihi wajaaala aala basarihi hishawatan faman yahdeehi min baadi Allahi afala tathakkaroona
Waqaloo ma hiya illa hayatuna alddunya namootu wanahya wama yuhlikuna illa alddahru wama lahum bithalika min ailmin in hum illa athunnoona
Waitha tutla aalayhim ayatuna bayyinatin ma kana hujjatahum illa an qaloo itoo biabaina in kuntum sadiqeena
Quli Allahu yuhyeekum thumma yumeetukum thumma yajmaaukum ila yawmi alqiyamati la rayba feehi walakinna akthara alnnasi la yaalamoona
Walillahi mulku alssamawati waalardi wayawma taqoomu alssaaatu yawmaithin yakhsaru almubtiloona
Watara kulla ommatin jathiyatan kullu ommatin tudaa ila kitabiha alyawma tujzawna ma kuntum taamaloona
Hatha kitabuna yantiqu aalaykum bialhaqqi inna kunna nastansikhu ma kuntum taamaloona
Faamma allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati fayudkhiluhum rabbuhum fee rahmatihi thalika huwa alfawzu almubeenu
Waamma allatheena kafaroo afalam takun ayatee tutla aalaykum faistakbartum wakuntum qawman mujrimeena
Waitha qeela inna waada Allahi haqqun waalssaaatu la rayba feeha qultum ma nadree ma alssaaatu in nathunnu illa thannan wama nahnu imustayqineena
Wabada lahum sayyiatu ma aamiloo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Waqeela alyawma nansakum kama naseetum liqaa yawmikum hatha wamawakumu alnnaru wama lakum min nasireena
Thalikum biannakumu ittakhathtum ayati Allahi huzuwan wagharratkumu alhayatu alddunya faalyawma la yukhrajoona minha wala hum ustaataboona
Falillahi alhamdu rabbi alssamawati warabbi alardi rabbi alaalameena
Walahu alkibriyao fee alssamawati waalardi wahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Hameem
Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi alaazeezi alhakeemi
Ma khalaqna alssamawati waalarda wama baynahuma illa bialhaqqi waajalin musamman waallatheena kafaroo aamma onthiroo muaridoona
Qul araaytum ma tadaoona min dooni Allahi aroonee matha khalaqoo mina alardi am lahum shirkun fee alssamawati eetoonee bikitabin min abli hatha aw atharatin min ailmin in kuntum sadiqeena
Waman adallu mimman yadaoo min dooni Allahi man la yastajeebu lahu ila yawmi alqiyamati wahum aan duaaihim ghafiloona
Waitha hushira alnnasu kanoo lahum aadaan wakanoo biaibadatihim kafireena
Waitha tutla aalayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qala allatheena kafaroo lilhaqqi lamma jaahum hatha sihrun mubeenun
Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul ini iftaraytuhu fala tamlikoona lee mina Allahi shayan huwa aalamu bima tufeedoona feehi kafa bihi shaheedan aynee wabaynakum wahuwa alghafooru alrraheemu
Qul ma kuntu bidaan mina alrrusuli wama adree ma yufaalu bee wala bikum in attabiau illa ma yooha ilayya wama ana illa natheerun ubeenun
Qul araaytum in kana min aindi Allahi wakafartum bihi washahida shahidun min banee israeela aala mithlihi faamana waistakbartum inna llaha la yahdee alqawma alththalimeena
Waqala allatheena kafaroo lillatheena amanoo law kana khayran ma sabaqoona ilayhi waith lam yahtadoo bihi fasayaqooloona hatha ifkun adeemun
Wamin qablihi kitabu moosa imaman warahmatan wahatha kitabun musaddiqun lisanan aarabiyyan liyunthira allatheena thalamoo wabushra ilmuhsineena
Inna allatheena qaloo rabbuna Allahu thumma istaqamoo fala khawfun aalayhim wala hum yahzanoona
Olaika ashabu aljannati khalideena feeha jazaan bima kanoo yaamaloona
Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi ihsanan hamalathu ommuhu kurhan wawadaaathu kurhan wahamluhu wafisaluhu thalathoona shahran hatta itha balagha ashuddahu wabalagha arbaaeena sanatan qala rabbi awzianee an ashkura niamataka allatee anaamta aalayya waaala walidayya waan amala salihan tardahu waaslih lee fee thurriyyatee innee tubtu ilayka wainnee mina almuslimeena
Olaika allatheena nataqabbalu aanhum ahsana ma aamiloo wanatajawazu aan sayyiatihim fee ashabi aljannati waada alssidqi allathee kanoo ooaadoona
Waallathee qala liwalidayhi offin lakuma ataaidaninee an okhraja waqad khalati alquroonu min qablee wahuma yastagheethani Allaha aylaka amin inna waada Allahi haqqun fayaqoolu ma hatha illa asateeru alawwaleena
Olaika allatheena haqqa aalayhimu alqawlu fee umamin qad khalat min qablihim mina aljinni waalinsi innahum kanoo khasireena
Walikullin darajatun mimma aamiloo waliyuwaffiyahum aamalahum wahum la yuthlamoona
Wayawma yuaradu allatheena kafaroo aala alnnari athhabtum tayyibatikum fee hayatikumu alddunya waistamtaatum biha faalyawma tujzawna athaba alhooni bima kuntum tastakbiroona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wabima kuntum tafsuqoona
Waothkur akha aadin ith anthara qawmahu bialahqafi waqad khalati alnnuthuru min bayni yadayhi wamin khalfihi alla taabudoo illa Allaha nnee akhafu aalaykum aathaba yawmin aatheemin
Qaloo ajitana litafikana aan alihatina fatina bima taaiduna in kunta mina alssadiqeena
Qala innama alailmu ainda Allahi waoballighukum ma orsiltu bihi walakinnee arakum qawman tajhaloona
Falamma raawhu aaridan mustaqbila awdiyatihim qaloo hatha aaridun mumtiruna bal huwa ma istaajaltum bihi reehun feeha aathabun aleemun
Tudammiru kulla shayin biamri rabbiha faasbahoo la yura illa masakinuhum kathalika najzee alqawma almujrimeena
Walaqad makkannahum feema in makkannakum feehi wajaaalna lahum samaan waabsaran waafidatan fama aghna aanhum samauhum wala absaruhum ala afidatuhum min shayin ith kanoo yajhadoona biayati Allahi wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona
Walaqad ahlakna ma hawlakum mina alqura wasarrafna alayati laaallahum yarjiaoona
Falawla nasarahumu allatheena ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi qurbanan alihatan bal dalloo aanhum wathalika ifkuhum wama kanoo yaftaroona
Waith sarafna ilayka nafaran mina aljinni yastamiaoona alqurana falamma hadaroohu qaloo ansitoo falamma qudiya wallaw ila qawmihim unthireena
Qaloo ya qawmana inna samiana kitaban onzila min baadi moosa musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi yahdee ila alhaqqi waila tareeqin mustaqeemin
Ya qawmana ajeeboo daaiya Allahi waaminoo bihi yaghfir lakum min thunoobikum wayujirkum min aathabin aleemin
Waman la yujib daaiya Allahi falaysa bimuajizin fee alardi walaysa lahu min doonihi awliyaa olaika fee dalalin mubeenin
Awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda walam yaaya bikhalqihinna biqadirin aala an yuhyiya almawta bala innahu ala kulli shayin qadeerun
Wayawma yuaradu allatheena kafaroo aala alnnari alaysa hatha bialhaqqi qaloo bala warabbina qala fathooqoo alaathaba bima kuntum akfuroona
Faisbir kama sabara oloo alaazmi mina alrrusuli wala tastaajil lahum kaannahum yawma yarawna ma yooaadoona lam yalbathoo illa saaatan in naharin balaghun fahal yuhlaku illa alqawmu alfasiqoona
Allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo aan sabeeli Allahi adalla aamalahum
Waallatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati waamanoo bima nuzzila aala muhammadin wahuwa alhaqqu min rabbihim kaffara aanhum sayyiatihim aaslaha balahum
Thalika bianna allatheena kafaroo ittabaaoo albatila waanna allatheena amanoo ittabaaoo alhaqqa min rabbihim kathalika yadribu Allahu ilnnasi amthalahum
Faitha laqeetumu allatheena kafaroo fadarba alrriqabi hatta itha athkhantumoohum fashuddoo alwathaqa faimma mannan baadu waimma fidaan hatta tadaaa alharbu awzaraha thalika walaw yashao Allahu laintasara minhum walakin liyabluwa baadakum bibaadin waallatheena qutiloo fee abeeli Allahi falan yudilla aamalahum
Sayahdeehim wayuslihu balahum
Wayudkhiluhumu aljannata aarrafaha lahum
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in tansuroo Allaha yansurkum wayuthabbit aqdamakum
Waallatheena kafaroo fataasan lahum waadalla aamalahum
Thalika biannahum karihoo ma anzala Allahu faahbata aamalahum
Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana aaqibatu allatheena min qablihim dammara Allahu aalayhim walilkafireena amthaluha
Thalika bianna Allaha mawla allatheena amanoo waanna alkafireena la mawla lahum
Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu waallatheena kafaroo yatamattaaoona ayakuloona kama takulu alanaamu waalnnaru mathwan lahum
Wakaayyin min qaryatin hiya ashaddu quwwatan min qaryatika allatee akhrajatka ahlaknahum fala nasira lahum
Afaman kana aala bayyinatin min rabbihi kaman zuyyina lahu sooo aamalihi waittabaaoo ahwaahum
Mathalu aljannati allatee wuaida almuttaqoona feeha anharun min main ghayri asinin waanharun min labanin lam yataghayyar taamuhu waanharun min khamrin laththatin lilshsharibeena waanharun min aasalin musaffan walahum feeha min kulli alththamarati wamaghfiratun min abbihim kaman huwa khalidun fee alnnari wasuqoo maan hameeman faqattaaa amaaahum
Waminhum man yastamiau ilayka hatta itha kharajoo min aindika qaloo lillatheena ootoo alailma matha qala anifan olaika allatheena abaaa Allahu aala quloobihim waittabaaoo ahwaahum
Waallatheena ihtadaw zadahum hudan waatahum taqwahum
Fahal yanthuroona illa alssaaata an tatiyahum baghtatan faqad jaa ashratuha faanna lahum itha jaathum thikrahum
Faialam annahu la ilaha illa Allahu waistaghfir lithanbika walilmumineena waalmuminati waAllahu yaalamu mutaqallabakum wamathwakum
Wayaqoolu allatheena amanoo lawla nuzzilat sooratun faitha onzilat sooratun muhkamatun wathukira feeha alqitalu raayta allatheena fee uloobihim maradun yanthuroona ilayka nathara almaghshiyyi aalayhi mina almawti faawla lahum
Taaatun waqawlun maaroofun faitha aazama alamru falaw sadaqoo Allaha lakana khayran lahum
Fahal aasaytum in tawallaytum an tufsidoo fee alardi watuqattiaoo arhamakum
Olaika allatheena laaanahumu Allahu faasammahum waaama absarahum
Afala yatadabbaroona alqurana am aala quloobin aqfaluha
Inna allatheena irtaddoo aala adbarihim min baadi ma tabayyana lahumu alhuda alshshaytanu sawwala lahum waamla lahum
Thalika biannahum qaloo lillatheena karihoo ma nazzala Allahu sanuteeaukum fee baadi alamri waAllahu yaalamu israrahum
Fakayfa itha tawaffathumu almalaikatu yadriboona wujoohahum waadbarahum
Thalika biannahumu ittabaaoo ma askhata Allaha wakarihoo ridwanahu faahbata aamalahum
Am hasiba allatheena fee quloobihim maradun an lan yukhrija Allahu adghanahum
Walaw nashao laaraynakahum falaaaraftahum biseemahum walataarifannahum fee lahni alqawli waAllahu yaalamu aamalakum
Walanabluwannakum hatta naalama almujahideena minkum waalssabireena wanabluwa akhbarakum
Inna allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo aan sabeeli Allahi washaqqoo alrrasoola min baadi ma tabayyana lahumu alhuda lan yaduroo Allaha shayan asayuhbitu aamalahum
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ateeaoo Allaha waateeaoo alrrasoola wala tubtiloo aamalakum
Inna allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo aan sabeeli Allahi thumma matoo wahum kuffarun falan yaghfira Allahu lahum
Fala tahinoo watadaoo ila alssalmi waantumu alaalawna waAllahu maaakum walan yatirakum aamalakum
Innama alhayatu alddunya laaibun walahwun wain tuminoo watattaqoo yutikum ojoorakum wala yasalkum amwalakum
In yasalkumooha fayuhfikum tabkhaloo wayukhrij adghanakum
Haantum haolai tudaawna litunfiqoo fee sabeeli Allahi faminkum man yabkhalu waman yabkhal fainnama yabkhalu aan nafsihi waAllahu lghaniyyu waantumu alfuqarao wain tatawallaw yastabdil qawman ghayrakum thumma la yakoonoo amthalakum
Inna fatahna laka fathan mubeenan
Liyaghfira laka Allahu ma taqaddama min thanbika wama taakhkhara wayutimma niamatahu aalayka wayahdiyaka siratan mustaqeeman
Wayansuraka Allahu nasran aazeezan
Huwa allathee anzala alssakeenata fee quloobi almumineena liyazdadoo eemanan maaa eemanihim walillahi junoodu alssamawati waalardi akana Allahu aaleeman hakeeman
Liyudkhila almumineena waalmuminati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wayukaffira aanhum sayyiatihim wakana thalika inda Allahi fawzan aatheeman
Wayuaaththiba almunafiqeena waalmunafiqati waalmushrikeena waalmushrikati alththanneena biAllahi thanna alssawi aalayhim dairatu lssawi waghadiba Allahu aalayhim walaaanahum waaaadda lahum jahannama wasaat maseeran
Walillahi junoodu alssamawati waalardi wakana Allahu aazeezan hakeeman
Inna arsalnaka shahidan wamubashshiran wanatheeran
Lituminoo biAllahi warasoolihi watuaazziroohu watuwaqqiroohu watusabbihoohu bukratan waaseelan
Inna allatheena yubayiaoonaka innama yubayiaoona Allaha yadu Allahi fawqa aydeehim faman nakatha fainnama yankuthu aala nafsihi waman wfa bima aahada aalayhu Allaha fasayuteehi ajran aatheeman
Sayaqoolu laka almukhallafoona mina alaarabi shaghalatna amwaluna waahloona faistaghfir lana yaqooloona bialsinatihim ma laysa fee quloobihim qul faman yamliku lakum mina Allahi shayan in arada bikum darran aw arada bikum nafaan bal kana Allahu bima taamaloona habeeran
Bal thanantum an lan yanqaliba alrrasoolu waalmuminoona ila ahleehim abadan wazuyyina thalika fee quloobikum wathanantum thanna alssawi akuntum qawman booran
Waman lam yumin biAllahi warasoolihi fainna aatadna lilkafireena saaeeran
Walillahi mulku alssamawati waalardi yaghfiru liman yashao wayuaaththibu man yashao wakana Allahu ghafooran raheeman
Sayaqoolu almukhallafoona itha intalaqtum ila maghanima litakhuthooha tharoona nattabiakum yureedoona an yubaddiloo kalama Allahi qul an tattabiaoona kathalikum qala Allahu min qablu fasayaqooloona bal tahsudoonana bal kanoo la yafqahoona illa qaleelan
Qul lilmukhallafeena mina alaarabi satudaawna ila qawmin olee basin shadeedin tuqatiloonahum aw yuslimoona fain tuteeaoo yutikumu llahu ajran hasanan wain tatawallaw kama tawallaytum min qablu yuaaththibkum aathaban aleeman
Laysa aala alaama harajun wala aala alaaraji harajun wala aala almareedi harajun waman yutiai Allaha warasoolahu yudkhilhu jannatin ajree min tahtiha alanharu waman yatawalla yuaaththibhu aathaban aleeman
Laqad radiya Allahu aani almumineena ith yubayiaoonaka tahta alshshajarati faaalima ma fee quloobihim faanzala alsakeenata aalayhim aathabahum fathan qareeban
Wamaghanima katheeratan yakhuthoonaha wakana Allahu aazeezan hakeeman
Waaadakumu Allahu maghanima katheeratan takhuthoonaha faaajjala lakum hathihi wakaffa aydiya alnnasi aankum walitakoona ayatan ilmumineena wayahdiyakum siratan mustaqeeman
Waokhra lam taqdiroo aalayha qad ahata Allahu biha wakana Allahu aala kulli shayin qadeeran
Walaw qatalakumu allatheena kafaroo lawallawoo aladbara thumma la yajidoona waliyyan wala naseeran
Sunnata Allahi allatee qad khalat min qablu walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeelan
Wahuwa allathee kaffa aydiyahum aankum waaydiyakum aanhum bibatni makkata min baadi an athfarakum aalayhim wakana Allahu bima aamaloona baseeran
Humu allatheena kafaroo wasaddookum aani almasjidi alharami waalhadya maakoofan an yablugha mahillahu walawla rijalun muminoona wanisaon muminatun lam taalamoohum an tataoohum fatuseebakum minhum maaarratun bighayri ailmin liyudkhila Allahu fee rahmatihi man ashao law tazayyaloo laaaththabna allatheena kafaroo minhum aathaban aleeman
Ith jaaala allatheena kafaroo fee quloobihimu alhamiyyata hamiyyata aljahiliyyati faanzala Allahu sakeenatahu aala rasoolihi waaala lmumineena waalzamahum kalimata alttaqwa wakanoo ahaqqa biha waahlaha wakana Allahu bikulli shayin aaleeman
Laqad sadaqa Allahu rasoolahu alrruya bialhaqqi latadkhulunna almasjida alharama in shaa Allahu amineena muhalliqeena ruoosakum amuqassireena la takhafoona faaalima ma lam taalamoo fajaaala min dooni thalika fathan qareeban
Huwa allathee arsala rasoolahu bialhuda wadeeni alhaqqi liyuthhirahu aala alddeeni kullihi wakafa biAllahi shaheedan
Muhammadun rasoolu Allahi waallatheena maaahu ashiddao aala alkuffari ruhamao baynahum tarahum rukkaaan sujjadan yabtaghoona fadlan mina Allahi waridwanan seemahum fee wujoohihim min athari alssujoodi thalika mathaluhum fee alttawrati wamathaluhum fee alinjeeli kazarain akhraja shatahu faazarahu faistaghlatha faistawa aala sooqihi yuajibu alzzurraaa liyagheetha bihimu alkuffara waaada Allahu llatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati minhum maghfiratan waajran aatheeman
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tuqaddimoo bayna yadayi Allahi warasoolihi waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha sameeaun aaleemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tarfaaoo aswatakum fawqa sawti alnnabiyyi wala tajharoo lahu bialqawli kajahri baadikum libaadin an ahbata aamalukum waantum la tashauroona
Inna allatheena yaghuddoona aswatahum ainda rasooli Allahi olaika allatheena imtahana Allahu quloobahum lilttaqwa lahum maghfiratun aajrun aatheemun
Inna allatheena yunadoonaka min warai alhujurati aktharuhum la yaaqiloona
Walaw annahum sabaroo hatta takhruja ilayhim lakana khayran lahum waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in jaakum fasiqun binabain fatabayyanoo an tuseeboo qawman bijahalatin fatusbihoo aala ma faaaltum nadimeena
Waialamoo anna feekum rasoola Allahi law yuteeaukum fee katheerin mina alamri laaanittum walakinna Allaha habbaba ilaykumu aleemana azayyanahu fee quloobikum wakarraha ilaykumu alkufra waalfusooqa waalaisyana olaika humu alrrashidoona
Fadlan mina Allahi waniamatan waAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Wain taifatani mina almumineena iqtataloo faaslihoo baynahuma fain baghat ihdahuma aala alokhra faqatiloo allatee tabghee hatta tafeea la amri Allahi fain faat faaslihoo baynahuma bialaadli waaqsitoo inna Allaha yuhibbu almuqsiteena
Innama almuminoona ikhwatun faaslihoo bayna akhawaykum waittaqoo Allaha laaallakum turhamoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la yaskhar qawmun min qawmin aasa an yakoonoo khayran minhum wala nisaon min nisain aasa an yakunna khayran minhunna wala talmizoo anfusakum wala tanabazoo bialalqabi bisa alismu alfusooqu baada aleemani waman lam yatub faolaika humu lththalimoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ijtaniboo katheeran mina alththanni inna baada alththanni ithmun wala tajassasoo wala yaghtab baadukum aadan ayuhibbu ahadukum an yakula lahma akheehi maytan fakarihtumoohu waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha tawwabun raheemun
Ya ayyuha alnnasu inna khalaqnakum min thakarin waontha wajaaalnakum shuaooban waqabaila litaaarafoo inna akramakum ainda Allahi tqakum inna Allaha aaleemun khabeerun
Qalati alaarabu amanna qul lam tuminoo walakin qooloo aslamna walamma yadkhuli aleemanu fee quloobikum wain tuteeaoo Allaha warasoolahu a yalitkum min aamalikum shayan inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Innama almuminoona allatheena amanoo biAllahi warasoolihi thumma lam yartaboo wajahadoo biamwalihim waanfusihim fee sabeeli Allahi laika humu alssadiqoona
Qul atuaallimoona Allaha bideenikum waAllahu yaalamu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi waAllahu bikulli shayin aaleemun
Yamunnoona aalayka an aslamoo qul la tamunnoo aalayya islamakum bali Allahu yamunnu aalaykum an hadakum lileemani in kuntum sadiqeena
Inna Allaha yaalamu ghayba alssamawati waalardi waAllahu baseerun bima taamaloona
Qaf waalqurani almajeedi
Bal aajiboo an jaahum munthirun minhum faqala alkafiroona hatha shayon aajeebun
Aitha mitna wakunna turaban thalika rajaun baaeedun
Qad aalimna ma tanqusu alardu minhum waaindana kitabun hafeethun
Bal kaththaboo bialhaqqi lamma jaahum fahum fee amrin mareejin
Afalam yanthuroo ila alssamai fawqahum kayfa banaynaha wazayyannaha wama laha min furoojin
Waalarda madadnaha waalqayna feeha rawasiya waanbatna feeha min kulli zawjin baheejin
Tabsiratan wathikra likulli aabdin muneebin

Rizqan lilaibadi waahyayna bihi baldatan maytan kathalika alkhurooju

Afaaayeena bialkhalqi alawwali bal hum fee labsin min khalqin jadeedin

Alqiya fee jahannama kulla kaffarin aaneedin

aala an nubaddila amthalakum wanunshiakum fee ma la taalamoona
Walaqad aalimtumu alnnashata aloola falawla tathakkaroona
Afaraaytum ma tahruthoona
Aantum tazraaoonahu am nahnu alzzariaoona
Law nashao lajaaalnahu hutaman fathaltum tafakkahoona
Inna lamughramoona
Bal nahnu mahroomoona
Afaraaytumu almaa allathee tashraboona
Aantum anzaltumoohu mina almuzni am nahnu almunziloona
Law nashao jaaalnahu ojajan falawla tashkuroona
Afaraaytumu alnnara allatee tooroona
Aantum anshatum shajarataha am nahnu almunshioona
Nahnu jaaalnaha tathkiratan wamataaan lilmuqweena
