Fala oqsimu bimawaqiai alnnujoomi
Wainnahu laqasamun law taalamoona aatheemun
Innahu laquranun kareemun
Fee kitabin maknoonin
La yamassuhu illa almutahharoona
Tanzeelun min rabbi alaalameena
Afabihatha alhadeethi antum mudhinoona
Watajaaloona rizqakum annakum tukaththiboona
Falawla itha balaghati alhulqooma
Waantum heenaithin tanthuroona
Wanahnu aqrabu ilayhi minkum walakin la tubsiroona
Falawla in kuntum ghayra madeeneena
Tarjiaoonaha in kuntum sadiqeena
Faamma in kana mina almuqarrabeena
Farawhun warayhanun wajannatu naaeemin
Waamma in kana min ashabi alyameeni
Fasalamun laka min ashabi alyameeni
Waamma in kana mina almukaththibeena alddalleena
Fanuzulun min hameemin
Watasliyatu jaheemin
Inna hatha lahuwa haqqu alyaqeeni
Fasabbih biismi rabbika alaatheemi
Sabbaha lillahi ma fee alssamawati waalardi wahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Lahu mulku alssamawati waalardi yuhyee wayumeetu wahuwa aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Huwa alawwalu waalakhiru waalththahiru waalbatinu wahuwa bikulli shayin aaleemun
Huwa allathee khalaqa alssamawati waalarda fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa aala alaarshi yaalamu ma yaliju fee alardi wama yakhruju inha wama yanzilu mina alssamai wama yaaruju feeha wahuwa maaakum ayna ma kuntum waAllahu bima taamaloona baseerun
Lahu mulku alssamawati waalardi waila Allahi turjaau alomooru
Yooliju allayla fee alnnahari wayooliju alnnahara fee allayi wahuwa aaleemun bithati alssudoori
Aminoo biAllahi warasoolihi waanfiqoo mimma jaaalakum mustakhlafeena feehi faallatheena amanoo minkum waanfaqoo lahum ajrun kabeerun
Wama lakum la tuminoona biAllahi waalrrasoolu yadaookum lituminoo birabbikum waqad akhatha meethaqakum in kuntum mumineena
Huwa allathee yunazzilu aala aabdihi ayatin bayyinatin liyukhrijakum mina alththulumati ila alnnoori wainna Allaha bikum laraoofun aheemun
Wama lakum alla tunfiqoo fee sabeeli Allahi walillahi meerathu alssamawati waalardi la yastawee minkum man anfaqa min qabli alfathi waqatala olaika aathamu darajatan mina allatheena anfaqoo min baadu waqataloo wakullan waaada Allahu alhusna waAllahu bima taamaloona habeerun
Man tha allathee yuqridu Allaha qardan hasanan fayudaaifahu lahu walahu ajrun kareemun
Yawma tara almumineena waalmuminati yasaa nooruhum bayna aydeehim wabiaymanihim bushrakumu alyawma jannatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu halideena feeha thalika huwa alfawzu alaatheemu
Yawma yaqoolu almunafiqoona waalmunafiqatu lillatheena amanoo onthuroona naqtabis min noorikum qeela irjiaoo waraakum failtamisoo ooran faduriba baynahum bisoorin lahu babun batinuhu feehi alrrahmatu wathahiruhu min qibalihi alaathabu
Yunadoonahum alam nakun maaakum qaloo bala walakinnakum fatantum anfusakum watarabbastum wairtabtum wagharratkumu alamaniyyu hatta jaa mru Allahi wagharrakum biAllahi algharooru
Faalyawma la yukhathu minkum fidyatun wala mina allatheena kafaroo mawakumu alnnaru hiya mawlakum wabisa almaseeru
Alam yani lillatheena amanoo an takhshaaa quloobuhum lithikri Allahi wama nazala mina alhaqqi wala yakoonoo kaallatheena ootoo alkitaba in qablu fatala aalayhimu alamadu faqasat quloobuhum wakatheerun minhum fasiqoona
Ialamoo anna Allaha yuhyee alarda baada mawtiha qad bayyanna lakumu alayati laaallakum taaqiloona
Inna almussaddiqeena waalmussaddiqati waaqradoo Allaha qardan hasanan yudaaafu lahum walahum ajrun kareemun
Waallatheena amanoo biAllahi warusulihi olaika humu alssiddeeqoona waalshshuhadao ainda rabbihim lahum ajruhum wanooruhum waallatheena afaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu aljaheemi
Ialamoo annama alhayatu alddunya laaibun walahwun wazeenatun watafakhurun baynakum watakathurun fee alamwali waalawladi kamathali ghaythin aajaba alkuffara nabatuhu thumma yaheeju fatarahu musfarran thumma yakoonu hutaman wafee alakhirati aathabun shadeedun amaghfiratun mina Allahi waridwanun wama alhayatu alddunya illa mataau alghuroori
Sabiqoo ila maghfiratin min rabbikum wajannatin aarduha kaaardi alssamai waalardi oaiddat lillatheena amanoo biAllahi warusulihi halika fadlu Allahi yuteehi man yashao waAllahu thoo alfadli alaatheemi
Ma asaba min museebatin fee alardi wala fee anfusikum illa fee kitabin min qabli an nabraaha inna thalika aala Allahi yaseerun
Likayla tasaw aala ma fatakum wala tafrahoo bima atakum waAllahu la yuhibbu kulla mukhtalin fakhoorin
Allatheena yabkhaloona wayamuroona alnnasa bialbukhli waman yatawalla fainna Allaha huwa alghaniyyu alhameedu
Laqad arsalna rusulana bialbayyinati waanzalna maaahumu alkitaba waalmeezana liyaqooma alnnasu bialqisti waanzalna alhadeeda feehi asun shadeedun wamanafiau lilnnasi waliyaalama Allahu man yansuruhu warusulahu bialghaybi inna Allaha qawiyyun aazeezun
Walaqad arsalna noohan waibraheema wajaaalna fee thurriyyatihima alnnubuwwata waalkitaba faminhum muhtadin wakatheerun minhum fasiqoona
Thumma qaffayna aala atharihim birusulina waqaffayna biaeesa ibni maryama waataynahu alinjeela wajaaalna fee quloobi allatheena ittabaaoohu rafatan warahmatan warahbaniyyatan ibtadaaooha ma katabnaha aalayhim illa ibtighaa ridwani Allahi fama raaawha haqqa iaayatiha faatayna allatheena amanoo minhum ajrahum wakatheerun minhum fasiqoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha waaminoo birasoolihi yutikum kiflayni min rahmatihi wayajaal lakum nooran tamshoona bihi ayaghfir lakum waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Lialla yaalama ahlu alkitabi alla yaqdiroona aala shayin min fadli Allahi waanna alfadla biyadi Allahi yuteehi man yashao waAllahu thoo lfadli alaatheemi
Qad samiaa Allahu qawla allatee tujadiluka fee zawjiha watashtakee ila Allahi waAllahu yasmaau tahawurakuma inna Allaha sameeaun aseerun
Allatheena yuthahiroona minkum min nisaihim ma hunna ommahatihim in ommahatuhum illa allaee waladnahum wainnahum layaqooloona munkaran ina alqawli wazooran wainna Allaha laaafuwwun ghafoorun
Waallatheena yuthahiroona min nisaihim thumma yaaoodoona lima qaloo fatahreeru raqabatin min qabli an yatamassa thalikum tooaathoona ihi waAllahu bima taamaloona khabeerun
Faman lam yajid fasiyamu shahrayni mutatabiaayni min qabli an yatamassa faman lam yastatia faitaamu sitteena miskeenan thalika ituminoo biAllahi warasoolihi watilka hudoodu Allahi walilkafireena aathabun aleemun
Inna allatheena yuhaddoona Allaha warasoolahu kubitoo kama kubita allatheena min qablihim waqad anzalna ayatin bayyinatin alilkafireena aathabun muheenun
Yawma yabaathuhumu Allahu jameeaan fayunabbiohum bima aamiloo ahsahu Allahu wanasoohu waAllahu aala kulli shayin shaheedun
Alam tara anna Allaha yaalamu ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi ma yakoonu min najwa thalathatin illa huwa rabiauhum wala khamsatin illa huwa sadisuhum wala adna min thalika wala akthara illa huwa maaahum ayna ma kanoo thumma yunabbiohum bima aamiloo yawma alqiyamati nna Allaha bikulli shayin aaleemun
Alam tara ila allatheena nuhoo aani alnnajwa thumma yaaoodoona lima nuhoo aanhu wayatanajawna bialithmi waalaudwani wamaasiyati alrrasooli waitha jaooka hayyawka bima lam yuhayyika bihi Allahu wayaqooloona fee anfusihim lawla yuaaththibuna Allahu bima naqoolu asbuhum jahannamu yaslawnaha fabisa almaseeru
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha tanajaytum fala tatanajaw bialithmi waalaudwani wamaasiyati alrrasooli watanajaw bialbirri waalttaqwa aittaqoo Allaha allathee ilayhi tuhsharoona
Innama alnnajwa mina alshshaytani liyahzuna allatheena amanoo walaysa bidarrihim shayan illa biithni Allahi waaala Allahi alyatawakkali almuminoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha qeela lakum tafassahoo fee almajalisi faifsahoo yafsahi Allahu lakum waitha qeela onshuzoo faonshuzoo arfaai Allahu allatheena amanoo minkum waallatheena ootoo alailma darajatin waAllahu bima taamaloona khabeerun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha najaytumu alrrasoola faqaddimoo bayna yaday najwakum sadaqatan thalika khayrun lakum waatharu fain lam ajidoo fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Aashfaqtum an tuqaddimoo bayna yaday najwakum sadaqatin faith lam tafaaloo wataba Allahu aalaykum faaqeemoo alssalata waatoo alzzakata aateeaoo Allaha warasoolahu waAllahu khabeerun bima taamaloona
Alam tara ila allatheena tawallaw qawman ghadiba Allahu aalayhim ma hum minkum wala minhum wayahlifoona aala alkathibi wahum yaalamoona
aaadda Allahu lahum aathaban shadeedan innahum saa ma kanoo yaamaloona
Ittakhathoo aymanahum junnatan fasaddoo aan sabeeli Allahi falahum aathabun muheenun
Lan tughniya aanhum amwaluhum wala awladuhum mina Allahi shayan olaika ashabu alnnari hum feeha khalidoona
Yawma yabaathuhumu Allahu jameeaan fayahlifoona lahu kama yahlifoona lakum wayahsaboona annahum aala shayin ala innahum humu lkathiboona
Istahwatha aalayhimu alshshaytanu faansahum thikra Allahi olaika hizbu alshshaytani ala inna hizba alshshaytani humu alkhasiroona
Inna allatheena yuhaddoona Allaha warasoolahu olaika fee alathalleena
Kataba Allahu laaghlibanna ana warusulee inna Allaha qawiyyun aazeezun
La tajidu qawman yuminoona biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri yuwaddoona man hadda Allaha warasoolahu walaw kanoo abaahum aw abnaahum aw ikhwanahum aw aasheeratahum olaika kataba fee quloobihimu aleemana waayyadahum biroohin minhu wayudkhiluhum jannatin tajree min tahtiha lanharu khalideena feeha radiya Allahu aanhum waradoo aanhu olaika hizbu Allahi ala inna hizba Allahi humu almuflihoona
Sabbaha lillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Huwa allathee akhraja allatheena kafaroo min ahli alkitabi min diyarihim liawwali alhashri ma thanantum an yakhrujoo wathannoo annahum maniaatuhum husoonuhum mina Allahi faatahumu Allahu min haythu lam yahtasiboo waqathafa fee quloobihimu alrruaba yukhriboona buyootahum iaydeehim waaydee almumineena faiatabiroo ya olee alabsari
Walawla an kataba Allahu aalayhimu aljalaa laaaththabahum fee alddunya walahum fee alakhirati aathabu alnnari
Thalika biannahum shaqqoo Allaha warasoolahu waman yushaqqi Allaha fainna Allaha shadeedu alaiqabi
Ma qataatum min leenatin aw taraktumooha qaimatan aala osooliha fabiithni Allahi waliyukhziya alfasiqeena
Wama afaa Allahu aala rasoolihi minhum fama awjaftum aalayhi min khaylin wala rikabin walakinna Allaha yusallitu rusulahu aala man ashao waAllahu aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Ma afaa Allahu aala rasoolihi min ahli alqura falillahi walilrrasooli walithee alqurba waalyatama waalmasakeeni waibni alssabeeli kay la yakoona doolatan bayna alaghniyai minkum wama atakumu alrrasoolu fakhuthoohu wama nahakum aanhu faintahoo waittaqoo Allaha inna llaha shadeedu alaiqabi
Lilfuqarai almuhajireena allatheena okhrijoo min diyarihim waamwalihim yabtaghoona fadlan mina Allahi waridwanan wayansuroona Allaha arasoolahu olaika humu alssadiqoona
Waallatheena tabawwaoo alddara waaleemana min qablihim yuhibboona man hajara ilayhim wala yajidoona fee sudoorihim hajatan mimma ootoo ayuthiroona aala anfusihim walaw kana bihim khasasatun waman yooqa shuhha nafsihi faolaika humu almuflihoona
Waallatheena jaoo min baadihim yaqooloona rabbana ighfir lana waliikhwanina allatheena sabaqoona bialeemani wala tajaal fee quloobina hillan lillatheena amanoo rabbana innaka raoofun raheemun
Alam tara ila allatheena nafaqoo yaqooloona liikhwanihimu allatheena kafaroo min ahli alkitabi lain okhrijtum lanakhrujanna maaakum ala nuteeau feekum ahadan abadan wain qootiltum lanansurannakum waAllahu yashhadu innahum lakathiboona
Lain okhrijoo la yakhrujoona maaahum walain qootiloo la yansuroonahum walain nasaroohum layuwallunna aladbara thumma la yunsaroona
Laantum ashaddu rahbatan fee sudoorihim mina Allahi thalika biannahum qawmun la yafqahoona
La yuqatiloonakum jameeaan illa fee quran muhassanatin aw min warai judurin basuhum baynahum shadeedun tahsabuhum jameeaan waquloobuhum hatta thalika biannahum qawmun la yaaqiloona
Kamathali allatheena min qablihim qareeban thaqoo wabala amrihim walahum aathabun aleemun
Kamathali alshshaytani ith qala lilinsani okfur falamma kafara qala innee bareeon minka innee akhafu Allaha rabba alaalameena
Fakana aaqibatahuma annahuma fee alnnari khalidayni feeha wathalika jazao alththalimeena
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha waltanthur nafsun ma qaddamat lighadin waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha khabeerun bima taamaloona
Wala takoonoo kaallatheena nasoo Allaha faansahum anfusahum olaika humu alfasiqoona
La yastawee ashabu alnnari waashabu aljannati ashabu aljannati humu alfaizoona
Law anzalna hatha alqurana aala jabalin laraaytahu khashiaan mutasaddiaan min khashyati Allahi watilka alamthalu nadribuha lilnnasi aaallahum yatafakkaroona
Huwa Allahu allathee la ilaha illa huwa aalimu alghaybi waalshshahadati huwa alrrahmanu alrraheemu
Huwa Allahu allathee la ilaha illa huwa almaliku alquddoosu alssalamu almuminu almuhayminu alaazeezu aljabbaru almutakabbiru subhana llahi aamma yushrikoona
Huwa Allahu alkhaliqu albario almusawwiru lahu alasmao alhusna yusabbihu lahu ma fee alssamawati waalardi wahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo aaduwwee waaaduwwakum awliyaa tulqoona ilayhim bialmawaddati waqad kafaroo bima jaakum mina alhaqqi yukhrijoona alrrasoola waiyyakum an tuminoo biAllahi rabbikum in kuntum kharajtum jihadan fee sabeelee waibtighaa mardatee usirroona ilayhim bialmawaddati waana aalamu bima akhfaytum wama aalantum waman yafaalhu minkum faqad dalla sawaa alssabeeli
In yathqafookum yakoonoo lakam aadaan wayabsutoo ilaykum aydiyahum waalsinatahum bialssooi wawaddoo law takfuroona
Lan tanfaaakum arhamukum wala awladukum yawma alqiyamati yafsilu baynakum waAllahu bima taamaloona baseerun
Qad kanat lakum oswatun hasanatun fee ibraheema waallatheena maaahu ith qaloo liqawmihim inna buraao minkum wamimma taabudoona min dooni Allahi kafarna bikum wabada baynana wabaynakumu alaadawatu waalbaghdao abadan hatta tuminoo biAllahi wahdahu illa qawla ibraheema iabeehi laastaghfiranna laka wama amliku laka mina Allahi min shayin rabbana aalayka tawakkalna wailayka anabna wailayka almaseeru
Rabbana la tajaalna fitnatan lillatheena kafaroo waighfir lana rabbana innaka anta alaazeezu alhakeemu
Laqad kana lakum feehim oswatun hasanatun liman kana yarjoo Allaha waalyawma alakhira waman yatawalla fainna Allaha huwa alghanniyyu lhameedu
aasa Allahu an yajaala baynakum wabayna allatheena aadaytum minhum mawaddatan waAllahu qadeerun waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
La yanhakumu Allahu aani allatheena lam yuqatilookum fee alddeeni walam yukhrijookum min diyarikum an tabarroohum watuqsitoo ilayhim nna Allaha yuhibbu almuqsiteena
Innama yanhakumu Allahu aani allatheena qatalookum fee alddeeni waakhrajookum min diyarikum wathaharoo aala ikhrajikum an tawallawhum aman yatawallahum faolaika humu alththalimoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha jaakumu almuminatu muhajiratin faimtahinoohunna Allahu aalamu bieemanihinna fain aalimtumoohunna muminatin fala tarjiaoohunna ila alkuffari la hunna hillun lahum wala hum yahilloona lahunna waatoohum ma anfaqoo wala junaha aalaykum an tankihoohunna itha ataytumoohunna ojoorahunna wala tumsikoo biaisami alkawafiri waisaloo ma anfaqtum walyasaloo ma anfaqoo thalikum ukmu Allahi yahkumu baynakum waAllahu aaleemun hakeemun
Wain fatakum shayon min azwajikum ila alkuffari faaaqabtum faatoo allatheena thahabat azwajuhum mithla ma anfaqoo waittaqoo Allaha llathee antum bihi muminoona
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu itha jaaka almuminatu yubayianaka aala an la yushrikna biAllahi shayan wala yasriqna wala yazneena wala yaqtulna awladahunna wala yateena bibuhtanin yaftareenahu bayna aydeehinna waarjulihinna wala yaaseenaka fee maaroofin fabayiahunna waistaghfir ahunna Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tatawallaw qawman ghadiba Allahu aalayhim qad yaisoo mina alakhirati kama yaisa alkuffaru min ashabi lquboori
Sabbaha lillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi wahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo lima taqooloona ma la tafaaloona
Kabura maqtan ainda Allahi an taqooloo ma la tafaaloona
Inna Allaha yuhibbu allatheena yuqatiloona fee sabeelihi saffan kaannahum bunyanun marsoosun
Waith qala moosa liqawmihi ya qawmi lima tuthoonanee waqad taalamoona annee rasoolu Allahi ilaykum falamma zaghoo azagha Allahu uloobahum waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeena
Waith qala aeesa ibnu maryama ya banee israeela innee rasoolu Allahi ilaykum musaddiqan lima bayna yadayya mina alttawrati amubashshiran birasoolin yatee min baadee ismuhu ahmadu falamma jaahum bialbayyinati qaloo hatha sihrun mubeenun
Waman athlamu mimmani iftara aala Allahi alkathiba wahuwa yudaa ila alislami waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alththalimeena
Yureedoona liyutfioo noora Allahi biafwahihim waAllahu mutimmu noorihi walaw kariha alkafiroona
Huwa allathee arsala rasoolahu bialhuda wadeeni alhaqqi liyuthhirahu aala alddeeni kullihi walaw kariha almushrikoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo hal adullukum aala tijaratin tunjeekum min aathabin aleemin
Tuminoona biAllahi warasoolihi watujahidoona fee sabeeli Allahi biamwalikum waanfusikum thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum taalamoona
Yaghfir lakum thunoobakum wayudkhilkum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu wamasakina tayyibatan fee jannati aadnin thalika alfawzu laatheemu
Waokhra tuhibboonaha nasrun mina Allahi wafathun qarreebun wabashshiri almumineena
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo koonoo ansara Allahi kama qala aeesa ibnu maryama lilhawariyyeena man ansaree ila Allahi qala alhawariyyoona nahnu ansaru Allahi faamanat taifatun min banee israeela wakafarat taifatun faayyadna allatheena amanoo aala aaduwwihim aasbahoo thahireena
Yusabbihu lillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi almaliki alquddoosi alaazeezi alhakeemi
Huwa allathee baaatha fee alommiyyeena rasoolan minhum yatloo aalayhim ayatihi wayuzakkeehim wayuaallimuhumu alkitaba waalhikmata wain anoo min qablu lafee dalalin mubeenin
Waakhareena minhum lamma yalhaqoo bihim wahuwa alaazeezu alhakeemu
Thalika fadlu Allahi yuteehi man yashao waAllahu thoo alfadli alaatheemi
Mathalu allatheena hummiloo alttawrata thumma lam yahmilooha kamathali alhimari yahmilu asfaran bisa mathalu alqawmi allatheena aththaboo biayati Allahi waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alththalimeena
Qul ya ayyuha allatheena hadoo in zaaamtum annakum awliyao lillahi min dooni alnnasi fatamannawoo almawta in kuntum sadiqeena
Wala yatamannawnahu abadan bima qaddamat aydeehim waAllahu aaleemun bialththalimeena
Qul inna almawta allathee tafirroona minhu fainnahu mulaqeekum thumma turaddoona ila aalimi alghaybi waalshshahadati fayunabbiokum bima untum taamaloona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha noodiya lilssalati min yawmi aljumuaati faisaaw ila thikri Allahi watharoo albayaa thalikum khayrun akum in kuntum taalamoona
Faitha qudiyati alssalatu faintashiroo fee alardi waibtaghoo min fadli Allahi waothkuroo Allaha katheeran laaallakum tuflihoona
Waitha raaw tijaratan aw lahwan infaddoo ilayha watarakooka qaiman qul ma ainda Allahi khayrun mina allahwi wamina alttijarati waAllahu hayru alrraziqeena
Itha jaaka almunafiqoona qaloo nashhadu innaka larasoolu Allahi waAllahu yaalamu innaka larasooluhu waAllahu yashhadu inna lmunafiqeena lakathiboona
Ittakhathoo aymanahum junnatan fasaddoo aan sabeeli Allahi innahum saa ma kanoo yaamaloona
Thalika biannahum amanoo thumma kafaroo fatubiaa aala quloobihim fahum la yafqahoona
Waitha raaytahum tuajibuka ajsamuhum wain yaqooloo tasmaa liqawlihim kaannahum khushubun musannadatun yahsaboona kulla sayhatin alayhim humu alaaduwwu faihtharhum qatalahumu Allahu anna yufakoona
Waitha qeela lahum taaalaw yastaghfir lakum rasoolu Allahi lawwaw ruoosahum waraaytahum yasuddoona wahum mustakbiroona
Sawaon aalayhim astaghfarta lahum am lam tastaghfir lahum lan yaghfira Allahu lahum inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeena
Humu allatheena yaqooloona la tunfiqoo aala man ainda rasooli Allahi hatta yanfaddoo walillahi khazainu alssamawati waalardi walakinna lmunafiqeena la yafqahoona
Yaqooloona lain rajaana ila almadeenati layukhrijanna alaaazzu minha alathalla walillahi alaizzatu walirasoolihi walilmumineena alakinna almunafiqeena la yaalamoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tulhikum amwalukum wala awladukum aan thikri Allahi waman yafaal thalika faolaika humu alkhasiroona
Waanfiqoo min ma razaqnakum min qabli an yatiya ahadakumu almawtu fayaqoola rabbi lawla akhkhartanee ila ajalin qareebin faassaddaqa aakun mina alssaliheena
Walan yuakhkhira Allahu nafsan itha jaa ajaluha waAllahu khabeerun bima taamaloona
Yusabbihu lillahi ma fee alssamawati wama fee alardi lahu almulku walahu alhamdu wahuwa aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Huwa allathee khalaqakum faminkum kafirun waminkum muminun waAllahu bima taamaloona baseerun
Khalaqa alssamawati waalarda bialhaqqi wasawwarakum faahsana suwarakum wailayhi almaseeru
Yaalamu ma fee alssamawati waalardi wayaalamu ma tusirroona wama tualinoona waAllahu aaleemun bithati alssudoori
Alam yatikum nabao allatheena kafaroo min qablu fathaqoo wabala amrihim walahum aathabun aleemun
Thalika biannahu kanat tateehim rusuluhum bialbayyinati faqaloo abasharun yahdoonana fakafaroo watawallaw waistaghna Allahu waAllahu haniyyun hameedun
Zaaama allatheena kafaroo an lan yubaathoo qul bala warabbee latubaathunna thumma latunabbaonna bima aamiltum wathalika aala Allahi aseerun
Faaminoo biAllahi warasoolihi waalnnoori allathee anzalna waAllahu bima taamaloona khabeerun
Yawma yajmaaukum liyawmi aljamai thalika yawmu alttaghabuni waman yumin biAllahi wayaamal salihan yukaffir aanhu sayyiatihi wayudkhilhu annatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan thalika alfawzu alaatheemu
Waallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu alnnari khalideena feeha wabisa almaseeru
Ma asaba min museebatin illa biithni Allahi waman yumin biAllahi yahdi qalbahu waAllahu bikulli shayin aaleemun
Waateeaoo Allaha waateeaoo alrrasoola fain tawallaytum fainnama aala rasoolina albalaghu almubeenu
Allahu la ilaha illa huwa waaala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo inna min azwajikum waawladikum aaduwwan lakum faihtharoohum wain taafoo watasfahoo wataghfiroo fainna llaha ghafoorun raheemun
Innama amwalukum waawladukum fitnatun waAllahu aindahu ajrun aatheemun
Faittaqoo Allaha ma istataatum waismaaoo waateeaoo waanfiqoo khayran lianfusikum waman yooqa shuhha nafsihi faolaika humu almuflihoona
In tuqridoo Allaha qardan hasanan yudaaifhu lakum wayaghfir lakum waAllahu shakoorun haleemun
aalimu alghaybi waalshshahadati alaazeezu alhakeemu
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu itha tallaqtumu alnnisaa fatalliqoohunna liaiddatihinna waahsoo alaiddata waittaqoo Allaha rabbakum la tukhrijoohunna min buyootihinna wala yakhrujna illa an yateena bifahishatin mubayyinatin watilka hudoodu Allahi waman yataaadda hudooda llahi faqad thalama nafsahu la tadree laaalla Allaha yuhdithu baada thalika amran
Faitha balaghna ajalahunna faamsikoohunna bimaaroofin aw fariqoohunna bimaaroofin waashhidoo thaway aadlin minkum waaqeemoo lshshahadata lillahi thalikum yooaathu bihi man kana yuminu biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri waman yattaqi Allaha yajaal lahu makhrajan
Wayarzuqhu min haythu la yahtasibu waman yatawakkal aala Allahi fahuwa hasbuhu inna Allaha balighu amrihi qad jaaala Allahu likulli hayin qadran
Waallaee yaisna mina almaheedi min nisaikum ini irtabtum faaiddatuhunna thalathatu ashhurin waallaee lam yahidna waolatu alahmali jaluhunna an yadaana hamlahunna waman yattaqi Allaha yajaal lahu min amrihi yusran
Thalika amru Allahi anzalahu ilaykum waman yattaqi Allaha yukaffir aanhu sayyiatihi wayuathim lahu ajran
Askinoohunna min haythu sakantum min wujdikum wala tudarroohunna litudayyiqoo aalayhinna wain kunna olati hamlin faanfiqoo aalayhinna atta yadaana hamlahunna fain ardaana lakum faatoohunna ojoorahunna watamiroo baynakum bimaaroofin wain taaasartum fasaturdiau lahu okhra
Liyunfiq thoo saaatin min saaatihi waman qudira aalayhi rizquhu falyunfiq mimma atahu Allahu la yukallifu Allahu nafsan illa ma ataha ayajaalu Allahu baada ausrin yusran
Wakaayyin min qaryatin aatat aan amri rabbiha warusulihi fahasabnaha hisaban shadeedan waaaththabnaha aathaban nukran
Fathaqat wabala amriha wakana aaqibatu amriha khusran
aaadda Allahu lahum aathaban shadeedan faittaqoo Allaha ya olee alalbabi allatheena amanoo qad anzala Allahu ilaykum thikran
Rasoolan yatloo aalaykum ayati Allahi mubayyinatin liyukhrija allatheena amanoo waaamiloo alssalihati mina alththulumati ila alnnoori waman yumin biAllahi wayaamal salihan yudkhilhu jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan qad ahsana Allahu lahu izqan
Allahu allathee khalaqa sabaa samawatin wamina alardi mithlahunna yatanazzalu alamru baynahunna litaalamoo anna Allaha aala kulli hayin qadeerun waanna Allaha qad ahata bikulli shayin ailman
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu lima tuharrimu ma ahalla Allahu laka tabtaghee mardata azwajika waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun
Qad farada Allahu lakum tahillata aymanikum waAllahu mawlakum wahuwa alaaleemu alhakeemu
Waith asarra alnnabiyyu ila baadi azwajihi hadeethan falamma nabbaat bihi waathharahu Allahu aalayhi aarrafa baadahu waaarada aan aadin falamma nabbaaha bihi qalat man anbaaka hatha qala nabbaaniya alaaleemu alkhabeeru
In tatooba ila Allahi faqad saghat quloobukuma wain tathahara aalayhi fainna Allaha huwa mawlahu wajibreelu wasalihu almumineena aalmalaikatu baada thalika thaheerun
aasa rabbuhu in tallaqakunna an yubdilahu azwajan khayran minkunna muslimatin muminatin qanitatin taibatin aabidatin saihatin hayyibatin waabkaran
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo qoo anfusakum waahleekum naran waqooduha alnnasu waalhijaratu aalayha malaikatun ghilathun shidadun la aasoona Allaha ma amarahum wayafaaloona ma yumaroona
Ya ayyuha allatheena kafaroo la taatathiroo alyawma innama tujzawna ma kuntum taamaloona
Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo tooboo ila Allahi tawbatan nasoohan aasa rabbukum an yukaffira aankum sayyiatikum wayudkhilakum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu yawma la yukhzee Allahu alnnabiyya waallatheena amanoo maaahu nooruhum yasaa bayna aydeehim wabiaymanihim aqooloona rabbana atmim lana noorana waighfir lana innaka aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Ya ayyuha alnnabiyyu jahidi alkuffara waalmunafiqeena waoghluth aalayhim wamawahum jahannamu wabisa almaseeru
Daraba Allahu mathalan lillatheena kafaroo imraata noohin waimraata lootin kanata tahta aabdayni min aibadina salihayni fakhanatahuma alam yughniya aanhuma mina Allahi shayan waqeela odkhula alnnara maaa alddakhileena
Wadaraba Allahu mathalan lillatheena amanoo imraata firaawna ith qalat rabbi ibni lee aindaka baytan fee aljannati wanajjinee min iraawna waaamalihi wanajjinee mina alqawmi alththalimeena
Wamaryama ibnata aimrana allatee ahsanat farjaha fanafakhna feehi min roohina wasaddaqat bikalimati rabbiha wakutubihi wakanat mina lqaniteena
Tabaraka allathee biyadihi almulku wahuwa aala kulli shayin qadeerun
Allathee khalaqa almawta waalhayata liyabluwakum ayyukum ahsanu aamalan wahuwa alaazeezu alghafooru
Allathee khalaqa sabaa samawatin tibaqan ma tara fee khalqi alrrahmani min tafawutin fairjiai albasara hal tara min futoorin
Thumma irjiai albasara karratayni yanqalib ilayka albasaru khasian wahuwa haseerun
Walaqad zayyanna alssamaa alddunya bimasabeeha wajaaalnaha rujooman lilshshayateeni waaatadna lahum aathaba alssaaeeri
Walillatheena kafaroo birabbihim aathabu jahannama wabisa almaseeru
Itha olqoo feeha samiaoo laha shaheeqan wahiya tafooru
Takadu tamayyazu mina alghaythi kullama olqiya feeha fawjun saalahum khazanatuha alam yatikum natheerun
Qaloo bala qad jaana natheerun fakaththabna waqulna ma nazzala Allahu min shayin in antum illa fee dalalin kabeerin
Waqaloo law kunna nasmaau aw naaqilu ma kunna fee ashabi alssaaeeri
Faiatarafoo bithanbihim fasuhqan liashabi alssaaeeri
Inna allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bialghaybi lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeerun
Waasirroo qawlakum awi ijharoo bihi innahu aaleemun bithati alssudoori
Ala yaalamu man khalaqa wahuwa allateefu alkhabeeru
Huwa allathee jaaala lakumu alarda thaloolan faimshoo fee manakibiha wakuloo min rizqihi wailayhi alnnushooru
Aamintum man fee alssamai an yakhsifa bikumu alarda faitha hiya tamooru
Am amintum man fee alssamai an yursila aalaykum hasiban fasataalamoona kayfa natheeri
Walaqad kaththaba allatheena min qablihim fakayfa kana nakeeri

Amman hatha allathee huwa jundun lakum yansurukum min dooni alrrahmani ini alkafiroona illa fee ghuroorin
